fifth@［ˈfifθ］@num. 第五 n. 五分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's the fifth time that I've been to Chengdu. 这是我第五次去成都。</p>
popcorn@［ˈpɒpkɔ:n］@n. 爆米花</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：pop（流行的）+corn（玉米）→流行的玉米，大家都爱吃→爆米花</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My sister and I like popcorn very much. 我和姐姐都非常喜欢吃爆米花。</p>
impress@［imˈpres］@v. 给…深刻印象，使铭记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：im（进入）+press（压）→压进去→使铭记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> inpress sb. with sth. 用某事物给某人留下深刻印象</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy impressed his girlfriend with his sincerity. 男孩用他的真诚感动了女朋友。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> impression（n. 印象，感觉）</p>
back@［bæk］@adv. 回原处，回原状；向后，后仰着；还；以前；回，往回 n. 背，背部；后面，后部；背面，反面 adj. 后面的，背后的；反向的 v. 后退，使倒退；支持</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> get back to 回到，恢复；take back 收回；使回忆起；at the back of 在…后面；back and forth 来回地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will come back home in ten minutes. 我十分钟后回家。</p>
strong@［strɒŋ］@adj. 强壮的，强有力的，强大的；牢固的；坚强的，坚定的；强烈的，浓的；精通的，擅长的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“死撞”→觉得自己很强壮，一直撞门→强壮的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Which is ______, an elephant or a tiger? （2008年 荆州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. strong</p> <p class="bodytext">B. stronger</p> <p class="bodytext">C. strongest</p> <p class="bodytext">D. the strongest</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>大象和老虎，哪一个更强壮？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是strong的比较级，两者进行比较用比较级，strong的比较级是stronger，因此本题选择B。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> strongly（adv. 强有力地，坚固地）</p>
college@［ˈkɒlidʒ］@n. 大学，学院</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> go to college 上大学；be in college 在上大学</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom's father is a college teacher. 汤姆的父亲是一名大学教师。</p>
white@［wait］@adj. 白色的，白的；白种的 n. 白色；蛋白；眼白</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He likes wearing white clothes. 他喜欢穿白色的衣服。</p>
knee@［ni:］@n. 膝，膝盖</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> His right knee was hurt in a traffic accident. 他的右膝在一次交通事故中受了伤。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">knee中的字母k不发音，注意不要误读。</p></div>
part@［pa:t］@n. 一部分，部分；零件；角色；职责，作用；器官，部位 v. （使）分开 adv. 部分地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take part in 参加；play a part in... 在…中起作用；in part 在某种程度上；部分地；part with... 与…分离</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Henry wanted to take part in the club. 亨利想加入这个俱乐部。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00132.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">depart, part</p>   <p class="bodytext">depart有“离开，启程”的意思，常与from形成搭配，如：depart from this city 离开这座城市；而part是“分开”的意思，如：No one can part the two friends. 没有人能把这两个好朋友分开。</p></div>
chop@［tʃɒp］@n. 排骨 v. ［chopped-chopped, chopping］ 砍，伐，劈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：去商店（shop），买排骨（chop）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The farmer chopped the block of wood into two. 农民将这块木头劈成两半。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> chopper（n. 砍刀）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00133.jpeg"/></div>
nobody@［ˈnəʊbədi］@pron. 没有人，无人 n. 无足轻重的人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：no（不，无）+body（人）→无人，没有人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Nobody knows who broke the glass. 没有人知道是谁打碎了玻璃。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">nobody=no one，两者都只能指代人而不能指物，注意它们后面一般不能接of 短语，作主语的时候谓语动词要用单数，如：Nobody likes the picture. 没有人喜欢这幅画。</p></div>
kiss@［kis］@n. / v. 吻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：和思念（miss）一起记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy kissed his parents before he got on the train. 男孩在上火车之前与他的父母吻别。</p>
upon@［əˈpɒn］@prep. 在…之上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：up（向上）+on（在…上）→在…之上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> look down upon 蔑视，瞧不起</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Parents always rest their hopes upon their children. 父母经常把希望寄托在自己的孩子身上。</p>
week@［wi:k］@n. 星期，周</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She works five days a week. 她每周工作五天。</p>
America@［əˈmerikə］@n. 美国；美洲</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am from America. 我来自美国。</p>
license@［ˈlaisns］@n. 许可（证），执照 vt. 准许</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“来审视”→审视合格才能发执照→执照</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will get my driver's license this July. 今年七月我将拿到驾照。</p>
habitat@［ˈhæbitæt］@n. （动物或植物的）栖息地；住处</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The forest is an important habitat for many animals. 这片森林是许多动物的重要栖息地。</p>
fool@［fu:l］@n. 蠢人，笨蛋 v. 欺骗，愚弄；干蠢事 adj. 愚蠢的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> April Fool's Day is a day celebrated in many countries on April 1. 很多国家都在4月1日过愚人节。</p>
reason@［ˈri:zn］@n. 原因，理由；理性，理智 v. 推断，分析；推论，推理；理喻，劝告</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：和season（n. 季节）一起记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Most people have reasons for changing their names. 多数人改名字是有原因的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> reasonable（adj. 合情合理的；适度的；公道的）；reasoning（n. 推理）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">cause, reason</p>   <p class="bodytext">cause一般表示造成某一事物或现象的直接原因或起因，而在说明或解释某种情况出现的理由时，可以用cause，也可以用reason。另外, cause是不可数名词，且后面不能跟 why 引导的定语从句；而reason是可数名词，后面可以跟why引导的定语从句。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">（〇） The teacher knows the reason why I didn't go to school. 或The teacher knows the cause that I didn't go to school. 老师知道我没去上学的原因。</p>   <p class="bodytext">（✕） The teacher knows the cause why I didn't go to school.</p></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">reason后面跟介词for，不能跟of，如：What's the reason for your help? 你来帮忙的原因是什么？另外，比较常见的是reason后面跟why引导的从句，如：Do you know the reason why I cry? 你知道我哭的原因吗？或者I don't know the reason why he didn't come. 我不知道他没来的理由是什么。</p></div>
picture@［ˈpiktʃə(r)］@n. 画，图片，照片；（生动的）描绘；电影；头脑中的情景，印象 v. （生动地）描绘，描述；设想，想象</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The satellites take pictures of the atmosphere. 人造卫星拍摄大气的图片。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00134.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">picture, painting</p>   <p class="bodytext">picture有“图画；照片”等意思，意义比较宽泛，如：There are many pictures on the wall. 墙上有许多画。而painting是“油画”或“画作”的意思，多指专业画作，如：the paintings of Da Vinci 达·芬奇的画作。</p></div>
than@［ðæn］@conj. 比 prep. 与…比较</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> more than 多于，不仅仅；no more than 只是，仅仅；not more than 不超过，不如…多；rather than 而不是；other than 除了，不同于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> His English is much better than his brother's. 他的英语比他弟弟好多了。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">more...than...与less...than...如何转换？请看下面的例子：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Skiing is more interesting than swimming. 滑雪比游泳有趣多了。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Swimming is less interesting than skiing. 游泳可没有滑雪有趣。</p></div>
OK@［əʊˈkei］@adv. / int. 不错，很好；对吧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> OK, I'll go with you if you're afraid of the dog. 好吧，如果你怕狗，我陪你一起走。</p>
yourself@［jɔ:ˈself］@pron. 你自己；你亲自</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：your（你的）+self（自己）→你自己</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Believe in yourself and in the end you'll make great progress. 相信自己，你最终会取得很大进步的。</p>
alien@［ˈeiliən］@adj. 外国的；外星的；陌生的；格格不入的 n. 外国人；外星人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jack was interested in alien culture. 杰克对异国文化感兴趣。</p>
give@［giv］@v. ［gave-given］ 给予，赠送；供给，提供（信息等）；做出（某一动作），发出（声音等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> give up 放弃；give in 屈服，让步；give off 放出，发出（光、热等）；give out 分发；发出（气味等）；用尽</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">I feel it hard to keep up with my classmates. But whenever I want to ______, my teacher always encourages me to work harder. （2008年 湖北）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. go on</p> <p class="bodytext">B. give up</p> <p class="bodytext">C. run away</p> <p class="bodytext">D. give back</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>我觉得自己的成绩很难赶上我们班同学，但是每当我想放弃的时候，老师总是鼓励我，让我更加刻苦地学习。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>go on意为“继续下去，发生”，give up意为“放弃”，run away意为“潜逃；失控”，give back意为“归还；恢复”，本题根据句意应选B。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">give常用在give sb. sth.这一结构中，还可以说give sth. to sb.，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I gave Tom a book. 我给了汤姆一本书。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I gave a book to Tom. 我给了汤姆一本书。</p></div>
cloud@［klaʊd］@n. 云；一群，一团；阴影；天空 v. 使模糊，使阴暗；遮盖，笼罩</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The sun went behind the cloud and it was going to rain. 太阳躲到了云彩后面，马上要下雨了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> cloudy（adj. 多云的，阴天的）</p>
send@［send］@v. ［sent-sent］ 送，寄；派遣，打发；发送（信号等）；发射</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> send out 发出，放出；send off 送行；寄出；send up 发射；send for sb. 让人去请某人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— ______ did you tell him about the news?</p> <p class="bodytext">—By ______ an e-mail. （2008年 湖北）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. How; sending</p> <p class="bodytext">B. How; send</p> <p class="bodytext">C. How; sent</p> <p class="bodytext">D. What; sending</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—你通过什么方式告诉他这条新闻的呢？</p> <p class="bodytext4">—发邮件。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>by后通常跟名词或动名词形式，表示“通过…方式做某事”。“发送邮件”的固定搭配是send an e-mail。故此题选A。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">send, fetch, deliver</p>   <p class="bodytext">send是“送去”或“发送”的意思，宾语一般是物，如：I will send you a letter. 我会给你寄一封信。而fetch后可跟人或物，意为“去请某人”或“去取某物”，如：Can you fetch a chair from that room? 你能从那个房间拿一把椅子来吗？deliver常用于贸易领域，表示货物或订单已经“交付”，如：They should deliver the goods today according to the contract. 根据合同，他们应该今天交货。</p></div>
instruction@［inˈstrʌkʃn］@n. 命令，指示；教学，教导</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Follow the instructions on the pamphlet carefully. 仔细按照小册子上面的指示执行。</p>
dress@［dres］@n. 连衣裙；衣服，服装 v. 给…穿衣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> dress up 打扮；伪装</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She wore a beautiful dress to join the party. 她穿了件漂亮的连衣裙去参加聚会。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00135.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">dress, skirt</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“裙子”的意思。dress指连衣裙，而skirt指短裙，如：mini-skirt 超短裙。</p></div>
separate@［ˈseprət］@adj. 分离的，分开的；不同的，相区别的</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［ˈseｐəｒｅiｔ］</span> v. 使分离，使分开；划分，区分，区别；分离，分开；分居</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher separated the students into four groups. 老师把学生们分为四个组。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> separately（adv. 分别地；分离地）；separable（adj. 可分离的）</p>
now@［naʊ］@adv. 现在，如今；此刻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> now and then 偶尔</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I used to live in Shanghai but now I'm living in Beijing. 我曾经住在上海，但现在住在北京。</p>
theater/theatre@［ˈθiətə(r)］@n. 戏院，剧场；影剧院</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The National Theater will give two famous performances this Sunday. 国家大剧院本周日将上演两场著名的演出。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00136.jpeg"/></div>
airline@［ˈeəlain］@n. 航空公司；航线</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：air（天空）+line（线）→航线</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I often travel by the international airline. 我经常乘坐国际航空公司的班机旅行。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> airliner（n. 客机，班机）</p>
mine@［main］@pron. 我的（所有物） n. 矿，矿山；地雷；水雷 v. 开矿，采矿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This pen is Linda's, not mine. 这支钢笔是琳达的，不是我的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> miner（n. 矿工）</p>
world@［wɜ:ld］@n. 世界，地球，天下；领域 adj. 世界的，世界范围的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：世界（world）上的人说话都离不开词语（word）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> all over the world 全世界，世界各地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The world is becoming smaller and smaller. 世界变得越来越小。</p>
ring@［riŋ］@n. 戒指；环，圆圈；铃声；（打）电话；团伙，帮派；拳击台，摔跤台，马戏场</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［rang-rung］ 把…圈起来，包围；打电话给；按（铃），敲（钟）；（铃、钟等）鸣，响</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：好莱坞魔幻大片《指环王》（The Lord of the Rings）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The telephone is ringing. It must be mom. 电话响了。一定是妈妈。</p>
learn@［lɜ:n］@v. ［learnt/learned-learnt/learned］ 学，学习；获悉，了解；记住；认识到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：学习（learn）好，挣（earn）钱多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> learn of/about 获悉，了解</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Peter had learned about Britain before he went there. 彼得去英国之前先了解了一下英国。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> learner（n. 学习者）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">learn后面可以接动词不定式，不可以直接接动名词。</p></div>
charity@［ˈtʃærəti］@n. 慈善，施舍；慈善机构</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tina donated her favorite necklace for charity. 蒂娜捐出了她最喜欢的项链用于慈善。</p>
purple@［ˈpɜ:pl］@n./ adj. 紫色（的）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My favorite color is purple while Lily likes pink the best. 我最喜欢的颜色是紫色，而莉莉最喜欢粉色。</p>
school@［sku:l］@n. 学校；（大学里的）学院，系；学业，上课（时间）；学派，流派</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our headmaster usually addresses the whole school on Monday morning. 我们校长通常在周一早上向全校讲话。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">at school与at the school的含义不同，前者是“求学”或“在学校读书”，而后者是“在这个学校（不一定是读书）”。类似的词还有hospital，at hospital表示“住院”，而at the hospital表示“在医院”。</p></div>
hey@［hei］@int. （引起注意或表示兴趣、惊讶或生气） 嘿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I say hey to everyone I know on my way to school. 上学路上，我向每个认识的人打招呼。</p>
daily@［ˈdeili］@adj. 每日的；日常的 adv. 每日，天天 n. 日报</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I do exercises daily. 我每天都锻炼身体。</p>
suitcase@［ˈsu:tkeis］@n. 手提箱，衣箱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Stick a label on your suitcase in case it gets lost. 把你的行李贴上标签以防丢失。</p>
worldwide@［ˈwɜ:ldwaid］@adj. 世界范围的，全世界的 adv. 在世界各地，在全世界</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：world（世界）+wide（宽的）→世界那样宽的→世界范围的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The famous five-star hotel has a worldwide reputation for good service. 这家五星级酒店以其优质服务享誉世界。</p>
celebrate@［ˈselibreit］@v. 庆祝，欢庆；赞扬，歌颂</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old couple celebrated their golden wedding anniversary in a famous 5-star hotel. 这对老夫妇在一家著名的五星级酒店庆祝了他们的金婚纪念日。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> celebration（n. 庆祝，庆典）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00137.jpeg"/></div>
text@［tekst］@n. 正文，原文；课文，课本</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：来测试（test）一下课本（text）上的内容学会没有</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I was asked to read the text first and then answer the question. 老师让我先读课文，然后回答问题。</p>
proper@［ˈprɒpə(r)］@adj. 正确的，适当的；合乎体统的，正当的；固有的，特有的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Some cabbage will be a proper choice for a good soup! 要熬出美味的汤，放一些卷心菜是个不错的选择！</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> properly（adv. 适当地，正确地）；improperly（adv. 不适当地，错误地）</p>
health@［helθ］@n. 健康（状况）；卫生，保健</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：健康（health）是人生最大的财富（wealth）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm worried about my grandmother's health. 我很担心外婆的健康状况。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> healthy（adj. 健康的）</p>
movie@［ˈmu:vi］@n. 电影，影片；电影院，电影业</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：动着（move）的影像就是电影（movie）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually watch movies in my spare time. 我经常在空闲时间看电影。</p>
spider@［ˈspaidə(r)］@n. 蜘蛛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher asked the students to watch the spider. 老师要求学生观察蜘蛛。</p>
goodbye@［ˌgʊdˈbai］@int. 再见</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The actors said goodbye to all the audience. 演员们向在场的所有观众道了别。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00138.jpeg"/></div>
wheel@［wi:l］@n. 轮，车轮 v. 转动，旋转</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are four wheels in the car. 车有四个轮子。</p>
sour@［ˈsaʊə(r)］@adj. 酸的，酸味的；馊的，酸臭的；乖戾的，尖酸刻薄的；发酸的；酸痛的</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. （使）变酸，（使）变馊；（使）变得乖戾（或暴躁）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“馊啊”→饭菜馊了就变酸了→酸的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't like this kind of cherry. It is very sour. 我不喜欢这种樱桃，太酸了。</p>
mall@［mɔ:l］@n. 购物中心，商店区</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：商店（mall）失火，房塌屋倒（fall）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I went to the shopping mall last weekend. 我上周末去了购物中心。</p>
fix@［fiks］@v. 修理；固定；安装；安排，确定；整理，收拾；供给或准备（尤指食物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> fix up 修理；使固定；fix one's eyes on... 注视…；fix one's thoughts/attention on... 专注于…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The new couple have to fix a date for the wedding. 这对新婚夫妇需要确定婚礼的日期。</p>
poem@［ˈpəʊim］@n. 诗</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are four verses in the poem. 这首诗有四节。</p>
sentence@［ˈsentəns］@n. 句子；判决，宣判 v. 宣判，判决</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher asked Jim to make a sentence. 老师让吉姆造一个句子。// The man was sentenced to three years in prison. 这个人被判入狱三年。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">sentence, trial</p>   <p class="bodytext">sentence在法律上是“宣判”的意思，强调审判的结果；而trial是“审判”，侧重于审判的过程。</p></div>
percent@［pə:ˈsnt］@n. 百分比，百分率 adj. 百分之…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：per（每）+cent（百）→每个一百里有多少→百分之…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Fifty-five percent of people didn't like this president. 55%的人不喜欢这位总统。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> percentage（n. 百分比，百分率）</p>  <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00139.jpeg"/></div>
tasty@［ˈteisti］@adj. 美味的；引起食欲的 n. 好吃的东西；吸引人的东西</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These cakes are so tasty that I cannot stop eating. 这些蛋糕太好吃了，让我控制不住一直吃。</p>
marriage@［ˈmæridʒ］@n. 结婚，婚姻，婚礼</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I wish that her marriage is full of happiness. 我祝她婚姻幸福。</p>
grade@［greid］@n. 等级，级别；成绩，分数；（学校的）年级 v. 将…分等级；对…进行评分</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I got good grades last term and won the first class scholarship. 我上学期的成绩不错，获得了一等奖学金。</p>
Thursday@［ˈθɜ:zdei］@n. 星期四</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a meeting on Thursday night. 周四晚上有一个会议。</p>
road@［rəʊd］@n. 路，道路；途径</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：美国乡村音乐《乡村路带我回家》（Take Me Home, Country Road）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> All roads lead to Rome. 条条大路通罗马。</p>
result@［riˈzʌlt］@n. 结果；效果；成绩，成果</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 导致，结果是；起因于，由…造成</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My parents are satisfied with my exam results. 父母对我的考试成绩很满意。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">as a result, because of</p>   <p class="bodytext">两个词组都表示因果关系，要掌握它们的异同：</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00140.jpeg"/></div></div>
any@［ˈeni］@pron. 无论哪个，无论哪些 adj. 任一的，任何的；什么，一些；丝毫的</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 略，稍，丝毫</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We didn't have any lessons yesterday. 我们昨天没有课。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">any, some</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都可作“一些”讲。any用在疑问句和否定句中，some一般用于肯定句中。有一点值得考生注意，在表示征求对方意见或表示发出邀请，以及表示期望得到肯定回答的疑问句中要用some，如：Would you like some water? 要不要喝点儿水？</p></div>
football@［ˈfʊtbɔ:l］@n. 足球；橄榄球</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：foot（足）+ball（球）→足球</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is going to be a football match in our school this afternoon. 今天下午我们学校有一场足球赛。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00141.jpeg"/></div>
room@［ru:m］@n. 房间，室；空间，地方；余地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is not enough room in my house for these boxes. 我家没有足够的空间放这些箱子。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">room, space, place</p>   <p class="bodytext">三个词都有“地方”的意思。room作“空间，地方”讲的时候是不可数名词，如：The large bed takes up too much room. 那张大床太占地方了。space作“空间”讲的时候是不可数名词，如：The desk takes up too much space. 桌子占了很大空间。作“空出来的地方”讲时是可数名词，如：I'll clear a space for your books. 我会给你的书腾出一块地方。place是可数名词，表示“位置，地点”，含义比较具体。比较下面一组对话：</p>   <p class="bodytext">A: Is there any room/space in the ship?</p>   <p class="bodytext">B: Yes, that place in the corner is empty.</p>   <p class="bodytext">A：船上有空地方吗？</p>   <p class="bodytext">B：有，在那边角落里还有个空位子。</p></div>
cause@［kɔ:z］@n. 原因，理由 v. 使发生，引起；使遭受；给…带来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：和because（conj. 因为）一起记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Laziness and unemployment are major causes of poverty. 懒惰和失业是贫穷的主要原因。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> because（conj. 因为）；causable（adj. 可引起的）；causeless（adj. 偶然的，无显著原因的）</p>
bad@［bæd］@adj. 坏的；不利的；差的，有缺陷的；邪恶的，道德败坏的；严重的，厉害的；腐烂的，腐败的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Dan caught a bad cold. 丹得了重感冒。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">bad的比较级和最高级是不规则的，分别是worse和worst，要牢记。</p></div>
unhealthy@［ʌnˈhelθi］@adj. 不健康的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：un（不）+healthy（健康的）→不健康的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People should get rid of unhealthy life styles. 人们应该戒除一些不健康的生活方式。</p>
holiday@［ˈhɒlədei］@n. 假期，假日</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> summer/winter holiday 暑/寒假</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I spent my summer holiday in Japan last year. 去年我在日本过的暑假。</p>
draw@［drɔ:］@v. ［drew-drawn］ 画，描绘；拖，拉；拔出，抽出；提取，汲取；引起；吸引；推断出；打成平局 n. 平局，和局；抽签，抽彩</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> draw a conclusion 得出结论；draw one's attention 吸引某人的注意</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do you know how the painter draws a picture? 你知道画家是如何画画的吗？</p>
create@［kriˈeit］@v. 创造；创作；引起，产生</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The government plans to create more job opportunities for young people. 政府计划为年轻人创造更多的工作机会。</p>
wish@［wiʃ］@v. 希望，想要；但愿；祝，祝愿；盼望，企求</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 愿望，心愿；［pl.］ 祝愿，致意；请求</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> wish for 希望得到，渴望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I wish I could do the work as perfectly as you do. 我希望自己能把工作做得像你一样完美。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">wish, hope</p>   <p class="bodytext">wish一般表示不太可能实现的希望，常用于虚拟语气，也可以用作wish to do sth.，表示“想要做某事”，如：I wish I could fly to the moon. 我希望自己能飞到月亮上去。而hope不用虚拟语气，如：I hope that we will win the game. 我希望我们能赢得比赛。wish是及物动词，可以接双宾语，构成wish sb. sth.的形式，如：We wish you success. 我们希望你成功。而hope不能直接跟名词作宾语，可以跟“for+名词”，表示可实现的希望，如：I hope for success. 我希望成功。</p></div>
exam@［igˈzæm］@n. 考试；试题；检查，调查</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom had tried his best but he failed the exam in the end. 汤姆已经尽了最大的努力，但最终还是没有通过考试。</p>
art@［a:t］@n. 美术，艺术；技术，技艺；［pl.］ 人文科学，文科</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm greatly interested in art. 我对艺术很感兴趣。</p>
sweet@［swi:t］@adj. 甜的；和蔼的，温柔的；可爱的，讨人喜欢的；芳香的，悦耳的，悦目的</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. ［pl.］ 糖果，甜食；亲爱的（人）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：浑身流汗（sweat）的人可不是芬芳（sweet）扑鼻的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Too much sweet food is bad for your health. 太多的甜食对你的健康不利。</p>
donate@［dəʊˈneit］@v. 捐赠，赠送</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> donate sth. to sb. 向某人捐赠某物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He decided to donate a large part of his wealth to homeless children. 他决定把自己的一大部分财产捐给无家可归的儿童。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> donation（n. 捐款；捐赠物）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00142.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">donate常用在donate sth. to sb.这一结构中，表示“向某人捐赠某物”，值得注意的是其中的to为介词，后面如果不跟sb.则要跟动名词。</p></div>
too@［tu:］@adv. 也，还；太，过于；很，非常</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You'd better not spend too much time surfing online. 你最好不要花太多的时间上网。</p>
him@［him］@pron. 他</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I met him ten days ago. 我十天前见过他。</p>
rule@［ru:l］@n. 规则，规章；习惯，惯例，惯常的事；统治，管辖</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 统治，控制；（作出）裁决（或裁定）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I generally make it a rule to be up by 7 to read English. 我养成了一个习惯，一般早上七点起来读英语。</p>
autumn@［ˈɔ:təm］@n. 秋，秋季</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think autumn is the most beautiful season of a year. 我觉得秋天是一年中最美的季节。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在美式英语中，常用fall来代替autumn。</p></div>
yellow@［ˈjeləʊ］@adj. 黄的 n. 黄色</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do you like the yellow coat? 你喜欢那件黄色的外套吗？</p>
these@［ði:z］@pron. 这些</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These two countries had three wars in the past 50 years. 这两个国家在过去50年中打过三次仗。</p>
advertisement@［ədˈvɜ:tismənt;ˌædvərˈtaizmənt］@n. 广告，公告；广告活动，宣传</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Because of an advertisement you may buy something you don't need.你可能因为一则广告而购买并不需要的东西。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">注意该词英式发音和美式发音的区别。有时该词还会缩写为ad。</p></div>
whom@［hu:m］@pron. （who的宾格）谁</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The girl with whom you traveled to Beijing is my sister. 和你一起去北京旅游的女孩是我妹妹。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">whom是疑问代词who的宾格形式，在从句中只能作宾语，如：The man whom you met yesterday is my brother. 你昨晚见的人是我哥哥。</p></div>
rise@［raiz］@v. ［rose-risen］ 升起，上升；起立；起床；上涨，增加；反抗，起义</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 上涨，增加；兴起；（地位的）升高；岗，坡，高地；起源，发源</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man was excited to see the sun rising from the east. 看到太阳从东方升起来，那个人兴奋不已。</p>
term@［tɜ:m］@n. 措词，术语；期限，任期；学期；［pl.］ 条款，条件；关系</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 把…称为，把…叫做</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There will be another exam at the end of this term. 这学期期末还有一场考试。</p>
operation@［ˌɒpəˈreiʃn］@n. 操作，运转，经营；手术；（军事）行动，活动；运算</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：operat（看作operate，经营）+ion→经营，操作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Don't tell me the operation of the machine is simple. 别跟我说操作这台机器很简单。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> operational（adj. 操作的）；operative（adj. 实施的）</p>
coal@［kəʊl］@n. 煤，煤块</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The explorers found a coal mine nearly two hundred meters deep. 勘探者发现了一个将近200米深的煤矿。</p>
until@［ənˈtil］@prep. / conj. 直到…时，到…为止；直到…（才）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> not...until... 直到…才…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He did not leave until I returned home last night. 昨晚直到我回家他才离开。</p>
habit@［ˈhæbit］@n. 习惯，习性</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> develop / form / get into a habit （of...） 养成一个（…）习惯；have a habit of... 有…的习惯</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have a habit of eating an apple every day. 我习惯每天吃一个苹果。</p>
tour@［tʊə(r)］@n. / v. 旅行，旅游</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We were given a guided tour of the Summer Palace. 我们由导游带领游览了颐和园。</p>
regular@［ˈregjələ(r)］@adj. 规则的；有规律的，定期的；整齐的，匀称的；正规的，正式的；常规的，经常的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I live a healthy and regular life. 我过着健康而有规律的生活。</p>
polar@［ˈpəʊlə(r)］@adj. 地极的，近地极的；磁极的；正好相反的，截然对立的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：pol（看作pole，极）+ar（形容词后缀）→地极的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> the polar regions 极地地区</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> polarity（n. 极性）；polarize（v. 使极化）</p>
many@［ˈmeni］@adj. 许多的，多的 pron. 许多人，许多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> many a 许多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You can help other people in many ways. 你可以通过很多途径来帮助他人。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">many, much</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“许多的”之意，但修饰的名词不同。many常修饰可数名词，如：many students 许多学生；而much修饰不可数名词，如：much time 许多时间。</p></div>
them@［ðəm］@pron. 他（她、它）们</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> When I told them the news, none of us could stop crying. 当我告诉他们这则消息时，大家都禁不住哭了起来。</p>
single@［ˈsiŋgl］@adj. 单一的，单个的；未婚的，独身的；（床或房间）单人的；单程的</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 单程票；［pl.］ （网球等的）单打</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I couldn't understand a single word the teacher said. 老师说的话我一句都不懂。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00143.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">single, only</p>   <p class="bodytext">single与“双”相对应，强调“单”，如：I am single. 我是单身。only指在一类中绝无仅有时，前面常加the，如：The boy is the only child in his family. 这个男孩是家里的独生子。</p></div>
church@［tʃɜ:tʃ］@n. 教堂；礼拜；教会（组织）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I went to the church to visit the priest the day before yesterday. 前天我去教堂拜访了牧师。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00144.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">go to church和go to the church意义不同，前者指“做礼拜”，后者指“去教堂”，注意区分。</p></div>
subway@［ˈsʌbwei］@n. 地铁；地道，地下过道</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：sub（在…下面）+way（道路）→地铁；地下过道</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I take the subway to go to work every day. 我每天乘地铁上班。</p>
pro@［prəʊ］@n. ［pl. pros］ 投票赞成者；赞成的意见（或理由）；从事某种职业的人，职业运动员 adj. 赞成的；正面的 adv. 赞成地 prep. 赞成</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Simon is a basketball pro. 西蒙是一个职业篮球运动员。</p>
pen@［pen］@n. 钢笔；圆珠笔；（牲畜等的）围栏</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy bought a new pen for his friend as a gift. 男孩给朋友买了一支新钢笔作为礼物。</p>
calendar@［ˈkælində(r)］@n. 日历，月历；日程表</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I bought a new desk calendar for the Year 2012 yesterday. 昨天我买了一本2012年的新台历。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00145.jpeg"/></div>
hold@［həʊld］@v. ［held-held］ 拿，握；使保持某种状态（或姿势）；掌握（权力），担任（职务等）；容纳，包含；托住，支撑；举行，主持</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> hold on 稍等，别挂电话；hold on to... 紧紧抓住…；坚持…；hold to... 坚持…；握紧…；hold up 举起；hold back 隐瞒；抑制</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a meeting being held in the conference room. 会议室里正在开会。</p>
earthquake@［ˈɜ:θkweik］@n. 地震</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：earth（地球）+quake（震动）→地震</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> In 2008 a massive earthquake happened in Sichuan. 2008年四川发生了强烈的地震。</p>
collect@［kəˈlｅｋｔ］@v. 收集，采集；收（账、欠款等）；领取；聚集，汇集 adj. （打电话）由对方付费的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> collect stamps 集邮</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I've been collecting information on the Wenchuan earthquake. 我一直在搜集汶川地震的信息。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> collective（adj. 共同的；集体的）；collection（n. 收藏品）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">collect, gather</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“收集”的意思，但是有区别。collect侧重于为了研究、爱好或欣赏而进行的精心且有选择的收集，如集邮、收集古钱币等，如：I like collecting stamps. 我喜欢集邮。gather指把分散的东西聚拢在一起，表示“集合”，如：Martin is gathering information. 马丁正在收集信息。</p></div>
seventeen@［ˌsevnˈti:n］@num. 十七，十七个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My grandmother got married at the age of seventeen. 我的祖母在17岁时就结婚了。</p>
poor@［pʊə］@adj. 贫困的，贫穷的；可怜的；低劣的，差的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“破”→东西都很破，家里很穷→贫穷的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lily lives a poor but happy life. 莉莉过着贫穷却幸福的生活。</p>
government@［ˈgʌvənmənt］@n. 政府；内阁；治理，统治；方法；政体</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The government tried to make the society peaceful. 政府试图使社会和平。</p>
haircut@［ˈheə（r）kʌt］@n. 理发</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：hair（头发）+cut（剪）→理发</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will have a haircut this weekend. 这个周末我要去理发。</p>
French@［frentʃ］@n. 法国人；法语 dj. 法国的；法国人的；法语的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think French films are more splendid than American films. 我觉得法国电影比美国电影更精彩。</p>
dear@［diə(r)］@adj. 亲爱的；昂贵的 int. 啊，哎呀 n. 亲爱的人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：心爱的（dear）小狗死（dead）了</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to share this good news with my dear friends. 我想跟我亲爱的朋友们一起分享这个好消息。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00146.jpeg"/></div>
take@［teik］@v. ［took-taken］ 带（去），携带；需要，花费；拿，取得；接受；吃，喝，服（药等）；乘（车），上（船）；测定，量（体温、尺寸等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take advantage of... 利用…；take charge of... 负责…；take one's time 不用着急，慢慢来；take it easy 放松；不要着急；take part in 参加</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can you take these books to the classroom? 你能把这些书带到教室去吗？</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">take, bring, fetch</p>   <p class="bodytext">take意为“带去”，表示把东西从说话人这里带走，如：Take these food away. 把这些食物拿走。而bring正好相反，意为“带来”，表示把东西带到说话人这里来，如：Please bring me some apples. 请给我拿来一些苹果。fetch则表示“取来”，即过去拿了并带回来，如：The dog fetched the stick that I had tossed. 狗取回了我扔出去的棍子。</p></div>
mirror@［ˈmirə(r)］@n. 镜子 v. 反映；反射，映照</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The woman has a mirror in her bag. 这个女人的包里有面镜子。</p>  <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00147.jpeg"/></div>
city@［ˈsiti］@n. 城市，都市</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I was born in a small city in the North of China. 我出生在中国北方的一座小城市里。</p>
stupid@［ˈstju:pid］@adj. 愚蠢的，迟钝的；无聊的；恼人的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I made a really stupid mistake. 我犯了一个很愚蠢的错误。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00148.jpeg"/></div>
wine@［wain］@n. （葡萄）酒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：获胜（win）了喝酒（wine）庆祝</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> France is world famous for its wine. 法国以其葡萄酒闻名世界。</p>
guilty@［ˈgilti］@adj. 有罪的，犯罪的；感到惭愧的，内疚的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I felt guilty when I broke the vase. 我打碎了花瓶后，感到非常内疚。</p>
shape@［ʃeip］@n. 形状，体形；幻象；状况，状态</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 使成形，塑造，形成；决定…的进程（或发展方向）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：美国流行音乐组合Backstreet Boys（后街男孩）的歌曲Shape of My Heart</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in shape 在外形上处于良好状态；健康；out of shape 变形；不健康</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A few roads in Singapore are named by their shapes. 新加坡的很多道路都是根据它们的形状命名的。</p>
dead@［ded］@adj. 死的；无感觉的；呆板的 n. 死者 adv. 完全地；绝对地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：头脑（head）呆板（dead）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The prison breaker was shot dead by the police outside the prison. 越狱者在监狱外被警方击毙了。</p>
obey@［əˈbeｉ］@v. 服从，听从</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“儿背”→儿子背着父辈的话，言听计从→服从</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Everyone who walks on the street should obey the traffic rules. 每一个走在大街上的人都应该遵守交通规则。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00149.jpeg"/></div>
almost@［ˈɔ:lməʊst］@adv. 几乎，差不多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Education plays an important part in almost everyone's life. 教育几乎在每个人的生活中都扮演着重要的角色。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">almost, nearly</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“几乎”的意思，但是用法有些不同。almost可与no, nothing, none, never等连用，此时不能用nearly代替，如：Almost no one escaped from the accident. 几乎无人逃过那场事故。在具体数字前面常用nearly，如：I am nearly 30 years old. 我快30岁了。</p></div>
seventh@［ˈsevnθ］@num. 第七（个） n. 七分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows is the seventh and final of the Harry Potter novels written by J. K. Rowling. 《哈利·波特与死亡圣器》是J. K. 罗琳写的《哈利·波特》系列小说的第七本，也是最后一本。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00150.jpeg"/></div>
chance@［tʃa:ns］@n. 可能性；机会，机遇；偶然的事 v. 碰巧，偶然发生；偶然看见</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> by chance 偶然，凑巧；by any chance 万一，可能；take one's chance 碰运气，冒险</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lucy thought that she had only a slim chance of passing the exam. 露西认为自己通过考试的可能性微乎其微。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> chancy（adj. 冒险的；不确定的）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">chance, opportunity</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“机会”的含义。chance指偶然出现的好机会，如：Jim had a chance to go to college. 吉姆有机会上大学。而opportunity常指有利的客观条件或恰好的时候，如：I have no opportunity to talk to her. 我没有机会和她说话。</p></div>
microwave@［ˈmaikrəweiv］@n. 微波；微波炉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：micro（微）+wave（波）→微波</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> microwave oven 微波炉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do you often use the microwave oven? 你经常用微波炉吗？</p>
doubt@［daʊt］@n. 疑惑，怀疑 v. 怀疑，不相信</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：双重（double）身份，值得怀疑（doubt）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> no doubt 毫无疑问；without doubt 毫无疑问；beyond doubt 毋庸置疑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I doubt whether he can pass the exam. 我怀疑他能否通过考试。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">doubt作名词时常和about连用；作动词时，其后常接whether或if引导的从句，但在否定句和疑问句中只能接that引导的从句，考生要注意辨别，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I doubt whether he reached the train station. 我怀疑他是否到火车站了。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I don't doubt that Jack can finish the task. 我不怀疑杰克能够完成任务。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Do you doubt that Linda will succeed? 你怀疑琳达会成功吗？</p></div>
master@［ˈma:stə(r)］@n. （男）主人，雇主；能手；名家，大师 v. 掌握，精通；征服 adj. 主要的，最重要的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man is a master of language. 这个人是个语言大师。</p>
cheer@［tʃiə(r)］@v. 使振奋，使高兴；为…欢呼，为…喝彩 n. 欢呼，喝彩</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：喝着啤酒（beer），为中国队欢呼（cheer）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> cheer sb. on 为某人鼓劲、加油；cheer sb. up 使某人高兴；使某人振奋</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> All the students cheered up at the thought of seeing their teacher again. 一想到可以再见到老师，所有同学都高兴起来。</p>
across@［əˈkrɒs］@prep. 穿过，越过，横过；在…对面；遍及</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 从一边到另一边，横过；在对面</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：a（表加强）+cross（横过）→横过</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> come across 偶遇，不期而遇</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We walked across the field. 我们穿过农田。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00151.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">across, through</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“穿过”的意思。across是指从表面穿过，如：go across the street 穿过马路；through 指从里边穿过，如：go through the forest 穿过森林。</p></div>
cake@［keik］@n. 饼，糕，蛋糕</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Betty wants to make a cake for her friends. 贝蒂想为她的朋友们做一个蛋糕。</p>
oak@［əʊk］@n. 橡树；橡木</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a big oak tree in the garden. 花园里有一棵大橡树。</p>
spot@［spɒt］@n. 地点，处所；斑点，污点；少量</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［spotted-spotted, spotting］ 认出，发现；玷污，弄脏；用点做记号</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There was a guy on the spot seeing the whole process of the crime. 案发现场有一个人目睹了犯罪的整个经过。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> spotless（adj. 没有污点的）；spotted（adj. 有斑点的，斑纹的）</p>
yog(h)urt@［ˈjɒgət］@n. 酸奶，酵母乳</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：常吃的“优格乳”就是yogurt的音译</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Paul likes yogurt very much. 保罗非常喜欢酸奶。</p>
taste@［teist］@n. 滋味；味觉，口味；鉴赏力；兴趣，爱好 v. 有…味道；品尝；体验，感受</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> taste of 品尝，体验到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Oh. I'm hungry. Mum, can I have the hamburger on the plate?</p> <p class="bodytext">— No. It tastes ______. （2009年 淄博）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. terribly</p> <p class="bodytext">B. terrible</p> <p class="bodytext">C. good</p> <p class="bodytext">D. well</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 我饿了，妈妈，我可以吃盘子里的汉堡吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 不可以，它的味道很糟糕。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>taste意为“品尝”，是表示人体感官的系动词，后面直接加形容词，表示“尝起来如何”，只有B和C两项是形容词，但是根据上下文的意思，应该是味道很糟糕，因此答案选B。</p>
circle@［ˈsɜ:kl］@n. 圆，圆圈；圈子，界；阶层 v. 围着，圈出；环绕…移动；盘旋，环行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：circ（圆，圈）+le→圆，圆圈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The group of people sat down in a circle and started to chat. 一行人环坐成一圈开始聊天。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> circular（adj. 圆形的；循环的 n. 通知）</p>
medium@［ˈmi:diəm］@adj. 中等的；平均的 n. 媒介，工具；手段，方法</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：medi（中间）+um→中等的；媒介</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> mass media 大众传媒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span>—What size does your son wear?</p> <p class="bodytext6">—Medium.</p> <p class="bodytext6">—你儿子穿多大号？</p> <p class="bodytext6">—中号。</p>
greet@［gri:t］@v. 问候，迎接；对…作出反应</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：见面（meet）的时候互致问候（greet）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Uncle Wang greeted me at the door. 王叔叔在门口迎接了我。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> greeting（n. 祝贺，问候）</p>
dangerous@［ˈdeindʒərəs］@adj. 危险的，不安全的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be dangerous to 对…是危险的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The traffic here is very dangerous. 这里的交通很危险。</p>
perfect@［ˈpɜ:fikt］@adj. 完美的，无瑕的；完全的，十足的；最佳的，理想的</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 使完美，改善</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's a perfect day for climbing the mountain. 这是爬山的绝好天气。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> perfection（n. 完美，完善）；perfectionist（n. 完美主义者）</p>
lion@［ˈlaiən］@n. 狮子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：狮子（lion）走过来，动物排成排（line）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The lion has yellowish-brown hair. 这头狮子长着黄褐色的毛。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00152.jpeg"/></div>
coffee@［ˈkɒfi］@n. 咖啡，咖啡豆；咖啡树；咖啡色</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I prefer tea to coffee. 比起咖啡来，我更喜欢喝茶。</p>
thing@［θiŋ］@n. 事，事情，事件；物，东西；局面，情况，事态；所有物，用品</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The most important thing is to keep a balanced diet. 最重要的事情就是保持均衡的饮食。</p>
go@［gəʊ］@v. ［went-gone］ 去；离开；变得，成为；运转，运行；被放置；伸展；通往</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> go over 复习；查看；查阅；go through 通过；经历；全面检查；go along with 陪伴；赞同；go about 着手做某事；四处走动；go on （doing） sth. 继续（做某事）；go into 进入；从事某一行业；go after 追逐；追求；go around 来回走动；go by 走过；顺便拜访</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Will you go to the park tomorrow? 你明天去公园吗？</p>
experience@［ikˈspiəriəns］@n. 经历，阅历；经验，体验 v. 经历，体验，感受</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Going to Disney Land was really an unforgettable experience for me. 迪士尼乐园之旅对我来说真是一段难忘的经历。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">experience作“经历”讲时是可数名词，作“经验”讲时是不可数名词。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">It was interesting to hear about your experiences as a doctor. 听你讲当医生的经历很有意思。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I have no experience of this type of work. 我没有做这种工作的经验。</p></div>
fry@［frai］@v. 油煎，油炸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：油炸（fry）产生的烟熏得她想哭（cry）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will fry up some fish for dinner. 晚餐我要炸鱼。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">fry的过去分词是fried，常用来修饰名词，如：fried chicken 炸鸡；fried chips 炸薯条。</p></div>
transportation@［ˌtrænspɔ:ˈteiʃn］@n. 运输，运输系统；运输工具</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：transport （传送，运输）+at+ion（名词后缀）→运输，运输系统</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The train is recognized as a safe means of transportation. 火车被认为是一种安全的运输工具。</p>
serve@［sɜ:v］@v. 为…服务；任（职）；招待，接待，伺候；符合，适用于，满足；供应；发（球）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> serve as 作为；用作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The dining room will serve three meals a day from 7:00 am to 7:00 pm. 餐厅每日提供三餐，从早7点开始到晚7点结束。</p>
avenue@［ˈævənju:］@n. 林荫道；道路，大街</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The bookstore is on Fifth Avenue. 这家书店位于第五大道。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00153.jpeg"/></div>
weak@［wi:k］@adj. 虚弱的，无力的；（能力等）弱的，差的；微弱的，稀薄的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：每上完一周（week）的课，总觉得浑身无力（weak）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She was very weak after the operation. 她手术后非常虚弱。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">weak, slight</p>   <p class="bodytext">weak可以指“身体虚弱”或者“信号差”，如：a weak heart 内心软弱；而slight意为“轻微的”，侧重“小”的意思，也有“微不足道的”之意，如：slight matters 微不足道的小事。</p></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">be weak in意思是“在某方面差”，跟be good at的含义正好相反，如：The boy is weak in English. 那个男孩英语比较差。</p></div>
fish@［fiʃ］@n. 鱼 v. 钓（鱼），捕（鱼）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：第一盘菜（dish）是水煮鱼（fish）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I always buy some fish for my cat. 我总是给我的猫买鱼吃。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">fish在作“鱼”这个整体概念讲时是不可数名词，作“各种鱼”讲时是可数名词，结尾加-es。</p></div> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00154.jpeg"/></div>
rapid@［ˈræpid］@adj. 迅速的，快的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：兔子（rabbit）跑得相当快（rapid）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mark made rapid progress in his studies. 马克在学习上进步很快。</p>
ride@［raid］@v. 骑（马）；乘（车）</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 骑（马），乘（车）；骑马（或乘车等）旅行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I enjoy bike riding in the mountains. 我喜欢在山路上骑自行车。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00155.jpeg"/></div>
meaning@［ˈmi:niŋ］@n. 意思，含义；意义</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't understand the meaning of the sentence. 我不理解这句话的意思。</p>
everyone@［ˈevriwʌn］@pron. 每人，人人，各人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Everyone has a chance to win the competition. 每个人都有赢得比赛的机会。</p>
France@［fra:ns］@n. 法国</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Paris is the capital city of France. 巴黎是法国的首都。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">France, French</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者经常出现在考试中，考生要注意区分。France是名词，意思是“法国”，而French有两种词性，作名词时意思是“法国人；法语”，作形容词时意思是“法国的；法国人的；法语的”。</p></div>
moment@［ˈməʊmənt］@n. 片刻，瞬间，时刻；机会，时机</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> at this moment 此时，此刻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Bob is not at home at this moment. 鲍勃此刻不在家。</p>
bathroom@［ˈba:θru:m］@n. 浴室；盥洗室</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> John is in the bathroom at the moment. 约翰此刻在浴室里。</p>
ancient@［ˈeinʃənt］@adj. 古代的，古老的；年老的，看上去很老的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Linda lives in an ancient house. 琳达住在一所老房子里。</p>
park@［pa:k］@n. 公园；停车场 v. 停放（车辆等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's forbidden to park here. 这里禁止停车。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> parking（n. 停车场）</p>
near@［niə(r)］@adv. 近，在近处 prep. 靠近，接近 adj. 近的，接近的；亲近的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom's home is near the school. 汤姆家离学校很近。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">near, nearly</p>   <p class="bodytext">near和nearly都是副词，含义却不一样。near表示“在附近”，如：I live near here. 我住在这附近。nearly是程度副词，表示“几乎”，如：I nearly passed the exam. 我差点就通过考试了。</p></div>
expensive@［ikˈspensiv］@adj. 昂贵的，花钱多的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The necklace is too expensive. I can't afford it. 这条项链太贵了。我买不起。</p>
refrigerator@［riˈfridʒəreitə(r)］@n. 电冰箱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary stored a lot of food in the refrigerator. 玛丽在冰箱里储存了大量食物。</p>
skate@［skeit］@n. 冰鞋 v. 溜冰，滑冰</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It was so cold these days that we were able to go skating on the lake. 这几天很冷，我想我们可以去湖上滑冰了。</p>
sure@［ʃʊə(r)］@adj. 肯定的，有把握的；一定的，必然的；可靠的，稳妥的 adv. 确实；当然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be sure about 有把握，确信；make sure that 确定；for sure 确实</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Are you sure you'll study abroad? 你确定要出国留学吗？</p>
Chinese@［ˈtʃaini:z］@n. 中国人；中国话，中文 adj. 中国（人）的；中国话的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I feel proud that I am Chinese. 作为一个中国人，我感到很自豪。</p>
cry@［krai］@v. 哭，哭泣；叫喊，鸣，叫；大声地说 n. 哭；哭声；叫喊；叫声</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The baby is crying for his mother. 婴儿在哭着要妈妈。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">cry的第三人称单数要变y为i再加-es，即cries。它的过去式和过去分词都是cried。</p></div>
first@［fɜ:st］@num. 第一 adj. 最先的，最早的 adv. 先，在首位；第一次，首次</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> at first 起初</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I first met Lisa three years ago. 我三年前第一次见到莉萨。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">first是one的序数词，在句子中时前面常加定冠词the。</p></div>
among@［əˈmʌŋ］@prep. 在…之中，在…之间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— How long has the nationwide ban（禁止） on plastic bags been put into practice?</p> <p class="bodytext">— ______ the beginning of June. （2009年 宜昌）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. Behind</p> <p class="bodytext">B. Since</p> <p class="bodytext">C. Among</p> <p class="bodytext">D. At</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 全国范围的限塑令实施多长时间了？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 从6月初开始的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查几个介词的用法。behind意为“在…之后”；among意为“在…之间”；而at the beginning of是固定搭配，意为“在…之初”。句中使用的是现在完成时，故本题应该选B。since表示“自…以来”。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00156.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">among, between</p>   <p class="bodytext">among, between都有“在…之间”的意思。前者指在三者或三者以上事物之间，如：I find the letter among a pile of books. 我在一堆书中找到了这封信。between指在两者之间，常用在between...and...这一结构中，如：The little boy stands between his father and mother. 小男孩站在他父母之间。</p></div>
conjunction@［kənˈdʒʌŋkʃn］@n. 联合；连词</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The workbook is used in conjunction with the textbook. 练习册是与教科书配套使用的。</p>
carry@［ˈkæri］@v. 提，挑，背；运送，运载；输送，传送，传播；携带，怀着；支撑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little boy was carrying a big suitcase. 小男孩背着一个很大的行李箱。</p>
office@［ˈɒfis］@n. 办公室，办事处，营业所；处，所，局；公职，官职，职责；帮忙，服务</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boss is still in the office. 老板仍然在办公室里。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> officer（n. 军官）；official（n. 官员，行政人员 adj. 官方的，正式的；公职的）；officialism（n. 官僚主义）</p>
importance@［imˈpɔ:tns］@n. 重要（性）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I finally realized the importance of using cloth bags. 我最终意识到了用布袋的重要性。</p>
stress@［stres］@n. 压力，紧张；强调，重要性；重音 v. 强调，着重；重读</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：s+tress（看作dress，穿衣）→穿什么衣服，强调什么身份→强调</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People are trying their best to bear the stress of modern life. 人们都在竭尽全力来承受现代生活的压力。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> stressful（adj. 充满压力的）</p>
fever@［ˈfi:və(r)］@n. 发热，发烧；狂热</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：一剂感冒药，发热（fever）永不（never）来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I got a fever when I was in Hainan. 我在海南时发烧了。</p>
island@［ˈailənd］@n. 岛，岛屿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The experts are exploring every part of the island. 专家们正在探索岛屿的每一部分。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00157.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">注意该词的字母s不发音，听的时候要留心。</p></div>
energy@［ˈenədʒi］@n. 干劲，精力；能量；能源</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：en+erg（活动，能量）+y→能量</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It costs me a great deal of energy to finish this task. 完成这项任务花了我大量的精力。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">energy, strength</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“力”的含义，但是侧重点不同。energy侧重于精力或能量，而strength指体力。</p></div>
provide@［prəˈvaid］@v. 供应，提供</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> provide sb. with sth. / provide sth. for sb. 为…提供…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Ms. Smith provided me with an English reference book. 史密斯女士给我提供了一本英文参考书。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext5">provide, supply, afford</p>   <p class="bodytext">provide有免费供给的含义，如：The hotel provided network service. 酒店提供网络服务。supply则无此含义，如：We supply goods with perfect quality. 我们提供的货物有绝好的质量。provide和supply都不接双宾语。afford可接双宾语，一般只用于抽象事物，如：He can hardly afford the pleasure. 他几乎无法承受这欢乐。</p></div>
ourselves@［ˌaʊəˈselvz］@pron. 我们自己；我们亲自</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：our（我们的）+selves（self的复数，自己）→我们自己</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We enjoyed ourselves at the party. 我们在聚会上玩得很愉快。</p>
bowl@［bəʊl］@n. 碗，钵</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Helen drunk a bowl of water. 海伦喝了一碗水。</p>
carrot@［ˈkærət］@n. 胡萝卜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：鹦鹉（parrot）在吃胡萝卜（carrot）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Vegetables like carrots, celery and spinach are very healthy. 像胡萝卜、芹菜和菠菜这样的蔬菜对健康非常有益。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00158.jpeg"/></div>
reach@［ri:tʃ］@v. 抵达；达到；延伸到；伸出（手）；够到；与…取得联系；达成（协议等）</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. （智力、影响等的所及）范围；理解力</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> reach out 伸出</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Frank would call me if he reached the airport. 如果弗兰克到达机场了，他会给我打电话的。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">arrive, reach</p>   <p class="bodytext">arrive是不及物动词，表示“到达，抵达”，后面经常接介词at（跟小地方）或者in（跟大地方），如：I arrived at school. 我到学校了。I arrived in Beijing. 我到北京了。reach是及物动词，直接接宾语，无需加介词，如：They reached the airport on time. 他们准时到了机场。</p></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">out of (one's) reach是“无法得到”或者“够不到”之意，这一搭配在一些阅读文章中经常出现，如：The apples on the tree are out of the children's reach. 孩子们够不着树上的苹果。</p></div>
partner@［ˈpa:tnə(r)］@n. 配偶，搭档；伙伴，合伙人 v. 做…的搭档</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：part（部分）+ner→生活的一部分→搭档</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> China and America are trading partners. 中国和美国是贸易伙伴。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00159.jpeg"/></div>
strict@［strikt］@adj. 严格的，严厉的；严谨的，精确的；完全的，不折不扣的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be strict with... 对…很严格/严厉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My father is very strict with my study. 父亲对我的学习要求非常严格。</p>
ready@［ˈredi］@adj. 准备好的，现成的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be ready to do sth. / for sth. 准备好做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Maria has been ready for school. 玛丽亚已经准备好去上学了。</p>
fence@［fens］@n. 栅栏，篱笆 v. （用栅栏、篱笆或围栏）围住，隔开；回避，搪塞</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“粉丝”→“粉丝”拥在栅栏外寻求签名→栅栏</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The garden was fenced around with wire. 花园用铁丝网围起来了。</p>
entertainment@［ˌentəˈteinmənt］@n. 娱乐；表演会；招待，款待</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The local hotel is famous for its entertainment. 这家旅馆以其殷勤待客而著名。</p>
chalk@［tʃɔ:k］@n. 粉笔</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher wrote on the blackboard with a piece of chalk. 老师用一支粉笔在黑板上写字。</p>
desk@［desk］@n. 书桌，办公桌</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a desk in the boy's room. 男孩的房间里有一张桌子。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00160.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">desk, table</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“桌子”的意思，但是有区别。desk指学生学习时用的课桌、书桌或老师、办公室工作人员用的办公桌。table指供人们吃饭、喝茶、游戏娱乐时用的餐桌、桌子等，一般不带抽屉，可以是方的，也可以是圆的。</p></div>
sport@［spɔ:t］@n. 运动；［pl.］ 运动会 v. 炫耀，卖弄</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Fishing is my favourite sport. 钓鱼是我最喜欢的一项运动。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> sporting （adj. 和体育运动有关的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00161.jpeg"/></div>
print@［print］@v. 印刷，出版；用印刷体写；冲洗（照片）</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 字体；印刷，印刷品；（用底片印出的）照片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The print in this book is too small for me to read without glasses. 如果不戴眼镜，这本书的字对我来说太小了，无法阅读。</p>
tell@［tel］@v. ［told-told］ 讲，告诉；吩咐，命令；说明，显示；分辨，区分</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：个子高（tall）的人，说话（tell）嗓门大</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> tell from 区分</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Please tell my mother that I'll be home late today. 请告诉我妈妈，我今天晚一点回家。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> telling（n. 讲述，叙述）；teller（n. 叙述者）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">tell, speak, say, talk</p>   <p class="bodytext">tell一般都是把事情告诉别人，属于单方面的交流，如：I will tell you something very important. 我会告诉你一些很重要的事。speak指比较正式的讲话或演讲，也指一个人语言的表达，如：I can speak English. 我会说英语。say是“说”，强调的是“说”的动作，如：Please say something and don't keep silent. 请说点什么，别一言不发。talk强调的是双方互动式的交谈，如：Do you want to talk to me? 你想跟我谈谈吗？</p></div>
attitude@［ˈætitju:d］@n. 态度；看法，意见</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“爱踢球的”→孩子爱踢球，家长态度各异→态度</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> one's attitude to/toward... 某人对…的态度</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I change my attitude towards Mary when I get along with her. 当我和玛丽相处时，我改变了对她的态度。</p>
spell@［spel］@n. 咒语，符咒；魅力；连续的一段时间</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［spelled/spelt-spelled/spelt］ 拼写；意味着，招致</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> His name is so difficult that I can't spell it. 他的名字太难写了，我不会拼写。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> spelling（n. 拼写，拼法）</p>
king@［kiŋ］@n. 君主，国王；（特定领域的）巨子，大王</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The king was very cruel. He killed all the prisoners. 国王太残暴了。他杀死了所有的犯人。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00162.jpeg"/></div>
juice@［dʒu:s］@n. 汁，液</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like a cup of orange juice. 我想来一杯橙汁。</p>
notebook@［ˈnəʊtbʊk］@n. 笔记本</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：note（笔记）+book（书，卷）→笔记本</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm not sure whom I should give the notebook to. 我不确定我该把这个笔记本给谁。</p>
before@［biˈfɔ:(r)］@prep. 在…以前；在…之前，先于；在…前面，在…面前 conj. 在…以前</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 以前，以往</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Don't forget to wash your hands ______ you have meals. （2009年 浙江）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. until</p> <p class="bodytext">B. before</p> <p class="bodytext">C. when</p> <p class="bodytext">D. while</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>饭前不要忘记洗手。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查连词的用法。when和while都有“当…的时候”的意思，when既可指时间点，也可指一段时间，从句多用一般时态；而while只能表示某一段时间，不能表示某一时间点，从句多用进行时态。until是“直到”的意思，常用在not...until...这一固定搭配中，表示“直到…才…”。只有before符合题意，故选B。</p>
test@［test］@n. / v. 试验，测试；检验</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I studied very hard in the hope of getting a good mark in the test. 我努力学习，期望考试取得好成绩。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00163.jpeg"/></div>
pass@［pa:s］@v. 经过，穿过；传递，传送；度过；通过（考试等）；批准</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 通行证，许可证；通道，出口</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> pass on 去世；传递；pass by 经过</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Did you pass the English exam of last term? 上学期的英语考试你通过了吗？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> passable（adj. 可通过的）；passage（n. 通道）</p>
balance@［ˈbæləns］@n. 天平，称；均衡，平衡；结存，结欠 v. 使平衡，使均衡；称；权衡</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> keep balance 保持平衡</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's very important for us to keep a balanced diet. 对我们而言，保持均衡的饮食很重要。</p>
crowd@［kraʊd］@n. 人群，群众；一群，一批 v. 聚集，群集；挤，推</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：一群（crowd）乌鸦（crow）向南飞</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A small crowd gathered outside the building. 一小群人聚集在这栋建筑外。</p>
robot@［ˈrəʊbɒt］@n. 机器人；自动机械</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Boys like toy robots most while girls like Barbies. 男孩子最喜欢玩具机器人，而女孩子喜欢芭比娃娃。</p>
seat@［si:t］@n. 座位，（椅子等的）座部；所在地，场所；席位，职位 v. 使坐下；供给…座位，容纳…人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Henry lost his seat in the election. 亨利在选举中失去了席位。</p>
creative@［kriˈeitiv］@adj. 创造性的，具有创造力的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The creative process is very difficult and it will take a lot of time. 这个创造性的过程非常艰难而且会花很多时间。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> creativity（n. 创造力；创造性）</p>
time@［taim］@n. 时间，时刻；次，回；时机，机会；倍；时代，时期</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 为…安排时间，为…定时；测定…时间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have no time to finish my work. 我没时间完成我的工作。// It is time for me to buy a new house. 是该我买新房子的时候了。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext7">some time, sometime, sometimes</p>   <p class="bodytext">some time是“相当一段时间”，如：It took me some time to find the good. 我花了相当一段时间才找到这个物品。sometime是“某一时间”或“以前的某一时间”，如：I think we have met each other sometime. 我想我们以前见过面。sometimes是“有时”，表示频率，如：Sometimes I go to work by bus. 我有时候坐公交车去上班。</p></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">time作“时间”讲的时候是不可数名词，但是作“次，回”讲的时候是可数名词，如：one time 1次，five times 5次。</p></div>
soccer@［ˈsɒkə(r)］@n. 足球</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People love to play soccer in England. 在英国，人们喜欢踢足球。</p>
thirty@［ˈθɜ:ti］@num. 三十，三十个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are 30 apples in the basket. 篮子里有30个苹果。</p>
glad@［glæd］@adj. 高兴的，快活的；令人高兴的，给人带来喜悦的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be glad to do sth. 乐意或高兴做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'll be glad if you bring me a cup of coffee. 如果你帮我端一杯咖啡，我将非常高兴。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在国外，初次见面时，常会说Glad to meet/see you. 很高兴见到你。或者How do you do? 你好吗？语气上后者比前者更正式一些。</p></div>
crazy@［ˈkreizi］@adj. 精神失常的；疯狂的；迷恋的，狂热爱好的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be crazy about 对…疯狂</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am crazy for Sichuan cuisine. 我对川菜简直着了迷。</p>
monster@［ˈmɒnstə(r)］@n. 怪物；妖怪；巨人，巨兽，巨大的东西 adj. 巨大的，庞大的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy likes listening to stories of monsters. 男孩喜欢听怪兽的故事。</p>
interview@［ˈintəvju:］@n. 接见，会见；面谈，面试 v. 面试；会见，采访</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：inter（相互）+view（看）→相互观察→面试</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have an interview this afternoon. 我今天下午有一个面试。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> interviewer（n. 主持面试者；采访者）</p>
compare@［kəmˈpeə(r)］@n. / v. 比较；比喻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：com（一起）+pare（看作pair，对）→比来比去，天生一对→比较</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> compare with 与…相比；compare to 把…比作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Shall I compare you to a summer's day? 我可以将你比作夏日吗？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> comparable（adj. 可比较的）；comparison（n. 比较；对比）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00164.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">compare既可以与介词with搭配，也可以与介词to搭配，有细微的差别。compare with意为“与…相比”；compare to意为“把…比作”。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">The poet compared children to flowers. 诗人将孩子比喻成花朵。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Mother always compares Lily with her sister. 妈妈总是把莉莉和她的姐姐相比较。</p></div>
sea@［si:］@n. 海，海洋</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to travel to South Korea by sea. 我想坐船去韩国。</p>
use@［ju:z］@v. 用，使用；耗费，消费 n. 使用，应用；用途，效用</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> make (better / the best) use of （较好地/充分地）利用；come into use 开始投入使用；use up 用光</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The use of solar power makes life more convenient. 太阳能的使用使我们的生活更加方便。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">表示“…没有用”时，用It is no use+动词不定式/动名词，如：It's no use to ask him. 问他也没有用。It's no use waiting for him. 等他是没用的。</p></div>
spotlight@［ˈspɒtlait］@n. 聚光灯；公众的注意 v. 用聚光灯照；特别关注；突出报道</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：spot（斑点）+light（光）→把光聚成一点→聚光灯</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are many spotlights on the stage. 舞台上有很多聚光灯。</p>
album@［ˈælbəm］@n. 粘贴簿；集邮簿；相册；音乐专辑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My friend bought me an album as a birthday present. 我的朋友给我买了一本相册作为生日礼物。</p>
inside@［inˈsaid］@prep. 在…里面，在…内部 adv. 在里面，在内部 n. 里面，内侧 adj. 里面的，内幕的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You can find a letter inside the box. 你可以在盒子里找到一封信。</p>
fourteen@［ˌfɔˈti:n］@num. 十四</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> When I was fourteen years old, I went to middle school. 我14岁的时候上了中学。</p>
whole@［həʊl］@adj. 全部的，全体的；完整的，无缺的 n. 全部，整体</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on the whole 大体上，基本上；the whole life 一生</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The whole story is very attractive. 整个故事都很吸引人。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">all, whole</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“全部的”之意。all可以修饰各类名词，且限定词要放在all之后，如：All the windows are open. 所有的窗户都敞开着；而whole只能修饰具有整体意义的单数名词，且限定词要放在whole之前，如：I can't waste my whole life. 我不能浪费自己的一生。</p></div>
thick@［θik］@adj. 厚的，粗的；笨的，迟钝的；稠的，浓的；密的，密集的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have had to put on a thick sweater since the weather grew cold. 自从天气变凉，我就把厚毛衣穿上了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> thicken 〔v. （使）变厚；（使）变粗；（使）变浓〕</p>
share@［ʃeə(r)］@v. 分享，分担；分摊，分开 n. 一份；份儿，股份</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> share sth. with sb. 与某人分享某物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Sue shares a house with other students. 苏和另外几个学生一起住在这所房子里。</p>
online@［ˌɒnˈlain］@adj. 在线的；联机的，联网的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：on（在…上）+line（线）→在线的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually play online games after work. 下班后，我常常玩网络游戏。</p>
garage@［ˈgæra:ʒ；gəˈｒa:ʒ］@n. 车库；汽车修理行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to drive my car to the garage first. 我需要将我的车先开到汽车修理行。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">要注意该词英式发音<span class="yinbiao1">［ˈｇæｒa:ʒ］</span>和美式发音<span class="yinbiao1">［ｇəˈｒa:ʒ］</span>的差别。</p></div>
big@［big］@adj. 大的，巨大的；重大的，主要的；年龄较大的，长大了的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This box is bigger than that one. 这个箱子比那个大。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">big的比较级和最高级都要双写g，分别为bigger和biggest。</p></div>
somebody@［ˈsʌmbədi］@pron. 某人，有人 n. 重要人物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：some（某个）+body（人）→某人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My grandmother mistook me for somebody else. 我的祖母把我错认成了其他人。</p>
mouth@［maʊθ］@n. 嘴，口</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The doctor asked the little boy to open his mouth. 医生让小男孩张开嘴。</p>
noon@［nu:n］@n. 正午，中午</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher talked to a student at noon. 老师中午的时候跟一个学生谈话。</p>
prison@［prizn］@n. 监狱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The thief was put into prison for three years. 这名窃贼被判入狱三年。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> prisoner（n. 战俘; 囚犯）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">“坐牢”和“出狱”的英文表达分别为in prison和out of prison，prison之前不加任何冠词，这一点要注意。</p></div> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00165.jpeg"/></div>
enter@［ˈentə(r)］@v. 进入；参加，加入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> enter a school 入学；enter a country 进入一个国家；enter into 进入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is polite to knock on the door before entering a room. 进房间之前先敲门，这是一种礼貌。</p>
chemistry@［ˈkemistri］@n. 化学</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have been learning chemistry in university for a year. 我已经在大学里学了一年化学了。</p>
storm@［stɔ:m］@n. 暴风雨，暴风雪；激动，爆发 v. 猛攻，直捣；怒气冲冲地走</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Only a few minutes later the storm broke. 仅仅过了几分钟，暴风雨就来了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> stormy（adj. 暴风雨的）</p>
challenge@［ˈtʃæləndʒ］@n. 挑战，艰巨任务；质疑，质询；（比赛写的）邀请 v. 向…挑战；对…质疑；考查，考验</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：穷则思变（change），富有挑战（challenge）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> beyond challenge 无与伦比，不可比拟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Father told me to face challenges bravely in life. 父亲告诉我要勇敢面对生活中的挑战。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> challenger（n. 挑战者）；challenging（adj. 激励的；挑战的）</p>
specifically@［spəˈsifikli］@adv. 明确地，特定地，具体地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> They decided to make a magazine aimed specifically at farmers. 他们决定做一本专门针对农民的杂志。</p>
interest@［ˈintrəst］@n. 兴趣，爱好；利息，利率；利益，好处；利害关系 v. 使感兴趣；引起…关注</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> have an interest in... 对…感兴趣；place of historical interest 名胜古迹</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The young man has an interest in pop music. 这个年轻人对流行音乐很感兴趣。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">interest在作“兴趣”讲时是不可数名词，而作“利益，好处”讲时是可数名词，要注意区分。</p></div>
cola@［ˈkəʊlə］@n. 可乐饮料</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do not drink tea, coffee, cola or chocolate four hours before sleep. 睡觉前四个小时不要喝茶、咖啡、可乐和巧克力。</p>
golden@［ˈgəʊldən］@adj. 黄金的；金（黄）色的；珍贵的；极好的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's a golden opportunity for him to get the job. 对于他来说，获得这份工作是个难得的机会。</p>
put@［pʊt］@v. ［put-put, putting］ 放，摆，使处于（某种状态）；说，表达；提出，提交；记下，写下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> put on 穿上；上演，演出；put out 扑灭；put off 推迟；put forth 提出；put down 放下；拒绝；put back 放回原处</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">They had to ______ the 800-meter race because of the bad weather. （2009年 重庆）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. put on</p> <p class="bodytext">B. put off</p> <p class="bodytext">C. get on</p> <p class="bodytext">D. get up</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>由于糟糕的天气，他们不得不推迟800米赛跑。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查几个词组的含义。put on意为“穿上”，put off意为“推迟，拖延”，get on 意为“相处”，get up意为“起床”，故选B。</p>
net@［net］@n. 网；网状系统 adj. 净的，纯的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You can never imagine how to make this fishing net. 你简直无法想象怎样做出这样的渔网。</p>
show@［ʃəʊ］@v. 表明，证明；显示，出示；带领；（通过示范）教，告知；演出，放映；显现，显露 n. 演出，上映；展览，展览会</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> show sb. around 领某人到处参观；on show 在展出；show off 炫耀；show up 露出，露面</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can you show me your passport? 可以出示一下你的护照吗？</p>
treasure@［ˈtreʒə(r)］@n. 财宝，珍品 v. 珍爱，珍视</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The police found the lost treasure in a trash barrel. 警方在一个垃圾桶里找回了丢失的珍宝。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> treasurer （n. 司库，会计）；treasurable （adj. 宝贵的，贵重的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00166.jpeg"/></div>
basket@［ˈba:skit］@n. 篮，篓，筐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm going to buy a basket of eggs. 我打算买一篮鸡蛋。</p>
high@［hai］@adj. 高的，高度的；高级的，重要的；高兴的，愉快的；（时间、季节等）正盛的，（时机）成熟的 adv. 高，高高地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：高（high）山（hill）流水</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The mountain is 2,500 meters high. 这座山海拔2500米。</p>
deal@［di:l］@v. 发放；给予；处理，对付 n. 交易；协议；大量，很多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：真的（real）交易（deal）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a great deal （of） 大量（的）；make a deal 成交；deal with 处理，解决</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lily has to deal with all kinds of people in her job. 莉莉在工作中不得不和各种各样的人打交道。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">a great deal of后面接不可数名词，如：Tom made a great deal of money last year. 汤姆去年挣了很多钱。</p></div>
why@［wai］@adv. 为什么；…的理由 int. 咳，哎呀</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Why are you walking to school? 你为什么步行去上学？</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">why not是“为什么不”的意思，后面一般跟不带to的不定式，如：Why not go there now? 为什么不现在去呢？</p></div>
saying@［ˈseiiŋ］@n. 话，言语；俗话；成语，格言，谚语；口头禅</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：say（说）+ing（名词后缀）→所说的话→言语</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> As a Chinese saying goes,“Where there is a will, there is a way.”中国有句谚语：“有志者事竟成。”</p>
apple@［ˈæpl］@n. 苹果，苹果树</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My mother likes eating apples. 我妈妈喜欢吃苹果。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00167.jpeg"/></div>
sometimes@［ˈsʌmtaimz］@adv. 不时；有时，间或</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to work late sometimes. 我有时候要工作到很晚。</p>
dark@［da:k］@adj. 暗的，黑暗的；深色的，黑色的 n. 黑暗，暗处；暗色，阴影</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It was dark outside and I couldn't see much. 天黑了，我看不太清楚。</p>
sun@［sʌn］@n. 太阳，日</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The sun rises from the east. 太阳从东方升起。</p>
firm@［fɜ:m］@n. 公司，商行 adj. 坚实的，结实的；稳固的；坚定的，坚决的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：大楼失火（fire），殃及公司（firm）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Athletes have firm muscles because they do a lot of exercise. 运动员有结实的肌肉，因为他们做大量的运动。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> firmly（adv. 稳固地）</p>
coat@［kəʊt］@n. 上衣，外套；表皮，皮毛；覆盖物，层 v. 涂上，覆盖</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to buy a new coat during spring festival. 春节期间我要买一件新外套。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> coated（adj. 涂上一层的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00168.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">coat, dress</p>   <p class="bodytext">两个单词虽然意思相差较大，但考生容易混淆。coat作名词时，有“外套”之意，但作动词时却没有“给…穿衣服”的意思。dress作名词时，意为“服装，衣服”，作动词时，意为“给…穿衣服”。</p></div>
suitable@［ˈsu:təbl］@adj. 适当的，相配的；合适的，适宜的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：suit（合适）+able（形容词后缀）→合适的；适当的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This kind of game is not suitable for children. 这类游戏不适合孩子玩。</p>
mouse@［maʊs］@n. 鼠；胆小的人；鼠标</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：一只老鼠（mouse）张嘴（mouth）咬东西</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little girl was afraid of mice. 这个小女孩以前害怕老鼠。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> mousey（adj. 像老鼠的；灰褐色的；胆小的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00169.jpeg"/></div>
beauty@［ˈbju:ti］@n. 美，美丽；美人；美的东西</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：迪斯尼经典动画片《美女与野兽》的英文名是Beauty and the Beast</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many people pay a visit to the natural beauty every year. 每年都有许多人来游览这一自然美景。</p>
excuse@［ikˈskju:z］@v. 原谅，宽恕；使免除（责任、惩罚等）；为…辩解，作为开脱…的理由</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 借口，理由</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> Excuse me. 对不起。/ 借光。/ 打扰一下。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Excuse me, can you tell me the way to the station? 打扰一下，您能告诉我去火车站怎么走吗？// I have no excuse for my mistake. 对于我的错误，我没有借口。</p>
choose@［tʃu:z］@v. ［chose-chosen］ 选择，挑选</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> choose between A and B 在A和B中挑选；choose... from... 从…中挑选…；cannot choose but do sth. 别无选择，只好…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I was asked to choose the best title for the passage. 我被要求来选择这篇文章的最佳标题。</p>
bulb@［bʌlb］@n. 植物的球茎；灯泡</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The light bulb in the washroom burnt out. 卫生间里的灯泡坏了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> bulbous（adj. 球茎状的）</p>
secret@［ˈsi:krət］@adj. 秘密的，机密的 n. 秘密</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Little Tom tried to keep this thing secret from his mother. 小汤姆试图向他的妈妈隐瞒这件事。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00170.jpeg"/></div>
job@［dʒɒb］@n. 职业，职位；（一件）工作，活儿；职责，责任</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：有一份工作（job）是一件乐（joy）事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to find a part-time job in my spare time. 我想在业余时间找份兼职工作。</p>
lead@［li:d］@ v. ［led-led］为…带路，指引；领导，引导；诱使，致使；过（某种生活）；导致，通向 n. 领先，榜样；主角，主要演员</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［led］</span> n. 铅</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> lead to 导致，通向</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The guide leads us to the river. 向导将我们带到河边。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> leader（n. 领导人，领导者）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">lead可以和to连用表示“导致”，考生注意to在这里是介词，后接名词或动名词。</p></div>
once@［wʌns］@adv. 一次，一回；曾经，一度 conj. 一旦…就…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> at once 立刻，马上；同时；once again / once more 再一次；once in a while 偶尔；all at once 突然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I saw the man once in this city. 我曾经在这个城市见过这个男人。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">at once表示“马上”，相当于immediately，不能与持续性动词一起用。</p></div>
by@［bai］@prep. 被，由；凭借，通过；从…旁过去，经由；在…旁边，靠近；在…之前，不迟于；根据，按照；按…计算 adv. 在近旁；经过，过去</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> by oneself 独自，单独地；by the way 顺便；by the end of 到…结束时；by means of 通过，依靠；by way of 经由；by accident 偶然；by chance 偶然，意外地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually went to school by bike when I was in high school. 我上高中时经常骑自行车去上学。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">by是被动语态的一个标志，by后的名词往往是施动者，如：Jim was hit by his elder brother. 吉姆被他哥哥打了。</p></div>
evening@［ˈi:vniŋ］@n. 傍晚，晚上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My father will come home early this evening. 我父亲今天晚上会早些回家。</p>
clap@［klæp］@n. / v. ［clapped-clapped, clapping］ 拍手，鼓掌</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：c+lap（轻拍）→拍手，鼓掌</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The audience was so excited that they clapped their hands all the time. 观众十分兴奋，他们一直不停地鼓掌。</p>
gift@［gift］@n. 礼物，赠品；天赋，才能</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：举起（lift）手来接礼物（gift）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I want to buy something for my friend as a gift. 我想买点什么给我朋友作礼物。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> gifted（adj. 有天赋的）</p>
add@［æd］@v. 添加，增加；把…加起来，计算…的总和</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> add...to... 把…加到…；add to... 增加；add （sth.） up 把…加起来；add up to... 总计达到…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Shall I add this novel to the book list? 我能把这本小说添加到书目里吗？</p>
luck@［lʌk］@n. 运气；好运，幸运</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Good luck to you. 祝你好运。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> lucky（adj. 幸运的）；luckily（adv. 幸运地）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00171.jpeg"/></div>
accident@［ˈæksidənt］@n. 意外遭遇，事故</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> by accident 偶然，意外</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A traffic accident happened last week. 上周发生了一起交通事故。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00172.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">accident, incident</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者词形相近，但意义不同。accident一般指意外发生且发生几率很低的事，比如事故、遭遇等，如：A car accident happened in a street. 大街上发生了一起汽车事故。而incident一般表示政治事件，或者某件事情的变故、变数，如：an international incident 国际事件。</p></div>
talk@［tɔ:k］@v. 说，讲话；交谈，谈论</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 谈话，会话；演讲，讲话；会谈，谈判；闲话，流言蜚语</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> talk to/with sb. 和…交谈；talk about sb./sth. 谈论某人/某事物；give a talk 做讲座，演讲</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have never talked to him before. 我以前从没有跟他讲过话。</p>
count@［kaʊnt］@v. 点…的数目，计算；把…算入；认为，看作；值得考虑，有重要意义</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 计数，总数</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> count on sb. 依靠某人，指望某人；count for 占…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little girl is only three years old but she can count up to 100 in English. 这个小女孩只有三岁，但是她可以用英语数到100。</p>
permission@［pəˈmiʃn］@n. 许可，允许</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：permis（看作permit，许可）+sion→许可，允许</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can I get permission to go to the park today? 我今天能去公园吗？</p>
