rope@［rəʊp］@n. 绳索，线缆 v. 用绳捆（或扎等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The rope was not strong enough so we used wire instead. 这根绳子不够结实，所以我们用金属线代替。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00173.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">rope, string, thread</p>   <p class="bodytext">rope指用于捆绑大物件的粗壮而结实的绳子或绳索，如：I should buy some ropes of the tent. 我应该买一些搭帐篷用的绳子。string是捆绑小物件的绳子或带子，如：I need a string to tie the bag. 我需要一条绳子把这个包捆起来。thread指用棉、毛等纤维制成的很细的线，可用于缝纫或纺织，引申为“线索”，如：Can you find the thread of the story? 你能找到这个故事的线索吗？</p></div>
act@［ækt］@v. 行动，做事；表现；起作用；扮演，表演</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 行为，行动；法令，条例；（一）幕</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：做事（act）要实事（fact）求是</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> act as 担任</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The police should act immediately. 警方应立即采取行动。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> action（n. 动作；作用）</p>
honey@［ˈhʌni］@n. 蜜，蜂蜜；甜蜜；宝贝儿，亲爱的（常作爱称）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The recipe says you can substitute honey for sugar. 食谱上说可以用蜂蜜代替白糖。</p>
kid@［kid］@n. 小孩，年轻人 v. ［kidded-kidded, kidding］ 戏弄；（与…）开玩笑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Aunt Lee has three kids. 李阿姨有三个孩子。</p>
increase@［inˈkri:s］@ v. 增加，增强</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［ˈinkri:s］</span> n. 增加，增强</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a steady increase in China's population. 中国的人口正稳步增长。</p>
hometown@［ˈhəʊmˈtaʊn］@n. 家乡 adj. 家乡的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：home（家）+town（乡镇）→家乡</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I spent my childhood in my hometown. 我在家乡度过了孩提时代。</p>
documentary@［ˌdɒkjuˈmentri］@adj. 文件的，文献的 n. 纪录片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The documentary explains the development of the technology. 纪录片解释了这项技术的发展。</p>
shampoo@［ʃæmˈpu:］@n. 洗发剂；（地毯等的）洗涤剂 vt. 用洗发剂洗头</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to go to the supermarket to buy some shampoo. 我得去超市买些洗发水了。</p>
prize@［praiz］@n. 奖赏，奖金，奖品；值得追求的东西 adj. 第一流的，了不起的 v. 珍视，珍惜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I won the first prize in the speech contest. 我获得了演讲比赛一等奖。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">注意prize与price的区别：prize是“奖品，奖赏”，price是“价格，价钱”。</p></div>
better@［ˈbetə(r)］@adj. 更好的；（病况、心情）有好转的 adv. 更，更好地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">We're in class. You'd better not ______. （2008年 北京）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. talk</p> <p class="bodytext">B. talking</p> <p class="bodytext">C. talked</p> <p class="bodytext">D. to talk</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>我们在上课。你最好不要说话。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查you'd better （not） do sth.这一固定结构，应选动词原形，故选A。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">考试中常会考到固定搭配you'd better do sth.，意思是“你最好做某事”。其后接动词原形，考生注意不要误用。如：You'd better stay at home. 你最好待在家里。它的否定式是you'd better not do sth.。</p></div>
sort@［sɔ:t］@n. 种类，类别；某一种人，某一类人 v. 分类，整理</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> sort of 有几分，多少</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The newly picked apples are sorted according to size. 新摘下来的苹果被根据大小进行分类。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> sorter（n. 分类机；分类人员）；sortable（adj. 可分类的）</p>
teenager@［ˈti:neidʒə(r)］@n. 十几岁的青少年</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The new book is aimed at teenagers. 这本新书是面向青少年的。</p>
but@［bʌt］@conj. 但是，可是，然而；而（是） prep. 除…以外 adv. 只，仅仅</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> not only...but （also）... 不但…而且…；not...but... 不是…而是…；but for 要不是…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like this jacket, but it's too expensive. 我喜欢这件夹克，但是它太贵了。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">but, however</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“但是”的意思，但是用法不同。but常作连词，引导一个转折性的句子，however常作副词，与引导的句子间用逗号隔开。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">I invited five people but only one came. 我邀请了五个人，但是只来了一个。</p>   <p class="bodytext">I feel a little tired. However, I don't give up. 我感觉有点累了，但是我不放弃。</p></div>
follow@［ˈfɒləʊ］@v. 跟随；接着；遵照，听从；听懂，领会 n. 跟随</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> as follows 如下；follow one's advice 听从某人的劝告</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Follow my steps and make sure you do not get lost. 跟上我的步伐，不要走丢了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> following（adj. 下列的）</p>
else@［els］@adv. 其他，另外</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> What else do I need to do? 我还需要做什么？</p>
cotton@［ˈkɒtn］@n. 棉，棉花；棉线，棉纱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The shirts are 100% pure cotton. 这种衬衫是100%纯棉的。</p>
sister@［ˈsistə(r)］@n. 姐，妹</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have a brother and a sister. 我有一个兄弟，一个姐妹。</p>
record@［riˈkɔ:d］@ v. 记录，登记；将（声音、图像等）录下</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［ˈrekɔ:d］</span> n. 记录，记载；唱片；最高纪录，最佳成绩</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Susan holds the world record in the long-distance race. 苏珊保持着世界长跑纪录。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> recorder（n. 录音机；录像机）</p>
butter@［ˈbʌtə(r)］@n. 黄油</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't like to spread butter on bread. 我不喜欢在面包上抹黄油。</p>
hard@［ha:d］@adj. 坚硬的，坚固的；困难的，艰苦的；勤勉的，刻苦的；冷酷的，严厉的；猛烈的，强烈的</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 努力地；艰难地；猛烈地，严重地；严厉地</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00174.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">hard本身可以作副词，不要误以为hardly是它的副词形式，其实hardly意为“几乎不”。</p></div>
statement@［ˈsteitmənt］@n. 陈述，声明；结算单，报表</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：state（状态，情况）+ment（抽象名词后缀）→把状况说出来→陈述，声明</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The spokesman of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs made a statement to the press. 外交部发言人向媒体发表了一份声明。</p>
off@［ɔ:f］@adv. 距，离，到；离开；出发，起跑；（计划的事）不发生，取消；断开，不供应；未连接，不工作；下班，休息；在后台，不在台上</p> <p class="bodytext1">prep. 落下，离开；从…去掉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> put off 推迟；脱下；turn off 关掉；使转变方向；take off 起飞；cut off 切断，隔绝；send off 寄出；派遣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Please ______ the light when you leave the room. （2008年 鹤岗）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. turn on</p> <p class="bodytext">B. turn down</p> <p class="bodytext">C. turn off</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>请在离开屋子时把灯关掉。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是turn跟不同介词搭配的区别。turn on意为“打开”，turn off意为“关闭”，两个词组正好相反，而turn down意为“把声音关小”。因此选C。</p>
break@［breik］@v. ［broke-broken］ 打破；损坏，弄坏；破坏，违反；中止，中断；打破（纪录）；减弱…的势头，减轻（打击等的）力度；（天）破晓，（天气）转晴</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. （课间或工间）休息，间歇；破裂</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> break away from 从…脱离，打破；break down 出故障，坏掉；break in 插嘴；破门而入；break into 强行进入；渗进；break off 中止，中断；break out 爆发；have/take a break 休息一下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I want to take a break after work. 下班后我想休息一下。</p>
seal@［si:l］@n. 封铅，封条；印，图章；海豹 v. 封，密封</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The seal on this package is broken. 这个包装上的封条坏了。// There are many types of seal in this ocean park. 这座海洋公园里有很多种海豹。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> sealed（adj. 密封的）</p>
plastic@［ˈplæstik］@adj. 塑料（制）的；可塑的 n. ［常作pl.］ 塑料；塑料制品</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The cup I have used for five years is made of plastic. 这只我用了五年的杯子是塑料制品。</p>
artist@［ˈa:tist］@n. 艺术家，画家；能手</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The young man over there is an artist. 那边的那个年轻人是一位艺术家。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00175.jpeg"/></div>
glue@［glu:］@n. 胶，胶水 v. 胶合，粘贴</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：买胶水（glue）就买蓝（blue）瓶的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to glue a stamp onto the envelope before sending it. 邮寄之前我需要在信封上粘好邮票。</p>
alright@［ɔ:lˈrait］@adv. 好，好吧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> —Shall we go fishing this Sunday?</p> <p class="bodytext6">—Alright.</p> <p class="bodytext6">—我们这周日去钓鱼好吗？</p> <p class="bodytext6">—好的。</p>
shoot@［ʃu:t］@v. ［shot-shot］ 发射，射击；投，射门，投篮；拍摄；射杀，射伤；发芽</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 新枝，幼苗，嫩芽；狩猎；射击；拍摄</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> shoot up 射出；发芽；暴涨</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The guards were ordered to shoot anyone trying to escape. 警卫接到命令，向任何试图逃跑的人开枪。// The king was on a shoot when his little princess was taken away by the witch. 小公主被巫婆带走的时候，国王正在打猎。</p>
doctor@［ˈdɒktə(r)］@n. 医生；博士</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The doctor takes good care of his patients. 这位医生悉心照顾病人。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext5">doctor, physician, surgeon</p>   <p class="bodytext">以上三个词都指的是“医生”，但是侧重点不同。doctor泛指一般的医生，physician指内科医师，surgeon指外科医生。</p></div>
convenient@［kənˈvi:niənt］@adj. 方便的，便利的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：亚欧大陆（continent）桥，方便（convenient）你我</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be convenient to sb. 对某人来说方便；convenient to do sth. 便于做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A bicycle is often more convenient than a car in towns. 在镇上，自行车通常要比汽车方便。</p>
terrible@［ˈterəbl］@adj. 极度的，厉害的；可怕的，骇人的；很糟的，极坏的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can't go to school today because I feel terrible. 今天我不能去上学，因为我感觉不舒服。</p>
of@［ɔ:v］@prep. （属于）…的；由…制成（或组成）的；含有…的，装有…的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man in the white coat is the son of a famous writer. 穿白外套的男子是一位著名作家的儿子。</p>
glass@［gla:s］@n. 玻璃，玻璃杯；［pl.］ 眼镜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：众里寻它千百度，眼镜（glasses）却在草丛（grass）处</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like a glass of ice water. 我想要一杯冰水。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> glassful 〔n. 一（满）杯〕；glassy （adj. 玻璃状的，透明的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00176.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">glass有两层意思，作“玻璃”讲时是不可数名词，作“眼镜”讲时常用复数，如：a pair of glasses 一副眼镜。</p></div>
careful@［ˈkeəfl］@adj. 小心的，仔细的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think you should be careful when you drive on the street. 我认为你在大街上开车时，应该小心才是。</p>
more@［mɔ:(r)］@adv. 更，更多 adj. 更多的；更大的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> more or less 或多或少，大体上；more than 多于，超过；not more than 至多；what's more 而且，此外，更有甚者；once more 再一次</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like eating cheese, the more, the better. 我喜欢吃奶酪，越多越好。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00177.jpeg"/></div>
under@［ˈʌndə(r)］@prep. 在…下面，在…底下；少于；低于；在…管辖下，在…影响下</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 在下面，往下面</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> under control 在控制之中；under...condition 在…情况下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a white cat under the table. 桌子下面有一只白猫。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">below, under</p>   <p class="bodytext">两个词都可以表示“在…下面”。under指垂直的正下方，如：The boy is standing under the tree. 男孩站在树下。而below是表示不一定在正下方，另外below还可以指抽象意义的“低于”，如：My sister's score is below mine. 我妹妹的分数比我低。</p></div>
diary@［ˈdaiəri］@n. 日记簿，日记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have the habit of making notes in my diary. 我习惯在日记里做笔记。</p>
shout@［ʃaʊt］@v. 呼喊，呼叫 n. 呼喊，喊叫声</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> shout at 对…喊叫</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a boy shouting for help. 一个男孩在喊救命。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00178.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">shout, cry</p>   <p class="bodytext">shout指为了让别人听见或使别人注意到而大声喊叫，如: People shouted all the night. 人们整夜不停地喊叫。而cry一般指的是因心情悲伤、委屈或恐惧而哭喊，如：He cried out for mercy. 他大声求饶。</p></div>
eighty@［ˈeiti］@num. 八十</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My grandpa is eighty years old. 我爷爷80岁了。</p>
supply@［səˈplai］@n. 供给，供应（量）；存货，必需品 v. 供给，供应；满足（需要），弥补（不足）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> supply sth. to sb. / supply sb. with sth. 为某人提供某物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Vegetables and fruits supply most of the vitamins we need. 蔬菜和水果提供了我们身体所需的大部分维生素。</p>
fashion@［ˈfæʃn］@n. 流行款式，时兴式样；时尚，时兴</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Blue jeans have come into fashion again. 蓝色牛仔裤又开始流行起来了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> fashionable（adj. 流行的，时髦的）</p>
punish@［ˈpʌniʃ］@v. 惩罚，处罚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：没有完成（finish）任务将受到惩罚（punish）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher punished the naughty student. 老师惩罚了那个顽皮的学生。</p>
bridge@［bridʒ］@n. 桥，桥梁；桥牌 v. 架桥于；把…连接（或弥合）起来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The bridge was built three years ago. 这座桥建于三年前。</p>
radio@［ˈreidiəʊ］@n. 无线电广播；设备；收音机 v. 用无线电传送（或广播）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like to listen to the radio in my spare time. 我业余时间喜欢听收音机。</p>
somewhere@［ˈsʌmweə(r)］@adv. 在某处，到某处；大约，大概</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：some（某个）+where（哪里）→在某处</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There must be somewhere in this town where we can have a nice dinner. 这个镇上一定有某个我们可以享受一顿美味晚餐的地方。</p>
product@［ˈprɒdʌkt］@n. 产品，产物；乘积</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The country's main export products are gold and wool. 这个国家主要出口黄金和羊毛。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> by-product（n. 副产品）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00179.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">product, production</p>   <p class="bodytext">product是“产品”，侧重于物品，如：We need new products to sell. 我们需要有新产品来卖。而production是“生产”，侧重于过程，还有“产量”的意思，如：production costs 生产成本。</p></div>
never@［ˈnevə(r)］@adv. 从不，永不；决不，千万不</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— I'm sorry for losing your book. I will buy a new one for you.</p> <p class="bodytext">— ______. I have another copy. （2006年 德州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. Thank you</p> <p class="bodytext">B. Happy to hear that</p> <p class="bodytext">C. Never mind</p> <p class="bodytext">D. Of course</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 很抱歉把你的书弄丢了。我再给你买一本新的吧。</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 别在意。我还有一本。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是对道歉的回答。一般来说，可以回答It doesn't matter.或者Never mind.，表示“没关系”或者“别介意”，因此选C。</p>
several@［ˈsevrəl］@adj. 几个，若干</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Yesterday I bought several DVDs including the Twilight series and High School Musical. 我昨天买了几张DVD盘，包括《暮光之城》系列和《歌舞青春》。</p>
insect@［ˈinsekt］@n. 昆虫，虫</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Locusts are a kind of destructive insect. 蝗虫是一种破坏性昆虫。</p>
banana@［bəˈna:nə］@n. 香蕉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“剥拿了”→剥完香蕉皮，拿着吃→香蕉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Monkeys like eating bananas. 猴子喜欢吃香蕉。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00180.jpeg"/></div>
volunteer@［ˌvɒlənˈtiə(r)］@n. 志愿者，志愿兵 v. 自愿（做）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are many volunteers providing their help to the children in Sichuan. 有许多志愿者为四川的孩子们提供帮助。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> voluntary（adj. 自愿的，志愿的）</p>
district@［ˈdistrikt］@n. 地区，区域；管区，行政区</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：严格（strict）划分地区（district）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The security is good in this district. 这一地区的治安状况良好。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">district, region</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“地区”的意思，但是侧重点不同。district多指行政区划，如：London district 伦敦区；region表示形成了独具特色的事物或风情的某区域，如：desert region 沙漠地区。</p></div>
all@［ɔ:l］@adj. 一切的，所有的；全部的，总的，整个的 adv. 完全地；十分，很</p> <p class="bodytext1">pron. 全部，一切</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> after all 毕竟，终究；above all 最重要的是；in all 总共；all over 遍及；all through 一直，始终；not at all 一点也不；all day/night/week/month/year 整日/夜/周/月/年</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Would you like to go to the concert with me tonight?</p> <p class="bodytext">— I'd love to, but ______ of us couple has tickets. Do you have some? （2009年黄冈）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. both</p> <p class="bodytext">B. all</p> <p class="bodytext">C. neither</p> <p class="bodytext">D. none</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 你们愿意今晚和我一起去听音乐会吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 我愿意，但是我们俩都没票。你还有吗？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查几个代词的区别。both指“两者都…”，用在肯定句中，其反义词是neither；all指“三者或三者以上都…”，其反义词是none。根据题中的couple可知是两个人，排除B和D。而句子表达的是转折关系，因此选C。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00181.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">all, both</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“都”的意思。all针对三者或三者以上，如：All the students in our class like pop music. 我们班所有的学生都喜欢流行音乐；而both则针对两者，常和and连用，如：Both the girl and her boyfriend went to the theater. 女孩和她男朋友都去看戏剧了。</p></div>
reveal@［riˈvi:l］@v. 揭露，揭示；泄露；展现，显示</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom didn't reveal where he had hidden Lucy's book. 汤姆没有透露他把露西的书藏在哪儿了。</p>
marathon@［ˈmærəθən］@n. 马拉松长跑；（各种）持久比赛；〈喻〉拖时长久令人难以忍受的事情 adj. （比赛等）需要极大持久力的；马拉松式的，漫长的 v. 参加马拉松长跑（比赛）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：马拉松</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A lot of people took part in the marathon competition. 许多人参加了马拉松比赛。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00182.jpeg"/></div>
smile@［smail］@n. 微笑，笑容 v. 微笑，露出笑容；笑，用微笑表示</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A lovely girl's smile can make her even more beautiful. 可爱女孩子的笑容可以使她看起来更加漂亮。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">smile表示“微笑，露出笑容”时是不及物动词，后面经常跟介词at，如：They all smiled at the joke. 听了那个笑话，他们都笑了。</p></div>
rather@［ˈra:ðə(r)］@adv. 相当；有点儿；宁愿，宁可；更确切地说</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> would/had rather do sth. （than do sth.） 宁愿做某事（也不愿做某事）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would rather listen to the radio than watch TV. 我宁愿听收音机也不看电视。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">would rather do sth. 是习惯用法，如：Would you rather buy the blue coat or the white one? 你愿意买蓝色的外套，还是买白色的？would rather还可以与than连用，构成would rather do sth. than do sth.，表示“宁愿…也不愿…”，如：I would rather read some books than talk to others. 我宁愿读书，也不愿跟人交谈。rather than连接的是两个平行的结构，表示“与其…倒不如…”，如：It's an essay rather than a letter. 与其说这是一封信，倒不如说是一篇散文。</p></div>
ink@［iŋk］@n. 墨水；油墨</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：惜墨（ink）如金，思考（think）得多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Professor Li has run out of his red ink. 李教授用光了他的红墨水。</p>
discovery@［diˈskʌvəri］@n. 发现，发觉；被发现的事物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The discovery attracted much attention in scientific circles. 这项发现在科学界引起了极大关注。</p>
camera@［ˈkæmərə］@n. 照相机；摄影机，摄像机</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：拿来（came）照相机（camera）照相</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lily forgot to take her camera when she visited the Forbidden City. 去故宫游玩的时候，莉莉忘记带相机了。</p>
idea@［aiˈdiə］@n. 想法，主意；思想，概念</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have no idea how to deal with this problem. 我不知道怎么处理这个问题。</p>
advantage@［ədˈva:ntidʒ］@n. 优点，好处，优势</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take advantage of 利用</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are many advantages of a daily nap. 每天小睡一会儿有很多好处。</p>
hill@［hil］@n. 小山，山冈；斜坡</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Their small cabin stands on a hill. 他们的小木屋盖在小山上。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00183.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">hill, mountain</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“山”的意思，但是程度不同。hill指一般意义的小山，而mountain常指高大的山脉。</p></div>
clothes@［kləʊðz］@n. 衣服，服装；被褥</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Frank wants to buy some clothes this Sunday. 弗兰克这周日想去买些衣服。</p>
anything@［ˈeniθiŋ］@pron. 无论什么东西，随便什么事情；任何东西，任何事情</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> anything but 绝不</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">I have ______ to do. Please give me ______ to read. （2007年 济南）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. something, anything</p> <p class="bodytext">B. nothing, something</p> <p class="bodytext">C. nothing, everything</p> <p class="bodytext">D. anything, nothing</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>我没什么事可做。请给我一些东西读。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查不定代词的用法。something意为“某事”，用在肯定句中；anything意为“任何事”，用在否定句和疑问句中；nothing意为“没有什么”；everything意为“每件事；一切”。因此选B。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在考试中，还会出现短语nothing but，注意与anything but相区别。nothing but意为“只；除了”，如：I have nothing but you. 除了你，我一无所有。</p></div>
purpose@［ˈpɜ:pəs］@n. 目的，意图；用途；效果</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on purpose 故意</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our purpose is to help the disabled children. 我们的目的是帮助残疾儿童。</p>
boat@［bəʊt］@n. 船，小船</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are several boats on the lake. 湖面上有几只小船。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">boat, ship</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“船”的意思。boat指航行在河流或湖泊上的小船，而ship指海上的轮船。</p></div> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00184.jpeg"/></div>
association@［əˌsəʊʃiˈeiʃn］@n. 协会，联盟，社团；联合，结合</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mike found a job in the Football Association. 迈克在足协找到了一份工作。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00185.jpeg"/></div>
to@［tu:］@prep. 向，往，对着；对，给，于；趋于，倾向；直到…为止，在…之前；比，对；到，达</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> To my surprise, Jonny found his new job in London. 令我惊讶的是，乔尼在伦敦找到了新工作。</p>
lonely@［ˈləʊnli］@adj. 孤独的，寂寞的；荒凉的，人迹稀少的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I felt very lonely when I was alone. 我孤身一人的时候感到很孤独。</p>
keep@［ki:p］@v. ［kept-kept］ 使保持（某种状态），使继续；阻止，防止；履行，遵守；保存，保留；供养，饲养；经营，料理；守卫，看守</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> keep in touch with sb. 和某人保持联系；keep off 禁止接近；防止；keep in mind 记住，谨记；keep up （天气）持续不变；keep up with 跟上，不落后</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> If people keep cutting down the forest, the animals will have nowhere to live. 如果人类继续砍伐森林，那么动物将无处可住。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">keep是考试中的高频词，keep后面可以接动名词，但不能接不定式。</p></div>
when@［wen］@adv. 什么时候，何时；在…的时候 conj. 在…时，当…时；然后</p> <p class="bodytext1">pron. 什么时候</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> When will you come back to China? 你什么时候回中国？</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">when, while</p>   <p class="bodytext">when表示片刻时间，也可表示一段时间，主句动词与从句动词既可以同时发生，也可以不同时发生，如：I remembered him when I saw the photo. 我看到照片时想起了他。while表示一段时间，主句动作和从句动作同时发生，从句用延续性的动词，如：Don't speak loudly while the guests are visiting. 客人来访的时候不要大声喧哗。</p></div>
author@［ˈɔ:θə(r)］@n. 作家，作者；创始人，发起者</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I dreamed of being an author when I was young. 小时候，我梦想成为一名作家。</p>
Jew@［dʒu:］@n. 犹太人；犹太教徒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> As far as I know, Jews are very clever. 据我所知，犹太人很聪明。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> Jewish（adj. 犹太人的；犹太的）</p>
total@［ˈtəʊtl］@adj. 总的，全部的；完全的，彻底的 n. 总数，总计 v. 合计，总计</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The club has a total membership of 300. 这个俱乐部总共有300名会员。</p>
globe@［gləʊb］@n. 地球，世界；地球仪；球体</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“哥伦布”→哥伦布环游地球发现新大陆→地球</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The sun looks like an orange globe with dark glasses. 戴上墨镜看，太阳像一个橙色的球。</p>
mention@［ˈmenʃn］@n. / v. 提及，说起</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> mention sth. to sb. 向某人提起某事；not to mention 更不用说；Don't mention it. 不用谢。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Hi, Sunny. Your new flat is so nice!</p> <p class="bodytext">— Thanks, ______. （2009年 武汉）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. don't mention it</p> <p class="bodytext">B. my pleasure</p> <p class="bodytext">C. help yourself</p> <p class="bodytext">D. make yourself at home</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 你好，珊妮。你的新公寓真不错。</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 谢谢，请随便一点。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是make yourself at home的含义，意思是“随意，不要拘束”或者“自便”。don't mention it 和my pleasure是回答感谢的，而help yourself 是“自己随便吃”。因此选D。</p>
work@［wɜ:k］@v. （使）工作，（使）劳动；（使）运转；（使）起作用，（使）有效；生产，经营</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 工作，作业；职业，职务；工作成果，产品；著作，作品；功，做功</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：这项工作（work）就是把每个单词（word）都区分开来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> work out 计算出；（事情）进展顺利或结果令人满意；work on 继续工作；影响；work for... 为…工作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He works in a construction company. 他在一家建筑公司工作。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">work, job</p>   <p class="bodytext">work多指生产或完成某物的体力或脑力劳动，一般是不可数名词，如：plenty of work 大量工作；而job侧重于为换取报酬而从事的行业或职业，是可数名词，如：a new job 一份新工作。</p></div>
cabbage@［ˈkæbidʒ］@n. 卷心菜，洋白菜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mother likes to cook dishes with cabbage but I don't like it. 妈妈做菜时喜欢放洋白菜，但我不喜欢吃。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00186.jpeg"/></div>
tenth@［tenθ］@num. 第十（个） n. 十分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Kate's birthday is on the tenth of April. 凯特的生日是4月10日。</p>
hallway@［ˈhɔ:lwei］@n. 走廊，回廊；门厅，过道</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The waiter was so kind that he helped me carry the luggage to the hallway. 服务员人很好，他帮我把行李拿到了走廊。</p>
yet@［jet］@adv. 还，尚，仍然；已经；甚至，更 conj. 然而，但是</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have not yet worked out the problem. 我还没有解决这个问题。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">yet意思是“还没”，主要用在现在完成时的否定句中，如：I haven't get the book yet. 我还没有得到那本书。肯定句中一般用still或者already。</p></div>
soap@［səʊp］@n. 肥皂</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The dirty clothes should be washed thoroughly with soap. 这件脏衣服应该用肥皂彻彻底底地洗干净。</p>
Atlantic@［ætˈlæntik］@adj. 大西洋的 n. 大西洋</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The huge ship sunk in the Atlantic Ocean. 这艘巨轮在大西洋沉没了。</p>
dialogue@［ˈdaiəlɒg］@n. 对话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary sent me a book on English dialogues for language learners. 玛丽寄给我一本为语言学习者编写的英语会话书。</p>
not@［nɒt］@adv. 不，没，不是</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I did not hear anything. 我什么也没听到。</p>
hear@［hiə(r)］@v. ［heard-heard］ 听见；听到，得知；审讯，听证；收到…的信（或电话等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：聆听（hear）心（heart）灵之音</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> hear of/about 听说；hear from 收到…的来信；hear sb. doing/do sth. 听见某人做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—Where is Mary now? Do you know?</p> <p class="bodytext">—No, but I heard ______ in her room a few minutes ago. （2007年 青岛）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. her singing</p> <p class="bodytext">B. her sing</p> <p class="bodytext">C. she was singing</p> <p class="bodytext">D. All the answers are right</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—玛丽现在在哪儿? 你知道吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">—不知道，但是几分钟前我听到她在房间里唱歌。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>hear sb. do sth.表示“听见某人做了某事”，hear sb. doing sth.表示“听见某人正在做某事”。因此本题选B。</p>
pain@［pein］@n. 痛，疼痛；痛苦，悲痛；［pl.］ 辛苦，苦心 v. 使痛苦</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：一下雨（rain），关节就疼（pain）得厉害</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in pain 痛苦地；take pains to do sth. 不辞辛苦去做某事；have a pain in... 某个部位痛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man said he had a pain in the back. 这个人说他背疼。</p>
bill@［bil］@n. 账单；议案，法案；纸币，钞票；单子，节目单；招贴，海报</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 给…开账单；宣传</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：填 （fill） 写支票来买单（bill）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> pay one's bill 买单</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Helen always pays her bills on time. 海伦总是按时还账单。</p>
positive@［ˈpɒzətiv］@adj. 积极的，正面的；肯定的；【电】正的，阳性的；确实的，明确的；十足的，完全的 n. 【摄影】正片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：以乐观的（positive）态度在职位（position）上工作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Animal-related vocabulary is used in positive or negative ways in different cultures. 在不同的文化中，关于动物词汇的用法褒贬不一。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> positively（adv. 明确地；肯定地；带正电地）</p>
gray@［grei］@adj. 灰色的；阴沉的 n. 灰色</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I do not like the color gray. It looks old. 我不喜欢灰色。这个颜色看起来太旧了。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在英式英语中还可以写成grey。</p></div>
fiction@［ˈfikʃn］@n. 小说</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I started writing science fiction two weeks ago. 我两星期前开始写科幻小说。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> fictional（adj. 虚构的；小说的）</p>
pear@［peə(r)］@n. 梨（树）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's good for your health to eat pears. 吃梨有益健康。</p>
tower@［ˈtaʊə(r)］@n. 塔；高楼 v. 高于，优于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> tower above 高出，超过</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The tower in the park has a thousand year history. 公园里的那座塔有1000年的历史了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> towering（adj. 高耸入云的；杰出的）</p>
dig@［dig］@v. ［dug-dug, digging］ 挖，掘；戳，刺；搜寻，探究，细查 n. 戳，捅</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> dig for 发掘；dig into 钻研</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little children were digging a hole. 小孩子们正在挖洞。</p>
two@［tu:］@num. 二，两个 n. 两个（人或物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are two ways to solve this math problem. 解决这道数学难题有两种方法。</p>
death@［deθ］@n. 死，死亡；毁灭</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Two children were burnt to death in the fire. 两个孩子在大火中丧生。</p>
safe@［seif］@n. 保险箱，保险柜 adj. 安全的，平安的；牢靠的，可靠的；谨慎的，稳健的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little girl was very timid so she didn't feel safe on her own. 小女孩太胆小了，她一个人待着时会感觉不安全。</p>
age@［eidʒ］@n. 年龄；老年；时代，时期；很长的一段时间</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. （使）变老；（使）变陈旧；（使）成熟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> at the age of... 在…岁的时候</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Bob could read at the age of 4. 鲍勃四岁就识字了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> aged（adj. …岁的；成年的）；ageing（n. 成熟，变老）</p>
straight@［streit］@adj. 直的，笔直的；连续的，不间断的；直率的；整齐的，端正的；正直的</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 直接地，径直地；立即，马上；正直地，直率地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：这条街道（street）是笔直的（straight）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Go straight along the street and you'll find the church on the right. 沿着这条街一直走，教堂在街道的右边。</p>
onion@［ˈʌnjən］@n. 洋葱，洋葱类植物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little boy didn't like eating onions. 小男孩不喜欢吃洋葱。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00187.jpeg"/></div>
afford@［əˈfɔ:d］@v. 买得起，负担得起；提供，给予</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：af+ford（福特汽车）→能买一辆福特汽车→买得起</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> afford to do sth. 能够做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">This type of MP4 is my favorite, but I can't ______ it. （2009年 兰州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. spend</p> <p class="bodytext">B. cost</p> <p class="bodytext">C. pay</p> <p class="bodytext">D. afford</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>这款MP4是我最喜欢的，但是我买不起。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查近义词的辨析。spend常和介词on连用，表示“在…上花多少钱或时间”；cost的主语是物；pay不能直接接物，而要说pay for sth. 。afford常用于否定句中，表示“负担不起”，因此选D。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> affordable（adj. 负担得起的）</p>
ground@［grａｕｎｄ］@n. 地，地面；场地，场所；根据，原因</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mike was so careless that he fell on the ground. 迈克太不小心了，以至于摔倒在地上。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> groundless（adj. 无理由的，无根据的）</p>
cap@［kæp］@n. 帽子，便帽；盖，罩，套 v. 覆盖；笼罩</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：盖上车（car）盖（cap）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy in a school cap is my little brother. 戴着校帽的那个男孩是我弟弟。</p>
animal@［ˈæniml］@n. 动物，兽，牲畜 adj. 动物的，野兽的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little boy likes animals very much. 这个小男孩非常喜欢动物。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00188.jpeg"/></div>
card@［ka:d］@n. 卡，卡片；请帖；贺卡；纸牌</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This is my membership card. 这是我的会员卡。</p>
escalator@［ˈeskəleitə(r)］@n. 〈美〉自动扶梯</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The escalator in the building brought me to the third floor. 我乘大厦里的扶梯来到三楼。</p>
heart@［ha:rt］@n. 心，心脏；内心，感情；勇气，热忱；中心，要点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man has something wrong with his heart. 老人的心脏有些问题。</p>
surf@［sɜ:f］@n. 拍岸浪花；拍岸涛声；拍岸碎浪 v. 冲浪；（互联网上）冲浪，浏览</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like listening to the sound of surf breaking on the beach. 我喜欢听浪花拍岸的声音。</p>
breakfast@［ˈbrekfəst］@n. 早餐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I didn't have breakfast this morning. 我今天早上没吃早餐。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00189.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">“吃早餐”用英语说就是have breakfast，考生要注意，breakfast等表示三餐的名词前没有任何冠词，如：have lunch, have supper, have dinner。</p></div>
guide@［gaid］@n. 导游，领路人；指南，手册 v. 给…导游，给…领路；指导，引导</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We hired a local guide to help us find the cave. 我们雇了一位当地导游帮我们寻找山洞。</p>
weekend@［ˈwi:kˌend］@n. 周末 adj. 周末的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：week（周）+end（末端）→每周的末端→周末</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We are going to visit our teacher this weekend. 这周末我们去看望老师。</p>
practice@［ˈpræktis］@n. 实践；实践行动；练习；惯例，习俗</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> put...into practice 把…付诸实践</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We have made a plan and now what we have to do is to put it into practice. 我们已经制订好了计划，现在要做的就是把它付诸实践。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> practicable（adj. 可行的；适用的）；practical（adj. 实用的；符合实际的）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">考试中，经常会有同学搞不清楚practise与practice。要记住practise是动词，practice是名词，类似的词还有advise（v. 劝告）和advice（n. 忠告，建议）。但需要注意的是，在美式英语中，practice一词既作名词，又作动词，而practise一词则很少使用。</p></div>
a/an@［ə ; æn］@art. 一（个）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Millie has ______ e-dog and its name is Hobo. （2008年 上海）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. a</p> <p class="bodytext">B. an</p> <p class="bodytext">C. the</p> <p class="bodytext">D. 不填</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>米莉有一只电子狗，它的名字叫Hobo。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查冠词的用法。以元音音素开头的可数名词前用不定冠词an，故选B。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">以元音音素开头的可数名词前用不定冠词an；以辅音音素开头的可数名词前用不定冠词a。一般以元音字母a, e, i, o, u开头的单词第一个音是元音，但也有一些例外需要注意，如：an hour<span class="yinbiao1">［ˈaʊə(r)］</span> 一小时（h不发音），a university <span class="yinbiao1">［ˌju:niˈvɜ:səti］</span> 一所大学（字母u发<span class="yinbiao1">［ju:］</span> 的音，以辅音音素<span class="yinbiao1">［j］</span>开头）。</p></div>
schoolbag@［ˈsku:lbæg］@n. 书包</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> What's your schoolbag like? 你的书包是什么样子的？</p>
kilo@［ˈki:ləʊ］@n. 千克</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The fish is 2 kilos. 这条鱼重2千克。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> kilogram（n. 千克）</p>
other@［ˈʌðə(r)］@adj. 别的，其他的，另外的；另一的，其余的</p> <p class="bodytext1">pron. 另一个人（或物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> each other 彼此；other than 除了；at any other time 在其他任何时间；the other day 前几天</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">If the question ______ incorrectly, ______ question will be given to you.（2009年 兰州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. is answered, other</p> <p class="bodytext">B. answers, other</p> <p class="bodytext">C. is answered, another</p> <p class="bodytext">D. answers, another</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>如果这个问题回答错了，会问你另一个问题。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是被动语态和不定代词的用法。问题被人回答，用被动语态be answered；如果回答错了，就会再给出一个问题，这里选用another，因为other往往跟冠词the连用，表示二者中的另一个。因此只能选C。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00190.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext5">other, the other, another</p>   <p class="bodytext">other是形容词，表示“其他的”，others是other的复数形式，如：I don't care about what other people think. 我不在乎其他人怎么想。the other是二者中的另一个，如：I have two apples；one is green, the other is red. 我有两个苹果，一个是绿色的，另一个是红色的。another指的是三者或三者以上的事物中的另一个，是泛指，如：I don't like the color of the clothes. Can you show me another one? 我不喜欢这件衣服的颜色，你能再给我看一件吗？</p></div>
matter@［ˈmætə(r)］@n. 事情，情况；物质；麻烦事，毛病 v. 要紧，有关系</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> as a matter of fact 实际上；It doesn't matter. 不要紧，没关系。（用于回答别人的道歉）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> No matter what happens, you should face it bravely. 无论发生了什么事，你都应该勇敢面对。</p>
full@［fʊl］@adj. 满的，装满的；完全的，完整的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be full of... 充满…；at full speed 全速地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I cannot speak because my mouth is full. 我说不了话，因为我的嘴里塞满了食物。</p>
pressure@［ˈpreʃə(r)］@n. 压（力）；压强；强制，压迫 v. 对…施加压力（或影响）；迫使，说服</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：press（压）+ure（名词后缀）→压力</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boiling point of liquids changes with pressure. 液体的沸点随着压力的变化而变化。</p>
diet@［ˈdaiət］@n. 日常饮食；（病人或减肥者的）特种饮食，规定饮食 v. 进特种饮食，节食</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：过度节食（diet）会死（die）人的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm on a diet to lose weight. 我正在节食减肥。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> dietary（adj. 饮食的）；dieter（n. 节食者，减肥者）</p>
hurt@［hɜ:t］@v. ［hurt-hurt］ 使受伤，弄痛；伤…的感情；危害，损害 n. 伤害，痛苦</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to help her but she hurt my feelings. 我想帮她，但是她伤害了我的感情。</p>
project@［ˈprɒdʒekt］@n. 方案，计划；课题，项目；工程</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［prəˈdʒekt］</span> v. 投射，发射；放映；（使）凸出，（使）伸出；设计，规划</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The new project is to establish a new national park in the city center. 新方案是在市中心建一个新的国家公园。// A missile was projected into space. 导弹被发射升空。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> projecting（adj. 凸出的，伸出的）；projector（n. 放映机）；projection（n. 设计，规划；放映）</p>
enemy@［ˈenəmi］@n. 敌人，仇敌</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> All the enemies were killed in the battle. 战斗中所有的敌人都被消灭了。</p>
supermarket@［ˈsu:pəma:kit］@n. 超市</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：super（超级）+market（市场）→超市</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The supermarket sells all sorts of goods. 超市里卖各种各样的商品。</p>
nature@［ˈneitʃə(r)］@n. 大自然，自然界；本性，性格，性情；性质，类型</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> by nature 生来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Nature provides so many things for human beings. 大自然为人类提供了如此多的东西。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> natural（adj. 自然的，天然的）；naturalism（n. 自然主义）</p>
vocabulary@［vəˈkæbjələri］@n. 词汇；词汇量；词汇表</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> If your vocabulary is limited, you cannot become a good translator. 如果词汇量有限，你不可能成为优秀的译员。</p>
list@［list］@n. 表；目录，名单 v. 把…编列成表；列举</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a list which shows who will take part in the party. 这有一张名单，上面列出了将要参加聚会的人的名字。</p>
comma@［ˈkɒmə］@n. 逗号</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There should be a comma in this sentence. 这句话里应该有一个逗号。</p>
zoo@［zu:］@n. 动物园</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I brought my son to the zoo to see the elephants. 我带儿子去动物园看大象。</p>
hide@［haid］@v. ［hid-hidden］ 把…藏起来，躲藏；隐瞒，遮掩 n. 皮革，兽皮</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lisa tried to hide her feelings. 莉萨试图掩饰她的情绪。</p>
quality@［ˈkwɒləti］@n. 质，质量；品德，品质；性质，特性 adj. 优良的，优质的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：商品质量（quality）好，卖出去的数量（quantity）就多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I believe that her English reflected the quality of the school education. 我认为，她的英语水平反映了该校的教学质量。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> qualitative（adj. 定性的）</p>
grass@［gra:s］@n. 草；草坪；牧场</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：班里（class）的同学在草地（grass）上野餐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Walking on the grass is not allowed. 禁止践踏草坪。</p>
conversation@［ˌkɒnvəˈseiʃn］@n. 交谈，谈话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> have a conversation with 和…交谈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> They had a conversation with each other but they didn't reach an agreement. 他们之前谈过话，但是没有达成一致意见。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> conversational（adj. 口语的；会话的）</p>
flower@［ˈflaʊə(r)］@n. 花；花卉 v. 开花；发育，成熟；繁荣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man bought some beautiful flowers for his girlfriend. 这位男士给他女朋友买了一些漂亮的花。</p>
continue@［kənˈtinju:］@v. 继续；延续；延伸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> continue to do / doing sth. 继续做某事；continue with sth. 继续做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The snow continued falling all the evening. 雪持续下了一个晚上。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">continue后既可以接动名词，也可以接不定式，但是有区别。接不定式表示继续做其他的事，而接动名词表示继续做刚才的事。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">After work, I continue to watch TV. 下班后，我接着看电视。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I continue watching TV this evening. 今天晚上我一直在看电视。</p></div>
furniture@［ˈfɜ:nitʃə(r)］@n. 家具</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm going to buy some furniture for my new house. 我要为我的新房子买一些家具。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">furniture是不可数名词，不能与冠词a直接连用，要表达“一件家具”，可以说a piece of furniture。</p></div>
Christmas@［ˈkrisməs］@n. 圣诞节</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We usually go to the church to celebrate Christmas Eve. 我们通常去教堂庆祝平安夜。</p>
snow@［snəʊ］@n. （一场）雪 v. 下雪；用雪覆盖</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：大家都听过白雪公主（Snow White）和七个小矮人的故事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is sunny today and the snow has begun to melt. 今天是个大晴天，雪开始融化了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> snowy（adj. 下雪的；多雪的；雪白的）</p>
comedy@［ˈkɒmədi］@n. 喜剧，喜剧性（事件）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I prefer comedies to tragedies. 比起悲剧，我更喜欢喜剧。</p>
miss@［mis］@n. 小姐 v. 未击中，未达到；未赶上，错过；思念，想念；未明白；避免，逃脱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">He went with me to the hospital, which made him ______ his train. （2009年 陕西）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. catch</p> <p class="bodytext">B. miss</p> <p class="bodytext">C. drop</p> <p class="bodytext">D. meet</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>他和我去了医院，结果没赶上火车。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查几个动词的意思。catch意为“赶上”，miss意为“错过，没赶上”，drop意为“丢掉”，meet意为“见面”，应该选B。</p>
Africa@［ˈæfrikə］@n. 非洲</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have never been to Africa. 我从来没去过非洲。</p>
object@［ˈɒbdʒikt］@n. 物体，实物；对象，客体；目的，目标；宾语</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［əbˈdʒekt］</span> v. 反对，不赞成</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：确定目标（object）和主题（subject）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> object to （doing） sth. 反对（做）某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> No one has objected to the plan so far. 到目前为止，没有人反对这项计划。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> objection（n. 反对）；objective（adj. 客观的）</p>
Canada@［ˈkænədə］@n. 加拿大</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have been to Canada twice. 我去过两次加拿大。</p>
invite@［inˈvait］@v. 邀请；征求，请求；吸引，招致（麻烦等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> invite sb. to do sth. 邀请某人做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> They invited Lucy to join in the party. 他们邀请露西参加聚会。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> invitation（n. 邀请；邀请书）</p>
mind@［maind］@n. 头脑，精神，理智；智力；注意力，心思；意向，想法</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 介意；注意，留心；照料</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“慢的”→头脑反应慢的→头脑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> keep...in mind 牢记在心；make up one's mind 下定决心</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Would you ______ turning down the music a little bit? It's too noisy.</p> <p class="bodytext">— Of course not. I'll do it right away. （2008年 宜昌）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. advise</p> <p class="bodytext">B. succeed</p> <p class="bodytext">C. like</p> <p class="bodytext">D. mind</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 你介意把音乐的音量调小一点吗？太吵了。</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 当然不介意。我这就去。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是固定搭配would you mind doing sth. 的用法。would you mind后面可以直接跟动名词形式，而would you like后面跟动词的不定式。advise和succeed不与would you连用，因此选D。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> absent-minded （adj. 心不在焉的）；open-minded （adj. 思想开放的）；single-minded （adj. 坚决的）</p>
easily@［ˈi:zəli］@adv. 容易地，不费力地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The climber reached the top of the mountain easily. 登山者轻松登上了山顶。</p>
win@［win］@v. ［won-won, winning］ 在…中获胜；赢得，获得 n. 胜利，赢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our basketball team won the championship. 我们的篮球队赢得了冠军。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">win, beat</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都可以用作及物动词，作“赢，战胜”讲。win的宾语是比赛、战争或奖品类，如：win the prize 赢得奖品；而beat的宾语是比赛或者竞争的对手，即人或者球队等，如：We beat the strongest team. 我们打败了最强的队伍。</p></div>
glove@［glʌv］@n. 手套</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's getting cold and I have to take out my cotton gloves. 天气变凉了，我得把我的棉手套拿出来了。</p>
president@［ˈprezidənt］@n. 总统；主席；（大学）校长，会长；董事长，总经理</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：preside（主持）+nt→主持国家事务的人→主席；总统</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mr. Bush used to be the President of America. 布什先生曾经是美国总统。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> presidential（adj. 总统的）</p>
bell@［bel］@n. 钟，铃；钟声，铃声</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You can't leave the classroom until the bell rings. 铃响了你才能离开教室。</p>
medicine@［ˈmedsn］@n. 内服药；医学；内科学</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take medicine 吃药</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span>—Don't worry! Take some medicine and you'll be fine.</p> <p class="bodytext6">—Thank you very much, doctor.</p> <p class="bodytext6">—别担心！吃点药，你就会好的。</p> <p class="bodytext6">—谢谢您，医生。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">drug, medicine, pill</p>   <p class="bodytext">提到“药”，常见的单词有drug, medicine, pill。drug一般指片剂，有时也指毒品；medicine是药物的统称，比较宽泛，作“药”讲的时候是不可数名词，如：take medicine 吃药；pill是指药丸、药片，如：take sleeping pills 吃安眠药片。</p></div>
though@［ðəʊ］@conj. 尽管，虽然 adv. 可是，不过，然而</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> even though 尽管，虽然；as though（=as if） 好像，仿佛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">______ the story is short and there are no new words in it, it is difficult to understand. （2007年 济南）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. But</p> <p class="bodytext">B. Though</p> <p class="bodytext">C. And</p> <p class="bodytext">D. For</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>虽然这则故事很短，并且没有生词，但是很难理解。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查几个连词的区别。though用作连词时表示“尽管”，后面表达的意思跟前面所列举的情况相反。此外，在英语中，although或though不能跟but同时出现。but表示转折，意思是“但是”；and是并列连词，连接两个并列的句子；for作连词时表示“因为”。根据题意，应该选B。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">though和but都是转折连词，但两个词不能同时出现在一个句子里，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（〇） Though Mary is quite small, she's very strong. 虽然玛丽很小巧，但是她很强壮。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（〇） Mary is quite small, but she's very strong. 虽然玛丽很小巧，但是她很强壮。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（✕） Though Mary is quite small, but she's very strong. 虽然玛丽很小巧，但是她很强壮。</p></div>
lift@［lift］@v. 提，抬起 n. 电梯；抬，上升；搭便车</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The lift took Peter to the tenth floor. 电梯将彼得送到了10层。</p>
tale@［teil］@n. 故事，传说</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's an ancient tale which tells us how to be good people. 这是一则古老的故事，故事告诉我们怎样做好人。</p>
message@［ˈmesidʒ］@n. 信息，便条，口信；要点；要旨</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Signs can carry as many ______ as words. （2009年 兰州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. questions</p> <p class="bodytext">B. examples</p> <p class="bodytext">C. tears and smiles</p> <p class="bodytext">D. messages</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>符号能够承载的信息和词语一样多。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是单词的含义。questions意为“问题”，examples意为“例子”，tears and smiles意为“泪水与欢笑”，messages意为“消息，信息”，因此选D。</p>
repair@［riˈpeə(r)］@n. 修理，修补；维修状态，保养情况 v. 修理，修补；弥补，补救</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Father sent his car to the garage for repair. 父亲把车送到修理厂去修理。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> reparable（adj. 能补救的）；reparation（n. 补偿）</p>
god@［gɔd］@n. 神；［G-］ 上帝</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：去（go）见上帝（God）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> God bless everybody. 上帝保佑每一个人。</p>
run@［rʌn］@v. ［run-run, running］ 跑，奔跑；行驶，驾驶；蔓延，（道路等）伸展；操作；竞选；流，淌 n. 跑步，奔跑；路程，行程，航程</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Henry runs faster than his friends. 亨利比他的朋友们跑得快。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> runner（n. 奔跑者）</p>
the@［ðə］@art. 这，那</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Of all the classmates, I like Mary most. 在所有的同学中，我最喜欢玛丽。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">“the+比较级…，the+比较级…”，表示“越…越…”，如：The warmer the weather is, the better I feel. 天气越暖和，我感觉越舒服。</p></div>
ship@［ʃip］@n. 船（舶），舰 v. 用船运；装运，运送</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：用船（ship）运送羊（sheep）出口外国</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The aged man used to be the captain of a ship. 这位年长者曾经是一艘船的船长。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">ship, boat</p>   <p class="bodytext">ship一般指体积比较大的船，可以运载货物，也可以指“轮船”；boat是小舟或小艇，通常只能容纳几个人。</p></div>
invent@［inˈvent］@v. 发明，创造；捏造，虚构</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：捏造（invent）事件（event）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't know who invented the mouse. 我不知道谁发明的鼠标。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> invention（n. 发明，创造）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">invent, discover</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者意思相近，注意区分。invent强调通过研究制造出从前没有的东西，如：Henry invented a computer program. 亨利设计了一种电脑程序。discover指发现本来存在但没人知道的事物，如：Scientists discovered a new animal in the forest. 科学家在森林里发现了一个新物种。</p></div>
special@［ˈspeʃl］@adj. 特殊的，特别的；专门的，特设的；附加的，额外的 n. 特价；特刊；（电视）特别节目</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is nothing special in today's newspaper. 今天的报纸上没报道什么特别的事。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> specialist（n. 专家）；specialty（n. 专业；特长）；specialization（n. 专门化，特殊化）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00191.jpeg"/></div>
population@［ˌpɒpjuˈleiʃn］@n. 人口；（统称）某领域的生物；族群；人口</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">______ is the population of Shandong Province? （2006年 德州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. How many</p> <p class="bodytext">B. Which</p> <p class="bodytext">C. How much</p> <p class="bodytext">D. What</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>山东省有多少人口？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是What's the population of...这一句型。在这句话中，population意指“人口”，强调人口的数量，通常用作单数。how many和how much都直接接名词表示“数量多少”，前者接可数名词，后者接不可数名词。which意为“哪一个”，与题意不符，因此选D。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">population作主语时，谓语用单数，如：The population of this country is very large. 这个国家的人口很多。而当population与分数连用时，后面的谓语动词用复数，如：Three fifths of the population are white people. 五分之三的人口是白人。</p></div>
condition@［kənˈdiʃn］@n. 状况，状态；［pl.］ 环境，形势；条件，前提 v. 训练，使适应；对…有重要影响</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on condition that 条件是…，如果…；under/in...condition 在…情况下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> In the past, the living conditions were very bad. 过去生活条件非常差。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> conditional（adj. 条件的；附带条件的）；conditioner（n. 护发素；柔顺剂）</p>
hum@［hʌm］@v. ［hummed-hummed, humming］ 哼曲子；发出嗡嗡声；忙碌，充满活力</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 嗡嗡声，嘈杂声</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little girl hums the song over and over again. 小女孩一遍一遍地哼着歌曲。</p>
sell@［sel］@v. ［sold-sold］ 卖，出售；推销</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> sell at... 以某种价格出售</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> They sold the tickets for 3D Alice in Wonderland at a very high price. 他们以很高的价格出售《爱丽丝漫游仙境》3D版的电影票。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00192.jpeg"/></div>
usual@［ˈju:ʒuəl］@adj. 通常的，惯常的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> as usual 照常，照例</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> As usual, he goes to work by bus. 同往常一样，他乘公共汽车上班。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> usually（adv. 通常，大抵）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext5">usual, normal, common</p>   <p class="bodytext">usual意为“惯常的”，指的是人的行为习惯，如：Everything is as usual. 一切都像平常一样。而normal意为“正常的，常规的”，是相对非正常而言的，如：normal temperature 正常温度。common意为“普通的，平常的”，指大多数人或者事物共同具备的，如：The common people didn't like this movie. 老百姓不喜欢这部电影。</p></div>
jazz@［dʒæz］@n. 爵士乐 adj. 爵士乐的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't have any interest in jazz. 我对爵士乐没有任何兴趣。</p>
wolf@［wʊlf］@n. 狼；残忍贪婪之人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Wolves are a kind of cruel animal. 狼是一种残忍的动物。</p>
offer@［ˈɒfə(r)］@v. 给予，提供；表示愿意（做）；提出，提议 n. 提供（物），提议；报价，开价</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My friend offered me a cup of coffee. 我朋友给我倒了一杯咖啡。</p>
display@［diˈsplei］@n. / v. 陈列，展览；显示，表现</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on display 展览，陈列</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many precious treasures are displayed in the exhibition. 展览会上展出了许多珍贵的宝物。</p>
around@［əˈraʊnd］@adv. 在周围，在附近；到处，四周；大约 prep. 在…各处，遍及；在…四周；在</p> <p class="bodytext">那边</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are many different kinds of fish around the world. 全世界有很多不同种类的鱼。</p>
water@［ˈwɔ:tə(r)］@n. 水，雨水，［pl.］ 河（湖、海）水；水域；水位，水面</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 浇水；给…供（或加）水；流泪水，流口水</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These areas have a shortage of water. 这些地区缺水。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">表达“乘船”或者“经水路”，经常用by water或者by sea，如：I went to the country by sea. 我乘船去了那个国家。</p></div>
accept@［əkˈsept］@vt. 接受；承认；相信</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：ac+cept（拿，抓）→抓住把柄，只好承认→承认</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jim accepted my present. 吉姆接受了我的礼物。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> acceptable（adj. 可接受的）；unacceptable（adj. 不可接受的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00193.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">accept, receive</p>   <p class="bodytext">accept表示主观上接受，而receive表示客观上收到，如：Lily received a birthday present from a boy but did not accept it. 莉莉收到了一个男孩送的生日礼物，但没有接受。</p></div>
instead@［inˈsted］@adv. 作为替代，顶替；反而，却</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：in（在…内）+stead（看作steal，偷）→从中做手脚，偷天换日→代替</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> instead of 代替；而不是</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy didn't go to school—he went to the Internet bar instead. 男孩并没去上学，而是去了网吧。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">instead, instead of</p>   <p class="bodytext">instead是副词，是“顶替，替代”的意思，如：The professor is ill today, so I take his class instead. 教授今天病了，我给他代课。instead of是介词短语，后面可以跟名词、代词、动名词或介词短语等，如：We'll play basketball instead of playing badminton. 我们要去打篮球，而不是打羽毛球。</p></div>
rice@［rais］@n. 稻；大米；米饭</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I had some rice for supper. 我晚餐吃的是米饭。</p>
here@［hiə(r)］@adv. 在这里，到这里；在这一点上 int. 嘿（用于引起注意）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：这里（here） 那里（there），到处都是</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Stop here and have a good weekend. 就到这里吧，周末愉快。</p>
rain@［rein］@n. 雨；雨天；雨季 v. 下雨</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> What bad weather! I don't like the rain! 天气太糟糕了！我不喜欢下雨。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> rainy（adj. 下雨的，多雨的）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">形容雨势的大小多用heavy或slight，不能用big或small。rain是不可数名词，但是如果前面有修饰词时，则可以与不定冠词a或an连用。</p></div>
pick@［pik］@v. 挑选，选择；采摘 n. 挑选；选中的人（或物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：捡起（pick）球用脚踢（kick）出去</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> pick sth. up / pick up sth. 捡起；收拾；获得（尤指不经意间学到）；重新开始；pick sb. up / pick up sb. 用车接某人；pick out 精心挑选</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Father will pick me up on his way home. 父亲会在回家路上顺便接我。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> picky（adj. 挑剔的）</p>
anybody@［ˈenibɒdi］@pron. 任何人；随便哪一个人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">I knocked on the door several times but ______ answered, so I left. （2008年上海）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. somebody</p> <p class="bodytext">B. nobody</p> <p class="bodytext">C. anybody</p> <p class="bodytext">D. everybody</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>我敲了几下门，但是没有人开，于是我便离开了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查不定代词的区别。somebody意为“某人”；nobody意为“无人”；anybody意为“任何人”；everybody意为“每个人”。根据句意，应该选B。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">anybody在考试中经常出现，其用法如下：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（1）作主语时，动词用单数。如：Is anybody here? 有人吗？</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（2）作主语时，动词不用否定式，要想表示否定，应使用nobody，后接肯定句式，如：Nobody likes this game. 没有人喜欢这个游戏。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（3）该词是不定代词，修饰它的词要放在它的后面，如：anybody famous名人。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（4）注意区别下面两个句子：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">a. Tom's taller than anybody else in his class. 汤姆比他们班的其他任何人都高。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">b. Tom's taller than anybody in my class. 汤姆比我们班的任何一个人都高。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">第一句中Tom是his class中的一员，所以anybody后面要加else，表示“比他们班除他以外的任何人都高”；第二句中anybody后面没有加else是因为Tom不是my class中的一员。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（5） anybody只能指人，不能指物；其后一般不接 of 短语。如果指物或后接of 短语，需使用分开写的any one，如：any one of the bags 书包中的任何一个。</p></div>
teach@［ti:tʃ］@v. ［taught-taught］ 教，讲授；教导，教训</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mr. Green taught English in our class. 格林先生以前教我们班英语。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">teach经常用的搭配是teach sb. sth.，如：The teacher teaches me English. 这位老师教我英语。</p></div>
far@［fa:(r)］@adv. 远；久远；很大程度上，极 adj. 远的，远方的；久远的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> as/so far as I know 据我所知；as/so far as I am concerned 就我而言，我认为；so far 迄今；by far 最…，…得多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The station is far from where I live. 车站离我住的地方很远。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">far的比较级和最高级比较特殊，分别是farther/further和farthest/furthest。</p></div>
hope@［həʊp］@n. / v. 希望，期望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I hope the weather will be fine tomorrow. 我希望明天天气会变好。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">hope, wish</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“希望”的意思。hope常指可实现的愿望，而wish指难以实现的愿望。wish可以接双宾语和从句，接从句时要用虚拟语气，如：I wish I could fly. 我希望我会飞。</p></div>
our@［ˈaʊə(r)］@pron. 我们的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think all of us should respect our teachers. 我认为我们所有人都应该尊敬我们的老师。</p>
sixteenth@［ˈsiksˈti:nθ］@num. 第十六（个） n. 十六分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Peter's score ranks sixteenth in his class. 彼得的成绩在他们班排第16名。</p>
twenty@［ˈtwenti］@num. 二十，二十个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My younger brother is twenty years old. 我弟弟20岁了。</p>
building@［ˈbildiŋ］@n. 建筑物，房屋；建筑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The building near the Tea House is the People's Hospital. 靠近茶馆的建筑是人民医院。</p>
important@［imˈpɔ:tnt］@adj. 重要的，重大的；有势力的，有地位的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's very important to take your ID card when you travel. 旅行时，带着身份证十分重要。</p>
model@［ˈmɒdl］@n. 模型；模特儿；模范，典型</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 做…的模型；仿效，模仿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy said he wanted to be a model. 男孩说他想成为模特。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00194.jpeg"/></div>
mistake@［miˈsteik］@n. 错误；过失 v. ［mistook-mistaken］ 误解，误会，弄错；把…误认为</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：mis（错）+take（拿）→拿错→弄错</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> make a mistake / make mistakes 犯错误；by mistake 错误地；mistake...for... 错把…当做…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I made a mistake at the meeting. 我在会上犯错误了。</p>
they@［ðei］@pron. 他（她、它）们</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have a cat and a dog, and they fight with each other all the time. 我有一只狗和一只猫，它们总是打架。</p>
instrument@［ˈinstrəmənt］@n. 乐器；仪器，器械</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little girl can play two kinds of musical instruments. 小女孩能演奏两种乐器。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> instrumental（adj. 有帮助的；乐器的）；instrumentalist （n. 器乐演奏者，器乐家）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00195.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">instrument, tool</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者意思相近，注意区别。instrument常指乐器或仪器等，而tool泛指一般的工具，如农具等。</p></div>
coach@［kəʊtʃ］@n. 教练，指导；长途公共汽车；（客机的）经济舱 v. 训练；指导，辅导</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Meimei's mother is a volleyball coach. 梅梅的妈妈是一位排球教练。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00196.jpeg"/></div>
elementary@［ˌeliˈmentri］@adj. 基本的，基础的；初级的，小学的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I went to the elementary school when I was 7. 我七岁上的小学。</p>
call@［kɔ:l］@v. 把…叫做，把…称为；打电话给；叫，大声说出；召唤，传唤；召开，召集；访问，拜访 n. 喊叫，鸣叫；（一次）电话，通电话；访问，拜访</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> call sb. 给某人打电话；call at 访问（某地）；call on 拜访（某人）；call for 要求；去拿，去接；call off 取消，放弃；call out 大喊；call up 打电话；回忆起</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> If you want to make a call in the company, you must dial“9”first. 如果你想在公司打外线，必须先拨9。</p>
talented@［ˈtæləntid］@adj. 有才能的，有才干的；天才的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Susan is a talented musician as well as an excellent athlete. 苏珊是一个很有天赋的音乐家，还是一名优秀的运动员。</p>
mixture@［ˈmikstʃə(r)］@n. 混合；混合物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：mix（使混合）+t+ure（名词后缀）→混合；混合物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Henry decided to taste the hot mixture. 亨利决定尝尝这种热腾腾的混合物。</p>
duty@［ˈdju:ti］@n. 责任，义务；职责，职务；税，关税</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on duty 值班；a sense of duty 责任感</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is our duty to protect the natural environment. 保护自然环境是我们的责任。</p>
note@［nəʊt］@n. 短笺，便条；记录，笔记；注解；音调，音符</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 注意，留意；记录，记下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take notes 做笔记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Chinese students prefer taking notes when they have classes. 中国学生上课时喜欢做笔记。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> noted（adj. 闻名的，著名的）</p>
unhappy@［ʌnˈhæpi］@adj. 不快乐的；不幸的，悲惨的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：un（不）+happy（快乐的）→不快乐的；不幸的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Beth's unhappy childhood led her to have a negative attitude towards life. 贝丝不幸的童年导致她对人生持消极态度。</p>
doll@［dɒl］@n. 玩偶，玩具娃娃</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This doll was my first birthday present. 这个洋娃娃是我的第一件生日礼物。</p>
stream@［stri:m］@n. 小河，溪流；流，一股；一连串 v. 流（出），涌（出）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A stream of blood flowed from the wound. 伤口涌出一股血来。</p>
below@［biˈləʊ］@prep. 在…下面，到…下面；在…以下；低于</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 在下面，到下面</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher asked the students to write down the class number below their names. 老师要求学生在姓名下面写上班级号。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00197.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">below, under</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“在…下”的意思。below指任意的下方，也可以用来表示在平面、价值、程度、水平之下，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">The bird is flying below the clouds. 小鸟在云层下飞翔。</p>   <p class="bodytext">Ann's work is below average. 安的工作低于一般水平。</p>   <p class="bodytext">而under指正下方，可以用于年龄等抽象事物，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">The dog is under the table. 狗在桌子底下。</p>   <p class="bodytext">The teacher is under thirty. 这位老师不到30岁。</p></div>
kill@［kil］@v. 杀死，扼杀；终止，否决；使疼痛，使非常痛苦；消磨，打发（时间）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：宰杀（kill）病（ill）鸡</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> His wife was killed in a car accident. 他的妻子在车祸中丧生。</p>
fold@［fəʊld］@n. 褶痕，褶缝 v. 折叠，合拢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：和old（adj. 旧的，老的）、hold（v. 拿，握）一起记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> fold up 折叠起来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I folded a paper airplane and threw it into the sky. 我叠了一只纸飞机，将它向空中掷去。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> folder（n. 文件夹，纸夹）</p>
discuss@［diˈskʌs］@v. 谈论，讨论，论述</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> discuss the problem with sb. 与某人讨论问题</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Don't discuss the problems with your competitor. 别和你的竞争对手讨论问题。</p>
peace@［pi:s］@n. 和平，和睦；平静，安宁，安静</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People in this village share the life of peace. 这个村子里的人共享和平生活。</p>
good@［gʊd］@adj. 好的，令人满意的；有道德的，高尚的；有本事的，擅长的；好心的，慈善的；乖的，恭顺的；适合的，有益的 n. 善，好事；好处，利益；［pl.］ 货物，商品</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：仁慈的（good）上帝（God）请宽恕他</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be good for 有益于；be good at 擅长，善于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Simon is good at playing basketball. 西蒙很擅长打篮球。</p>
toy@［tɔi］@n. 玩具 v. 漫不经心地考虑；摆弄</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：儿童玩玩具（toy），他们带来许多欢乐（joy）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> toy with 玩弄</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Children nowadays are so lucky. They have many toys. 现在的小孩太幸运了。他们有许多玩具。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00198.jpeg"/></div>
final@［ˈfainl］@adj. 最后的，最终的；决定性的，确定性的 n. 期末考试；决赛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm preparing for the final exam. 我正在为期末考试做准备。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> finally（adv. 终于）</p>
none@［nʌn］@pron. 没有一人（或物），没有一点儿 adv. 一点也不，毫不，毫无</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> None of these people can speak Chinese. 这些人没有一个会说汉语。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">none, nobody</p>   <p class="bodytext">none单独使用的时候，常用来回答how many或者how much的问句，可以跟of形成搭配，可以指物，也可以指人。nobody=no one，一般用来回答who提出的问句，只能指人，而且不能与of 构成搭配。</p></div>
even@［ˈi:vn］@adv. 甚至；即使 adj. 平的；均匀的，平稳的；相等的，均衡的；偶数的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> even if/though 即使；even so 即便如此</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I didn't even get a chance to perform on the stage. 我甚至没有机会上台表演。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> evenly（adv. 平坦地；均匀地）</p>
insist@［inˈsist］@v. 坚持要求，强调；坚决主张；坚持说，固执地声称</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> insist on （doing） sth. 坚持（做）某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is difficult for you to insist on doing exercises. 坚持锻炼对于你来说很难。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">insist作“坚持”讲的时候后面的宾语从句要用虚拟语气，即“主语+insist+that+（should）+动词原形”的结构，其中should可以省略，如：Mary insists that she should come. 玛丽坚持强调她会来。</p></div>
winter@［ˈwintə(r)］@n. 冬，冬季；萧条期，衰退期 adj. 冬天的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Last winter we went skiing. 去年冬天我们去滑雪了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00199.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">季节前要用介词in，如果有季节，也有具体的日子，介词的运用要依照具体的日子，如：on the first day of winter 冬季的第一天。</p></div>
party@［ˈpa:ti］@n. 社交聚会；党，政党；一方，当事人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'll hold a party for my friend this evening. 我今晚要为朋友举办一个聚会。</p>
opinion@［əˈpinjən］@n. 意见，主张</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：opin（看作open，公开的）+ion→公开表达自己的看法→意见</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in one's opinion 在某人看来，某人认为；opinion on/about... 对…的看法或观点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have different opinions about this. 在这件事上我持不同的意见。</p>
guess@［ges］@n. 推测，猜测 v. 猜测；以为，相信</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We can guess what will happen next. 我们可以猜一下接下来会发生什么。</p>
pool@［pu:l］@n. 池塘，水池；游泳池；（液体等的）一摊，一片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our middle school is building a pool behind the teaching building. 我们中学正在教学楼后面建一个游泳池。</p>
nineteen@［ˌnainˈti:n］@num. 十九，十九个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The young man will have a party when he is nineteen years old. 这个年轻人19岁时将举办一个聚会。</p>
money@［ˈmʌni］@n. 钱，货币</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have no money on me now. 我身上现在没钱。</p>
do@［du:］@v. ［did-done］ 做，从事；实行，进行；尽力；可用；制作；算出，解答</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> do away with 摆脱，废除；do well in 在…方面做得好；do sb. a favor 帮某人忙；have something to do with... 和…有关</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's such a difficult thing to do. 做这件事可真难。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">do用在肯定句中可加强语气，如：You did come after all! 你还是来了！</p></div>
watermelon@［ˈwɔ:təˌmelən］@n. 西瓜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：water（水）+melon（瓜）→水分很足的瓜→西瓜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Watermelon is one of my favorite fruits. 西瓜是我最喜欢的水果之一。</p>
have@［hæv］@v. aux. 已经，曾经 v. 有；进行，从事；享受，经受；使，让；必须，不得不</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> have trouble/difficulty (in) doing sth. 做某事有困难；have nothing to do with... 和…无关</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mrs. Green is out and I have to look after her baby. 格林夫人外出了，我得照顾她的小孩。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">have to, must</p>   <p class="bodytext">两者都有“必须”的意思。have to是考试中经常出现的短语，表示“不得不”，其后接动词原形，强调客观上要做某事，它的否定形式是not have to；而must强调主观上要做某事。由must引起的疑问句，肯定回答用must或have to，而否定回答要用needn't或don't have to，不能用mustn't，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">— Must I finish the task this week?</p>   <p class="bodytext">— Yes, you must. / No, you don't have to. / No, you needn't.</p>   <p class="bodytext">— 我必须在这周内完成任务吗？</p>   <p class="bodytext">— 是的。/ 不，你不用。</p></div>
protect@［prəˈtekt］@v. 保护，保卫</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> protect...from （doing）... 保护…免受…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These children are learning how to protect themselves. 这些孩子正学习如何保护自己。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">protect, defend</p>   <p class="bodytext">这两个词意思相近，都有“防护，保护”的意思。protect指一般意义上的保护，如：The father protects his child from big guy. 父亲保护他的孩子不受大孩子的欺负。而defend更正式，有“防御，守卫”的意思，如：The army defends the country. 军队保卫国家。</p></div>
build@［bild］@v. ［built-built］ 建造，修建；建立，创立 n. 体型，体格</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> build up 建设；增进；树立；build on/upon... 建立在…的基础上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—Do you take exercise every day?</p> <p class="bodytext">—Yeah, I want to be a sport player. Doing that can build me up. （2009年 黄冈）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. cheer me up</p> <p class="bodytext">B. make me stronger</p> <p class="bodytext">C. keep me active</p> <p class="bodytext">D. change me more</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—你每天都做运动吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">—是的，我想成为一名运动员，这样做可以使我变得更加强壮。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>build sb. up是固定搭配，表示“增强体质，强身健体”，故选B。cheer up意为“使感到振奋”；keep active意为“保持积极活跃”；change more意为“变化更多”。</p>
grandchild@［ˈgræntʃaild］@n. （外）孙子；（外）孙女</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man has no grandchildren and he feels lonely. 老人没有孙子孙女，感觉很孤独。</p>
birth@［bɜ:θ］@n. 出生，分娩；出身；起源，根源</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I moved from my place of birth to London. 我从出生地搬到了伦敦。</p>
swim@［swim］@v. ［swam-swum, swimming］ 游泳；眩晕；浸，泡 n. 游泳</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tina is a trainer who teaches the children to swim. 蒂娜是一位教孩子们游泳的教练。</p>
twentieth@［ˈtwentiθ］@num. 第二十（个） n. 二十分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Simon won the twentieth place in this year's math competition. 今年的数学竞赛上，西蒙位列第20名。</p>
praise@［preiz］@v. 赞扬，表扬 n. 称赞，赞美；赞美的话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：p+raise（提高）→业绩提高，受到表扬→表扬</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> praise sb. for sth. 因某事表扬某人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The new leader received high praise from people in the city. 新的领导人受到了该市市民的高度称赞。</p>
solid@［ˈsɒlid］@adj. 固体的；实心的；结实的，稳固的；可靠的；纯质的，纯色的 n. 固体</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The frame is as solid as a rock. 这个门框像岩石一样结实。// The husband sent his wife a solid gold necklace. 丈夫送给妻子一串纯金项链。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> solidarity（n. 团结）；solidify（v. 凝固）；solidly（adv. 牢固地）</p>
husband@［ˈhʌzbənd］@n. 丈夫</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary's husband is two years older than her. 玛丽的丈夫比她大两岁。</p>
farm@［fa:m］@n. 农场；养殖场 v. 耕作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on the farm在农场</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are more than fifty people working on the farm. 有50多个人正在农场干活。</p>
well@［wel］@adv. 好；妥善地，有利地；令人满意地；完全地；充分地，足够地；很，相当</p> <p class="bodytext1">adj. 良好的；妥善的，有利的；健康的，没病的，康复的 n. 井</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> as well 也</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man can deal with the problem very well. 这个人可以很好地处理问题。//There is a well on the street. 街上有一口井。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">as well, as well as</p>   <p class="bodytext">as well是副词短语，意思是“也”，相当于too，一般放在句尾，如：She likes this dress and I like it as well. 她喜欢这套礼服，我也喜欢。as well as的含义是“还有，不但…而且…”，放在句中，如：I can speak English as well as French. 我不但会说英语，还会说法语。当as well as连接的词作主语时，句子的谓语动词由as well as前面的词决定，如：John as well as I has been to Shanghai. 约翰和我都去过上海。</p></div>
thirsty@［ˈθɜ:sti］@adj. 口渴的；渴望的，渴求的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man was thirsty because it was too hot. 这个人非常渴，因为天气太热了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00200.jpeg"/></div>
mess@［mes］@n. 凌乱的状态，脏乱的状态；混乱的局面，困境 v. 弄糟，弄脏</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> What a mess!太乱了!mess up 把东西弄乱；把某事搞砸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Everything is a mess because there is something wrong with the computer. 电脑出了问题，所以一切都乱了。</p>
culture@［ˈkʌltʃə(r)］@n. 文化；文明；教养，教育</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> traditional Chinese culture 中国传统文化</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We need to learn to respect different cultures. 我们需要学会尊重不同的文化。</p>
Mars@［ma:z］@n. 火星；战神</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：古罗马神话里的战神马尔斯（Mars）脾气火爆，出了名的能惹是生非，用他的名字来命名火星，再恰当不过了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I want to see Mars at night. 我想在夜里看火星。</p>
structure@［ˈstrʌktʃə(r)］@n. 结构，构造；建筑物 v. 构造，建造</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This is the blueprint which shows us the structure of the building. 这是这幢大楼的图纸，从中我们可以看出大楼的结构。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> well-structured（adj. 结构完善的）</p>
meal@［mi:l］@n. 膳食，一餐，一顿（饭）；进餐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：每顿饭（meal）都吃肉（meat）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> three meals a day 一日三餐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Don't forget to brush your teeth before meals. 别忘了饭前刷牙。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">dinner, meal</p>   <p class="bodytext">dinner是“正餐”，一般都是比较正式的晚餐；而meal指的是一日中的每一餐，并不特指哪一顿。</p></div>
during@［ˈdjʊəriŋ］@prep. 在…期间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jane woke up several times during the night. 简夜里醒来好几次。</p>
costume@［ˈkɒstju:m］@n. 戏装；（特定场合穿的）成套服装</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Kids are busy preparing Halloween costumes. 孩子们都在忙着准备万圣节的服装呢。</p>
unimportant@［ˌʌnimˈpɔ:tnt］@adj. 不重要的，琐碎的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：un（不）+important（重要的）→不重要的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do not spend too much time on unimportant things. 别在不重要的事情上花费太多时间。</p>
try@［trai］@v. 试图，努力；试验，试用；审讯，审理；考验，磨炼</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 努力，尝试</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> try one's best 尽某人最大的努力；try on 试穿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will try my best to solve the problem. 我会尽最大的努力来解决这个问题。</p>
get@［get］@v. ［got-gotten/got］ 获得，弄到；收到；变得；（去）拿来；理解，听到；到达</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> get along/on （well） with... 与…相处得（好）；get down to 开始认真做…；get rid of 摆脱，除去；get through 通过；打通（电话）；get out of 从…出来；get away 逃脱，离开；get across 通过；（使）被理解；get over 克服；恢复；get off 下来；出发</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Did you get your friend's message? 你收到你朋友的信息了吗？</p>
write@［rait］@v. ［wrote-written］ 写，书写，写字；写作，作曲；写信（给）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> write out 写出；write to 给…写信；write down 写下，记下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> John keeps writing letters to his family once a week. 约翰坚持每周给家里写一封信。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00201.jpeg"/></div>
hall@［hɔ:l］@n. 门厅；礼堂，会堂；办公大楼</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：在大厅（hall）里办舞会（ball）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are three dining halls in our school. 我们学校有三个食堂。</p>
major@［ˈmeidʒə(r)］@adj. 较大的；主要的 n. 专业；（陆军）少校 v. 主修，专攻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My major is English. 我的专业是英语。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> majority（n. 多数，大半）</p>
legend@［ˈledʒənd］@n. 传说；传奇人物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to listen to the legend of Robin Hood. 我想听罗宾汉的传奇故事。</p>
guard@［ga:d］@n. 警戒，警备；警卫员，看守 v. 守卫，保卫；防止，防范</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：私家花园（garden）没有看守（guard）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are three soldiers on guard at the gate of the movie star's villa. 那位电影明星的别墅门口有三名卫兵守护。</p>
fine@［fain］@adj. 健康的，舒适的；极好的，优秀的；纤细的，细小的；精制的，高质量的；颗粒微小的 adv. 很好，妙 v. 处…以罚金 n. 罚金，罚款</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：旅游要选好（fine）路线（line）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is a fine day today. 今天天气真不错。</p>
agent@［ˈeidʒənt］@n. 代理人，代理商，经纪人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom is an agent in the company. 汤姆是公司的代理人。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> agency（n. 代理，代理处）</p>
gallery@［ˈgæləri］@n. 画廊，美术馆；（大厅的）楼座；廊台，走廊</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：gall（看作hall, 大厅）+ery（表地点的名词后缀）→陈列美术品的大厅→画廊</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is an art gallery in the center of the city. 市中心有一家美术馆。</p>
regard@［riˈga:d］@v. 把…看作，认为；考虑；注视，打量；注意；尊敬，尊重</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 尊敬，尊重；［pl.］ 致意，问候；考虑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> regard...as... 把…当做…；in/with regard to 关于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old professor is generally regarded as one of the best scientists in the country. 那位年迈的教授被公认为是这个国家最优秀的科学家之一。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">regard, consider</p>   <p class="bodytext">regard和consider都有“把…看作”的意思。regard指基于表面的观察，一般与as连用，如：I regard picking pocket as a crime. 我认为扒窃是一种犯罪。而consider指经过深思熟虑或亲身经历得出结论，如：I consider him to be my best friend. 我把他视为我最好的朋友。</p></div>
spirit@［ˈspirit］@n. 精神；灵魂，幽灵；勇气，气概；［pl.］ 情绪，心情；酒精，烈酒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary has a strong independent spirit. 玛丽的独立性很强。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> spiritual（adj. 精神的；心灵的）；spirited（adj. 精神饱满的；英勇的）</p>
