front@［frʌnt］@n. 前面，正面；前线，战线 adj. 前面的，在前面的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The lady standing in front of me is beautiful and elegant. 站在我前面的女士漂亮而优雅。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00202.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在考试中常会遇到以下两个短语，注意区别：in front of 表示在某物体的前面，如：He stands in front of the car. 他站在车前。in the front of 指在某物体内部的前面，如：He sits in the front of the car. 他坐在车的前座。</p></div>
sound@［saʊnd］@n. 声音，声响 v. （使）发声，（使）发出响声；测量…的深度，探测；听起来，似乎 adj. 正确的，合理的，有根据的；扎实的，精湛的；健全的，完好的，健康的；酣睡的 adv. 充分地，酣畅地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My physics teacher said that light travels faster than sound. 我的物理老师说光的传播速度比声音快。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> soundly（adv. 不错地；明智地；健全地）</p>
wild@［waild］@adj. 野生的，未驯化的；荒凉的，荒芜的；狂热的，疯狂的；野蛮的，未开化的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mandy was completely wild in high school. 曼迪在高中很野蛮。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> wildness（n. 野生；野蛮）；wilderness（n. 未开垦的荒地，荒漠）</p>
confident@［ˈkɒnfidənt］@adj. 确信的，肯定的；有信心的，自信的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be confident in 对…有信心</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> After the severe discussion, he felt at ease and was confident about the future. 激烈讨论之后，他感到如释重负，对未来也充满了信心。</p>
snake@［sneik］@n. 蛇 v. 蜿蜒；弯弯曲曲地行进</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：蛇（snake）可不喜欢吃点心（snack）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I screamed at the sight of the snake. 我一看到蛇就尖叫起来。</p>
till@［til］@prep. / conj. 直到（…为止）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> till now 到现在为止，迄今</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The shop's open till 9 p.m. on Fridays. 这家店周五营业到晚上9点。</p>
consider@［kənˈsidə(r)］@v. 考虑，细想；认为，把…看作；关心，照顾</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I consider it a great honor to be invited to the party. 应邀参加此次聚会，我深感荣幸。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">consider后可以直接接动名词，表示“考虑做…”，这是考试中的一个考点。如：I'm considering buying a new house. 我正考虑买一栋新房子。</p></div>
foreign@［ˈfɒrən］@adj. 外国的，外国产的；对外的，涉外的；外来的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy wants to make more foreign friends. 男孩想交更多外国朋友。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> foreigner（n. 外国人）</p>
homeland@［ˈhəʊmlænd］@n. 祖国，家乡</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Denny started to miss his homeland as soon as he got to England. 丹尼一到英国就开始想念家乡了。</p>
myself@［maiˈself］@pron. 我自己；我亲自，我本人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：my（我的）+self（自己）→我自己</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span>“I will buy the flowers myself”, said Clarrisa. 克拉丽莎说：“我要自己去买花。”</p>
passenger@［ˈpæsindʒə(r)］@n. 乘客，旅客</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These passengers cannot leave the airport because of the storm. 由于暴风雨的缘故，这些旅客无法离开机场。</p>
clean@［kli:n］@adj. 清洁的，干净的；爱清洁的；清白的，公正的；干净利落的 adv. 完全地，全部地 v. 打扫，把…弄干净</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> clean up 整理，打扫干净</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—How clean the bedroom is!</p> <p class="bodytext">—Yes, I am sure that someone ______ it. （2009 年 武汉）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. cleans</p> <p class="bodytext">B. cleaned</p> <p class="bodytext">C. has cleaned</p> <p class="bodytext">D. had cleaned</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—卧室真干净啊！</p> <p class="bodytext4">—是的，肯定是有人打扫过了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>clean作动词时表示“打扫”，“打扫房间”是clean the room，本题强调过去某一件事情的发生对现在造成的影响，因此应使用现在完成时，故选C。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00203.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">clean, tidy</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者意思相近，但有细微区别。clean强调干净，而tidy除了干净，还有整洁之意。</p></div>
situation@［ˌsitʃuˈeiʃn］@n. 形势，局面，处境；环境，状况；位置，地点，场所；职位，职务</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People usually use their nicknames in that kind of situation. 在那种情况下，人们通常会使用他们的昵称。</p>
look@［lʊk］@v. 看，注视；显得，看上去；朝着，面向</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 看，（一）瞥；脸色，表情；容貌，样子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：看（look）书（book）百遍，其义自现</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> look out 留神，当心；look at 看，观看；look after 照看；look for 寻找；look forward to 盼望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Look at the blackboard. 看黑板。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">look, see</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“看”的意思。look强调看的动作，是不及物动词，与介词at搭配，如：Look at the bird. 看那只鸟。而see强调看的结果，可以直接接名词，如：I can see the bird. 我能看到那只鸟。</p></div>
baseball@［ˈbeisbɔ:l］@n. 棒球</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually play baseball in my free time. 我闲的时候经常打棒球。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">“打棒球”用英语说就是play baseball，要注意的是球类名词前不加任何冠词，如：play football 踢足球，play basketball 打篮球。</p></div>
pleasant@［ˈpleznt］@adj. 舒适的；令人愉快的；讨人喜欢的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：pleas（看作please，令人高兴）+ant（形容词后缀）→令人愉快的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's pleasant to sit down after standing for hours. 站了几个小时后能坐下来真是舒服。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext5">pleasant, pleased, pleasure</p>   <p class="bodytext">pleasant, pleased, pleasure 几个形近词的区别：</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00204.jpeg"/></div></div>
over@［ˈəʊvə(r)］@prep. 在…上方，在…上面；越过，从一侧到另一侧；高于，超过；在…期间；遍及 adv. 落下，倒下，翻转；从一侧到另一侧；全部；再，又；过于，太 adj. 上面的；结束的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> all over 浑身；全部；over and over again 一遍一遍地；take over 接管；look over 从上面看过去；检查；think over 反复考虑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The plane is flying over the city. 飞机正飞过城市上空。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">above, over</p>   <p class="bodytext">above表示在某物的上方，强调高于某一点或某一物体，但不一定是垂直的上方，如：a light above the table 桌子上方的一盏灯；此外，above还可以表示温度等。over表示垂直的上方或正上方，且两个物体之间有距离，如：a bridge over the river 河上的一座桥。</p></div>
skin@［skin］@n. 皮（肤）；兽皮，毛皮；外皮，外壳</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> In James Cameron's Avatar, the Navi have blue skin. 在詹姆斯·卡梅隆的电影《阿凡达》里，纳威人的皮肤是蓝色的。</p>
become@［biˈkʌm］@v. ［became-become］ 变成，成为；开始变得</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I believe our lives will become better and better. 我相信我们的生活会变得越来越好。</p>
surface@［ˈsɜ:fis］@n. 表面，面；外表，外观 v. 浮出水面；浮现，显露</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：sur（在…上）+face（脸，面容）→在脸上，在表面上→表面</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Dead leaves floated on the surface of the water. 落叶在水面上漂浮。</p>
mountain@［ˈmaʊntən］@n. 山；［pl.］ 山脉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We are going to climb the mountain next week. 我们打算下周去爬山。</p>
black@［blæk］@adj. 黑色的；黑暗的；黑人的；（咖啡或茶）不加奶的；黯淡的，毫无希望的</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. （使）变黑 n. 黑色；黑人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like black hats. 我喜欢黑色的帽子。</p>
hour@［ˈaʊə(r)］@n. 小时，钟点；时间，时刻；［pl.］ 课时，（工作或学习等的）固定时间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's about two hours' walk from here to my school. 从这儿到我的学校步行要两小时。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在听力中要注意hour中的h不发音，并且前面的冠词用an而不是a。</p></div>
found@［faʊnd］@v. 创立，创办，创建</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The company was founded at the beginning of this year. 这家公司是今年年初创立的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> foundation（n. 地基；基础）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">考生在见到found这个词时不要误以为是find的过去式或过去分词，found可以作动词“创立”讲，它有自己的过去式和过去分词founded。</p></div>
often@［ˈɒfn］@adv. 常常，经常</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：of+ten（十）→十有八九→经常</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— John sings so well. Has he ever been trained?</p> <p class="bodytext">— No. He learns all by himself. He ______ goes to any training class. （2009年 常州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. usually</p> <p class="bodytext">B. often</p> <p class="bodytext">C. never</p> <p class="bodytext">D. even</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 约翰唱得太棒了，他受过训练吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 没有，他完全是自学的。没有上过任何培训课程。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是频度副词的用法。usually意为“经常”；often意为“常常”，稍次于usually；never意为“从未”；even是程度副词，意为“甚至”。因此选C。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">always, usually, often, seldom, never这几个词都是频度副词，都表示事情发生的几率，且频度是由高到低的。always意为“总是”，表示事情发生的频率极高；usually意为“通常”，表明事情发生的次数相对比较多；often意为“经常”，稍稍比usually少一些，但也是隔三差五地出现；seldom意为“很少”，频率相对就低多了；而never指根本没有发生过，几率是零。</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00205.jpeg"/></div></div>
trust@［trʌst］@n. 信任，信赖；受托（物） v. 信任，信赖；希望，想；确信；托付；对…放心</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> At first, there was a lack of trust between them. 最开始时，他们之间缺乏信任。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> trusty（adj. 可信赖的，可靠的）</p>
past@［pa:st］@adj. 以前的，过去的；结束了的，不复存在的 prep. 晚于，在…之后 n. 昔日，往事 adv. 穿过；（时间）过去</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in the past 在过去</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually get up at half past six in the morning. 我通常早上六点半起床。</p>
beyond@［biˈjɒnd］@prep. 在（向）…的那边；远于；迟于；超出，非…所及</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 在更远处，往更远处；再往后</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：香港著名乐队Beyond</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> beyond doubt 毋庸置疑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The path continues beyond the village up into the hills. 这条小径一直延伸到村外的小山上。</p>
kangaroo@［ˌkæŋgəˈru:］@n. 袋鼠</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The kangaroo is an animal unique to Australia. 袋鼠是澳大利亚特有的动物。</p>
food@［fu:d］@n. 食物，食品</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：好（good）食品（food）有益健康</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like Chinese food better than western food. 比起西餐，我更加喜欢中餐。</p>
cover@［ˈkʌvə(r)］@v. 盖，覆盖；范围为，占；行，行过（一段路）；包括；报道；掩护 n. 盖子；套子；封面；掩蔽（物），掩护（物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little girl was so shy that she covered her face with her hands. 小女孩太害羞了，她用手遮住了脸。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> covering（n. 掩盖物）</p>
square@［skweə(r)］@adj. 正方形的；平方的；直角的 n. 正方形；平方；广场 v. 求平方；求…的面积；（使）相符，（使）一致；使（比分）打平；使平直；结清；使成方形</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tian'anmen Square is one of the largest squares in the world. 天安门广场是世界上最大的广场之一。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> squarely（adv. 坚固地，坚实地）</p>
girl@［gɜ:l］@n. 姑娘，女孩；女儿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little girl is so smart that she can recite nearly 300 poems. 这个小女孩太聪明了，她可以背诵将近300首诗。</p>
worst@［wɜ:st］@adv. / adj. 最坏（的），最差（的），最糟（的）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have experienced the worst situation. 我经历过最糟的境遇。</p>
someone@［ˈsʌmwʌn］@pron. 有人，某人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is someone at the door. 门口有个人。</p>
opportunity@［ˌɒpəˈtju:nəti］@n. 机会，良机</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I didn't have an opportunity to say sorry to Harry. 我没有机会向哈里道歉。</p>
force@［fɔ:s］@n. ［pl.］ 军队，兵力；暴力，武力；力，力气；影响力，效力</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 强迫，迫使；用力推动，用力打开</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> come into force 生效，实行；put in/into force 施行，实施；by force 用暴力，强迫地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I had to force myself to get up early this morning. 今天早上我不得不强迫自己早起。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">force, energy</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“力”的意思，但是用法不同。force指的是兵力、武力以及力气，而energy指的是精力或能量。</p></div>
weather@［ˈweðə(r)］@n. 天气，气候，气象</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> What's the weather like today? 今天的天气怎么样？</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">weather的发音和whether完全一致，拼写也极为相似，注意不要混淆。</p></div>
police@［pəˈli:s］@n. 警方，警察；治安</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The police tried to find out the real thief. 警方努力找出真正的盗贼。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> policeman（n. 警察）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">police是单复数同形的单词。当它作单数时，意思是“警方”，谓语动词用单数；作复数时，意思是“警察们”，谓语动词用复数。</p></div>
kind@［kaind］@n. 种类 adj. 亲切的，和蔼的，仁慈的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：国王（king）亲切（kind）友好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are many kinds of apples in the market. 市场上有许多种苹果。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00162.jpeg"/></div>
feed@［fi:d］@v. ［fed-fed］ 喂（养），为…提供食物；吃，以…为食 n. 饲料</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：播种就是给土地喂（feed）种子（seed）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> feed on 以…为食；be fed up （with...）（对…）厌倦，受够了</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to study how to feed the pets and how to keep them clean. 我不得不学习怎样喂养宠物，以及怎样使它们保持清洁。</p>
railway@［ˈreilwei］@n. 铁道，铁路</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：rail（铁轨，横栏）+way（路）→铁道</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My home is very close to a railway station so it is very noisy. 我家离火车站很近，所以非常吵。</p>
headache@［ˈhedeik］@n. 头痛；令人头痛的人（或事物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：head（头）+ache（痛）→头痛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I had a bad headache this morning. 今天早晨我的头很痛。</p>  <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00206.jpeg"/></div>
search@［sɜ:tʃ］@n. / v. 搜索，寻找；搜查</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：搜索网页就用这个词</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> search out 找出；in search of... 搜寻…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary went into the kitchen in search of something to drink. 玛丽走进厨房找喝的东西。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">search, search for</p>   <p class="bodytext">search后面直接跟sth.时，意思是“搜寻某物”，强调的是搜寻的过程，如：He searched every corner in the house. 他搜寻了这个房间的各个角落。search 后直接跟sb.时，意思是“搜某人的身”，如：Police searched everyone present. 警察搜了在场每个人的身。而search for后面跟sb.或sth.，表示搜寻是为了找到某人或某物，强调寻找的目的，如：They searched for the lost child. 他们搜寻失踪的孩子。</p></div>
chopsticks@［ˈtʃɒpstiks］@n. 筷子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：chop（砍）+sticks（棍）→砍棍子，做筷子→筷子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Peter has the hobby of collecting chopsticks. 彼得有收集筷子的爱好。</p>
we@［wi］@pron. 我们</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We have been good friends for almost ten years. 我们是近十年的好友。</p>
six@［siks］@num. 六，六个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My little nephew is only six years old. 我的小侄子只有六岁。</p>
picnic@［ˈpiknik］@n. 野餐 v. ［picnicked-picnicked, picnicking］ 去野餐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We will go on a picnic this weekend. 这个周末我们要去野餐。</p>
nearby@［ˌniəˈbai］@adj. 附近的 adv. 在附近</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：near（在近旁）+by（在附近）→附近的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jack's father lived in a nearby apartment. 杰克的爸爸住在附近的公寓。</p>
hers@［hɜ:z］@pron. 她的（所有物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This pen isn't mine; it's hers. 这支钢笔不是我的，而是她的。</p>
with@［wið］@pron. 和…一起，跟，同；具有，带有；用，以，藉；对…，关于；随着</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like hot milk with sugar and chocolate. 我喜欢加糖和巧克力的热牛奶。</p>
shut@［ʃʌt］@v. ［shut-shut, shutting］ 关闭，关上；打烊</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> shut down 关闭，倒闭；shut off 关掉，切断；shut up 住口</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span>“Shut up! ” the man shouted rudely.“闭嘴！”那个人粗鲁地喊道。</p>
marry@［ˈmæri］@v. 娶，嫁，和…结婚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：结婚（marry）是令人幸福快乐的（merry）事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> get married 结婚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom married Mary last October. 去年十月汤姆娶了玛丽。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">marry是及物动词，直接接宾语，即marry sb.。另外，“和…结婚”还可以表达为 get married to sb.，考生注意此处介词用的是to，而不是with，如：Marry got married to John last year. 玛丽去年和约翰结婚了。</p></div>
native@［ˈneitiv］@adj. 出生地的；当地（人）的 n. 土生土长者，本国人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This school wants to have some native English teachers. 这个学校想要一些以英文为母语的英语老师。</p>
original@［əˈridʒənl］@adj. 最初的，原始的；新颖的，有创意的；原创性的 n. 原件</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：origin（起源）+al（形容词后缀）→原始的，最初的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> What do you think of the original music of the movie? 你觉得这部电影的原声音乐怎么样？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> originality（n. 创意，新奇）；originally（adv. 最初）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">original, primary</p>   <p class="bodytext">original和primary都有“最初的”之意，差别在于：original强调最初的、原始的，如：original work 原作；primary指的是初步的、初级的，如：primary school 小学。</p></div>
purse@［pɜ:s］@n. 钱包；女用小包</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My purse was stolen when I was on the bus. 在公交车上时，我的钱包被偷了。</p>
are@［a:r］@v. 存在，是（be动词的复数形式）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We are students from the same school. 我们是同一所学校的学生。</p>
discussion@［diˈskʌʃn］@n. 讨论，谈论</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Last week we held a discussion on what we should do for our school. 我们上周针对应该为学校做些什么进行了讨论。</p>
bow@［bəʊ］@ n. 弓，弓形物；蝴蝶结</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［baʊ］</span> n. / v. 鞠躬，低头</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many young people don't know how to bow. 许多年轻人不知道如何鞠躬。</p>
ninety@［ˈnainti］@num. 九十，九十个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old lady of ninety years showed her beauty and calmness. 那个90岁高龄的老太太显现出她的美丽和安详。</p>
sing@［siŋ］@v. ［sang-sung］ 唱（歌），演唱；鸡鸣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like singing very much. 我非常喜欢唱歌。</p>
mix@［miks］@v. 使混合，配制；相混，搞混 n. 混合，搅和</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> mix up 弄乱；混淆</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Everyone knows that oil can't mix with water. 人人都知道，油和水不能相溶。</p>
postman@［ˈpəʊstmən］@n. 邮递员</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：post（邮递）+man（人）→做邮递工作的人→邮递员</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This morning a postman brought me a large package. 今天早上，邮递员给我送来一个大包裹。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00207.jpeg"/></div>
smell@［smel］@n. 气味；臭味；嗅觉 v. ［smelt-smelt］ 散发（或有）…的气味；嗅，闻到；察觉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> smell of 有…的味道</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Bill drank so much that I could smell alcohol on his breath. 比尔喝了太多酒，我都能从他的呼吸中闻到酒味。</p>
live@［liv］@v. 居住；活，生活；（回忆等）留存，难忘</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［laiv］</span> adj. 活的，充满活力的；现场直播的，现场演出的 adv. 以现场直播（或表演）的方式</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> lead/live a...life 过着…的生活；live on... 以…为食；live off 靠…生活</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Linda lives two miles away from my house. 琳达家离我家有2英里。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> lively （adj. 活泼的；栩栩如生的）</p>
Paris@［ˈpæris］@n. 巴黎</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are so many people who want to have a trip to Paris. 有太多人想去巴黎游玩。</p>
sauce@［sɔ:s］@n. 沙司；调味汁，酱汁；佐料</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to choose the cake with chocolate sauce. 我想选带有巧克力酱的蛋糕。</p>
deaf@［def］@adj. 聋的；不愿听的，装聋的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“大夫”→聋了找大夫→聋的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Li Ming usually turns a deaf ear to his mother's talk. 李明经常把妈妈说的话当做耳旁风。</p>
thought@［θɔ:t］@n. 想法，见解；思考，思维；关心，注意；思想，思潮</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I've just had a thought on how to solve this problem. 我刚刚想出解决这个问题的方法。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00208.jpeg"/></div>
sir@［sɜ:(r)］@n. 先生；<span class="yinbiao1">［S-］</span> 爵士</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You're welcome, sir. Have a nice day!不用客气，先生，祝您愉快！// I was told that Sir William would come. 我听说威廉爵士会来。</p>
fetch@［fetʃ］@v. （去）拿来；请来，叫来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：和catch（v. 抓住）一起记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She went upstairs to fetch some towels. 她上楼去拿了几条毛巾。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00209.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">fetch, take</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者词义相近，注意区别。fetch指从说话的地方出发到某地把某物取回来，如：Mary has fetched her children from school. 玛丽把孩子们从学校接了回来。take是把某物从说话的地方带走，如：Please take your umbrella. 请带上你的伞。</p></div>
those@［ðəʊz］@pron. 那些</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Those watches are broken. 那些手表坏了。</p>
dry@［drai］@adj. 干（燥）的，干旱的；口渴的 v. 使干，使脱水</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You need to drink a lot of water in dry weather. 天气干燥时你要多喝水。</p>
save@［seiv］@v. 救助，搭救，拯救；储蓄；贮存，保存 prep. 除…之外</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—Dear, why not ______ money by yourself for your 8th birthday present?</p> <p class="bodytext">—Good idea. I'll not let a pence go to waste. （2006年 德州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. save</p> <p class="bodytext">B. spend</p> <p class="bodytext">C. keep</p> <p class="bodytext">D. take</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—亲爱的，你为什么不攒钱为自己买8岁的生日礼物呢？</p> <p class="bodytext4">—好主意，我不会再浪费一便士了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查save money这一固定搭配，意思是“攒钱”。spend可以和表示“钱”的词连用，意思是“花钱”，但根据答语可知，spend不符合题意。keep money的意思是“留下钱”，与题意不符。take常指花费时间，因此本题选A。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> saver（n. 拯救者；储蓄者）；savings（n. 储蓄，存款）</p>
calculator@［ˈkælkjuleitə(r)］@n. 计算器</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My calculator doesn't work. 我的计算器坏了。</p>
baby@［ˈbeibi］@n. 婴儿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jane had a baby last year. 简去年生了个孩子。</p>
October@［ɒkˈtəʊbə(r)］@n. 十月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't know whose birthday is in October. 我不知道谁的生日在十月。</p>
zebra@［ˈzｉ:brə］@n. 斑马</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Zebras can be seen in the zoo. 人们在动物园里可以看到斑马。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00210.jpeg"/></div>
that@［ðæt］@adj. / pron. 那，那个 conj./adv. 那样，那么</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> That's all right. 没关系。so/such...that... 如此…以至于…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I wish you wouldn't say things like that. 我希望你没有那么说。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">so...that...表示“如此…以至于…”，跟too...to...的结构有相似点，但注意too...to...句型是用肯定句表达否定的意思，对比一下：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I was so tired that I couldn't finish the work. 我太累了，以至于无法完成工作。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I was too tired to finish the work. 我太累了，以至于无法完成工作。</p></div>
forty@［ˈfɔ:ti］@num. 四十</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My uncle is forty years old this year. 我叔叔今年40岁了。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">考生在书写该词时一定不要写成fourty，注意没有字母u。</p></div>
surprise@［səˈpraiz］@n. 惊奇，诧异；令人惊奇（或意想不到）的事物</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 使诧异，使惊奇；突然袭击，奇袭</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It was a pleasant surprise to learn of his marriage. 得知他结婚了，我感到很惊喜。// It surprises me that you've failed the final exam. 你期末考试不及格让我很吃惊。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> surprised（adj. 感到惊讶的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00211.jpeg"/></div>
mother@［ˈmʌðə(r)］@n. 母亲，妈妈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Susan said her mother passed away a few years ago. 苏珊说她母亲几年前就去世了。</p>
soft@［sɒft］@adj. 柔软的，细嫩的，光滑的；（声音）轻的，轻柔的；（颜色、光线等）柔和的；温和的，温柔的；不含酒精的；柔弱的，娇嫩的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like to listen to soft music to help me get to sleep. 我喜欢听轻音乐来帮我入睡。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> soften（v. 使…变柔软）；softness（n. 柔和，柔软）</p>
computer@［kəmˈpju:tə(r)］@n. 计算机，电脑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I got a new computer last year from my father as my birthday present. 去年我得到了爸爸送给我作为生日礼物的新电脑。</p>
criticize@［ˈkritisaiz］@v. 批评；评论；非难</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The police have been criticized for not taking action quickly. 警方因未迅速采取行动而受到了批评。</p>
court@［kɔ:t］@n. 法庭，法院；宫廷，朝廷；球场 v. 献殷勤；追求，求爱；招致，导致</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> go to court 上法庭</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The defendant of the case will appear in court tomorrow. 明天，这起案件的被告将会出庭。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> courtship（n. 求爱；求爱期）</p>
together@［təˈgeðə(r)］@adv. 在一起，共同；一致地，协调地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> gather together 集合在一起；get together 聚集</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is difficult for these five sisters to get together. 五姐妹想聚在一起很困难。</p>
long@［lɒŋ］@adj. 长的；长期的 v. 渴望，热望 adv. 长期地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The girl was slender and had long dark hair. 女孩很苗条，还留着长长的黑发。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00212.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在考试中，常会出现含有long的两个短语，考生要注意区分。before long意思是“不久以后”，而long before指的是“很久以前”。</p></div>
strange@［streindʒ］@adj. 奇怪的，奇异的；陌生的，生疏的；外地的，异乡的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> With so many strange faces around him, my brother started to cry. 看到周围有那么多陌生的面孔，我弟弟哭了起来。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> stranger（n. 陌生人）</p>
decide@［diˈsaid］@v. 决定，对…作出抉择；使下决心</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The writer decided to donate some money to the poor students. 这位作家决定为贫困学生捐一些钱。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> decision（n. 决定；决心）</p>
row@［rəʊ］@n. （一）排，（一）行；划船 v. 划船，荡桨</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［rａʊ］</span> n. / v. 争吵；斥责</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Students stand hand in hand in a row. 学生们手牵手站成一排。// The new couple are always rowing with each other. 这对年轻夫妇经常争吵。</p>
as@［əz; æz］@adv. 同样，一样地 prep. 当做，作为；像，如同</p> <p class="bodytext1">conj. 当…时，随着；以…的方式，像…一样；因为，由于；尽管，虽然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> as if/though 好像；as a matter of fact 事实上，实际上；as to/for 关于，至于；as well 也，又，同样；so as to 以便；so/as long as 既然，这样；as a result 因此</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> John left the office as quickly as possible. 约翰尽快离开了办公室。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">as, like</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“像”的意思，但是用法不同。</p>   <p class="bodytext">（1）as作连词，引导比较状语从句和方式状语从句，而like作介词。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">Betty is a good dancer, as her mother used to be. 贝蒂是一位优秀的舞蹈家，和她妈妈过去一样。</p>   <p class="bodytext">The computer can't work like man. 计算机不能像人一样工作。</p>   <p class="bodytext">（2）as可对同类事物进行比较，而like只是单纯表示比较，而且通常不是同类事物之间的比较。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">This tree is as high as that one. 这棵树和那棵一样高。</p>   <p class="bodytext">The black cat looks like a hat. 这只黑猫看上去像个帽子。</p></div>
large@［la:dʒ］@adj. 大的；（数量）多的，众多的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The T-shirt is quite large for Tom. 这件T恤汤姆穿太大了。</p>
wrong@［rɒŋ］@adj. 错误的，不正确的；不道德的，不正当的，不合法的 n. 错误；坏事；不公正的行为，冤屈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> go wrong 走错路；发生故障</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The answer that you offered is wrong. 你提供的答案是错误的。</p>
film@［film］@n. 影片，电影；胶片，胶卷；薄层，薄膜 v. 拍摄电影</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our class will see a film at Rainbow Theatre tomorrow. 我们班明天要去彩虹剧院看电影。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> filmy（adj. 薄得几乎透明的）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">film, movie</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都用来指“电影”：film是英式英语，movie是美式英语。</p></div>
yours@［jɔ:z］@pron. 你（们）的（所有物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The umbrella in the corner is yours. 角落里的那把伞是你的。</p>
safety@［ˈseifti］@n. 安全，保险；安全设备，保险装置；安全场所</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> In the zoo, we were able to watch the tiger in complete safety. 在动物园，我们可以非常安全地观看老虎。</p>
lot@［lɒt］@n. 许多，大量；签，抽签；一块地，场地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are a lot of teachers in our school. 我们学校有很多教师。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">lot常用在短语a lot of或lots of中，其后既可以接可数名词复数，也可以接不可数名词。</p></div>
exhibition@［ˌeksiˈbiʃn］@n. 展览（会）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have never seen the Picasso exhibition. 我从来没看过毕加索的画展。</p>
awful@［ˈɔ:fl］@adj. 极坏的；糟糕的，令人不快的；可怕的；非常的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：aw（看作awe，敬畏）+ful→令人敬畏的→可怕的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Last winter was awful. 去年冬天的天气非常糟糕。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> awfully（adv. 非常，很）</p>
mean@［mi:n］@v. ［meant-meant］ 表示…的意思；意欲，打算；意指，意味着</p> <p class="bodytext1">adj. 卑鄙的，卑贱的；吝啬的；恶意的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> mean a lot / nothing （to...） （对…）很重要/根本不重要</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> What does that sentence mean? 那个句子是什么意思？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> meaning（n. 意义）</p>
sign@［sain］@n. 标志，符号；招牌；征兆，迹象 v. 签（名）；签署</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：叹息（sigh）是失望的迹象（sign）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a sign saying smoking is not allowed. 此处有禁止吸烟的标志。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext5">mark, sign, signal, symbol</p>   <p class="bodytext">这四个词的含义相似，但有区别。mark一般指眼睛可以直接看到的“记号”或“标记”；sign多指不可见的“迹象”或“征兆”；signal指为某一目的而有意发出的信号；symbol是指象征意义的标志。</p></div>
minute@［ˈminit］@n. 分，分钟；一会儿，片刻；此时此刻，立刻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in a minute 立刻，马上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'll leave the classroom in a minute. 我马上就离开教室。</p>
require@［riˈkwaiə(r)］@v. 需要；要求，命令；规定</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This work requires patience and hard working. 这项工作需要耐心和勤奋。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> required（adj. 必需的）；requirement（n. 要求，需要；命令）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext7">require, request, need, demand</p>   <p class="bodytext">require比较正式，指要求遵守规则等；request是比较客气地表达需求；need比较口语化；demand意为“命令”，语气通常比较强硬。</p></div>
unless@［ənˈles］@conj. 除非，如果不</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Bill won't make any progress ______ he studies harder than before. （2008年 上海）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. if</p> <p class="bodytext">B. when</p> <p class="bodytext">C. because</p> <p class="bodytext">D. unless</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>比尔如果不比之前更加刻苦的话，他就不会取得任何进步。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>unless意为“除非，如果不”，本身就表示否定，相当于if not，引导条件状语从句时常常与否定形式搭配，因此本题根据句意衔接选择D项。</p>
allow@［əˈlaʊ］@v. 允许，准许，容许；允许…进入（或停留）；同意给；承认</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：降低（low）门槛，允许（allow）进入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—Look at the sign on the right.</p> <p class="bodytext">—Oh, smoking ______ here. （2009年 河南）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. doesn't allow</p> <p class="bodytext">B. isn't allowed</p> <p class="bodytext">C. didn't allow</p> <p class="bodytext">D. wasn't allowed</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—看右边的标牌。</p> <p class="bodytext4">—哦，此处禁止吸烟。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查时态和语态问题。根据语境，“禁止吸烟”其实就是“吸烟是不被允许的”，可知本题应该是一般现在时的被动语态。故选B。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> allowable（adj. 允许的；承认的）</p>
discover@［disˈkʌvə(r)］@v. 发现，发觉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：dis（去掉）+cover（盖子）→揭掉盖子，一探究竟→发现</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The scientists discovered some new stars. 科学家发现了一些新的星星。</p>
Australia@［ɒˈstreiliə］@n. 澳大利亚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lucy was born in Sydney, Australia. 露西出生在澳大利亚的悉尼。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> Australian（n. 澳大利亚人 adj. 澳大利亚的）</p>
stage@［steidʒ］@n. 舞台，后台；平台，高台；楼层，楼架</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The children are at different stages of development. 孩子们正处于不同的发展阶段。</p>
player@［ˈpleiə(r)］@n. 选手，队员；做游戏的人；演员；演奏者；播放器</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：play（玩，比赛）+er（表人的后缀）→参加比赛的人→队员，选手</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The football players tried their best to win the game. 足球运动员尽了最大的努力赢取比赛。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00213.jpeg"/></div>
student@［ˈstju:dnt］@n. 学生，学者，大学生；研究生</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are fifty students in our class. 我们班有50名学生。</p>
popularity@［ˌpɒpjuˈlærəti］@n. 普及；流行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：popular（流行的）+ity（抽象名词后缀）→流行；普及</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The movie Harry Potter has enjoyed popularity recently. 近来，电影《哈利·波特》深受人们喜爱。</p>
pay@［pei］@v. 付钱，支付，交纳 n. 工资，薪金</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“赔”→赔钱→付钱，支付</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> pay for 为…付款；pay back 偿还（借款）；报复；pay up 全部付清；pay attention to 注意；pay a visit 访问</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to pay for the expense of the medical care. 我不得不支付医疗保健费。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">pay作名词时，意思是“薪金，报酬”，如：The workers ask for a higher pay. 工人们要求更高的工资。pay在多数情况下作动词，意为“付钱，支付”，后面可以跟人，也可以跟钱，还可以接双宾语，如：I paid one hundred dollars to the man. 我付给那个人100美元。</p></div>
toast@［təʊst］@n. 烤面包，吐司；祝酒，祝酒词 v. 烘，烤；敬酒，为…干杯</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to choose toast as my breakfast. 我想选择吐司作早餐。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> toaster（n. 烤面包片机）</p>
beach@［bi:tʃ］@n. 海滩，沙滩</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm going to the beach for a holiday this summer. 我打算今年夏天去海滩度假。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00214.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">beach, bank</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者的区别主要在于：beach指的是海滩，而bank主要指沙滩或河岸。</p></div>
retire@［riˈtaiə(r)］@v. 退休，退役；退下，退出；退却，撤退；就寝</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：re（又，再）+tire（疲劳）→总是感到疲劳，该退休了→退休</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My father retired at the age of 60. 我父亲60岁时退休了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> retired（adj. 退休的）；retirement（n. 退休）</p>
believe@［biˈli:v］@v. 相信；认为</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：《我的野蛮女友》的主题歌是 I Believe</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> believe in 信仰；相信；believe it or not 信不信由你</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I believe your parents will be proud of you. 我相信你的父母会以你为荣。</p>
stick@［stik］@n. 棍，棒，手杖 v. ［stuck-stuck］ 刺，戳，插；粘贴，粘住，钉住；被粘住，被钉住，卡住；留下，长久保留</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man stuck to his own opinion and no one else could change it. 这位老人固执己见，没有人能改变这一点。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> sticky 〔adj. 黏的，有黏性的；（天气）湿热的〕</p>
chore@［tʃɔ:(r)］@n. 家庭杂务；困难的工作；令人厌烦的工作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to do some chores, such as cleaning the kitchen table. 我需要做一些家务活，例如清理厨房的餐桌。</p>
realistic@［ˌri:əˈlistik］@adj. 现实的；现实主义的；逼真的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：real（真的）+ist+ic（形容词后缀）→现实的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mother told me to be realistic. 母亲告诉我要现实一些。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> unrealistic（adj. 不切实际的）</p>
hair@［ˈheə(r)］@n. 头发，毛发</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I used to have short hair when I was in middle school. 上中学的时候，我留短发。</p>
each@［i:tʃ］@pron. / adv. 各个，每个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> each other 互相，彼此</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The twin brothers didn't meet each other until now. 这对双胞胎兄弟直到现在才见面。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">each, every</p>   <p class="bodytext">each和every都有“每个”的意思，都用于单数可数名词前，但用法有区别。each是代词，而every是形容词；有each of的搭配，但不能说every of，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">（〇） Each of the team members was preparing for the game.每位队员都在为比赛做准备。</p>   <p class="bodytext">（✕） Every of the team members was preparing for the game.每位队员都在为比赛做准备。</p>   <p class="bodytext">另外，在意思上，each强调集体里的每个人或事物，而every强调整体，如：Every girl was there and each did her part. 所有女孩都在那里，每个人都做了自己的工作。</p></div>
fork@［fɔ:k］@n. 叉，餐叉；耙；分叉，岔口</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：f+ork（看作pork, 猪肉）→用叉子叉猪肉→叉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't think it's convenient to eat food with a fork and knife. 我认为吃饭用刀叉不方便。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00215.jpeg"/></div>
wheat@［wi:t］@n. 小麦；淡黄色；朴实的人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：wh（o）+eat→谁吃？→人人都要吃小麦→小麦</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Some people are allergic to wheat. 一些人对小麦过敏。</p>
shame@［ʃeim］@n. 羞耻，羞愧；可耻的人（或事物）；遗憾的事，可惜 v. 使蒙受羞辱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The fashionable girl was full of shame under the criticism of the public. 那个时髦的女孩在众人的指责下羞愧不已。</p>
lookout@［ˈlʊkaʊt］@n. 警戒，监视；瞭望台，监视哨；瞭望员，监视者；与个人有关的事情，任务</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We were instructed to keep a lookout for enemy aircraft. 我们接到命令监视敌机。</p>
prevent@［priˈvent］@v. 阻止，妨碍</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> prevent sb. from doing sth. 阻止某人做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We were prevented from entering the house. 我们不能进入这所房子。</p>
singular@［ˈsiŋgjələ(r)］@adj. 单数的；单一的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span>“Mouse”is the singular form of“mice”.“mouse”是“mice”的单数形式。</p>
land@［lænd］@n. 陆地，地面；土地，田地；国家，国土 v. （使）靠岸，（使）登陆；（使）降落</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The pilot landed the plane safely. 飞行员将飞机安全降落。</p>
seek@［si:k］@v. ［sought-sought］ 寻找，追求；征求（意见），请求（帮助）；试图，设法；探索</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：see（看）+k→更深入地看→寻找</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Susan calmed down and sought help from her neighbours. 苏珊平静下来，向邻居寻求帮助。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> seeker（n. 寻找者，探索者）</p>
introduce@［ˌintrəˈdju:s］@v. 介绍；引进，传入；提出（议案等）供讨论；采用</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> introduce...to... 把…介绍给…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to introduce myself to everyone. 我想向大家介绍一下自己。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> introduction（n. 介绍）</p>
lock@［lɒk］@v. 锁上；卡住 n. 锁；船闸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：可以和看（look）一起记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She locked her passport and cash in the drawer. 她将护照和现金锁在了抽屉里。</p>
return@［riˈtɜ:n］@v. 返回，回来；回复，回应；退回；回报 n. 返回，回来；偿还，归还；恢复；回报；收益，盈利；申报（表），（统计）报表；往返票 adj. 往返的，返回的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> return to 重新回到（地方、话题等）；return ticket 往返票</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Bob returned to America this spring. 鲍勃今年春天回美国了。// Farmers are trying to find ways to improve returns from their crops. 农民们正试着寻找方法来提高粮食收入。</p>
fan@［fæn］@n. 扇子；扇形物；狂热爱好者，迷 v. 煽动，激起</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are crowds of football fans waiting outside the stadium. 大群球迷在体育馆外等候。</p>
popular@［ˈpɒpjələ(r)］@adj. 流行的，通俗的，大众的；受欢迎的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be popular with 受…欢迎</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Swimming is very popular in summer. 在夏天，游泳非常流行。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> popularize（v. 普及）；popularization（n. 普及）</p>
aunt@［a:nt］@n. 姑姑，姨妈，伯母，婶婶，舅妈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm going to visit my aunt tomorrow. 我打算明天去看望我的姑姑。</p>
tiny@［ˈtaini］@adj. 极小的，微小的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I cannot imagine how such a tiny baby can grow up to be a big man. 我无法想象这么一个小不点如何能长这么高大。</p>
rest@［rest］@n. 剩余部分，其余的人（或物）；休息；停止，静止；撑架，支座 v. 休息，睡眠；放，靠；取决于；依靠，依赖；停留 adj. 其余的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> the rest of... 剩余的…；rest in/on... 取决于…，在于…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I always take rest for an hour after lunch. 我午餐后总会休息一个小时。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">the rest of 既可以修饰可数名词，也可以修饰不可数名词，但这一结构作主语时，谓语动词的单复数要与of后面的名词保持一致，如：The rest of my money is in my pocket. 我剩余的钱在口袋里。</p></div>
half@［ha:f］@adj. 一半的，半个的 n. 半，一半 adv. 一半</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I've only had this dog for half a month. 这只狗我才养了半个月。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">half of修饰主语时，如果接可数名词复数形式，则谓语动词用复数形式，如果接可数名词单数形式或不可数名词，则谓语动词用单数形式，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Half of the peaches have gone bad. 有一半的桃子都坏了。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Half of the peach has gone bad. 半个桃子坏了。</p></div>
gym@［dʒim］@n. 健身房；体育馆</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I go to the gym to exercise every Wednesday. 我每周三去健身房健身。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> gymnast（n. 体操运动员）</p>
misleading@［ˌmisˈli:diŋ］@adj. 令人误解的，导致错误结论的；引入歧途的；欺骗的；迷惑人的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：mis（错）+leading（领导的）→令人误解的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Some books are misleading. 一些书误人子弟。</p>
barbecue@［ˈba:bikju:］@n. 烧烤野餐；金属烤架 v. 在烤架上烧烤</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A group of us will have a barbecue this weekend. 我们一群人本周末要举行烧烤野餐。</p>
complete@［kəmˈpli:t］@adj. 十足的，彻底的；完成的 v. 完成，结束</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">______ the project in time, the staff were working at weekends. （2009年 天津）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. Competing</p> <p class="bodytext">B. Having completed</p> <p class="bodytext">C. To have completed</p> <p class="bodytext">D. To complete</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>为了按时完成该项目，员工在周末加班赶工。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>complete除表示一般性的“完成”外，还强调一切完备，没有欠缺的地方，尤其指通过填补失掉或缺陷的部分来配齐或完成。此外，to complete作目的状语，表示“为了完成…”，这个句子可以变成The staff were working at weekends in order to complete the project in time. 题目中省掉了in order，并把目的状语置于句首以示强调，因此本题选择D。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> completion（n. 完成；实现）；completely（adv. 十分；完全）</p>
hole@［həʊl］@n. 洞，孔眼；漏洞，缺陷</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a hole in the corner of the wall. 墙角有一个洞。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00216.jpeg"/></div>
earth@［ɜ:θ］@n. 地球；陆地，地面；土，泥</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Earth is the place that we are living on. 地球是我们生存的地方。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">earth, globe</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“地球”之义，但是有所区别。earth在表示地球时首字母要大写，还可以指“土”；而globe除“地球”之义外还可以表示“球体”。</p></div>
sorry@［ˈsɒri］@adj. 对不起的，抱歉的；遗憾的，惋惜的；可怜的，使人伤心的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am sorry to hear that your dog has died. 听说你的狗死了，我感到很遗憾。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00217.jpeg"/></div>
be@［bi］@v. 是，就是；在，存在</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary used to be a teacher. 玛丽以前是一名教师。</p>
aggressive@［əˈgresiv］@adj. 侵犯的，侵略的，挑衅的；敢作敢为的，有进取心的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Bill is an aggressive young man. 比尔是个有进取心的年轻人。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> aggressively（adv. 强劲地；侵略地；放肆地）</p>
flag@［flæg］@n. 旗，旗帜；标记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：面面红旗（flag）平（flat）地起</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The red flag is fluttering in the breeze. 红旗在微风中飘扬。</p>
later@［ˈleitə(r)］@adv. 后来；过一会儿 adj. 后来的，以后的，后面的；新近的；晚年的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'll come back later. 我一会儿就回来。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">later, soon</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“后来”的意思，但是用法不同。later常用在一般过去时的句子中，如：I found I made a mistake later. 后来，我发现自己犯错误了。而soon经常用于一般将来时的句子中，如：It will soon be Spring Festival. 很快就到春节了。</p></div>
wonderful@［ˈwʌndəfl］@adj. 极好的；惊人的，奇妙的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：wonder（惊奇）+ful（形容词后缀）→惊人的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Your picture is wonderful!你的照片拍得太棒了！</p>
therefore@［ˈðeəfɔ:(r)］@adv. 因此，所以</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You didn't listen to the teacher carefully and therefore your answer was wrong. 你没有仔细听老师讲，因此你的回答是错的。</p>
eye@［ai］@n. 眼，眼睛；虹膜；眼状物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The girl has beautiful eyes. 那个女孩有一双美丽的眼睛。</p>
moon@［mu:n］@n. 月球，月亮；卫星</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The moon is hanging in the sky. 月亮正挂在天空中。</p>
Mr.@［ˈmistə(r)］@n. 先生</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mr. Johnson has two sons and a daughter. 约翰逊先生有两个儿子，一个女儿。</p>
forbid@［fəˈbid］@v. ［forbade-forbidden］ 不许，禁止；妨碍，阻止</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> forbid sb. from doing sth. 禁止某人做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Smoking is forbidden in this office. 这间办公室禁止吸烟。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">forbid常用在forbid sb. from doing sth.这一结构中，表示“禁止某人做某事”。</p></div>
seldom@［ˈseldəm］@adv. 很少，不常</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I seldom see such a smart kid. 我很少见到这样聪明的小孩。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">seldom放在句首的时候，句子要倒装，如：Seldom have I met the man on the street. 我很少在街上看见这个人。</p></div>
outgoing@［ˈaʊtgəʊiŋ］@adj. 外出的，离开的；即将离职的；友好的，好交际的；外向的</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 动身，出发；支出，开销</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：out（出的）+going（去）→出去的→外出的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Cindy likes to tell jokes. She never stops talking. She is ______. （2008年 长春）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. serious</p> <p class="bodytext">B. quiet</p> <p class="bodytext">C. shy</p> <p class="bodytext">D. outgoing</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>辛迪喜欢讲笑话。她总是滔滔不绝。她是个开朗的人。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查词义辨析。serious意为“严肃的”，quiet意为“安静的”，shy意为“害羞的”，outgoing意为“开朗的”，根据句意应选D。</p>
pie@［pai］@n. 派，馅饼</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The apple pie tastes delicious. 这个苹果派味道很好。</p>
stomach@［ˈstʌmək］@n. 胃，胃口；肚子，腹部 v. 承受，忍受；吃得下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> It is unhealthy to swim on an empty stomach. 空腹游泳对健康有害。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> stomachache（n. 胃痛，肚子痛）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00218.jpeg"/></div>
burn@［bɜ:n］@v. ［burnt/burned-burnt/burned］ 燃烧，点燃；以…为燃料；烧毁，灼痛 n. 烧伤，灼伤</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> burn down 烧为平地；burn out 烧坏，烧掉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My grandmother's family burns coal to cook. 我祖母家里烧煤来做饭。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> burnout（n. 燃尽；烧毁；筋疲力尽）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00219.jpeg"/></div>
delicious@［diˈliʃəs］@adj. 美味的；芬芳的；宜人的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The fruit cake was quite delicious. 水果蛋糕实在是太美味了。</p>
perform@［pəˈfɔ:m］@v. 做，履行，完成；演出，表演</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：per（每个）+form（形式）→从形式上看每个人的一生都像一场演出→演出</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These students will perform a play this weekend. 本周末，这些学生要表演一出戏剧。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> performance（n. 表演；执行；绩效）；performer（n. 表演者）</p>
bored@［bɔ:d］@adj. 无聊的，无趣的；厌烦的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be bored with 厌倦</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am bored with city life. 我厌倦了城市生活。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">bored, boring</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“无聊的”之意，但是用法不同。bored形容人，boring形容物。如：I feel bored at home. 我待在家里觉得无聊。The book is very boring. 这本书很无聊。</p></div>
along@［əˈlɒŋ］@adv. 向前地；一道，一起 prep. 沿着，循着</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> As you go along the street, Big Ben is on your right. 沿着这条街走，大本钟就在你的右边。</p>
might@［mait］@v. aux. （may的过去式）可能，会</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 力量，能力；势力，权势</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You might understand if you were older. 如果你再大一点，可能就明白了。</p>
trade@［treid］@n. 贸易，商业；行业，职业 v. 贸易，交换</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> China does a lot of trade with France. 中国与法国间的贸易频繁。</p>
elbow@［ˈelbəʊ］@n. 肘部 v. 用肘推，用肘挤</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The player hurt his elbow in the game. 选手在比赛中伤了肘部。</p>
August@［ˈɔ:gəst］@n. 八月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Farmers are usually very busy in August. 农民在八月份通常很忙。</p>
eighteenth@［ˌeiˈti:nθ］@num. 第十八</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The American revolution happened in the eighteenth century. 美国革命发生在18世纪。</p>
least@［li:st］@adj. 最少的，最小的；最不重要的 adv. 最少，最小</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> at least 至少</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> At least I can do something to help the little child. 至少，我能做点事来帮助这个小孩。</p>
cheat@［tʃi:t］@v. 欺骗，骗取；作弊 n. 欺骗，欺骗行为；骗子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：骗（cheat）吃（eat）骗喝</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many people were cheated by the agent. 许多人都被这个中介骗了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> cheater（n. 骗子）；cheating（n. 欺骗）</p>
February@［ˈfebruəri］@n. 二月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary was born in February. 玛丽是二月出生的。</p>
train@［trein］@n. 列车，火车；一连串，一系列；行列 v. 训练；培养</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to go now or I will miss the train. 我现在得走了，否则我就赶不上火车了。// All members of the team have been trained in self rescue. 队里的所有成员都受过自救训练。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> trainer（n. 训练者）；trainee 〔n. 受训练的人（或动物）〕</p>
useful@［ˈju:sfl］@adj. 有用的，有益的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：use（使用）+ful（形容词后缀）→有用的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The calculator is very useful to my mother's work. 计算器对我妈妈的工作非常有帮助。</p>
Japan@［dʒəˈpæn］@n. 日本</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will fly to Japan next Thursday. 我下周四飞去日本。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> Japanese（n. 日本人 adj. 日本人的；日本的）</p>
April@［ˈeiprəl］@n. 四月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's usually warm in April. 四月通常很暖和。</p>
taxi@［ˈtæksi］@n. 出租车</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think you should take a taxi, or you'll be late. 我想你还是打车吧，不然会迟到的。</p>
uniform@［ˈju:nifɔ:m］@n. 制服 adj. 相同的，一致的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：uni（单一）+form（形式）→单一形式→制服</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Students have to wear school uniforms at school. 学生在学校时要穿校服。//These clothes have uniform style. 这些衣服风格相同。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> uniformly（adv. 一律地，均一地）；uniformity（n. 同样，一致）</p>
describe@［diˈskraib］@v. 描写，描述；说明</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The picture describes how the students study at school. 这张照片体现了学生们在学校是如何学习的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> description（n. 描述；性质）</p>
sad@［sæd］@adj. 悲哀的，伤心的；十分糟糕的，令人伤心（或遗憾）的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I felt so sad that I wasn't invited to Jim's birthday party. 我没有收到吉姆生日聚会的邀请，对此我感到很伤心。</p>
careless@［ˈkeələs］@adj. 粗心的；草率的；随便的；不关心的，满不在乎的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be careless of 不关心…的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—The accident was really terrible.</p> <p class="bodytext">—Yes, it was. The young man on the bicycle was too ______. （2007年 潜江）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. careless</p> <p class="bodytext">B. careful</p> <p class="bodytext">C. carelessly</p> <p class="bodytext">D. carefully</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—这场事故真的很严重。</p> <p class="bodytext4">—是啊，骑自行车的年轻人太不小心了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>careless是形容词，表示“粗心的，疏忽的”，通常与介词about, of, with等搭配；careful意为“小心的”；carelessly是副词，意为“粗心地，不注意地”；carefully意为“小心地”，也是副词。根据上下文的意思和所填词在句中充当的成分，应选择A。</p>
human@［ˈhju:mən］@adj. 人的；人性的；有人情味的，有人性的 n. 人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are many different cell types in the human body. 人体中有许多不同种类的细胞。</p>
competition@［ˌkɒmpəˈtiʃn］@n. 竞争；比赛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We are in competition with three other companies for the contract. 我们正在跟其他三家公司竞争合同。</p>
promise@［ˈprɒmis］@v. 允诺，答应；有…可能，有希望 n. 承诺，诺言；可能性，希望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary promised to return the book next Monday. 玛丽答应下周一还书。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> promising（adj. 有前途的，有希望的）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">promise, assure</p>   <p class="bodytext">promise是“承诺，保证”的意思，侧重于表达主观意向，如：I promise to help you. 我答应帮助你。而assure侧重于指消除别人思想上的怀疑和担忧，如：I can assure you of the reliability of the information. 我向你保证消息可靠。</p></div>
however@［haʊˈevə(r)］@adv. 然而，仍然；无论如何 conj. 不管怎样，然而</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I explained it to her; however, she still didn't understand. 我向她解释，然而，她仍然不理解。</p>
stand@［stænd］@v. ［stood-stood］ 站，站立；坐落，位于；继续存在，保持有效；处于特定状态（或地位、关系等）；竖放；容忍，经受，经得起；坚持，维持原状</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 台，座；售货处，摊；立场；抵抗，抵御</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> stand up 起立；stand for 代表</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Stand by the window and you'll be able to see outside better. 站在窗户边，你可以更好地看外面。</p>
low@［ləʊ］@adj. 低的，矮的；低下的，低等的；粗劣的，低俗的；不充分的，缺乏的；意气消沉的，情绪低落的 adv. 低；低声地；卑微地 n. 低点；低水平</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：人往高处走，水往低（low）处流（flow）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man spoke in a low voice. 男人低声说话。</p>
visit@［ˈvizit］@n. / v. 参观，访问</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> pay a visit to 参观；拜访</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We are going to visit the Summer Palace this weekend. 这周末我们要去颐和园游玩。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> visitor（n. 访问者，来宾）</p>
car@［ka:(r)］@n. 汽车，轿车；（火车）车厢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The red car was so attractive that all the passers-by could not help taking a look. 那辆红色的小汽车太吸引人了，以至于所有的路人都忍不住要看一眼。</p>
operate@［ˈɒpəreit］@v. 动手术；起作用；经营，管理</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> operate on sb. 给某人动手术</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This company operated very well. 这家公司运转得很好。</p>
eleventh@［iˈlevnθ］@num. 第十一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He ranked eleventh in the final exam. 他期末考试排第11名。</p>
jacket@［ˈdʒækit］@n. 短上衣，夹克（衫）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is cold and I have to put on a jacket. 天气很冷，我需要穿上一件夹克。</p>
cheese@［tʃi:z］@n. 干酪，奶酪</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：挑选（choose）奶酪（cheese）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are many kinds of cheese in this supermarket. 这家超市的奶酪品种很多。</p>
terrorist@［ˈterərist］@n. 恐怖主义者</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：恐怖分子（terrorist）总是向游客（tourist）发动袭击</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There has been an increase in terrorist attacks in this country. 这个国家的恐怖袭击事件有所上升。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00220.jpeg"/></div>
satisfy@［ˈsætisfai］@v. 满足，（使）满意；（使）确信，（使）信服</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I hope the new proposal will satisfy everyone. 我希望新的建议能使每个人都满意。</p>
bookcase@［ˈbʊkkeis］@n. 书柜，书架</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm going to buy a bookcase next week. 我打算下周买一个书架。</p>
free@［fri:］@adj. 自由的，无约束的；免费的，无偿的；空闲的，未被占用的；无…的，摆脱了…的 v. 使自由，解放 adv. 免费地，无偿地；自由地，随意地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> for free 免费；free of charge 免费；set...free 释放…；be free from/of 免受…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's free for the customers to taste the food. 顾客可免费品尝这些食物。//Please feel free and enjoy yourself. 请不要拘束，随便一点。</p>
loving@［ˈlʌviŋ］@adj. 爱的；充满爱的；钟爱的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is a warm and loving family and we all like it. 这是一个充满温暖和爱的大家庭，我们都喜欢它。</p>
housework@［ˈhaʊswɜ:k］@n. 家务劳动</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：house（房子）+work（工作）→家里的工作→家务劳动</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like doing housework in my spare time. 我喜欢在空余时间做些家务活。</p>
elevator@［ˈeliveitə(r)］@n. 电梯；升降机</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You can go to the office by elevator. 你可以乘电梯到办公室。</p>
born@［bɔ:n］@adj. 出生的，产生的；天生的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Joe was born in a small village. 乔出生在一个小村子里。</p>
air@［eə(r)］@n. 天空；空气，大气；样子，神态</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：怒发（hair）冲冠，神态（air）自然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in the air 在空中；by air 乘飞机</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boss often travels by air. 老板经常坐飞机旅行。</p>
how@［haʊ］@adv. 怎么，怎样；多么，多少</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I've just bought a new washing machine, but I don't know how to use it. 我新买了一台洗衣机，但是不知道该怎么使用。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">how可以引导感叹句，常放在形容词或副词的前面，构成“How+adj./adv.+主语+谓语”的结构，如：How beautiful the hat is!多漂亮的帽子呀！what也可以引导感叹句，结构是“What（+a/an）+adj.+n.（+主语+谓语）”，如：What a beautiful hat （it is）!这顶帽子真漂亮！</p></div>
read@［ri:d］@v. ［read-read］ 读，阅读；朗读，宣读；读懂；观察；解释，理解；读到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I read the ads in yesterday's newspaper. 我读了昨天报纸上的广告。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> readable（adj. 易读懂的）；reader（n. 读者）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00221.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">当我们说“标语显示”或“信上说”的时候也可以用read，如：The sign reads“No Photos!”标语上写着“禁止拍照！”read的过去式和过去分词都是read，读音是［red］。</p></div>
left@［left］@adj. 左边的，左侧的 adv. 在左边，向左 n. 左边，左侧；左派，左翼</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">表示“在左边”用短语on the left，注意介词是on而不是in或at。</p></div>
fax@［fæks］@n. 传真（机）；传真电文 v. 传真（文档、信件等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：办公室里安装（fix）传真机（fax）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tina received the report by fax. 蒂娜收到了报告的传真。</p>
say@［sei］@v. ［said-said］ 说，讲；说明；表明，宣称 n. 话语</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Don't forget to ______“Thank you”when someone has helped you. （2007年济南）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. speak</p> <p class="bodytext">B. tell</p> <p class="bodytext">C. say</p> <p class="bodytext">D. talk</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>当别人帮助了你，不要忘记说声“谢谢”。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查近义词的辨析。四个词都有“说”的意思。speak后面通常接某类语言；tell指把一件事传达给别人或讲述一件事、一个故事等；say通常强调讲话的内容，指有连贯性的说话；talk表示一般的谈话或者交谈。根据题意，本题选C。</p>
book@［bʊk］@n. 书，书籍；本子，簿册；［pl.］ 账目 v. 预订，预约</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The book on the desk is not mine. 桌子上的那本书不是我的。</p>
in@［in］@prep. 在…里，在…内；在…期间，在…之内；在…方面；处于…之中；用，以；从事，参加；穿着 adv. 进，入；在家，在里面；正当时令，正在流行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in one's size 某人尺码的大小；in a hurry 匆忙地；in the middle of 在…的中间；in danger 在危险中；in time 及时；take part in 参与；in order to 为了</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Alex dipped his pen in the ink and continued writing. 亚历克斯把钢笔蘸了蘸墨水，然后继续写作。// I will finish the project in five days. 我五天后将完成这项工程。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00222.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在表示时间、日期时，in用于表示世纪、年、季节、月份，以及非特指的上下午、夜晚，将来时中表示一段时间也用in，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">The Olympic Games was held in Beijing in 2008. 2008年北京举办了奥运会。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Plants begin to grow in spring. 植物春天开始生长。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Mother likes watching TV in the evening. 妈妈晚上喜欢看电视。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Tom will be back in several days. 汤姆几天后回来。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">在表达“说某种语言、用某种工具”的时候也用介词in，如：Can you sing the song in French? 你能用法语唱这首歌吗？</p>   <p class="bodytext3">另外，在表述地点的时候，in用于较大的地方，如大城市、国家等，at用于较小的地点，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">in Beijing 在北京</p>   <p class="bodytext3">at the station 在车站</p></div>
raise@［reiz］@v. 举起，提高；增加；筹集，征集；唤起，引起，激起；提出；养育，饲养，种植</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. （工资、薪金的）提高，增加</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> As time passed, people learned to raise animals and crops. 随着时间的推移，人们学会了饲养动物和种植庄稼。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">rise, raise</p>   <p class="bodytext">rise多用作不及物动词，多指客观事物自己升高或上升，如：The sun rises from the east. 太阳从东方升起。而raise是及物动词，多指人为地把事物升高，如：He raised his arms. 他举起手臂。</p></div>
fifteen@［ˌfifˈti:n］@num. 十五</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are fifteen students in this class. 这个班里有15名学生。</p>
kick@［kik］@n. / v. 踢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boys were kicking a ball around in the yard. 男孩们当时正在院子里踢球。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00223.jpeg"/></div>
between@［biˈtwi:n］@prep. 在…之间；介乎…之间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jim heard clearly the conversation between his mother and the teacher. 吉姆清楚地听到了他妈妈和老师的谈话。</p>
mysterious@［miˈstiəriəs］@adj. 神秘的，难以理解的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm afraid I don't like this mysterious story. 恐怕我不喜欢这个神秘的故事。</p>
cookie@［ˈkʊki］@n. 饼干</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I had cookies and coffee as afternoon tea. 我下午茶吃了饼干，喝了咖啡。</p>
magic@［ˈmædʒik］@n. 魔法，魔术；魔力，魅力 adj. 有魔力的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“卖即刻”→魔术卖弄的就是即刻的技巧→魔术</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have a cute magic toy sent by my elder brother. 我有一个可爱的魔法玩具，是哥哥寄来送我的。</p>
lay@［lei］@v. 放置，放下；铺，砌；下（蛋），产（卵）；设置，布置；使处于（某种状态）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He laid his hand on her shoulder. 他把手搭在她的肩上。</p>
friend@［frend］@n. 朋友，友人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lily is one of my best friends. 莉莉是我最好的朋友之一。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> friendly（adj. 友好的）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">friendly是从friend派生而来的，考生需要注意的是friendly不是副词，而是形容词，表示“友好的”。</p></div>
case@［keis］@n. 事例，实例；情况，事实；病例；案件；箱，盒；手提箱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：国事、家事、天下事，事事（case）关心（care）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in case 万一；如果；in the case of 在…的情况下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Father has ordered three cases of beer for the family party. 为了此次家庭聚会，父亲预订了三箱啤酒。</p>
twelfth@［ twelfθ］@num. 第十二（个） n. 十二分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary lives on the twelfth floor of the building. 玛丽住在大厦的12层。</p>
heavy@［ˈhevi］@adj. 重的，重型的；大量的，密集的；严重的，严厉的；剧烈的，繁重的；沉重的，忧郁的；充满的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There was a heavy snowstorm last night. 昨晚有一场暴风雪。</p>
combine@［kəmˈbain］@v. 联合，结合 n. 联合企业（或团体）；联合收割机</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：com（共同）+bi（两个）+ne→使两个在一起→结合</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> combine sth. with/and sth. 把…和…结合或混合起来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's quite difficult to combine all the information of this industry. 很难将这一行业的所有信息结合起来。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> combination〔n. 结合（体）〕</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00224.jpeg"/></div>
easy@［ˈi:zi］@adj. 容易的，不费力的；舒适的，安逸的；随和的，友善的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is very easy to finish this task. 完成这项任务非常容易。</p>
dictionary@［ˈdikʃənri］@n. 词典，字典</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think the dictionary is helpful to your study. 我认为字典对你的学习很有帮助。</p>
meeting@［ˈmi:tiŋ］@n. 会议，集会；会合，相会；运动会</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a meeting this afternoon. 今天下午有个会议。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00225.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">表达“举行会议”经常用动词hold，如：We'll hold a meeting this afternoon. 我们下午要举行一个会议。表达“有个会议”经常用have a meeting。</p></div>
waiter@［ˈweitə(r)］@n. （男）侍者，（男）服务员</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：wait（等待）+er（表人的名词后缀）→等候为他人服务的人→服务员</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The waiters provide good service for customers in this restaurant. 这家餐馆的服务员为顾客提供优质的服务。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> waitress（n. 女服务员）</p>
your@［jɔ:(r)］@pron. 你的，你们的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Your sister is driving me crazy. 你妹妹快把我逼疯了。</p>
survey@［ˈsɜ:vei］@n. 调查，勘察；测量，勘测；全面审视，概括论述</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［sɜ:ˈvei］</span> v. 调查，检视（建筑物等）；测量，勘测；全面审视，概括论述；俯瞰，眺望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our team was authorized to carry out a survey on the new subject. 我们小组被授权进行新课题的调研。// The next morning the police surveyed the damage caused by the accident. 第二天一早，警察调查了事故的破坏情况。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> surveyor（n. 测量员）</p>
appear@［əˈpiə(r)］@v. 出现，显露，来到；看起来好像，似乎；产生，问世；发表</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：app+ear（耳朵）→耳边响起，眼前出现→出现</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Helen suddenly appeared in front of us. 海伦突然出现在我们面前。</p>
possible@［ˈpɒsəbl］@adj. 可能的，做得到的；可接受的，合理的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> as...as possible 尽可能…的；if possible 如果可能的话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I quickly woke up my children and we left the building as quickly as possible. 我赶忙叫醒孩子们，然后我们尽快离开了大楼。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext5">possible, likely, probable</p>   <p class="bodytext">注意区分possible, likely, probable这几个表示“可能”的单词：</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00226.jpeg"/></div></div>
salad@［ˈsæləd］@n. 沙拉，凉拌菜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“沙拉”</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It only takes a short time to make fruit salad. 做水果沙拉只需要很少时间。</p>
another@［əˈnʌðə(r)］@pron. 再一个，另一个 adj. 又一的，再一个（或一批）的；另一的，别的；不同的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> one after another 一个接一个地；one another 彼此</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">My sister has two skirts. One is yellow, ______ is black.（2009年 北京）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. other</p> <p class="bodytext">B. another</p> <p class="bodytext">C. others</p> <p class="bodytext">D. the other</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>我姐姐有两条裙子，一条是黄色的，另一条是黑色的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查固定搭配one...the other...（一个…另一个…）。another常用来指三者或三者以上中的另一个。others是复数，表示“另外几个，其余的”。因此选D。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">another, other</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“另一个”之意。another主要指三者或三者以上中的另一个；other指两者中的另一个，常用在one..., the other... 结构中，如：I have two pencils. One is yellow, the other is green. 我有两支铅笔，一支是黄色的，另一支是绿色的。</p></div>
wash@［wɒʃ］@v. 洗，洗去；冲，冲掉；洗衣，洗脸（或手等）</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 洗涤；要洗的衣物，洗好的衣物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> wash up 洗手洗脸；洗盘子；wash out 冲掉；洗褪色；wash away 冲走</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do you usually wash clothes by yourself? 你经常自己洗衣服吗？</p>
passport@［ˈpa:spɔ:t］@n. 护照</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：pass（通过）+port（港口）→通过港口时使用的证件→护照</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The guest couldn't find his passport. 这位客人找不到自己的护照了。</p>
aid@［eid］@n. 帮助，救助；助手；辅助手段 v. 帮助，救助</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：制定目标（aim），准备救助（aid）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> first aid 急救</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man found his son with the aid of the police. 这位老人在警方的协助下找到了儿子。</p>
science@［ˈsaiəns］@n. 科学；学科</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The famous physicist dedicated all his life to science. 这位著名的物理学家把自己的一生都奉献给了科学。</p>
chase@［tʃeis］@v. 追捕；追求；寻求</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The dog at my grandmother's likes chasing chickens. 我奶奶家的狗喜欢追赶小鸡。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> chaser（n. 猎人；驱逐舰）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00227.jpeg"/></div>
sink@［siŋk］@v. ［sank-sunk］ 下沉，沉没；使下沉，使沉没；降低，下落 n. 水槽，水池</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：墨水（ink）滴入池（sink）中，染黑一池水</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> sink in 陷入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> As we drive on the beach, the car starts to sink into the sand. 当我们驾车在沙滩上行驶时，汽车开始往沙子里陷。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">sink, drown</p>   <p class="bodytext">sink指的是“下沉”或“沉没”，强调的是从表面沉到底部的过程；而drown是“淹死”，一般来说对象是有生命的人或动物。</p></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">sink的过去式是sank，过去分词是sunk。</p></div>
gun@［gʌn］@n. 枪，炮</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I saw the hunter carrying a gun. 我看见猎人拿着一支枪。</p>
research@［ˈｒｉ:ｓɜｔʃ］@n. 研究，调查 <span class="yinbiao1">［ｒiˈｓɜ:ｔʃ］</span> v. 研究，调查</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：re+search（搜寻）→不断搜寻资料进行研究→研究</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The conclusion is based on scientific research. 这个结论的提出是以科学研究为基础的。</p>
farmer@［ˈfa:mə(r)］@n. 农场主；农民</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The farmer has 20 cows and 30 sheep on his farm. 这个农场主有20头奶牛和30只羊。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00228.jpeg"/></div>
disadvantage@［ˌdisədˈvæntidʒ］@n. 缺点，不利条件</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：dis+advantage（有利条件）→不利条件</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This kind of product has its own advantages and disadvantages. 这类产品有自身的优缺点。</p>
prepare@［priˈpeə(r)］@v. 准备，预备</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> prepare for... 为…做准备；prepare to do sth. 准备做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to prepare for the next exam. 我不得不为接下来的考试做准备。</p>
hero@［ˈhiərəʊ］@n. 英雄，勇士；男主角，男主人公</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Conan is a hero in my heart. 柯南是我心目中的英雄。</p>
assistant@［əˈsistənt］@n. 助手；助教 adj. 助理的，辅助的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary worked as an assistant in a university. 玛丽曾在一所大学担任助教。</p>
nineteenth@［ˌnainˈti:nθ］@num. 第十九 n. 十九分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Everyone knows that it was the writer's nineteenth book. 人人都知道，这是这位作家的第19本书。</p>
passage@［ˈpæsidʒ］@n. 段落，章节；通道；流逝，推移</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：pass（通过，经过）+age→通道</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think you should read these passages carefully. 我认为你应该认真读一读这些章节。</p>
zigzag@［ˈzigzæg］@n. “之”字形；蜿蜒曲折 adj.“之”字形的 v. 弯弯曲曲行进</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：zig（急弯）+zag（急弯）→蜿蜒曲折</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A zigzag path leads to the top of the mountain. 曲折的小路通向山顶。</p>
and@［ənd］@conj. 和，与，及；那么，则；然后，接着；而且，还</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Harry and Bob are good friends. 哈里和鲍勃是好朋友。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">and, or</p>   <p class="bodytext">and常连接两个并列结构，表示“和”，只能用在肯定句中；而or在肯定句中通常表示“或”，在否定句中表示“和”，如：The little girl can't read or write. 这个小女孩既不会读也不会写。另外，or还可以连接句子，表示“否则”，如：Turn the heat down or it'll burn. 把灶火调小点，否则就要烧着了。</p></div>
treatment@［ˈtri:tmənt］@n. 治疗，疗法；对待，待遇；处理</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：treat（对待）+ment（名词后缀）→对待</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are various treatments available for this illness. 这种疾病有很多种治疗方法。</p>
corner@［ˈkɔ:nə(r)］@n. 角，角落；街角；遥远的地区，偏僻处；困境，绝路 v. 将…逼入困境，使走投无路</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I hit my head on the corner of the table. 我的头撞到了桌角上。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> corner-stone（n. 奠基石）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00229.jpeg"/></div>
cat@［kæt］@n. 猫；猫科动物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：加菲猫（cat）在开汽车（car）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are three cats in my house. One is white; the other two are black. 我家有三只猫，一只是白色的，另外两只是黑色的。</p>
nor@［nɔ:(r)］@conj. / adv. 也不，也没有</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Neither Tom nor Jack can go to the cinema, because they have homework to do. 汤姆和杰克都不能去看电影，因为他们有家庭作业要做。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext5">neither...nor, either...or</p>   <p class="bodytext">nor经常与neither搭配在一起，表示“既不…，也不…”，如：Neither Tom nor Jack will go. 汤姆和杰克都不会去。either经常与or搭配，表示“或者…或者…”，如：We'll go either on Saturday or Sunday. 我们要么周六去，要么周日去。</p></div>
recycle@［ˌri:ˈsaikl］@v. 回收利用（废物等），再应用</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：re（重新）+cycle（圈，循环）→再循环→回收利用</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People recycle waste batteries in all kinds of ways. 人们用各种方法回收废旧电池。</p>
trip@［trip］@n. 旅行，旅游 v. ［tripped-tripped, tipping］ （把…）绊倒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We went on a trip to Tibet last year. 去年我们去西藏旅游了。</p>
which@［witʃ］@pron. 哪一个，哪一些；…的那个，…的那些；那个，那些</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Which color do you like better, red or black? 红色和黑色，你更喜欢哪种颜色？</p>
background@［ˈbækgraʊnd］@n. 出身背景，经历；背景资料；（画等的）背景，底子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：back（背）+ground（地面）→背后的环境→背景</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom introduced his family background to us. 汤姆向我们介绍了他的家庭背景。</p>
night@［nait］@n. 夜，夜晚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is always cold on winter nights. 冬天的夜晚总是很冷。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00230.jpeg"/></div>
physics@［ˈfiziks］@n. 物理，物理学</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like studying physics. 我喜欢学习物理。</p>
airplane@［ˈeəplein］@n. 飞机</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The airplane will land in an hour. 飞机将于一小时后降落。</p>
lab@［læb］@n. 实验室</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The experts are doing the research in a lab. 专家们正在实验室里做研究。</p>
screen@［skri:n］@n. 屏幕，银幕；遮蔽；屏风 v. 掩蔽，遮蔽，包庇；放映（电影），播放（电视节目）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：在电视屏幕（screen）上看风景（scene）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Guo'an fans are all staring at the television screen to watch the game. 国安队的球迷都在盯着电视屏幕，关注比赛。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00231.jpeg"/></div>
dirty@［ˈdɜ:ti］@adj. 肮脏的；下流的，黄色的；卑鄙的，不道德的；暴风雨的，（天气）恶劣的</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 弄脏</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Your room is dirty. Please clean it. 你的房间不干净，请打扫一下。</p>
eighteen@［ˌeiˈti:n］@num. 十八</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Eighteen people took part in the game. 有18人参加了这个游戏。</p>
level@［ˈlevl］@n. 水平面，水平线；高度；水平，等级 adj. 平的，水平的；同高度的，同程度的；平稳的，冷静的 v. （使）变平坦</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Dolphins show a high level of intelligence. 海豚表现出很高的智商。</p>
India@［ˈindiə］@n. 印度</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I want to go to India this summer. 我今年夏天想去印度。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> Indian（n. 印度人 adj. 印度的）</p>
welcome@［ˈwelkəm］@v. / n. / int. 欢迎 adj. 受欢迎的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：wel（看作well，好）+come（来）→来得好→受欢迎的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> welcome to... 欢迎来到…；You are welcome. 不客气。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Welcome to all the new students here. 欢迎这里所有的新同学。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">一般在美国口语中，经常用You're welcome来回答Thank you。在英国，经常用That's all right或者Don't mention it来回答。</p></div>
hungry@［ˈhʌŋgri］@adj. 饥饿的，感到饿的；渴望得到的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I felt very hungry after four hours' hard work. 经过四个小时的努力工作后，我觉得很饿。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00232.jpeg"/></div>
social@［ˈsəʊʃl］@adj. 社会的；交际的，社交的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Helen cares so much about the social status of her family. 海伦十分注重她家庭的社会地位。</p>
super@［ˈsu:pə(r)］@adj. 极好的，上等的；超级的；过分的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Science and Technology Museum is a super place for kids. 科技馆对孩子们来说是个好去处。</p>
cupboard@［ˈkʌbəd］@n. 柜橱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：柜橱（cupboard）的板子（board）上放杯子（cup）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am not tall enough to reach the book on top of the cupboard. 我个子不够高，够不到柜橱顶上的书。</p>
telephone@［ˈtelifəʊn］@n. 电话 v. 打电话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Would you mind telling me your telephone number? 你介意告诉我你的电话号码吗？</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00233.jpeg"/></div>
smoke@［sməʊk］@n. 烟，烟尘；吸烟，抽烟 v. 冒烟，冒气；抽烟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Smith smokes a lot. He is a heavy smoker. 史密斯烟抽得很凶。他是个烟鬼。</p>
wonder@［ˈwʌndə(r)］@v. 对…感到疑惑（或好奇），想知道；（对…）感到惊讶（或诧异）</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 惊奇，惊异；奇迹，奇事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm wondering who won first prize. 我想知道谁得了第一。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">no wonder, no doubt</p>   <p class="bodytext">no wonder意为“怪不得”，如：No wonder you don't smoke. 难怪你不抽烟。no doubt意为“毫无疑问”，如：There is no doubt that we'll win the game. 毫无疑问，我们会赢得比赛。</p></div>
electric@［iˈlektrik］@adj. 电动的，电的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：electr（电）+ic→电的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Electric power is used in daily life. 电力被用于日常生活。</p>
what@［wɒt］@pron. 什么；多么，何等…的事物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> What does this word mean? 这个词是什么意思？</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">what引导的感叹句结构是what+（a/an）+形容词+可数名词单（复）数+（主语+谓语），如：What a beautiful lake （it is）! 多么漂亮的湖泊啊！或者是what+形容词+不可数名词+主语+谓语，如：What delicious food it is! 多么美味的食物啊！</p></div>
tie@［tai］@v. ［tying］ 拴，扎，捆；把…打结，系上；连接，使有关联；不分胜负</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 领带，领结；纽带，联系；束缚，牵连；平局</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：这人吃馅饼（pie）前不忘把领带（tie）解下来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> tie up 捆绑；束缚，阻碍；tie...to... 把…绑在…上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually tie back my hair when I'm cooking. 做饭的时候，我通常把头发扎在后面。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> tie-in（n. 关联，联系）</p>
both@［bəʊθ］@adj. 两个…（都） pron. 两者（都），双方（都）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Both of us have our own cars. 我俩都有各自的车。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在考试中经常会考到both...and...这一固定搭配，表示“两者都…”，如：Both Mary and I like drawing. 玛丽和我都喜欢绘画。</p></div>
lazy@［ˈleizi］@adj. 懒惰的，懒散的；慢吞吞的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Cats are lazy and always sleep in the daytime. 猫很懒，总在大白天睡觉。</p>
rocket@［ˈrɒkit］@n. 火箭 v. 迅速上升；猛涨</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The price of oil has suddenly rocketed up. 石油的价格突然高涨。</p>
ocean@［ˈəʊʃn］@n. 洋，海洋；许多，大量</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“噢，深！”→好深的大海啊！→海洋</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> an ocean of / oceans of 大量，众多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People have always wanted to explore the ocean. 人们一直想探索海洋。</p>
real@［ˈri:əl］@adj. 真的，真正的；真实的，现实的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Peter didn't tell me the real reason why he was late. 彼得没有告诉我他迟到的真实原因。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">real, actual</p>   <p class="bodytext">real强调人或事物真实存在，而不是想象或虚构的，如：All I saw was real. 我看到的一切都是真实的。而actual强调所说的东西是“实际的，真实的”，而不是估计或者杜撰的，如：the actual cost of the machine 机器的实际成本。</p></div>
helicopter@［ˈhelikɒptə(r)］@n. 直升机</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The criminals escaped by helicopter. 罪犯们乘直升机逃跑了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00234.jpeg"/></div>
appointment@［əˈpɔintmənt］@n. 约会；约定；任命，委派；职务，职位</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> make an appointment 约会；约定</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have an appointment with Anna tonight. 我今晚和安娜有约。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">appointment, date</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“约会”的意思。appointment指一般的约会或者会面，date常指男女朋友之间的约会。</p></div>
speak@［spi:k］@v. ［spoke-spoken］ 说话，讲话；演说，发言；表达意见；说（出），讲（出）；（会）讲（某种语言）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> speak out 大声地说；generally speaking 一般而言</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The foreign student can speak several languages. 那个外国学生能说好几种语言。</p>
begin@［biˈgin］@v. ［began-begun, beginning］ 开始</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> begin with... 以…开始</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> More and more people began to learn English. 越来越多的人开始学英语。</p>
Tuesday@［ˈtju:zdei］@n. 星期二</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Doctor Lee is not available on Tuesday. 李医生周二不出诊。</p>
announce@［əˈnaʊns］@v. 宣布，声称；预告</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The piece of good news was announced by the monitor yesterday. 班长昨天宣布了这个好消息。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> announcement（n. 公告，布告；宣布）；announcer（n. 广播员，播音员）</p>
England@［ˈiŋglənd］@n. 英格兰，英国</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I bought this book in England. 我在英格兰买的这本书。</p>
