whether@［ˈweðə(r)］@conj. 是否，会不会；不管，无论</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：明天天气（weather）是否（whether）会晴朗呢？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is not important whether you fail or succeed in the game. 你输了比赛或赢了比赛都不重要。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">whether, if</p>   <p class="bodytext">两个词都可以作宾语从句的引导词，一般情况下可以互换，但是有一些特殊情况需要注意。下面几种情况下只能用whether，不能用if：</p>   <p class="bodytext">（1）从句中出现or not时，只能用whether不能用if。如：I'm not sure whether I should go or not. 我不确定我应不应该去。也可以说I'm not sure if I should go.</p>   <p class="bodytext">（2）在动词不定式to do前，或在介词后面，只能用whether不能用if。如：Mike doesn't know whether to go to the cinema or to watch TV at home. 迈克不知道是去电影院还是在家看电视。</p>   <p class="bodytext">（3）引导词在句首或在表语从句中，只能用whether不能用if。如：Whether the manager is right or wrong is a question. 经理是对是错，这是个问题。</p>   <p class="bodytext">（4）discuss的宾语从句中，只能用whether不能用if。如：They discussed whether they had a conference next week. 他们讨论下周是否举行会议。</p>   <p class="bodytext">另外，以下几种情况中只能用if，不能用whether，需要注意：</p>   <p class="bodytext">（1）引导条件状语从句，作“如果”讲的时候，只能用if不能用whether。如：We'll go camping if it doesn't rain tomorrow. 如果明天不下雨我们就去野营。</p>   <p class="bodytext">（2）引导表示否定的宾语从句时一般用if不用whether。如：Teacher asked Tom if he hadn't finished his homework. 老师问汤姆是不是没有完成家庭作业。</p></div>
tennis@［ˈtenis］@n. 网球</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like to play real tennis rather than table tennis. 比起打乒乓球，我更喜欢打网球。</p>
ice@［ais］@n. 冰，冰块 v. 使变凉，冰冻，冰镇 adj. 冰的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like ice cream very much. 我非常喜欢吃冰淇淋。</p>
plan@［plæn］@n. 计划，打算，规划；平面图，示意图；设计图</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［planned-planned, planning］ 计划，给…制订计划</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I plan to go to Sanya this Spring Festival with my family. 我计划今年春节和家人去三亚。</p>
Brazilian@［brəˈziliən］@n. 巴西人 adj. 巴西的；巴西人的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man was a Brazilian. 这个老人是巴西人。</p>
height@［hait］@n. 高，高度；高处，高地；顶点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：high（adj. 高的）的名词形式</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The height of the chair is adjustable. 椅子的高度是可以调整的。</p>
clear@［kliə(r)］@adj. 清楚的，明白的；无疑的，确信的；晴朗的；清澈的 adv. 清晰地，清楚地</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 扫清，清除；使清楚，使明白；使清白无辜，证明…无罪；变晴；变清澈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is quite clear to me that Sammy was lying. 萨米在说谎，这点我很清楚。</p>
symphony@［ˈsimfəni］@n. 交响乐，交响曲；（色彩等的）和谐，协调</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：sym（共同）+phon（声音）+y→奏出共同的旋律→交响乐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Beethoven's Fifth Symphony is famous all over the world. 贝多芬的《第五交响曲》世界闻名。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> symphonic（adj. 交响乐的）</p>
century@［ˈsentʃəri］@n. 世纪，百年</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I was born in the 20th century. 我出生在20世纪。</p>
spare@［speə(r)］@adj. 备用的；多余的；空闲的 v. 留出，抽出（时间）；饶恕，不伤害；使免遭，免去；节约，吝惜 n. 备用品；备用轮胎</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like playing badminton in my spare time. 业余时间我喜欢打羽毛球。</p>
difficult@［ˈdifikəlt］@adj. 困难的；难懂的；难以取悦的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's difficult for me to go to work by bike. 骑自行车上班对于我来说很困难。</p>
festival@［ˈfestivl］@n. 节，节日，喜庆日</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm going home for Spring Festival. 春节期间我会回家。</p>
chest@［tʃest］@n. 胸，胸腔；柜子，橱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：和breast（n. 胸部）一起记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are a number of causes of chest pain. 有很多原因导致胸痛。</p>
gentle@［ˈdʒentl］@adj. 温柔的，慈祥的；文雅的，有礼貌的；（指天气、温度等）温和的，暖和的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：gen（=gener，出生，产生）+tle→产生感情的→温柔的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man is so gentle. 那位老人非常慈祥。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> gentility（n. 文雅，有教养）；gently（adv. 轻轻地；柔和地）</p>
home@［həʊm］@n. 家乡；家，家庭；原产地，发源地 adj. 家庭的；家用的；国内的</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 回家，在家；在本国，回本国</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> at home 在家</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a long way from the work place to his home. 他上班的地方离家很远。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">home, family</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“家”的意思，但是意思不同。home指某人长期居住的地方，带有一定的感情色彩；family指“家庭、家庭成员”，与居住的房子无关。</p></div>
injure@［ˈindʒə(r)］@v. 伤害，损害，损伤</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Andy injured his left hand in a fire. 安迪的左手在一场大火中受了伤。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00235.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">injure, harm, hurt</p>   <p class="bodytext">三个动词都有“伤害”或“损伤”的意思。injure主要指对健康、名誉、情感、智力等的伤害，如：It may injure your reputation. 这可能会损害你的名誉。harm用于指对人肉体或精神的损害，既可用于指对具体事物的损害，也可用于指对抽象事物的损害，强调造成的后果或损失，如：Smoking harms our health. 吸烟有害健康。hurt主要指“打击”或用其他方法使肉体或精神痛苦，如：She was hurt in a car accident. 她在车祸中受了伤。</p></div>
behave@［biˈheiv］@v. 表现；表现得体，有礼貌；（机器等）运转；起作用</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：be+have（有）→举止优雅→有礼貌</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> behave oneself 检点自己的行为</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Scientists try to explain why people behave in different ways. 科学家试图解释人们为什么有不同的表现。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> behavio（u）r（n. 举止，行为）</p>
spoken@［ˈspəʊkən］@adj. 口头的，口语的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：说话（speak）时，请尽量用口语化的（spoken）语言</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Chinese is the language spoken by the ______ number of people in the world, but it's not as ______ as English. （2007年 青岛）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. largest; widely spoken</p> <p class="bodytext">B. large; wide spoken</p> <p class="bodytext">C. larger; widely speaking</p> <p class="bodytext">D. largest; wide speaking</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>汉语是世界上使用人数最多的语言，但是不像英语那样被广泛使用。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>这里spoken是被动形式，意为“被说”。本题选A。</p>
medical@［ˈmedikl］@adj. 医学的，医疗的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jim took a medical course. 吉姆选了医学课。</p>
hamburger@［ˈhæmbɜ:gə(r)］@n. 汉堡包</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：汉堡包</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'd like a beef hamburger and salad. 我要一个牛肉汉堡和一份沙拉。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00236.jpeg"/></div>
anyone@［ˈeniwʌn］@pron. 任何人；随便哪一个人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I didn't want anyone to know my secret. 我不想让任何人知道我的秘密。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">anyone和anybody的意思相同，用法也相似，后面不接of，谓语动词用单数形式。</p></div>
after@［ˈa:ftə(r)］@adv. / prep./conj. 在…以后，在…后面</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> after all 毕竟，终究；be after 追逐，追求；soon after 不久以后</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">He didn't tell me anything ______ he left. （2007年 青岛）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. until</p> <p class="bodytext">B. before</p> <p class="bodytext">C. after</p> <p class="bodytext">D. since</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>他直到离开才告诉我一切。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查固定搭配not...until... （直到…才…）。before作连词时常指“在…前”，after指“在…后”，而since意为“自…以来”，常用于现在完成时的句子中。</p>
enough@［iˈnʌf］@adv. 足够地，充分地；相当，达到一定的程度 adj. 足够的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is not enough time for workers to relax. 工人们没有足够的时间休息。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">enough在修饰名词时必须放在名词前，如：I don't have enough money. 我没有足够的钱。在修饰形容词或副词时，一般放在形容词或副词之后，如：Bob is strong enough to carry the box. 鲍勃很强壮，足以搬动这个箱子。</p></div>
common@［ˈkɒmən］@adj. 共同的；平常的，普通的；共有的，公有的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> have... in common 有共同点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Kangaroos and koalas are common in Australia. 在澳大利亚，袋鼠和考拉都很常见。</p>
he@［hi:］@pron. 他；（不论性别的）一个人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> — Where's Paul?</p> <p class="bodytext6">— He's gone to the cinema.</p> <p class="bodytext6">— 保罗在哪儿？</p> <p class="bodytext6">— 他去看电影了。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">he的宾格形式是him，形容词性物主代词和名词性物主代词都是his，反身代词是himself。</p></div>
his@［hiz］@pron. 他的（所有物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is his fault that he drew pictures on the wall. 在墙上画画是他的错误。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">his既可以作形容词性物主代词，也可以作名词性物主代词，如：It's his pen. 这是他的钢笔。The pen is his. 这支钢笔是他的。</p></div>
establish@［iˈstæbliʃ］@v. 建立，设立；确定，证实</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our company was established last year. 我们公司是去年成立的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> establishment（n. 确立；建立；机构）；established（adj. 确定的）</p>
shock@［ʃɒk］@n. 震动，冲击；震惊，惊愕；电震，电击，触电</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. （使）震动；（使）震惊；（使）休克</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It shocked me that the bank had closed. 银行已经关门了，我感到很惊讶。</p>
disease@［diˈzi:z］@n. 疾病，病患；不健全，弊端</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：dis+ease（安心）→安心养病→疾病</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The disease spreads rapidly. 这种疾病传播得很快。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> diseased（adj. 【植】有病害的；患病的）</p>
need@［ni:d］@v. 需要；必须 v. aux. 必要，必须 n. 需要，必要；缺乏；迫切要求</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I need to buy several bottles of water. 我需要买几瓶水。</p>
last@［la:st］@adj. 刚过去的，紧接前面的；最后的，最后剩下的；最不可能的，最不合适的；最终的，结论性的 adv. 上一次，最近一次；最后 v. 持续，维持</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：持（last）之以恒，未为晚（late）矣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> at last 最后，最终；last night 昨晚；last summer 去年夏天</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Last week, I went to the city with my family. 上周，我和家人去了那个城市。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">last可以作不及物动词用，意思是“持续”，常和介词for连用，如：The war lasted for eight years. 战争持续了八年。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">在表述“昨天早晨”、“昨天下午”的时候不能用last，而要用yesterday morning, yesterday afternoon，而表示“昨天夜里”的时候要用last night。“last+星期几”是指上周几，前面不再用介词，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（〇） Susan went to the park last Sunday. 上周日苏珊去了公园。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（✕） Susan went to the park on the last Sunday. 上周日苏珊去了公园。</p></div>
rank@［ræŋk］@n. 等级；军衔，职衔 v. 排列，使排成行；将…分等级；属于某等级，居某地位</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：弗兰克（Frank）在军队里的军衔（rank）很高</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This badminton player ranked second in the world. 这名羽毛球运动员世界排名第二。// Uncle Li was promoted to the rank of captain last week. 上周李叔叔被提升为上尉。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> ranking（adj. 高级的）</p>
drink@［driŋk］@n. 饮料；酒 v. ［drank-drunk］ 饮，喝（酒等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：想（think）喝饮料（drink）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Would you like something to drink? 你想喝点什么吗？</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">考生要注意，drink的过去分词drunk还可以作形容词“喝醉的”和名词“喝醉的人”讲。</p></div>
seventy@［ˈsevnti］@num. 七十，七十个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Allen's grandfather is nearly seventy years old. 艾伦的祖父将近70岁了。</p>
number@［ˈnʌmbə(r)］@n. 数目，数字；号码，编号 v. 给…编号</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a number of 大量的（修饰可数名词）；the number of …的数目</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are a number of students in this class. 这个班有很多学生。</p>
progress@［ˈprəʊgres］@ n. 前进；进步；进展</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［prəˈgres］</span> v. 前进，行进</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in progress 在进行中；make progress （in...） （在某方面）取得进步</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The student is not making much progress in English. 这名学生的英语没有太大进步。</p>
town@［taʊn］@n. 镇，市镇；市区，市中心</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would rather live in a town than in the country but my father is the opposite. 我宁愿住在城市里也不愿住在乡下，而我爸爸恰恰相反。</p>
stair@［steə(r)］@n. ［pl.］ 楼梯；（楼梯的）梯级</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jerry ran up the stairs quickly as he heard the sound. 听到声音，杰里飞快地跑上楼去。</p>
light@［lait］@n. 光，光亮；光源，灯；（火柴、打火机等的）火 adj. 光线充足的，明亮的；淡色的，浅色的；轻的，少量的；愉快的，轻快的；（食物）清淡的，不油腻的</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［lit/lighted-lit/lighted］ 点，点燃；照亮；使发光</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：点燃（light）火把，准备战斗（fight）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> light up 点燃，亮起来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She could just read the book by the light of the candle. 她只能借着烛光读书。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">light在作“光”讲时是不可数名词，作“灯”讲时是可数名词。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I can see light in the distance. 我能看见远处的灯光。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Turn on the lights in the room, please. 请打开屋里的灯。</p></div>
yard@［ja:d］@n. 院子，场地；码</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We need a yard where our children can play. 我们需要个院子，孩子们可以在那里玩。</p>
serious@［ˈsiəriəs］@adj. 严重的，危急的；重要的，重大的；认真的，严肃的，庄重的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We all think that it is time to give serious consideration to this matter. 我们都认为现在是时候认真考虑一下这个问题了。</p>
certain@［ˈsɜ:tn］@adj. 某一，某种；肯定的，确信的；确实的，无疑的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The program appeals to an audience of a certain age. 这个电视节目吸引特定年龄的观众群体。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> certainly（adv. 的确，当然）</p>
illness@［ˈilnəs］@n. 病，疾病</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The terrible illness weakened his body day by day. 可怕的疾病使他的身体一天天地虚弱下去。</p>
word@［wɜ:d］@n. 词，单词；言语，话；消息，传说；诺言，保证</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in a word 总之；in other words 换言之；keep one's word 遵守诺言；have words with sb. 与某人争吵；have a word with sb. 与某人谈话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The same word has different meanings in different contexts. 在不同的语境中，同一词的含义不同。</p>
control@［kənˈtrəʊl］@n. 控制（能力），支配；管理；调节；抑制，自制；控制器，调节器 v. 控制，支配；克制，抑制；管理；调节</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> lose control over 对…失去控制；have control over / take control of 控制…；out of control 失控</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The car went out of control and crashed into a tree. 小汽车失去了控制，撞向了大树。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> controllable（adj. 可管理的，可控制的）；controller（n. 负责人） ；self-control （n.自控，自制力）</p>
will@［wil］@v. aux. ［would］ 将，会；要，愿意 n. 意志，决心；遗嘱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Will you help me with my task? 你会帮助我完成任务吗？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> willful（adj. 任性的；故意的）；willing（adj. 愿意的）</p>
madam@［ˈmædəm］@n. 女士，夫人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can I help you, madam? 女士，有什么需要帮助的吗？</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">Madam, Miss, Ms.</p>   <p class="bodytext">Madam是一种正式的用法，而Miss主要指单身女性，Ms.泛指女士，不表明是否已婚。</p></div>
chairman@［ˈtʃeəmən］@n. 主席；会议主持人；董事长</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Chairman of the company announced a new policy. 公司董事长宣布了一项新政策。</p>
really@［ˈri:əli］@adv. 真正地，实际上；很，十分，全然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's really cold today. 今天真冷。</p>
dozen@［ˈdʌzn］@n. （一）打，十二个 adj. 一打的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a dozen 一打；dozens of 几十个，很多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I spent three dollars on a dozen eggs. 我花三美元买了一打（12个）鸡蛋。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">dozen前有具体数词或a, many, several时不用复数，表示“几打”；但是在没有时可以用复数，常用搭配是dozens of，表示“几十个，很多”，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">two dozen eggs 两打鸡蛋</p>   <p class="bodytext3">dozens of eggs 很多鸡蛋</p></div>
report@［riˈpɔ:t］@v. 报告，汇报；报道；告发；报到；隶属，对（上司）负责</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 报道；报告，汇报；传说，传闻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The report has been sent to the child's parents. 报告已经送到了那个孩子的父母手中。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> reporter（n. 记者，通讯员）</p>
dad@［dæd］@n. 爸爸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The baby was able to call dad when he was six months old. 宝宝六个月大的时候就会叫爸爸了。</p>
loud@［laʊd］@adj. 响亮的，大声的；（色彩等）刺目的；（行为）太招摇的</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 响亮地，大声地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The television is so loud that I can hardly focus. 电视的声音太大了，我无法集中精力。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> loudly（adv. 大声地）</p>
basketball@［ˈba:skitbɔ:l］@n. 篮球</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I want to be a basketball player. 我想成为篮球运动员。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00237.jpeg"/></div>
jeans@［dʒi:nz］@n. 牛仔裤</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There aren't any black jeans in the shop. 这家店没有黑色的牛仔裤了。</p>
gate@［geit］@n. 大门；有大门的出入口；（比赛等的）观众人数，门票收入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：关门（gate）打讨厌（hate）的狗</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are soldiers on guard at the gate of Buckingham Palace. 白金汉宫门口有士兵把守。</p>
ant@［ænt］@n. 蚂蚁</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These children like watching ants. 这些孩子喜欢观察蚂蚁。</p>
courage@［ˈkʌridʒ］@n. 勇气，胆量</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：我们的（our）年纪（age）虽然小，可是勇气（courage）真不少</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> get courage 获得勇气；lose courage 失去勇气</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jim showed great courage and determination before the bungee jump. 吉姆在蹦极之前表现得很有勇气和决心。</p>
there@［ðeə(r)］@adv. 在那里，往那里；在那方面，在那点上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There will be an interesting cartoon on CCTV-6 at seven thirty this evening. 今晚七点半中央六台将会播出一部有意思的动画片。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">there be结构的时态变化是通过be动词的变形来体现的。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">There was a house near the river. 过去河边有座房子。（过去时）</p>   <p class="bodytext3">There will be a basketball game next week. 下周有场篮球赛。（将来时）</p>   <p class="bodytext3">There have been so many volunteers on the street since the Olympic Games opened. 自从奥运会开幕以来，街上有许多志愿者。（完成时）</p></div>
warm@［wɔ:m］@adj. 温暖的，暖和的；热情的，热心的；（色调）暖的</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. （使）暖起来；使热烈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> warm up 热身；变暖；warm to 同情，爱好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's very cold today; you should put on warm clothes. 今天很冷，你应该穿上保暖的衣服。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> warmth（n. 暖和；热情）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00238.jpeg"/></div>
musician@［mjuˈziʃn］@n. 音乐家，乐师</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The music teacher wants his students to become musicians. 音乐老师想让他的学生都成为音乐家。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00239.jpeg"/></div>
pack@［pæk］@v. 捆扎，打包；（使）挤在一起；塞满</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 包，包裹；小盒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> pack up 把…打包，整理</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man bought a pack of cigarettes. 男士买了一包香烟。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> packing（n. 包装）；packer（n. 包装机）</p>
orange@［ˈɒrindʒ］@n. 橙，柑，橘；橙汁，橘汁 adj. 橙色的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">He is thirsty. Please give him some ______ to drink. （2007年 济南）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. rice</p> <p class="bodytext">B. meat</p> <p class="bodytext">C. water</p> <p class="bodytext">D. oranges</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>他渴了。请给他一点水喝。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是名词及其单复数。例句中说要拿喝的东西，water是“水”，可以选择，而orange当“橙汁”讲的时候没有复数形式，因此只能选C。</p>
mad@［mæd］@adj. 疯的，神经错乱的；恼火的，狂怒的；狂热的，着迷的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：坏（bad）人装疯（mad）卖傻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> All the boys in our class are mad about football. 我们班所有的男生都狂热地迷恋足球。</p>
pet@［pet］@n. 宠物；宠儿 adj. 宠爱的，表示亲昵的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“拍它”→轻拍宠物，让它舒服→宠物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's not allowed to have pets in this apartment. 这座公寓不允许养宠物。</p>
twin@［twin］@n. 孪生儿之一，双胞胎之一 adj. 孪生的，成双的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My elder sister gave birth to twins last month. 上个月我姐姐生了一对双胞胎。</p>
underwater@［ˌʌndəˈwɔ:tə(r)］@adj. 水下的；水下使用的；水下行动的 adv. 在水下，在水中</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：under（在…下面）+water（水）→水下的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> They took some clear pictures with an underwater camera. 他们用一台水下照相机拍摄出一些清晰的照片。</p>
middle@［ˈmidl］@n. 中部，中间 adj. 中部的，中间的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm standing in the middle of the room. 我正站在房间的中间。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00240.jpeg"/></div>
prediction@［priˈdikʃn］@n. 预言；预料；预报</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：predict（预言）+ion（抽象名词后缀）→预言；预料</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> They all believe the witch's prediction that the storm will come. 他们都相信巫婆关于暴风雨将要来临的预言。</p>
awake@［əˈweik］@adj. 醒着的 v. ［awoke-awaken］ 醒，唤醒（某人）；意识到，醒悟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：a+wake（醒）→唤醒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> keep sb. awake 让某人醒着</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The noise outside the door was keeping everyone awake. 门外的嘈杂声吵得大家都睡不着觉。</p>
feature@［ˈfi:tʃə(r)］@n. 特征，特色；［pl.］ 面貌，相貌；特写，专题节目；故事片</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 以…为特色，是…的特征；起重要作用</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mutual help is a key feature of the training program. 互帮互助是这个培训项目的特色。</p>
street@［stri:t］@n. 街道，马路</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You must be careful when you walk on the street. 走在大街上，你一定要小心一点。</p>
you@［ju］@pron. 你，你们</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Good luck to all of you in the exam. 祝你们所有人考试顺利。</p>
penny@［ˈpeni］@n. 便士，分</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy found six pennies on the ground and gave them to the policeman. 男孩在地上捡到6便士并把它们交给了警察。</p>
pocket@［ˈpɒkit］@n. 衣袋，口袋；容器 v. 把…装入口袋 adj. 袖珍的，小型的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：口袋（pocket）里放着一个小小的火箭（rocket）模型</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are four pockets in my jacket. 我的夹克有四个兜。</p>
am@［æm］@v. 是（be动词的第一人称单数）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm your new teacher this term. 我是你们这学期的新老师。</p> <p class="bodytext">be动词的几种变化形式如下：</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00241.jpeg"/></div>
dormitory@［ˈdɔ:(r)mətɔ:ri］@n. 宿舍</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：dorm（睡眠）+itory→学生睡觉的地方→宿舍</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our dormitory is on the third floor. 我们的宿舍在三楼。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">在美式英语中，该词常被写成dorm。</p></div>
tall@［tɔ:l］@adj. 高的，身材高的；难以置信的；难以办成的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She is a little taller than her elder sister. 她比她姐姐高一点。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00242.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">tall, high</p>   <p class="bodytext">tall一般用来形容人、动物或树木等有生命的东西，如：a tall man或者a tall tree等；high是形容一个不与地面接触的事物的高度，如：The plane is so high in the sky. 飞机在天上飞得那么高。不过形容mountain时用high，但形容hill可以用tall。</p></div>
team@［ti:m］@n. 队，组 v. （使）合作；结成一队</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> team up 结成一队，合作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This new project needs the spirit of team work. 这个新项目需要团队协作精神。</p>
whatever@［wɒtˈevə(r)］@pron. 无论什么，不管什么；任何…的事物，凡是…的东西</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He will give you whatever you want. 他会给你任何你想要的东西。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">whatever在一些口语表达中独立成句，表示的意思是“无所谓”。如：How do you feel about the color? Whatever!你觉得这颜色怎么样？无所谓。</p></div>
country@［ˈkʌntri］@n. 国家；国土；国民，全国人民；农村，乡村</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My father would like to live in the country after retirement. 我的父亲退休后想去乡下住。</p>
belt@［belt］@n. 地带，地区；腰带，皮带</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The driver should fasten the safety belt. 司机应该系上安全带。</p>
seem@［si:m］@v. 好像，似乎</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It seems that it will rain soon. 看来马上要下雨了。</p>
recite@［riˈsait］@v. 背诵，朗诵；列举，逐一讲述</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like to recite Shakespeare's works. 我喜欢背诵莎士比亚的作品。</p>
pull@［pʊl］@v. 拉，拖，拔；移动 n. 拉，拖；拉力，牵引力，引力</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> pull down 推翻；使下跌；pull in 进站，靠岸；pull on 穿，戴；继续拉；pull out 拨出；pull away 脱身；离开</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The naughty boy pulled my hair. 那个淘气的小男孩扯了我的头发。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">drag, draw, pull</p>   <p class="bodytext">三个词都有“拉”的意思。如果表示将物体拉离原位置，可以用draw或pull；如果位置没有变化，则用pull。此外drag强调的是用力拉或拖。</p></div>
anxious@［ˈæŋkʃəs］@adj. 焦虑的，发愁的，令人焦急的；渴望的，急切的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary was anxious about her child's safety. 玛丽担心她孩子的安全。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00243.jpeg"/></div>
secretary@［ˈsekrətri］@n. 秘书；书记；部长，大臣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：secret（秘密）+ary（表人的后缀）→做秘密工作的人→秘书</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The general manager told me to contact his secretary to make an appointment. 总经理让我联系他的秘书预约见面时间。</p>
southern@［ˈsʌðən］@adj. 南方的，南部的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Have you seen the star in the southern sky? 你看到南方天空中的那颗星星了吗？</p>
afternoon@［ˌa:ftəˈnu:n］@n. 下午，午后</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am going to the park this afternoon. 我今天下午要去公园。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">afternoon常用在短语in the afternoon中，记住此处不能用介词on，on一般用于具体的、小范围的时间前，如：on a November afternoon 在11月的一个下午。</p></div>
role@［rəʊl］@n. 作用；职责；角色；任务</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> That boy played an important role in the band. 那个男孩是这支乐队的重要成员。</p>
express@［ikˈspres］@v. 表示，表达 adj. 特快的，直达的；明确的，明白表示的 adv. 用快递方式；乘直达快车 n. 快车；快邮，速递</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：ex（出）+press（挤，压）→挤出思想→表达</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tracy expressed a strong interest in visiting the Philippines. 特蕾西对去菲律宾表现出强烈的兴趣。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> expression（n. 表达，表述）；expressive（adj. 表现的，有表现力的）</p>
peel@［pi:l］@v. 削…的皮，剥…的壳 n. （水果等的）皮；外衣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The nurse peeled an apple for the patient. 护士为病人削了一个苹果。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> peeling（n. 削皮）</p>
sweep@［swi:p］@v. ［swept-swept］ 扫，打扫，拂（去）；扫过，掠过，（风）吹，（浪等）冲，席卷；（使）快速移动；（在…）迅速传播（或蔓延） n. 打扫；（手臂等的）挥动</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：拂去（sweep）脸上的泪水，不再哭泣（weep）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do you usually sweep the floor in your spare time? 你空闲的时候经常扫地吗？</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00244.jpeg"/></div>
busy@［ˈbizi］@adj. 忙的；专心的；繁忙的，热闹的；（电话线）正在被占用的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be busy with... 忙于…；be busy （in） doing sth. 忙于做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm too busy to take any exercise nowadays. 目前我太忙了，以至于没有时间运动。</p>
steal@［sti:l］@v. ［stole-stolen］ 偷盗，行窃；悄悄地移动</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：小偷经常去偷盗（steal）工厂的钢铁（steel）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'll send you to the police station if I catch you stealing again. 如果再让我发现你偷东西的话，我就把你送到警察局去。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00245.jpeg"/></div>
regret@［riˈgret］@n. / v. ［regretted-regretted, regretting］ 懊悔；遗憾，抱歉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> regret doing sth. 后悔做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I regret telling John the secret. 我后悔告诉了约翰这个秘密。</p>
tidy@［ˈtaidi］@adj. 整洁的，整齐的 v. （使）整洁，（使）整齐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lucy is a qualified housewife, and she keeps her house very tidy. 露西是一位称职的家庭主妇，把房子收拾得非常整洁。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">tidy, clean</p>   <p class="bodytext">tidy是“整洁的；整齐的”之意，侧重于物品摆放不凌乱，一切井井有条；而clean是“干净的”的意思，意思侧重于不脏，如：We make this room clean and tidy. 我们把屋子打扫得干净、整洁。</p></div>
writer@［ˈraitə］@n. 作者，作家</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Charles Dickens is a famous writer. 查尔斯·狄更斯是著名作家。</p>
understand@［ˌʌndəˈstænd］@v. ［understood-understood］ 理解，懂；了解，意识到；认为，以为</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can't understand what she said. 我不明白她的话。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">Do you understand? 意思是“你明白了吗？”不少同学容易出错，说成Are you understand? 注意understand是动词，应该用助动词do提问。</p></div>
shiny@［ˈʃaini］@adj. 光亮的，有光泽的；反光的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mr. Smith usually wears a pair of shiny black shoes. 史密斯先生经常穿着一双黑亮的皮鞋。</p>
photograph@［ˈfəʊtəgra:f］@n. 照片，相片 v. 拍照</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：photo（照片）+graph（书写）→照片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our teacher's photograph appeared in the local paper. 我们老师的照片出现在当地的报纸上了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> photographer（n. 摄影师）；photography（n. 摄影）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00246.jpeg"/></div>
wake@［weik］@v. ［woke-waken］ 醒来，唤醒；激起，唤起；警觉，振奋</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 醒；守夜；航迹，痕迹</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> wake up 醒来；wake sb. up 把某人叫醒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> When I woke up, I found myself lying on the beach. 当我醒来时，发现自己躺在沙滩上。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> wakeful （adj. 失眠的）；waking （adj. 醒着的）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">wake, awake</p>   <p class="bodytext">wake是“醒，叫醒”的意思，经常与副词up连用，如：Wake up! It's eight o'clock. 快醒醒，已经8点了。awake表示“醒，弄醒”，要比wake更正式一些，如：The noise awoke the sleeping child. 噪音把正在熟睡的孩子弄醒了。另外awake 还有“领会”的意思。</p></div>
envelope@［ˈenvələʊp］@n. 信封</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can you buy me an envelope? 你能给我买个信封吗？</p>
ball@［bɔ:l］@n. 球，球状物；（盛大、正式的）舞会</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Earth looks like a ball. 地球看上去像个球。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> football（n. 足球）；basketball（n. 篮球）；baseball（n. 棒球）；volleyball（n. 排球）</p>
pollution@［pəˈlu:ʃn］@n. 污染</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The air pollution is very serious nowadays. 现在空气污染非常严重。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> pollution-free（adj. 无污染的）</p>
battery@［ˈbætri］@n. 电池（组），蓄电池（组）；排炮，炮组；一系列，一套</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The battery in my toy is all used up. 我玩具上的电池用完了。</p>
sight@［sait］@n. 视力，视觉；看见，瞥见；视域，眼界；情景，景象，奇观；［pl.］ 风景，名胜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He began to lose his sight 10 years ago. 他十年前开始丧失视力。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">view, scene, sight</p>   <p class="bodytext">三者都有“看”的意思，注意它们的区别：</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00247.jpeg"/></div></div>
menu@［ˈmenju:］@n. 菜单</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Are you ready to order, sir?</p> <p class="bodytext">— ______ （2008年 荆州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. Yeah, probably.</p> <p class="bodytext">B. No, thanks.</p> <p class="bodytext">C. Let me look at the menu first.</p> <p class="bodytext">D. I am afraid I have no time.</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 先生，您准备点餐了吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 先让我看看菜单吧！</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>对话的场景是在餐馆里，服务员问道“先生，您准备点餐了吗？”，回答应该是“让我先看看菜单吧！”A选项是“好吧，有可能”。B选项是“不，谢谢”，是对邀请的答语。D选项是“恐怕我没有时间”。最符合的是C。</p>
adult@［ˈædʌlt; əˈdʌlt］@n. 成年人；成年动物 adj. 发育成熟的；（智力及情感上）成熟的，成人的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Quite a few adults have mobile phones. 相当多的成年人都有手机。</p>
fair@［feə(r)］@adj. 公平的，公正的；尚可的，不错的；浅色的，白皙的；晴朗的 adv. 公正地，公平地 n. （定期）集市；商品交易会，博览会</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：f+air（空气）→空气清新，天气晴朗→晴朗的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> To be fair, Tina behaved better than we had expected. 公平地讲，蒂娜的表现比我们预期的要好。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> unfair（adj. 不公平的）</p>
rural@［ˈrʊərəl］@adj. 乡村的，农村的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Uncle Lee usually spends his summer holiday in the rural area. 李叔叔通常在乡下过暑假。</p>
thin@［θin］@adj. 薄的；细的；瘦的；稀薄的；淡薄的 adv. 薄，细；稀疏 v. （使）变薄，（使）变细；（使）变稀</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The road is covered with a thin layer of ice. 路面上有一层薄薄的冰。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">thin是“薄的”之意，形容人的体态时，意为“瘦的”；其反义词一个是thick，表示“厚的”，另一个是fat，表示“胖的”。</p></div>
my@［mai］@pron. 我的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I lost my book when I came back home. 我回家的时候把书丢了。</p>
brain@［brein］@n. 脑，脑髓；脑袋；智慧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary died of a brain disease. 玛丽死于一种脑部疾病。</p>
quite@［kwait］@adv. 相当，颇；实际上，真正地；完全，十分</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：这片树林相当（quite）宁静（quiet）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> quite a few 很多的，大量的；quite a number of 相当多的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's quite cold outside so put your coat on. 外面很冷，把外套穿上吧！</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">fairly, quite</p>   <p class="bodytext">这两个词都是“相当”的意思，只是quite比fairly程度强，比较下面两个句子：</p>   <p class="bodytext">The room is fairly large for the four persons. 这屋子四个人勉强住得下。</p>   <p class="bodytext">The room is quite large for the four persons. 这屋子四个人住相当大了。</p></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">quite a既可以修饰人，也可以修饰事物，而quite some多用来修饰事物，不用来修饰人，如：John is quite a small boy. 约翰是个小男孩。</p></div>
realize@［ˈri:əlaiz］@v. 认识到；了解；实现</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：real（真实的）+ize（使…）→使变得真实→实现</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I believe people will realize their dreams if they keep on working hard. 我相信如果人们一直刻苦努力，就一定会实现他们的梦想。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">realize, recognize</p>   <p class="bodytext">realize不仅可以表达“认识到，了解”的意思，还可以表示“实现，完成”，如：The boy realized his dream. 男孩实现了他的梦想。而recognize表示“辨认出，认识”，也有“认定；承认”的意思，如：I recognized that I was wrong. 我意识到我错了。</p></div>
blank@［blæŋk］@adj. 空白的，空着的；茫然的，无表情的</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 空白（处）；空白表格</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：站在银行（bank）前，兜里空空（blank）没有钱，表情茫然（blank）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher asked the students to fill in the blanks. 老师要求学生填空。</p>
match@［mætʃ］@n. 比赛，竞赛；对手，敌手；匹配；火柴 v. 和…相配，和…相称</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There was a football match yesterday. 昨天有一场足球比赛。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> matchless（adj. 无比的，无敌的）</p>
side@［said］@n. 面，侧面，旁边；方面；一方，一边；山坡，坡，岸</p> <p class="bodytext1">adj. 侧面的，边的；枝节的，次要的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is an old man watching me from the other side of the road. 马路对面有一个老人在看我。</p>
opera@［ˈɒprə］@n. 歌剧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：歌剧（opera）开始（open）了</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This opera is popular in this country. 这部歌剧在这个国家很流行。</p>
bit@［bit］@n. 一点儿，少许；小片，小块</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a bit of 一点，一些（修饰不可数名词）；bit by bit 一点点地；not a bit 一点也不</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I had a bit of beef and several eggs this morning. 我今天早上吃了一点牛肉和几个鸡蛋。</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">a bit, a little</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“少许”的意思，且都可以修饰形容词。a bit不能直接作定语修饰名词，需要加介词of，构成a bit of sth.的结构，而a little可以直接跟名词。a bit of和a little都只能修饰不可数名词，如：There is only a bit of food for supper. 晚餐只有一点食物了。</p></div>
host@［həʊst］@n. 主人；东道主；节目主持人；许多，大量</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We thanked the host towards the end of the party. 宴会接近尾声的时候我们感谢了主办方。</p>
recipe@［ˈresəpi］@n. 烹饪法，食谱；方法；秘诀，诀窍</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I cooked this dish by following the recipe. 我按照食谱做的这道菜。</p>
handsome@［ˈhænsəm］@adj. （男子）漂亮的，英俊的；（女子）端庄健美的，好看的；慷慨的，可观的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We all think that our PE teacher is very handsome. 我们都认为体育老师非常帅气。</p>
anyway@［ˈeniwei］@adv. 不管怎么说，无论如何；不论以何种方式，无论从什么角度</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This isn't Annie's fault anyway. 反正这不是安妮的错。</p>
quarter@［ˈkwɔ:tə(r)］@n. 四分之一；季，季度；一刻钟；（美国、加拿大等）25分的硬币；［pl.］ 住处，住所 v. 将…四等分；供…住宿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually get up at a quarter to eight. 我通常早上7点45起床。</p>
choice@［tʃɔis］@n. 选择，选择权；供选择的东西；被选中的东西（或人）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> have no choice but to do sth. 别无选择，只能…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have no other choice right now but to run away. 我现在没有其他选择，只有跑开了。</p>
round@［raʊnd］@adj. 圆（形）的，球形的 adv. 在周围，在附近；朝反方向 prep. 围绕，绕过；向…各处；在…附近；大约 n. （一）回合，（一）局，（一）场；（一）圈；巡视（路线），巡回（路线） v. 环绕（…）而行；（使）成圆形</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> look round 环顾；观察；get round 避免；说服；走动；传开来；go round 流行，传播；all year round 终年，一年到头</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Earth moves round the Sun. 地球绕着太阳转。</p>
flight@［flait］@n. 航班，班机；飞行，飞翔</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：f+light（轻的）→身体轻飘飘的，飞了起来→飞行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I need to take a flight to London. 我需要坐飞机去伦敦。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> flighty（adj. 轻浮的；反复无常的）</p>
lake@［leik］@n. 湖</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：坐在湖（lake）边吃蛋糕（cake）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Which lake is the largest fresh water lake in China? 哪个湖是中国最大的淡水湖？</p>
ability@［əˈｂiｌəｔｉ］@n. 能力，本领；才能，才智</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：来自able（adj. 能够…的）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> ability to do sth. 有做某事的能力</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have the ability to wash clothes. 我会洗衣服。</p>
tense@［tens］@adj. 紧张的；拉紧的，绷紧的 v. （使）拉紧，（使）绷紧 n. （动词的）时态</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“弹死”→没有弹性了，因为拉得太紧了→拉紧的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The atmosphere in the meeting was getting more and more tense. 会议的气氛变得越来越紧张。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> tension（n. 紧张）</p>
unit@［ˈju:nit］@n. （工作）单位；（计量或计数用的）单位；部件，元件，装置；（住房的）单元</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The family can be considered the basic unit of society. 家庭可以被看作社会的基本单位。</p>
their@［ðeə(r)］@adj. / pron. 他（她、它）们的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We can see from the picture that their house is very beautiful. 从图上我们可以看出，他们的房子很漂亮。</p>
best@［best］@adj. 最好的 adv. 最好，最</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> all the best 万事如意</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Dogs are our best friends. 狗是我们最好的朋友。</p>
modern@［ˈmɒdn］@adj. 现代的，新式的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“摩登”→现代的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher told the students many things about modern art. 教师告诉学生们许多关于现代艺术的事。</p>
kite@［kait］@n. 风筝；纸鸢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have the hobby of collecting kites. 我喜爱收集风筝。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">kite常和动词fly一起构成固定词组fly a kite，表示“放风筝”，而不是和play搭配。</p></div>
tomato@［təˈmｅitəʊ］@n. ［pl. -es］ 西红柿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：西红柿（tomato）和土豆（potato）的味道可差远了</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like some tomato paste for my bread. 我想要在面包上抹一些番茄酱。</p>
neck@［nek］@n. 颈，脖子；（衣服的）领圈，领口</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The neck of the white coat is too wide. 这件白外套的领口开得太大了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00248.jpeg"/></div>
much@［mʌtʃ］@adv. 十分，非常 pron. 许多，大量</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> much more 更加</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">It takes Tom ______ time to watch matches. （2008年 鹤岗）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. little</p> <p class="bodytext">B. much</p> <p class="bodytext">C. a little</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>汤姆花了大量时间看比赛。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是修饰“时间”的形容词。time是不可数名词，much意为“大量的”，而little和a little表示“一点儿”，因此选B。</p>
wave@［weiv］@n. 波，波浪；（手等的）挥动 v. 挥手示意；波动，飘动；高潮，高涨</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Light is transmitted in the form of waves. 光以波的形式传播。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> wavy（adj. 波动的；波状的）</p>
hat@［hæt］@n. 帽子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My mother bought me a beautiful hat as my birthday gift. 妈妈给我买了一顶漂亮的帽子作为生日礼物。</p>
January@［ˈdʒænjuəri］@n. 一月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are 31 days in January. 一月份有31天。</p>
cheap@［tʃi:p］@adj. 便宜的，廉价的；劣质的，低劣的；卑鄙的，低级的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Taking buses in Beijing is ______ than taking a taxi. （2009年 吉林）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. more cheap</p> <p class="bodytext">B. much cheaper</p> <p class="bodytext">C. a little cheap</p> <p class="bodytext">D. less cheaper</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>在北京乘公交车比打车要便宜得多。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>cheap的比较级是cheaper，可以用much来修饰，不能用more或者less表示比较级，而a little是“一点儿”的意思，故选B。</p>
paper@［ˈpeipə(r)］@n. 纸，墙纸；报纸；文件；文章，论文；书面作业，试卷</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'd like to buy some red and green paper. 我想买一些红色和绿色的纸。</p>
scientific@［ˌsaiənˈtifik］@adj. 科学的，科学上的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a new scientific discovery in the field of physics. 在物理学领域有一个新的科学发现。</p>
fat@［fæt］@adj. 肥胖的；多脂肪的 n. 脂肪；肥肉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is very easy to get fat if you eat too much candy. 吃太多糖果很容易发胖。</p>
experiment@［ikˈsperimənt］@n. 实验，试验 v. 进行试验，做实验</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> do experiments 做实验</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our class will have an experiment in the laboratory tomorrow. 我们班明天要去实验室做实验。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00249.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext2">experiment, test</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都可以表示“试验，实验”的意思，但是test还可以指测试或医学检查。</p></div>
encourage@［inˈkʌridʒ］@v. 鼓励；激励，促进</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：en（使）+courage（精神）→使有精神→激励</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> encourage sb. to do sth. 鼓励某人做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">______ by the advances in technology, many farmers have set up wind farms on their land.（2009年 天津）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. Being encouraged</p> <p class="bodytext">B. Encouraging</p> <p class="bodytext">C. Encouraged</p> <p class="bodytext">D. Having encouraged</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>受到科技进步的激励，许多农民在他们的农场上建造了风力发电场。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>在这里encourage有被动含义，因此需要用过去分词，故选C。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> encouragement（n. 鼓励，激励）</p>
touch@［tʌtʃ］@v. 触摸，碰到；接触，涉及 n. 接触，碰到；触觉；修饰，润色；风格，手法</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> get in touch （with sb.） （和某人）取得联系；be/keep/stay in touch （with sb.）（与某人）保持联系</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I kept in touch with my primary school teachers. 我与小学老师一直保持着联系。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> touchable（adj. 可触的）；touching（adj. 感人的，动人的）</p> <div class="xian">  <p class="bodytext7">get in touch with, keep in touch with</p>   <p class="bodytext">get in touch with是“跟…取得联系”，侧重于联系到某人，强调动作；而keep in touch with是“跟…保持联系”，强调状态。</p></div>
spring@［spriŋ］@n. 春天，春季；弹簧，发条；（源）泉；跳，跃</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［sprang-sprung］ 跳，突然行动；涌现，突然出现；突然提出（或说出）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is usually cold, but sunny in early spring. 早春时节通常很冷，但是阳光明媚。// With a spring, the cat leapt onto the table. 这只猫纵身一跃，跳到了桌子上面。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> springy（adj. 有弹性的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00250.jpeg"/></div>
plenty@［ˈplenti］@n. 丰富，充足，大量</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> plenty of 许多的，充裕的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is plenty of rain this year. 今年雨水很充沛。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">  <p class="bodytext3">plenty of 既可以修饰可数名词，也可以修饰不可数名词，如：plenty of eggs 许多鸡蛋，plenty of time 充裕的时间。另外，a lot of与lots of也是“许多，大量”的意思，都是既可以修饰可数名词，也可以修饰不可数名词，其谓语动词的单复数要依修饰的名词而定。</p></div>
concert@［ˈkɒnsɜ:ｔ］@n. 音乐会，演奏会</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The world famous concert will be given this Saturday. 世界闻名的音乐会将在本周六上演。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> concerted（adj. 一致的，协调的；互相配合的）</p>
Russia@［ˈrʌʃə］@n. 俄国，俄罗斯</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The capital of Russia is Moscow. 俄罗斯的首都是莫斯科。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> Russian（n. 俄国人）</p>
unfriendly@［ʌnˈfrendli］@adj. 不友好的，冷漠的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：un（不）+friendly（友好的）→不友好的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My colleagues were so unfriendly to me before. 以前，同事们对我很不友善。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00251.jpeg"/></div>
happy@［ˈhæpi］@adj. 快乐的，愉快的；幸福的；令人满意的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I really had a happy time in my hometown last summer holiday. 去年暑假我在家乡度过了一段非常愉快的时光。</p>
because@［biˈkɒz］@conj. 因为</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> because of 由于，因为</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Betty didn't come to school yesterday ______ she was ill. （2008年 北京）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. but</p> <p class="bodytext">B. than</p> <p class="bodytext">C. if</p> <p class="bodytext">D. because</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>贝蒂昨天没来学校，因为她生病了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查连词的用法。but表示转折关系；than表示比较；if表示条件关系；只有because可以表示因果，故选D。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext5">because of, as a result</p>   <p class="bodytext">这两个短语都表示因果关系，注意它们的区别。because of 意为“由于”，后面接原因；as a result 意为“因此”，后面接结果。</p></div>
suit@［su:t］@n. 一套衣服（或西服）；套</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 合适，适合；中…的意，相配</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> suit to 与…相称</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The famous actor is wearing a black suit. 那位著名的演员穿着一套黑西装。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> suitable（adj. 相配的；合适的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00057.jpeg"/></div>
bank@［bæŋk］@n. 银行；库；（河等的）岸，堤 v. 把（钱）存入银行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a bank on this street. 这条街上有家银行。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">bank, shore</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“岸”的意思。前者指河岸，而后者指海岸。</p></div>
dinner@［ˈdinə(r)］@n. 正餐，主餐；宴会</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to have some porridge as dinner. 正餐我想喝点粥。</p>
fly@［flai］@v. ［flew-flown］ 乘飞机；飞；飘荡，飘扬；飞跑，飞逝；空运 n. 苍蝇；飞行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will fly to New York next week. 我下周要坐飞机去纽约。// It was so annoying that there was a fly buzzing all around me. 有一只苍蝇老在我周围嗡嗡，烦死了。</p>
travel@［ˈtrævl］@n. 旅行，游历 v. 旅行；行进；被传送，被传播；走过，驶过</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You should visit Big Ben when you travel to London. 你去伦敦旅行的话应该参观一下大本钟。</p>
wet@［wet］@adj. 湿的，潮的；多雨的，雨天的 v. 把…弄湿，使潮湿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She used a wet cloth to clean the kitchen. 她用湿布来清洁厨房。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00058.jpeg"/></div>
behind@［biˈhaind］@prep. 在…的背后，在（向）…的后面；落后于；支持，赞成；是…的原因</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 在（向）背后；（落）在后面；（留）在原处</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The bus station is behind the red building. 公交车站在那幢红色的建筑后面。</p>
English@［ˈiŋgliʃ］@n. 英语 adj. 英语的；英国的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I take my English book with me every day. 我每天都带着英语书。</p>
calm@［ka:m］@adj. 镇静的，镇定的；平静的，无风的 v. （使）平静；（使）镇静</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：接到求救电话（call），心里久久不能平静（calm）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> calm down （使）平静下来，（使）镇定下来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I tried my best to calm down but I failed. 我尽最大努力让自己平静下来，但是失败了。</p>
young@［jʌŋ］@adj. 年轻的，青年的；没有经验的；初期的 n. 青年人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：你们（you）都是年轻人（young）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Young people are the future of a nation. 年轻人是一个国家的未来。</p>
cream@［ˈkri:m］@n. 奶油；护肤霜；奶油色 adj. 奶油色的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to have cream in my coffee. 我想在咖啡里加奶油。</p>
scene@［si:n］@n. （戏剧的）一场，（电影、电视的）一个镜头，（小说等的）一节；（戏剧、事件等发生的）地点，背景，现场；景色，景象</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The audience were all moved by the opening scene. 观众们都被开始时的一幕打动了。</p>
thrill@［θril］@n. 兴奋，激动；引起激动的事物；震动，颤抖</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. （使）非常兴奋，（使）非常激动；抖动，颤抖</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：thr+ill（生病的）→病人不宜太激动→激动</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It really gave me a big thrill to meet my favourite writer in the Book Building. 能在图书大厦遇到我最喜欢的作家，我非常激动。</p>
July@［dʒuˈlai］@n. 七月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will have my summer vacation in July. 我七月放暑假。</p>
jungle@［ˈdʒʌŋgl］@n. （热带）丛林，密林</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Compared with my neighbor's, our garden is a complete jungle. 跟邻居家的花园相比，我家的花园简直就是一片丛林。</p>
dismiss@［disˈmis］@v. 不予考虑，不接受；解雇，开除；解散，遣散；驳回，不受理</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：dis+miss（想念）→不思不想，拒不接受→不接受</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom was dismissed because he had made a serious mistake.汤姆犯了严重的错误，被解雇了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> dismissal（n. 不考虑；解雇）</p>
hen@［hen］@n. 母鸡；雌禽</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：拿钢笔（pen），画母鸡（hen）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The hen laid a large brown egg. 母鸡下了一只大红皮蛋。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">hen, cock, chick</p>   <p class="bodytext">都有“鸡”的意思，但是所指不同。hen指的是母鸡，cock指的是公鸡，而chick指的是小鸡。</p></div> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00059.jpeg"/></div>
couple@［ˈkʌpl］@n. 夫妻，情侣；数个 v. 使成对；结合，结婚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：coup（看作cup，杯）+le→喝了交杯酒，成为夫妇→夫妻</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a couple of 几个；一对</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I saw the young couple watering the flowers in the garden. 我看见这对年轻夫妇在花园里浇花。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00060.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">couple, pair</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“对”的意思，但是所指不同。couple指任何两件同类的东西，如：a couple of cats 一对猫，而pair指两个不能分开使用的东西或两个相连的物体，如：a pair of eyes 一双眼睛。</p></div>
symbol@［ˈsimbl］@n. 符号，标志；象征</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：符号（symbol）是为了把意思用简单的（simple）方式表达出来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The dove and olive branch are symbols of peace. 鸽子和橄榄枝是和平的象征。</p>
fifteenth@［ˌfifˈti:nθ］@num. 第十五 n. 十五分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The love story happened in the fifteenth century. 这个爱情故事发生在15世纪。</p>
receive@［riˈsi:v］@v. 收到，接到；受到，遭到；接待；接见；欢迎</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Rita received a phone call from her mother. 丽塔接到妈妈的电话。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00061.jpeg"/></div>
plate@［pleit］@n. 盘子；金属牌；（照相用的）感光底片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My mom loves beautiful ceramic plates. 我妈妈喜欢漂亮的瓷盘子。</p>
walk@［wɔ:k］@v. 步行，散步；陪…走，护送…走</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 步行，散步；行走的路程（或距离）；散步场所，人行道</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：很多人步行（walk）去工作（work）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> go for a walk 散步；walk out 走出；walk around （sth.） 四处走走；绕着某物走</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's only five minutes' walk from my house to the bus station. 从我家里到公交车站只需要走五分钟。</p>
zero@［ˈziərəʊ］@num. 零 n. 零点，零度</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He got zero in Math. 他数学考了零分。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">当zero表示温度的时候，“零上”用above，“零下”用below，如：ten degrees above zero 零上10度，five degrees below zero 零下5度。</p></div>
riendship@［ˈfrendʃip］@n. 友谊，友好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Real friendship is more precious than gold. 真正的友谊比金子更珍贵。</p>
ear@［iə(r)］@n. 耳，耳朵；听力，听觉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：耳（ear）听（hear）八方</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary cried when the news reached her ears. 听到消息时玛丽哭了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00062.jpeg"/></div>
plain@［plein］@adj. 清晰的，明白的；相貌平平的，无姿色的；不矫饰的，朴素的 n. 平原</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：生活中，疼痛（pain）在所难免，再平常（plain）不过</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's plain that he told a lie. 很明显他说了谎。</p>
machine@［məˈʃi:n］@n. 机器，机械</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to learn the skill of running a machine. 我需要学习操作机器的技术。</p>
wait@［weit］@v. 等，等候；服侍，侍候 n. 等待，等待的时间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> wait for 等待；wait on 服侍，招待；wait a minute 等一下；can't wait to do sth. 迫不及待要做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many people are waiting for the bus in the bus station. 车站有很多人在等公交车。</p>
laugh@［la:f］@v. 笑 n. 笑，笑声</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> laugh at 嘲笑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You shouldn't laugh at others. It's impolite. 你不应该嘲笑别人。这很不礼貌。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00063.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">laugh, smile</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“笑”的意思。laugh强调出声的大笑，不但有面部表情，还有声音和动作，如：There is a loud laugh from the room. 屋里传来一阵大笑声。而smile指的是微笑，如：There is a big smile on her face. 她的脸上露出灿烂的笑容。</p></div>
math/maths@［ｍæθ; ｍæθｓ］@n. 数学</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy was not good at math. 这个小男孩不擅长数学。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00064.jpeg"/></div>
Friday@［ˈfraidei; -di］@n. 星期五</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a speech competition this Friday. 这周五有一场演讲比赛。</p>
eat@［i:t］@v. ［ate-eaten］ 吃，吃饭</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：心急吃（eat）不了热（heat）豆腐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She ate an apple before lunch. 午饭前她吃了个苹果。</p>
unpleasant@［ʌnˈpleznt］@adj. 使人不愉快的，厌恶的；煞风景的；（两人之间）不和的，不客气的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：un（不）+pleasant（令人愉快的）→使人不愉快的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The relationship between the two friends has become cold after an unpleasant quarrel. 一次不愉快的争吵后，这两个朋友之间的关系变得冷淡了。</p>
natural@［ˈnætʃrəl］@adj. 自然的，正常的；出于本性的，天赋的；自然界的，天然的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：natur（nature，大自然）+al（形容词后缀）→自然的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We visited a village of natural beauty. 我们参观了一个自然风景优美的村庄。</p>
asleep@［əˈsli:p］@adj. 睡着的，睡熟的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：a（…的）+sleep（睡觉）→睡着的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> fall asleep 入睡，睡着</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The medicine can help you fall asleep. 这种药有助于你入睡。</p>
private@［ˈpraivət］@adj. 私人的，个人的；秘密的，私下的；私立的，私营的 n. 士兵，列兵</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in private 私下里，秘密地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This report is private, and only the teacher, the student and his or her parents can see it. 这份报告是保密的，只有老师、学生以及该学生的家长可以看。</p>
translate@［ˈtrænsleit］@v. 翻译</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：trans（转）+late→将一种语言转为另外一种语言→翻译</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is difficult to translate this Chinese poem into English. 将这首中文诗歌翻译成英文很难。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">translate, interpret</p>   <p class="bodytext">translate侧重于笔译，也有“解释”和“转变”的意思，如：It's difficult to translate this book. 翻译这本书太难了。而interpret侧重于口译，还含有“说明”的意思，如：I will interpret when the foreign guest speaks. 外宾讲话的时候，我来翻译。</p></div>
knife@［naif］@n. 刀，餐刀</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Paul cut the apple with a knife. 保罗用刀将苹果切开。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">knife的复数不是在结尾加s，而是把fe变为v加es，即knives，考生要特别注意。</p></div>
indoors@［ˌinˈdɔ:z］@adv. 在屋内，在室内</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The party will be held indoors in the event of rain. 如果下雨的话，聚会就在室内进行。</p>
milk@［milk］@n. 牛奶 v. 挤（奶）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy didn't want to drink the milk. 男孩不想喝牛奶。</p>
feel@［fi:l］@v. ［felt-felt］ 摸，触摸；感觉到，感受到 n. 手感；触摸；感受</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> feel like doing sth. 想做某事；feel as if/though 仿佛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am hungry and feel like eating. 我饿了，想吃东西。</p>
type@［taip］@n. 类型，种类；铅字 v. （用打字机等）打（字）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This type of MP4 is my favorite, but I can't afford it. 这款MP4是我最喜欢的，但是我买不起。</p>
rush@［rʌʃ］@v. （使）冲，（使）突进，急速流动；仓促行事；猛冲 n. 冲，奔，急速行进；匆忙，急迫；（交通、事务等的）繁忙，（一天、一周等中的）繁忙时刻 adj. （交通）繁忙的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> rush hour （上下班时的）交通高峰期</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Kids all rushed up the stairs to fetch the gifts. 孩子们都跑上楼去拿礼物。// I went to school in a rush yesterday. 我昨天匆忙地赶往学校。</p>
teen@［ˈti:n］@n. 少年男女，青少年 adj. 青少年的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This pop star is a teen idol. 这个流行音乐歌星是青少年的偶像。</p>
it@［it］@pron. 它；他（指婴儿，尤指性别不详者）；（谈论天气、时间、距离等用作主语）；（用作形式主语、形式宾语）；（构成强调句型）；（用于谈论情况）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It must be my uncle who is knocking at the door. 一定是我叔叔在敲门。</p>
dessert@［diˈzɜ:t］@n. （餐后）甜食，甜点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：此甜点（dessert）美其名曰“沙漠（desert）飞狐”</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to have ice cream for dessert. 甜点我想要冰淇淋。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00065.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">考生注意不要把该词和desert弄混淆，后者意为“沙漠”。二者词形和发音都很接近。</p></div>
drop@［drɒp］@v. ［dropped-dropped］ （使）落下；（使）下降；略去；停止；放弃 n. 下降，下跌；滴；微量，一点点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> drop in/by 顺便拜访；drop off 离开；让某人下车；drop in on sb. 顺便拜访某人；drop in at 顺便拜访某地；drop out 放弃</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A drop of sunlight falls down from the sky. 从天上射下一缕阳光。</p>
three@［θri:］@num. 三，三个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are three monkeys in the picture. 图片上有三只猴子。</p>
post@［pəʊst］@n. 职位，岗位 ；（支）柱，标杆；（速度竞赛的）起点或终点标志</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 投寄，邮寄；贴出</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I posted the letter to Lucy the day before yesterday. 我前天把写给露西的信寄了出去。</p>
eighth@［ˈeitθ］@num. 第八 n. 八分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The eighth of March is Women's Day. 3月8日是妇女节。</p>
such@［sʌtʃ］@adj. 这样的，这种的；那么的，如此程度的；上述的，该 adv. 那么</p> <p class="bodytext1">pron. 这样的人（或事物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> such as 诸如，例如</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lily is such a nice girl that all her classmates like her. 莉莉是一个很好的女孩，她的同学都喜欢她。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext5">such... that..., so... that...</p>   <p class="bodytext">两个词组都表示“如此…以至于…”。但是so后边加的是形容词或副词，而such后面接的是名词，当然，这个名词可由形容词修饰。但如果后面的名词由many, much, few, little等词修饰，则不用such而用so，如：There are so many people that we can't go through. 人太多了，我们过不去。而不能说There are such many people that we can't go through.</p></div>
egg@［eg］@n. 蛋；卵</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I had eggs for breakfast this morning. 我早晨吃的是鸡蛋。</p>
cut@［kʌt］@v. ［cut-cut, cutting］ 切，剪；修剪，剪短；割破，划破；减少，削减；中断，停止</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 伤口，切口；削减，降低；修剪，裁剪；理发</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> cut down 砍倒，削减；cut in 插嘴，插入；cut off 切断</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Be careful not to cut your finger. 小心，不要切到手。// There will be a cut in staff. 员工人数将进行缩减。</p>
also@［ˈɔ:lsəʊ］@adv. 而且，也，此外（还）；同样</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">______ Tom ______ Mary speaks good Chinese, so they can communicate with these Chinese students very well. （2009年 兰州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. Neither, nor</p> <p class="bodytext">B. Not only, but also</p> <p class="bodytext">C. Both, and</p> <p class="bodytext">D. Either, or</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>不光汤姆的汉语说得不错，玛丽也是如此，因此他们能和这些中国学生很好地交流。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查几个重点固定搭配的用法。neither...nor...表示“两者都不”，与句意相反。both...and...表示“两者都”，但是谓语要用复数。either...or...表示“要么…要么…”，含有从二者中进行选择的意味，与句意不符。not only...but also...表示“不但…而且…”，谓语动词遵循就近原则，由but also后面的名词决定谓语的单复数，因此选B。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">also, too, either</p>   <p class="bodytext">三者都有“也”之意。also常用在句中，如：I also like music. 我也喜欢音乐。too常放在结尾，如：I like music, too. 我也喜欢音乐。either表示“也”的时候只用在否定句中，位于句子结尾，如：I don't like music, either. 我也不喜欢音乐。</p></div>
method@［ˈmeθəd］@n. 方法，办法；秩序，条理</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do you have good methods of learning English? 你有学习英语的好方法吗？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> methodical（adj. 有条不紊的）；methodology（n. 方法论）</p>
staff@［sta:f］@n. 全体职工，工作人员；杠，棒；参谋部 v. 为…配备人员，任职于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：每个明星（star）后面都跟着一帮工作人员（staff）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The staff in our company all work very hard. 我们公司的员工工作都非常努力。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> staffing（n. 安置职工）</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">staff, crew</p>   <p class="bodytext">staff主要指商务、教育、机关等领域的工作人员；crew特指飞机、轮船、列车等交通工具上的全体工作人员。</p></div>
dull@［dʌl］@adj. 乏味的，单调的；（色彩等）晦暗的；愚钝的，笨的；钝的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：生活充满（full）艰辛，单调无味（dull）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My diet is dull and boring. 我的食谱单调乏味。</p>
metal@［ˈmetl］@n. 金属</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have never seen this kind of metal. 我从来没有见过这种金属。</p>
perhaps@［pəˈhæps］@adv. 或许，大概，可能</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Perhaps I can do the same job better next time. 也许下次我能把相同的工作做得更好。</p>
huge@［hju:dʒ］@adj. 庞大的，巨大的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The discount was huge in this mall. 这家商场的打折幅度非常大。</p>
degree@［diˈgri:］@n. 度，度数；程度；学位；地位，身份</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：和agree（v. 同意）一起记</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I agree with my teacher to a certain degree. 我在一定程度上同意老师的看法。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00066.jpeg"/></div>
body@［ˈbɒdi］@n. 身体，躯体；躯干，主体；尸体；物体；（视作整体的）一群，一批</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Arms are parts of our body. 胳膊是我们身体的一部分。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00067.jpeg"/></div>
pretend@［priˈtend］@v. 假装，佯作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Little Tom pretended to know the answer to the question. 小汤姆假装知道问题的答案。</p>
lie@［lai］@v. ［lay-lain, lying］ 躺，平放；位于；处于（某种状态）；（问题、事情等）在于；［lied-lied, lying］ 说谎 n. 谎话，假话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a white lie 善意的谎言；lie down 躺下；lie in 存在于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many women lie about their age. 许多女人都会谎报她们的年龄。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00068.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">考生要特别注意，lie在作“说谎”讲时，其现在分词、过去式、过去分词分别是lying, lied, lied；作“平躺”讲时，其现在分词、过去式、过去分词分别是lying, lay, lain。</p></div>
tag@［tæg］@n. 标签；附加语 v. ［tagged-tagged, tagging］ 给…加标签；添加</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I didn't notice the price tag until I tried them on. 我试完衣服之后，才注意到价签。</p>
homeless@［ˈhəʊmləs］@adj. 无家的，无家可归的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little girl has sympathy for homeless pets. 小女孩对无家可归的小动物充满了同情。</p>
shoulder@［ˈʃəʊldə(r)］@n. 肩（部） v. 肩负，承担</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：肩膀（shoulder）就应当（should）扛起责任</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The witch has a crow on her right shoulder. 巫婆的右肩上站着一只乌鸦。</p>
hit@［hit］@v. ［hit-hit; hitting］ 打，击中；碰撞</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 一击，击中；轰动一时的人或事物，成功而风行一时的事物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：谁打（hit）了他（him）？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> hit on 偶然发现</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I hit the thief on his head with my bag. 我用包打了小偷的脑袋。</p>
hand@［hænd］@n. 手；指针；帮助，援助；手艺，技能 v. 交，给</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> hand in 上交；hand out 分发；be at hand 在手边；即将到来；hand over 移交；hand in hand 手拉手；联合；in hand 在手头上；在掌握中；give sb. a hand 帮助某人；hand down 把…传下去</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Please hand me the magazine. 请把杂志递给我。</p>
rat@［ræt］@n. 鼠</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are rats in our house. 我们房子里有老鼠。</p>
particular@［pəˈtikjələ(r)］@adj. 特定的，某一的；不寻常的，特别的，特有的；（过分）讲究的，挑剔的；详细的，详尽的 n. 详情，细目</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in particular 特别，尤其</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can still remember the particular smile of the teacher. 我还能记得那位老师特有的微笑。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> particularity（n. 特性，特殊性）；particularly（adv. 特别，尤其）</p>
organize@［ˈɔ:gənaiz］@v. 组织，安排；使有条理；使有机化</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The workers organized a party to celebrate the festival. 工人们组织了一次聚会来庆祝节日。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> organization（n. 组织）</p>
stay@［stei］@v. 逗留，暂住；保持，继续是；停止，延缓 n. 逗留，停留</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> stay up 熬夜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Don't ______ too late, or you will feel tired in class.</p> <p class="bodytext">— I won't, Mum. Good night！（2006年 德州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. wake up</p> <p class="bodytext">B. get up</p> <p class="bodytext">C. stand up</p> <p class="bodytext">D. stay up</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 不要熬夜，否则你在课堂上会感觉很疲惫。</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 我不会的，妈妈，晚安！</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查动词短语的用法区别。wake up是“醒过来”，get up是“起床”，stand up是“站起来，起立”，stay up表示“熬夜”。根据句意，本题选D。</p>
brother@［ˈbrʌðə(r)］@n. 兄弟；教友，会友</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The two brothers never saw each other again until 1949. 两兄弟直到1949年才再次相见。</p>
law@［lɔ:］@n. 法律，法规；法学；律师行业；规律，法则</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> In Sweden it is against the law to sell alcohol to children. 在瑞典，卖酒给孩子是违法的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> lawyer（n. 律师）</p>
son@［sʌn］@n. 儿子；孩子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> John has two sons and a daughter. 约翰有两个儿子、一个女儿。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00069.jpeg"/></div>
comfortable@［ˈkʌmftəbl］@adj. 舒适的，舒服的；宽裕的，小康的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These new shoes are not that beautiful but very comfortable. 这双新鞋不是很漂亮，但是很舒服。</p>
hardly@［ˈha:dli］@adv. 几乎不，简直不；刚刚，仅仅</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I could hardly believe I was the winner. 我几乎不敢相信自己是冠军。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">hardly表示否定含义，位于句首时，句子要局部倒装。如：Hardly did I believe what he said. 我几乎不相信他说的话。</p></div>
store@［stɔ:(r)］@n. 商店，店铺；贮存，储备；储备品；仓库 v. 贮藏，储备，存储</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Linda likes to store food so she always buys a lot of food each time. 琳达非常喜欢储藏食物，所以每次总是买很多食物。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">out of store是“耗尽”的意思，也有“售完，卖完”的意思，如：The book was out of store last week. 这本书上周卖完了。</p></div>
raincoat@［ˈreinkəʊt］@n. 雨衣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：rain（下雨）+coat（外套）→下雨时穿的外套→雨衣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Bring a raincoat with you in case it rains. 带上雨衣以防下雨。</p>
Yin@［jin］@n. 阴</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Yin and Yang are special features of the Chinese culture. 阴阳是中国文化的特点。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00070.jpeg"/></div>
noise@［nɔiz］@n. 声音，响声；噪音</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There was too much noise outside the house. 房子外面有很大的噪音。</p>
fire@［ˈfaiə(r)］@n. 火，炉火；火灾，失火；射击，火力 v. 放（枪、炮等），射出（子弹等）；解雇，开除</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：红红火火（fire），越来越好（fine）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> catch fire 着火；make a fire 生火；set fire to 放火；（be） on fire 着火，起火；fire at sb./sth. 朝…射击</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We have to ask for help because the house is on fire. 我们必须求救，因为房子着火了。</p>
drive@［draiv］@v. ［drove-driven］ 驾驶；驾车送（人）；迫使，驱使；推动 n. 驱车旅行；干劲</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Remember to drive carefully especially at night. 记住要小心驾驶，尤其是晚上。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> driver（n. 驾驶员，司机）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">drive的常用结构是“drive sb.+地点”，表示“载某人去某地”，如：drive me home 载我回家。</p></div>
stamp@［stæmp］@n. 邮票，印花；印，图章；标志，印记；跺脚，顿足</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 跺（脚），踩踏；在…上盖印，盖上（字样）；重步走</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My boyfriend is a stamp collector. 我的男朋友是一个集邮爱好者。</p>
edge@［edʒ］@n. 边，边缘；刀口，刃；优势，优越地位</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“挨挤”→被挤到了边缘→边缘</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> at the edge of 在…的边缘</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The edge of the knife is very sharp. 刀刃很锋利。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00071.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">edge, border</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“边”的意思，但是所指不同。edge常指刀等的边缘，而border常指边界。</p></div>
medal@［ˈmedl］@n. 奖牌，奖章</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：奖牌（medal）通常都是由金属（metal）制成的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Chinese Team won the gold medal in the match. 中国队在比赛中获得了金牌。</p>
neighbor@［ˈneibə(r)］@n. 邻居；邻国</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I want to get along well with my neighbors. 我想跟我的邻居们友好相处。</p>
remember@［riˈmembə(r)］@v. 记得，记住；缅怀；代…问候</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：re（又，再）+member（成员）→再次想起这个成员→记得</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The first thing you must do is to remember what your dream is. 你首先要做的是记住自己的梦想是什么。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">remember后面既可以跟不定式，也可以跟动名词，二者是有区别的。remember to do sth.表示“记得做某事”（还没有做），而remember doing sth.是“记得曾做过某事”（已经做过）。比较下面两个句子：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Remember to turn off the lights when you leave the room. 离开房间之前，记得把灯关上。（现在还没有关灯）</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I remembered turning off the lights when I left the room. 我记得我离开房间时关了灯。（灯已经关了）</p></div>
smart@［sma:t］@adj. 聪明的，精明的，高明的；漂亮的 n. 剧痛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lucy seems very smart in her new suit. 露西穿上新套装，看起来精明能干。</p>
leg@［leg］@n. 腿，腿部；（桌、椅等的）腿，（建筑物的）支柱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：抱腿（leg）乞求（beg）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The chair has only three legs so it can't stand firmly. 这把椅子只有三条腿，所以站不稳。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00072.jpeg"/></div>
relation@［riˈleiʃn］@n. 关系，关联；亲属，亲戚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in/with relation to 与…相关；涉及…；in relation to the murder 涉嫌谋杀</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can't see any relation between the two problems. 我看不出两个问题之间有何关系。</p>
singer@［ˈsiŋə(r)］@n. 歌手</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She's a world famous singer. 她是一位世界闻名的歌手。</p>
hello@［həˈləʊ］@int. 喂，你好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> They say hello to each other when they meet. 碰面的时候他们互相问好。</p>
nine@［nain］@num. 九，九个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old lady had nine children but five died. 这位老太太有九个儿女，但是五个都死了。</p>
swing@［swiŋ］@v. ［swang-swung］ （使）摇摆，（使）摇荡；回转，旋转；（使）突然转向</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 摆动，摇摆；秋千</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：挥着（swing）翅膀（wing）的天使</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The kids are playing on the swings in the park. 孩子们正在公园里荡秋千。</p>
creature@［ˈkri:tʃə(r)］@n. 生物，动物，人；创造物，产物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：人（creature）物生动，特征（feature）鲜明</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Pandas are precious creatures. 熊猫是珍稀动物。</p>
worry@［ˈwʌri］@v. （使）担心，（使）发愁；困扰，折磨 n. 担心，发愁，忧虑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> worry about 担忧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Don't worry if you don't understand what the teacher said in class. 课堂上听不懂老师讲课，不要担心。</p>
southeast@［ˌsaʊˈθi:st］@n. 东南（方），东南（部） adv. 向东南 adj. 东南方的，东南部的，来自东南的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：south（南方）+east（东方）→东南方</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There used to be a beautiful garden in the southeast part of the city. 这座城市的东南部曾经有一个漂亮的花园。</p>
custom@［ˈkʌstəm］@n. 习惯，风俗；惯例；［pl.］ 海关；关税</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's a local custom to exchange gifts at the first meeting. 第一次见面时互换礼物是当地的风俗。</p>
bear@［beə(r)］@n. 熊 v. ［bore-borne］ 负担；忍受</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：梨（pear）和熊（bear）掌，不可兼得</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a black bear in the zoo. 动物园里有一头黑熊。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> bearish（adj. 熊一样的；粗鲁的）；bearable（adj. 可忍受的）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">bear在作动词“忍受”讲时，其后接动名词，常用在否定句和疑问句中。如：Jim can't bear being laughed at by his classmates. 吉姆无法忍受被同学嘲笑。</p></div>
joy@［dʒɔi］@n. 欢乐，喜悦；乐事，乐趣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：买了玩具（toy），欢乐（joy）无比</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It brings us great joy to go skating. 滑冰给我们带来了很大的乐趣。</p>
ton@［tʌn］@n. 吨；大量，许多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The coal weighs a ton. 这些煤重约1吨。</p>
wealth@［welθ］@n. 财富，财产；丰富，大量</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：健康（health）是最大的财富（wealth）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Wealth is regarded as the symbol of social status. 财富被当做是社会地位的象征。</p>
direct@［diˈrekt; dai-］@adj. 直接的；率直的，坦率的；顺行的 adv. 直接地 v. 把…对准，针对；管理；指导；给…指路；导演；指挥</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The local reporter has direct contact with the refugees. 当地记者与难民有最直接的联系。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> directly（adv. 直接地）；direction（n. 方向；指导）</p>
class@［kla:s］@n. 阶级，社会等级；班，班级；课；种类，门类；等级，级别</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in class 在上课</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The students are having class right now. 学生们现在正在上课。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> classify（v. 分类，归类）</p>
agree@［əˈgri:］@v. 同意，赞同；相符，一致</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> agree with sb. 同意某人的意见；agree on 在…上取得一致；agree to 答应，同意</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Don't worry! I'm sure you'll ______ your classmates if you are kind and friendly to them. （2007年 济南）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. catch up with</p> <p class="bodytext">B. agree with</p> <p class="bodytext">C. get on well with</p> <p class="bodytext">D. make friend with</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>别担心！如果你对同学友善，我相信你会和他们相处得很好的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查介词短语的辨析。catch up with意为“赶上”；agree with意为“同意”；get on well with意为“与…相处融洽”；make friend with意为“与…交朋友”。结合上下文，本题选C。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> agreement（n. 同意；协议）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">agree可以和很多介词连用，要注意不同介词后接的宾语。agree about后常接讨论的话题；agree on后接要确定的事情；agree to后接建议或计划；agree with接人表示“同意某人的意见、想法”，接事物表示“与…一致”。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">They both agree about politics. 他俩政治观点一致。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Can you agree on a date for the interview? 你能不能确定采访的时间？</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Jane agreed to my plan about the holiday. 简同意我的假日计划。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">I can't agree with you. 我无法认同你的观点。</p></div>
tiger@［ˈtaigə(r)］@n. 虎</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are three tigers in this zoo. 这家动物园里有三只老虎。</p>
life@［laif］@n. 生命，性命；一生，寿命；生活，生存；人生；生物；生气，活力</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My life began to change because of the boy. 我的生活因为那个男孩开始发生变化。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">life的复数形式是lives，比较特殊，考生要注意。</p></div>
dream@［dri:m］@n. 梦；梦想，理想 v. ［dreamed/dreamt-dreamed/dreamt］ 做梦，梦想；想到，料到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“追梦”→梦</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> dream of （doing） sth. 梦想（做）某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Last night I dreamed about you. 昨晚我梦见你了。</p>
amazing@［əˈmeiziŋ］@adj. 令人惊异的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Timmy tells me that you have read ______ on the Internet. （2009年 连云港）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. something amazing</p> <p class="bodytext">B. anything amazing</p> <p class="bodytext">C. amazed something</p> <p class="bodytext">D. amazed anything</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>提米告诉我你在网上读到了一些令人惊奇的东西。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>something, anything等词和形容词连用时，应放在形容词前面。anything常用在疑问句中，故选A。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">amazing, amazed</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“惊奇的”之意，但是用法不同。amazing用来形容物，如：an amazing piece of news 一条令人惊奇的消息；amazed用来形容人的感受，如：I am amazed at the man's behavior. 我对那人的行为感到惊奇。</p></div>
set@［set］@n. （一）套，（一）副，（一）批；装置；机组 v. ［set-set, setting］ 放，安置，安装；调整，校正；树立，设定；（日、月等）落山，下沉；凝结，凝固 adj. 不变的，固定的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> set up 建立，建造；set out/off 出发；set aside 留出；set apart分开；set about开始；set fire to / set...on fire 纵火烧；set an example 树立榜样</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Liu Xiang and Yao Ming have set good examples for us. 刘翔和姚明为我们树立了很好的榜样。</p>
helpful@［ˈhelpfl］@adj. 有益的，有用的；给予帮助的，肯帮忙的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's helpful to take an extra pen in the exam. 考试时额外带一支钢笔很有帮助。</p>
general@［ˈdʒenrəl］@adj. 一般的，普通的；普遍的，全体的；笼统的，大体的 n. 将军；一般原则</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in general 一般而言，大体上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> In general, if you study hard, you will pass the exam easily. 一般来说，只要你努力学习，就很容易通过考试。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> generalization（n. 归纳，概括）</p>
root@［ru:t］@n. 根（部）；根本，根源；［pl.］ 祖籍，原籍 v. （使）生根，（使）扎根</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tree roots can cause damage to buildings. 树根会对建筑物造成损坏。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> rooted（adj. 生根的；根深蒂固的）</p>
little@［ˈlitl］@adj. 小的，矮小的；（时间、距离）短的；琐碎的，微不足道的；不多的，少到几乎没有的 n. 极少，几乎没有；短时间，短距离 adv. 少到几乎没有，毫不</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a little 一些，一点；not a little 一点也不；little by little 逐渐地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have a little white cat in my house. 我家里养了一只小白猫。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">little, few</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“少的”之意，表示否定，但是用法不同。little修饰不可数名词，如：Students spent little time on social practice. 学生们几乎不花时间参加社会实践。而few修饰可数名词，如：Few people go to work by car in this district. 这个区几乎没有人开车上班。</p></div>
problem@［ˈprɒbləm］@n. 问题，疑难问题；思考题，讨论题</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People there are checking whether they have health problems. 那里的人正在检查自己是不是有健康问题。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">problem, question</p>   <p class="bodytext">两个词都有“问题”的意思。question指主观存在的疑惑、疑问，是需要解答的，如：I have no question. 我没有问题。problem指客观存在的和遇到的疑难问题，往往是棘手的难题，是需要解决的，如：There are some problems in my work. 我的工作中有一些问题。</p></div>
thirteen@［ˌθɜ:ˈti:n］@num. 十三，十三个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The number thirteen is often considered unlucky in Western countries. 在西方国家，数字13通常被认为是不吉利的。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">thirteen和thirty常在听力中出现，注意thirteen的重音在/ti:n/上，而thirty的重音在第一个音节/θɜ:/上，要注意区分。</p></div>
parrot@［ˈpærət］@n. 鹦鹉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：那只鹦鹉（parrot）爱吃胡萝卜（carrot）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old lady said she wanted to have a parrot. 那个老太太说她想养一只鹦鹉。</p>
throat@［θrəʊt］@n. 咽喉，嗓子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：th+roat（看作road，道路）→咽喉是食物通过的道路→咽喉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have a sore throat today. 我今天嗓子疼。</p>
drum@［drʌm］@n. 鼓；鼓状物（如桶、筒） v. ［drummed-drummed］ 有节奏地敲击</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：敲锣打鼓（drum）卖假药（drug）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> John can play the drums and the guitar. 约翰会敲鼓，还会弹吉他。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> drummer（n. 鼓手）</p>
