blow@［bləʊ］@v. ［blew-blown］ 吹，吹气；吹奏；吹牛 n. 一击</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：风吹（blow）水流（flow）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> blow away 吹走；blow about 炫耀；blow down 刮倒；blow out 吹灭；blow up 使充气；爆炸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The wind is blowing strongly. 风刮得很大。</p>
name@［neim］@n. 名字，名称；名声，名誉</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 给…取名，为…定名；说出…的名字；提名；列举</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> name after 以…来命名</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am a student and my name is Tom. 我是一名学生，我的名字叫汤姆。</p>
whose@［hu:z］@pron. （who的所有格）谁的；那个（人）的，那些（人）的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Whose performance is the best in your team? 你的团队中谁表现得最好？</p>
sausage@［ˈsɒsidʒ］@n. 香肠，腊肠</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like pork sausage rather than chicken sausage. 与鸡肉肠相比，我更喜欢猪肉肠。</p>
future@［ˈfju:tʃə(r)］@adj. 将来的，未来的 n. 将来，今后；前途，前景</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“费油车”→费油的车将来一定会被淘汰→将来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in the future 将来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> In the future, there will be more robots in our life. 未来，我们的生活中会有更多机器人。</p>
could@［kʊd］@v. aux. ［can的过去式］ 可以，能，可能</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Could you tell me how far it is from our school to the zoo? 你可以告诉我从学校到动物园有多远吗？</p>
gold@［gəʊld］@n. 金，黄金；金色 adj. 金的，金制的；金色的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：绿色的童年，金色（gold）的暮年（old）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I want to buy a gold jacket. They are very popular this year. 我想买一件金色的夹克。今年非常流行。</p>
climb@［ˈklaim］@v. 攀登，爬；上升，增长</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We always climb mountains at weekends. 我们周末总是去爬山。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">考生要注意climb的发音，其中b不发音，因此在听力中要留心。</p></div>
catch@［kætʃ］@v. ［caught-caught］ 抓住，接住；偶然（或突然）撞见；染上，感染；赶上，追上；引起，吸引；听清楚，领会</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> catch up with 赶上；catch sight of 看到；catch fire 着火；catch cold 感冒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is so noisy outside that I can't catch what you say. 外面太吵了，我听不清你在说什么。</p>
chicken@［ˈtʃikin］@n. 小鸡；鸡肉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'd like to have fried chicken and Cola. 我想要炸鸡和可乐。</p>
service@［ˈsɜ:vis］@n. 公共设施，公共事业；公用机构，服务机构；服务，劳务；维修，保养</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 提供服务；维修，保养</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Paul registered to be a member of the Volunteer Service Expo. 保罗登记成为一名世博会志愿者。</p>
slow@［sləʊ］@adj. 慢的；迟钝的，不灵巧的；不忙碌的 v. （使）慢下来，减速 adv. 慢慢地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> slow down （使）慢下来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The new student is slow in learning English. 新来的学生英语学得很慢。</p>
bottle@［ˈbɒtl］@n. 瓶子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a bottle of 一瓶…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'd like a bottle of water. 我想喝瓶水。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> bottleful（n. 一瓶之量）；bottleneck（n. 瓶颈）</p>
fifty@［ˈfifti］@num. 五十</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My mother is fifty years old. 我母亲50岁了。</p>
honest@［ˈɒnist］@adj. 诚实的，正直的；坦诚的，直率的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Give me your honest opinion. 把你真实的想法告诉我。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">注意该词的h不发音，在修饰名词时，前面的冠词用an，如：an honest man 一个诚实的人。</p></div>
border@［ˈbɔ:də(r)］@n. 边，边缘；边界，边境 v. 给…加上边，围；邻接，毗连；近似，接近</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：边境（border）的秩序（order）井井有条</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on the border of 在…的边缘；border on 接近</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many people crossed the border between the two countries. 许多人越过两国的边界。</p>
adverb@［ˈædvɜ:b］@n. 副词</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span>“Hard”can be used as an adverb.“hard”可以用做副词。</p>
dislike@［disˈlaik］@n. / v. 不喜欢，讨厌</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：dis+like（喜欢）→不喜欢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Emma dislikes talking with those people. 艾玛不喜欢和那些人交谈。</p>
watch@［wɒtʃ］@v. 注视，观看；看守，监视，照看；小心，当心 n. 表；看管，监视</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> watch out 小心，注意；watch TV 看电视</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The nice watch was made in China. 那块漂亮的手表是中国制造的。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">watch后面跟的介词不一样，含义也大不相同。watch over有“照看，守护”的意思，如：The mother believes an angel will watch over her baby. 那位母亲相信，有位天使会照看她的宝宝。</p></div>
she@［ʃi:］@pron. 她</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She can speak English, French as well as Japanese. 她会说英语、法语和日语。</p>
con@［kɒn］@n. 反对票，反对论</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is no con during the election. 选举过程中没有反对票。</p>
table@［ˈteibl］@n. 桌子，台子；表格</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'd like to buy a new table for my mother. 我想给妈妈买一张新桌子。// There is a display in Table 2 which shows how prices and earnings have increased. 表2体现的是价格与收入的增长情况。</p>
forget@［fəˈget］@v. ［forgot-forgotten］ 忘记，遗忘</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will not forget my friends who helped me when I was poor. 我不会忘记那些在我穷困时帮助过我的朋友。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">forget常接动名词或不定式，但意思不同。forget doing sth.表示某件事已经做过，但忘记了，如: I forget telling him the news. 我忘记已经告诉他这个消息了。forget to do sth.表示忘记了要做的事，如: I forget to tell him the news. 我忘了告诉他这个消息。</p></div>
cute@［kju:t］@adj. 漂亮的，娇小可爱的；聪明的，伶俐的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The new born baby is very cute so the medical staff all like her very much. 这个新生儿非常可爱，所有的医护人员都非常喜欢她。</p>
China@［ˈtʃainə］@n. 中国</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Li Ming is from a remote poor village of China. 李明来自中国偏远地区的一个贫穷的小山村。</p>
voice@［vɔis］@n. 声音，嗓音；发言权；（表达出的）意见；语态</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 说（话），（用言语）表达</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man's voice is so low that no one can hear what he says. 老人的声音太低了，以至于没有人能听到他说的话。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00112.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">voice, sound, noise</p>   <p class="bodytext">voice是指嗓音、声音，侧重于生物发出的嗓音；而sound是自然界各种声音，涵盖voice；noise是噪音，带有厌恶的感情色彩。</p></div>
educate@［ˈedʒukeit］@v. 教育；培养，训练</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is the duty of parents to educate their children. 教育子女是父母的责任。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> education（n. 教育）</p>
song@［sɒŋ］@n. 歌，歌曲；（鸟等的）鸣声，歌声</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：唱（sing）首歌（song）吧！</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our foreign teacher Alice taught us a French song. 我们的外教艾丽斯教了我们一首法语歌曲。</p>
lamb@［læm］@n. 羔羊，小羊；羔羊肉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man said he didn't like eating lamb. 那人说他不喜欢吃羔羊肉。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">lamb, sheep</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“羊”的意思，但是所指不同。lamb指的是小羊，而sheep指的是绵羊。</p></div>
prove@［pru:v］@v. 证明，证实；结果是，原来是</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old treatment method is proved to be the best. 这种古老的治疗方法被证明是最好的。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">prove, justify</p>   <p class="bodytext">两个词都有“证明”的意思。prove是通过经验或实验证明事情的确切性或原理的可靠性，如：The theory was proved to be practical. 这个理论被证明是实用的。而justify是证明某事是正当的，或者某人是有理的，如：The expense was justified as unnecessary. 这项花费被证实是不必要的。</p></div>
for@［fɔ:(r)］@prep. 为，为了；给，供；代替，代表；因为，由于；就…而言；往，向</p> <p class="bodytext1">conj. 因为，由于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> pay for 为…付款；be for 支持，赞成；look for 寻找；care for 关心；照顾；stand for 代表</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Thanks for answering my questions. 谢谢你回答我的问题。</p>
story@［ˈstɔ:ri］@n. 故事，传说，小说；情况，事情；（新闻）报道；（=storey）层</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is boring to listen to the same story for a second and third time. 同一个故事听两三遍很无聊。</p>
lady@［ˈleidi］@n. 女士，小姐；举止文雅的女子，淑女</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mrs. Smith is a lady who has much knowledge. 史密斯夫人是一位知识渊博的女士。</p>
June@［dʒu:n］@n. 六月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is very hot in June in this area. 这个地区的六月非常热。</p>
some@［sʌm］@adj. 一些，若干，有些；某个，某一 pron. 一些，若干 adv. 大约；稍微</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like some fish for supper. 晚餐我想吃鱼。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">some构成的不定代词，如someone, somebody等，主要用于肯定句中；any构成的不定代词，如anyone, anybody等主要用于否定句、疑问句和条件句中。</p></div>
main@［mein］@adj. 主要的；最重要的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：长痛（pain）不如短痛，主要（main）是下决心</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to take the main courses to complete my credits. 我需要上一些主要课程来修满我的学分。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> mainly（adv. 大体上）</p>
solve@［sɒlv］@v. 解决，处理；解答</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is very urgent for mankind to solve the problem of“white pollution”.“白色污染”是人类面临的亟待解决的问题。</p>
language@［ˈlæŋgwidʒ］@n. 语言；措辞；说法</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can speak two languages: Chinese and English. 我会说两种语言：中文和英文。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">表示“说某种语言”要用speak，而不能用say。</p></div>
frog@［frɒg］@n. 蛙</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：井底之蛙（frog）问乌龟从（from）哪里来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The witch turned the prince into a frog. 女巫将王子变成了青蛙。</p>
talent@［ˈtælənt］@n. 天资，才能；人才</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：tal（看作tall，高的）+ent→高手→人才</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She showed considerable talents in the debate. 在辩论会上，她表现得很有才华。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> talented（adj. 有才能的，天才的）</p>
pencil@［ˈpensl］@n. 铅笔</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Have you ever used a pencil to draw a picture? 你曾用铅笔画过图吗？</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00113.jpeg"/></div>
great@［greit］@adj. 大的，极大的；伟大的；重要的；显著的，值得注意的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Susan is a great mother and she loves her child selflessly. 苏珊是一位伟大的母亲，她无私地爱着自己的孩子。</p>
yeah@［jeə］@adv. 是</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Yeah, what he said is true. 是，他所说的是事实。</p>
hotel@［həʊˈtel］@n. 旅馆，宾馆</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to find a hotel nearby. 我需要在附近找一家宾馆。</p>
normal@［ˈnɔ:ml］@adj. 正常的，平常的；正规的，规范的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The temperature of the child was normal. 这个孩子的体温正常。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> normally（adv. 正常地，通常地）；normality （n. 正常）</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">normal, common</p>   <p class="bodytext">normal指的是“正常的”、“正规的”，如：the normal weather 正常的天气。common强调的是“常见的”、“不足为奇的”，如：It's very common to catch a cold in winter. 冬天感冒很正常。</p></div>
door@［dɔ:(r)］@n. 门，出入口；家，户</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：家（door）境贫（poor）寒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man begged for food from door to door. 老人挨家挨户乞讨。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">door, gate</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“门”的意思，注意区分。door指房间的门，gate指房子的大门。</p></div>
cent@［sent］@n. 分，分币</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't have even a cent with me. 我身无分文。</p>
tea@［ti:］@n. 茶（叶）；茶点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like green tea better than black tea. 我喜欢绿茶胜过红茶。</p>
brown@［braʊn］@adj. 棕色的，褐色的 n. 棕色，褐色</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She looks great, with her kind brown eyes. 她有着棕色的眼睛，眼神温和，看上去非常漂亮。</p>
south@［saʊθ］@n. 南（方），南部 adv. 向南方 adj. 南方的，南部的，来自南方的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jim lives in the south part of the city while I live in the north part. 吉姆住在这座城市的南部地区，而我住在北部。</p>
color@［ˈkʌlə］@n. 颜色；颜料；肤色 vt. 给…着色（或染色）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I bought a new watch and the color is black. 我新买了一块黑色的表。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> colorful（adj. 鲜艳的；多姿多彩的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00114.jpeg"/></div>
drug@［drʌg］@n. 药，药物；麻醉药，毒品</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The drug store is still open in the evening. 药店晚上还开着门。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00115.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">drug, pill</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“药”的意思，但是有区别。drug除有“医药”的意思外，另有“毒品”和“有毒药物”的意思；pill是指药片、片剂。</p></div>
rent@［rent］@v. 租借，租用；出租，出借 n. 租金；出租；裂缝，（意见）分歧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will rent a house in this district. 我要在这个地区租一栋房子住。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> rental（adj. 租用的 n. 租金）；rentable（adj. 可出租的）</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">hire, rent</p>   <p class="bodytext">hire是“雇用”的意思，其主语一般为雇主，对象一般是人，如：hire an employee 雇用一名员工。rent是“租用，租赁”的意思，对象一般是物，如：I will rent a house. 我要租一栋房子。</p></div>
northern@［ˈnɔ:ðən］@adj. 北方的，北部的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：north（北方）+ern（形容词后缀）→北方的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can see clearly a star in the northern sky. 我能清晰地看到北方的天空中有颗星星。</p>
everything@［ˈevriθiŋ］@pron. 每件事，一切；最重要的东西</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Don't worry, and everything will be fine. 别担心，一切都会好的。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">在考试中常会考到everything和anything的区别。everything指“每件事”；anything指“任何事”，常用在否定句和疑问句中。</p></div>
funny@［ˈfʌni］@adj. 有趣的，可笑的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The story was so funny that I burst into laughter. 这故事太可笑了，我忍不住哈哈大笑。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00116.jpeg"/></div>
question@［ˈkwestʃən］@n. 问题，议题；疑问；询问；难题，需讨论（或考虑）的问题 v. 询问，审问；怀疑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Why don't you answer my question? 你为什么不回答我的问题？</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext7">out of question, out of the question</p>   <p class="bodytext">out of question意为“没问题，一定”，如：It is out of question that I will visit you next week. 我下周一定会去看你的。out of the question是“不可能”的意思，如：To buy a new bicycle is out of the question because I have no money. 买一辆新的自行车是不可能的，因为我没钱。</p></div>
come@［kʌm］@v. ［came-come］ 来，来到；达到，至；产生（于），来（自）；变成；实现；开始；发生，出现（于）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：回（come）家（home）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> come about 发生；come across 偶然遇到；come along 进展；一起；come from 来自；come in 进来，到达；come on 改善；快点；加油；come out 出来；开花；出版，发表；come to 到达；总计；come true 实现；come up 上来；即将发生</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—Will his new novel ______ in September this year?</p> <p class="bodytext">—Yes, we are all looking forward to it. （2009年 连云港）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. come over</p> <p class="bodytext">B. come back</p> <p class="bodytext">C. come out</p> <p class="bodytext">D. come from</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—他的这部新小说今年九月份可以出版吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">—是的，我们都在期待呢。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>come构成的词组非常多。come over意为“顺便拜访”；come back表示“回来”；come out意为“出来；开花；出版，发表”；come from表示“来自”。本题根据上下文意思应选C。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">come是非延续性动词，不能与表示时间段的状语连用，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（〇） Danny has been here for two weeks. 丹尼来这里两周了。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（✕） Danny has come here for two weeks. 丹尼来这里两周了。</p></div>
route@［ru:t］@n. 路线，路程</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The car took the shortest route. 汽车抄了一条捷径。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">route, path</p>   <p class="bodytext">route表示“路程，路线”，具有抽象含义，如：What's the best route to Beijing University? 去北京大学的最佳路线是什么？path是“路径”的意思，一般指现实中的道路，如: I walked along the path to the deep of the garden. 我沿着小路走到花园深处。</p></div>
temperature@［ˈtemprətʃə(r)］@n. 温度；体温；热度，发烧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You'd better go to the hospital now because your temperature is high. 你最好现在就去医院，因为你的体温很高。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00117.jpeg"/></div>
day@［dei］@n. 天，一昼夜；白昼，白天；时期，时代；工作日；节日，重要日子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> day after day 一天又一天；day and night 夜以继日</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The workers work day and night in order to finish the work on time. 为了按时完成工作，工人们不分昼夜地工作。</p>
skill@［skil］@n. 技能，技巧，手艺；熟练</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> skill in 对…熟练</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> His younger brother learned some skills in repairing bicycles. 他弟弟学了一些修理自行车的手艺。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">skill, technique</p>   <p class="bodytext">skill是“技巧”或“技能”，一般指人物具备的技巧和能力；而technique侧重于科学技术方面的技术。</p></div>
disappointing@［ˌdisəˈpɔintiŋ］@adj. 令人失望的，令人扫兴的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is very disappointing that he failed in the exam. 他考试不及格，真令人失望。</p>
planet@［ˈplænit］@n. 行星</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：宇航局有登陆行星（planet）的计划（plan）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Earth is a planet. 地球是一颗行星。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> planetary（adj. 行星的）</p>
candle@［ˈkændl］@n. 蜡烛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Red candles can set off a festive atmosphere. 红蜡烛可以烘托节日气氛。</p>
bag@［bæg］@n. 袋；（女子的）手提包，旅行袋 v. 把…装进袋子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Kate bought a new bag last week. 凯特上周买了个新包。</p>
explain@［ikˈsplein］@v. 讲解，说明</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：ex（出）+plain（明白的）→说明白→说明</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is difficult to explain the problem to new learners. 很难向初学者解释这个问题。</p>
grow@［grəʊ］@v. ［grew-grown］ 生长，发育；渐渐变得，成为；增长，发展；种植，栽种；留（须、发等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：田里的庄稼长（grow）得好，稻子排成行（row），大豆粒粒饱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> grow up 长大，成年</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tina is growing in confidence gradually. 蒂娜变得越来越自信了。</p>
if@［if］@conj. 如果，假如；是否；即使，虽然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will talk to him if I meet him tomorrow. 如果明天见到他的话，我会跟他谈一下。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">if 在引导条件状语从句时，主句用一般将来时，从句用一般现在时，只要记住“主将从现”就可以了，如：If it's sunny tomorrow, we'll go to the park. 如果明天天晴，我们就去公园。</p></div>
famous@［ˈfeiməs］@adj. 著名的，出名的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be famous for 因…而出名</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The music composed by Mozart is very famous. 莫扎特创作的乐曲非常著名。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">famous还可以与介词as连用，表示“作为…而出名”，注意区分。</p></div>
sixth@［siksθ］@num. 第六（个） n. 六分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Their new house is on the sixth floor. 他们的新房在6层。</p>
summer@［ˈsʌmə(r)］@n. 夏天，夏季</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like playing on the beach during summer vacation. 暑假的时候我喜欢在沙滩上玩耍。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00118.jpeg"/></div>
yes@［jes］@adv. / n. 是，是的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You should answer“yes”or“no”to that question. 你应该用“是”或“否”来回答那个问题。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">注意下面这个问句：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">A: You don't smoke, do you? 你不抽烟，是吗？</p>   <p class="bodytext3">B: No, I don't. / Yes, I do. 是的，我不抽烟。/ 不，我抽烟。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">注意反义疑问句的回答和一般疑问句的回答方式一样，肯定用yes，否定用no。</p></div>
possibly@［ˈpɒsəbli］@adv. 大概，也许</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The couple possibly bought a new house because their old one had been burned. 这对夫妇可能买了一座新房子，因为他们的老房子已被烧毁了。</p>
few@［fju:］@adj. （表示否定）很少，几乎没有 pron. 很少人（或事物）；有些，一些</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a few 少数几个；一些；only a few 只有几个；没有多少；quite a few 相当多；not a few 相当多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A few minutes later, the light turned on. 几分钟后，灯亮了。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">few, bit</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“少”的意思，但是用法不同。few用来修饰可数名词，表示否定，如：Few students understand the question. 几乎没有学生理解这个问题。bit相当于little，修饰不可数名词，常用在a bit这一结构中，如：The coat cost a bit more than I had expected. 这件外套比我预计的要贵一点。</p></div>
itself@［itˈself］@pron. 它自己，它本身；自身，本身</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The company has gotten itself into difficulties. 这家公司身陷困境。</p>
turtle@［ˈtɜ:tl］@n. 海龟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The fisherman caught a large turtle on the shore. 渔民在岸边抓到一只大海龟。</p>
fun@［fʌn］@adj. 有趣的，令人愉快的 n. 有趣的事；乐趣，娱乐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> make fun of sb. 取笑某人，和某人开玩笑；for fun 开玩笑地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— How about going to school by boat, Li Lei?</p> <p class="bodytext">— Good idea. That must be ______ than taking a bus. （2008年 达州）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. much fun</p> <p class="bodytext">B. more much fun</p> <p class="bodytext">C. a lot more fun</p> <p class="bodytext">D. fun</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 李雷，我们划船去学校怎么样？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 好主意，这一定比乘公交车去上学有意思多了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>fun有两种用法，一种是不可数名词，表示“有趣的事，娱乐”，另外一种是作为形容词，表示“有趣的，使人快乐的”，这里选取形容词的意思，a lot more fun是指“有趣得多”，因此本题选C。</p>
quiet@［ˈkwaiət］@adj. 轻声的，安静的，沉默的；平静的，寂静的；温和的，文静的 n. 安静，安宁 v. （使）安静，（使）平静</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tina is a quiet girl and all her classmates like her. 蒂娜是一个文静的小女孩，所有同学都喜欢她。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">quiet与quite读音与拼写都相似，极易混淆，一定要注意。</p></div> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00119.jpeg"/></div>
short@［ʃɔ:t］@adj. 短的，矮的；简短的；短缺的，不足的 adv. 简短地；突然地，唐突地</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. ［pl.］ 短裤</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> short of 缺乏，达不到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The story is short and easy to understand. 这则故事很短，很容易理解。</p>
humorous@［ˈhju:mərəs］@adj. 幽默的，诙谐的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Her husband is very humorous. 她丈夫很幽默。</p>
year@［jiə(r)］@n. 年，年份</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：是啊（yeah），新的一年（year）到了</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many people travel abroad every year. 很多人每年出国旅游。</p>
truth@［tru:θ］@n. 事实，真相；真实性；真理</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tell me the truth, or no one can help you. 跟我说实话，否则没人能帮你。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00120.jpeg"/></div>
prefer@［priˈfɜ:(r)］@v. （to）更喜欢，宁愿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> prefer...to... 宁愿…也不愿…；与……相比，更喜欢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—Tom prefers ______ to ______．</p> <p class="bodytext">—Let's ask him to take part in our dancing club! （2008年 鹤岗）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. singing; dancing</p> <p class="bodytext">B. dancing; singing</p> <p class="bodytext">C. to sing; dance</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—比起唱歌，汤姆更喜欢跳舞。</p> <p class="bodytext4">—那我们邀请他加入我们的舞蹈俱乐部吧！</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本句考查的是短语prefer...to...的用法，它表示“比起…更喜欢…”，to是介词，前后连接的词应是名词或动名词。根据答语中的“加入舞蹈俱乐部”，可知汤姆更喜欢跳舞，故本题选B。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">prefer后面跟动词时，既可跟不定式to do sth.又可以跟动名词doing sth.形式，如：I would prefer to eat out. 我宁愿去下馆子。I prefer walking. 我更喜欢散步。在固定搭配prefer...to...中prefer和to后也跟动名词或名词形式，如：I much prefer jazz to rock music. 比起摇滚乐，我更喜欢爵士乐。</p></div>
shoe@［ʃu:］@n. 鞋</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a shoe shop in the corner of the street. 街角有一家鞋店。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00121.jpeg"/></div>
trash@［træʃ］@n. 垃圾，废物；拙劣的文学（或艺术）作品；没用的人，社会渣滓 v. 捣毁，破坏</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：垃圾（trash）和现金（cash）可不要搞混了</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Everyone would be troubled to see trash everywhere. 每个人看到遍地的垃圾都会觉得不舒服。</p>
lighting@［ˈlaitiŋ］@n. 照明；照明设备；光线</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The musical had excellent sound and lighting effects. 这场音乐剧有很好的音响和灯光效果。</p>
relative@［ˈrelətiv］@adj. 相对的；比较的；有关的，相关的 n. 亲属，亲戚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：亲戚（relative）之间关系（relation）很和睦</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many people lost their relatives and their homes during the severe earthquake. 许多人在这场严重的地震灾害中失去了亲人和家园。</p>
shower@［ˈʃaʊə(r)］@n. 淋浴（器）；阵雨，暴雨 v. 洗淋浴；洒落；纷纷降落</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：去看展会（show），却被阵雨（shower）浇透了</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I enjoy having a hot shower after swimming. 我喜欢在游泳之后，冲个热水澡。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00122.jpeg"/></div>
yourselves@［jɔ:ˈselvz］@pron. 你们自己；你们亲自</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You need to find yourselves new opportunities. 你们需要为自己寻找新的机遇。</p>
cold@［kəʊld］@adj. 冷的，寒冷的；冷淡的，冷酷的 n. 冷，寒冷；伤风，感冒</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm afraid I've got a bad cold. 恐怕我是感冒了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00123.jpeg"/></div>
from@［frəm］@prep. 从…来，出自；离；去除，免掉；从，据；因为，由于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be/come from 来自；from time to time 不时；from now on 从现在起；from...to/till... 从…到…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I will try my best to help friends from all over the world. 我会尽全力帮助来自世界各地的朋友们。</p>
magazine@［ˈmægəzi:n］@n. 杂志，期刊</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We have a weekly magazine titled English Study. 我们有一本名为《英语学习》的周刊。</p>
stone@［stəʊn］@n. 石，石头；宝石；果核</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy threw a stone into the lake. 男孩向湖里扔了一块石头。</p>
window@［ˈwindəʊ］@n. 窗户，窗口</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Would you please open the window? 你能开下窗户吗？</p>
tail@［teil］@n. 尾巴，尾状物；后部，尾部；踪迹 v. 附于其后；尾随，跟踪</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The male peacock has beautiful tail feathers. 雄孔雀有漂亮的尾羽。</p>
develop@［diˈveləp］@v. 发展；开发；研制；成长；患（病）；详尽阐述，发挥；使（胶卷）显影</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The once little boy developed into a strong leader. 曾经的小男孩已经成长为一个强大的领导者了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> development（n. 发展）；undeveloped（adj. 欠发达的）；developing（adj. 发展中的）</p>
angry@［ˈæŋgri］@adj. 生气的，发怒的，愤怒的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be angry with sb. 生某人的气；be angry at （about） 因…而生气</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Yao Ming is one of the best players in NBA. We are all ______ him. （2009年 浙江）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. angry with</p> <p class="bodytext">B. strict with</p> <p class="bodytext">C. worried about</p> <p class="bodytext">D. proud of</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>姚明是NBA最佳球员之一。我们都以他为荣。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查短语的含义。be angry with意为“生…的气”；be strict with意为“对…严格”；be worried about意为“担心…”；be proud of意为“以…为荣”，因此选D。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00124.jpeg"/></div>
please@［pli:z］@int. 请（礼貌用语） v. 使愉快，使高兴；使满意，合…的心意</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Please come in—it's cold outside. 请进，外面很冷。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">please作动词时，一般后面直接跟宾语，如：please sb. 就是“使某人高兴”的意思。</p></div>
outdoor@［ˈaʊtdɔ:(r)］@adj. （在）户外的，（在）野外的 adv. 在户外，在野外</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：out（外面的）+door（门）→在户外的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These boys like outdoor sports. 这些男孩子喜欢户外运动。</p>
close@［kləʊz］@v. 关，关闭；结束，终止；（使）靠拢，（使）接近</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［kləʊs］</span> adj. 密切的，亲密的；近的，接近的；严密的，仔细的；不通风的，闷（热）的 adv. 接近地 n. 结束，终止</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> close to 接近</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The subway station is very close to our dormitory. 地铁站离我们宿舍很近。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> closure（n. 关闭；终止）</p>
plant@［pla:nt］@n. 植物；作物；工厂</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 种植，栽种；（秘密）安放，安置</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：计划（plan）就像植物（plant）一样，不会一下子就形成</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> All plants need water and light. 所有植物都需要水分和阳光。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> plantation（n. 种植园）；planter（n. 种植园经营者）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00125.jpeg"/></div>
page@［peidʒ］@n. 页，张</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I've read several pages of the new book. 我读了几页这本新书。</p>
freeze@［fri:z］@v. ［froze-frozen］ 结冰，凝固 n. 冻结；冰冻期</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：失去自由（free），永远凝固（freeze）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's so cold that even the river has frozen. 天气太冷了，连河水都结冰了。</p>
afraid@［əˈfreid］@adj. 害怕的，恐惧的；犯愁的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm afraid I will be late for school. 我恐怕上学要迟到了。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">afraid后常接of doing sth. 或to do sth. 这两种结构，二者意思有区别。be afraid of doing意为“生怕，恐怕”，指由于客观原因而害怕；而be afraid to do是主观上不敢或胆怯做某事。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Mary was afraid to wake her father. 玛丽不敢去叫醒爸爸。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">Mary was afraid of waking her father. 玛丽生怕吵醒爸爸。</p></div>
help@［help］@v. 帮助，援助；有助于，促进 n. 帮助，援助；帮手，佣人；（呼救时用）救命</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> with the help of 在…的帮助下；help sb. out 帮助某人摆脱困境；帮助某人解决困难；help oneself to sth. 自用某物；can't help doing sth. 忍不住做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Nothing can help me to lighten my pain. 没有什么可以帮我减轻疼痛。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">help在表示“帮助”之意时，可以接动词不定式，也可以接动词原形，接名词时要用help sb. with sth.这一结构。</p></div>
Asia@［ eiʃə］@n. 亚洲</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Susan loves traveling and decides to visit Asia. 苏珊喜欢旅行，她决定去亚洲观光。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> Asian（n. 亚洲人 adj. 亚洲的，亚洲人的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00126.jpeg"/></div>
either@［ˈaiðə(r)］@adj. （两者之中）任一的，每一的 adv. 也</p> <p class="bodytext1">pron. （两者之中的）任何一个，各方</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> either...or... 或者…或者…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You can go to school either by bus or by bike. 你可以乘公交车或骑自行车去上学。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">either常与or连用构成固定搭配，该结构作主语时，谓语动词的单复数遵循就近原则，即由or后面的名词决定，如：Either Tom or I am right. 要么汤姆是对的，要么我是对的。</p></div>
out@［aʊt］@adv. 出，向外；在外，不在（家或办公室）；出现；殆尽，完；大声地，出声地 n. 外面，外观</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Bill doesn't like the sunglasses in the ad because they can't ______ the sun well. （2009年 通化）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. take out</p> <p class="bodytext">B. keep out</p> <p class="bodytext">C. clean out</p> <p class="bodytext">D. look out</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>比尔不喜欢广告里的太阳镜，因为它们的遮光性不好。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是不同的动词跟out搭配的短语的含义。take out意为“拿出，取出，扣除”；keep out意为“使在外”；clean out意为“打扫干净，清除”；look out意为“向外看；当心”。因此应该选B。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00127.jpeg"/></div>
meter@［ˈmi:tə(r)］@n. 米，公尺</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“米特”→米</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The tree is three meters tall. 这棵树有3米高。</p>
box@［bɒks］@n. 箱，盒；包厢 v. 把…装箱（或盒）；（用拳或手掌）打，击；拳击</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I want to buy a box of candy. 我想买一盒糖。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00128.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">box的复数是boxes。以x, s, ch, sh结尾的名词的复数是在结尾加-es。</p></div>
fill@［fil］@v. 装满；使充满（感情）；满足 n. 填满…的量；吃饱的量</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> fill in 填写；fill up sth. with sth. 用…将…填满；be filled with 充满…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little actor's eyes were suddenly filled with tears. 小演员突然热泪盈眶。</p>
place@［pleis］@n. 地方，地点，场所；住所，寓所；地位；资格；名次，等级</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 放置，安置，安排</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take place 发生（不用于被动形式）；take the place of 取代</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I used to study in New York and I'm still fond of that place now. 我过去在纽约上学，现在我仍然喜欢那个地方。</p>
concentrate@［ˈkɒnsntreit］@v. 全神贯注，全力以赴；集中，聚集；浓缩 n. 浓缩物，浓缩液</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：con（共同）+centr（中心）+ate（使…）→使…都到中心→集中</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> concentrate （sth.） on/upon sth. （把某事物）集中在…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I advised my little brother to concentrate more on his study. 我建议弟弟多花些精力在学习上。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> concentration（n. 集中，聚集）</p>
gum@［gʌm］@n. 牙龈；口香糖；树胶</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like chewing mint gum. 我喜欢嚼薄荷味的口香糖。</p>
department@［diˈpa:tmənt］@n. 部，局，处，科；系</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：de+part（部分）+ment→部</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Although I am not a salesperson, I belong to the sales department. 尽管我不是销售员，但是我属于销售部门。</p>
fridge@［fridʒ］@n. 电冰箱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：冰箱（fridge）里的格层像路桥（bridge）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Please fetch some ice for me from the fridge. 去冰箱里帮我拿点冰块。</p>
chat@［tʃæt］@n. / v. ［chatted-chatted, chatting］ 闲谈，聊天</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：戴着帽子（hat）闲聊天（chat）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom has been on the phone for at least 20 minutes chatting with his friend. 汤姆一直占着电话跟朋友聊天，至少有20分钟了。</p>
rubbish@［ˈrʌbiʃ］@n. 垃圾，废物；荒谬的念头（或建议）；废话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can't believe that I've got so much rubbish on my desk. 真不敢相信我的桌上有这么多垃圾。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00129.jpeg"/></div>
plane@［plein］@n. 飞机；平面，水平面</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The plane circled the airport before landing. 飞机着陆前在机场上空盘旋。</p>
point@［pɔint］@n. 要点；观点；点；小数点；（某一）时刻，（某一）地点；尖，尖端；分数，得分</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 指，指向；指明</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> point of view 观点；point to/at 指着，指向；to the point of 到…的程度；at the point of 靠近；正要</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is impolite to point at someone with your finger. 用手指别人是不礼貌的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> pointed（adj. 尖的；锐利的）；pointer（n. 指针）</p>
postcard@［ˈpəʊstka:d］@n. 明信片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：post（邮递）+card（卡片）→邮递的卡片→明信片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My friends send me postcards every Christmas. 每个圣诞节，朋友们都会给我寄明信片。</p>

joke@［dʒəʊk］@n. 笑话，玩笑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Cindy likes to tell jokes. 辛迪喜欢讲笑话。</p>
spoon@［spu:n］@n. 匙，勺，调羹 v. 用匙舀</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The cook added two spoons of sugar into the dish. 厨师往菜里加了两匙白糖。</p>
manner@［ˈmænə(r)］@n. 方式，方法；态度，举止；［pl.］ 风度，礼貌；规矩</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：man（男人）+ner→男人要有风度→风度</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Nancy answered the question with good manners. 南希很有礼貌地回答了这个问题。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00130.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">manner, manners</p>   <p class="bodytext">考生要注意这二者的区别。manner指“方式；态度”，而其复数形式manners则指“风度，礼貌”。如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">The waiter's manner was very bad. 服务员的态度很差。</p>   <p class="bodytext">Children should behave with good manners. 孩子们应该表现得有礼貌。</p></div>
graduate@［ˈgrædjueit］@ v. （使）毕业；获学位</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［ˈgrædʒuət］</span> n. （尤指大学）毕业生；研究生，获（学士）学位者 adj. 研究生的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：grad（部，级，走）+uate→从学校走出来→毕业</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> graduate from... 从…（学校）毕业</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am a graduate of Peking University. 我是北京大学的毕业生。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> graduation（n. 毕业；毕业典礼）</p>
pleasure@［ˈpleʒə(r)］@n. 高兴，愉快；满足；乐事，快事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take/find pleasure in （doing） sth. 从（做）某事中得到/发现乐趣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's my pleasure to have lunch with you. 和你一起吃午餐是我的荣幸。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">在别人表示感谢后，可以用“It's my pleasure.”，“My pleasure.”或“With pleasure.”来回答。这三种回答都有“不客气”、“乐意效劳”的意思。</p></div>
success@［səkˈses］@n. 成就，成功；成功的事物，取得成就的人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The art show was a great success. 这次艺术展取得了巨大的成功。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> successful（adj. 成功的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00131.jpeg"/></div>

lap@［læp］@n. （坐着时的）腰以下到膝为止的大腿部；（跑道的）一圈；一段旅程</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［lapped-lapped, lapping］ （动物）舔，舔食；（波浪等）拍打</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：地图（map）放在膝（lap）盖上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The child sat on his mother's lap. 孩子坐在妈妈的膝盖上。</p>

value@［ˈvælju:］@n. 价值；价格；购买力；重要性；益处 v. 给…估价；评价</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“外流”→肥水不外流→价值；益处</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The value of friendship should not be measured by money. 友情的价值不应该用金钱衡量。</p>
review@［riˈvju:］@n. / v. 审查，复查；复习，温习，回顾；评论；检阅</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：re（重新）+view（看）→重新看→复习</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Your answers need reviewing. 你需要检查一下答案。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> reviewer（n. 评论家）</p>
eastern@［ˈi:stən］@adj. 东方的，东部的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Eastern cultural traditions are different from the western world. 东方的文化传统跟西方世界是不一样的。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">eastern, east</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“东方的”之意，但侧重点不同。eastern强调的是方位，如：in the eastern area 在东部地区；而east强调的是方向，如：in the east 在东方。</p> </div>
outside@［aʊtˈsaid］@prep. 在…外面，向…外面；除…以外 adv. 在外面，向外面 adj. 外面的，外部的，外界的 n. 外面，外部；外表</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> A boy climbed onto the tree outside the wall. 一个男孩爬上了墙外的那棵树。</p>
December@［diˈsembə(r)］@n. 十二月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The story happened on December 25th. 故事发生在12月25日。</p>

design@［diˈzain］@n. 设计，构想；图样，图案；企图，图谋 v. 设计；预订，指定；谋划，构思</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：de+sign（标记）→一路做标记，企图谋反→企图</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The dress of the model is of the latest design. 模特穿的服装是今年的最新设计。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> designer（n. 设计师）</p>
worse@［wɜ:s］@adv. / adj. 更坏（的），更差（的），更糟（的） n. 更坏的事，更恶劣的事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Today's weather is worse than yesterday's. 今天的天气比昨天差。</p>
finger@［ˈfiŋgə(r)］@n. 手指</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The woman had a ring on her finger, meaning that she was married. 那个女人手上戴着一枚戒指，说明她已经结婚了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00033.jpeg"/></div>
everywhere@［ˈevriweə(r)］@adv. 到处，各处，无论何处</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I've looked everywhere but couldn't find my key. 我到处都找遍了，但还是没找到我的钥匙。</p>
daughter@［ˈdɔ:tə(r)］@n. 女儿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old couple has three daughters but none of them live with them. 这对老夫妇有三个女儿，但是没有一个留在他们身边。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00034.jpeg"/></div>
impossible@［imˈpɒsəbl］@adj. 不可能的，办不到的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is impossible for our team to win the game. 对于我们队来说，想赢得这场比赛的胜利是不可能的。</p>
topic@［ˈtɒpik］@n. 题目，话题；主题</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> hot topic 热门话题</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The column of the website covered a wide range of topics. 这个网站的栏目涵盖的话题范围很广。</p>

meat@［mi:t］@n. 肉</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：这个人一顿没见到（meet）肉（meat），就想得慌</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The girl said she didn't like eating meat. 女孩说她不喜欢吃肉。</p>
size@［saiz］@n. 大小，尺寸，尺码；规模 v. 按大小排列（或分类）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">The shopkeeper said they ______ the shoes ______. （2007年 青岛）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. have sold out; in my size</p> <p class="bodytext">B. sold out; of my size</p> <p class="bodytext">C. had sold out; for my size</p> <p class="bodytext">D. had sold out; in my size</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>店主说我穿的尺码的鞋已经卖完了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>表示“某人的尺码”时要用介词in，比如 in my size是“我的尺码”的意思。由于主句是一般过去时，从句要用与过去相关的时态，因此本题选D。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext">我们常见的表示服饰尺寸大小的有三个标志：S(small)，M(medium)和L(large)。注意在询问对方衣服或鞋帽的大小时通常要用What size...来提问。</p> </div>
bicycle@［ˈbaisikl］@n. 自行车 v. 骑自行车</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Harry often goes to work by bicycle. 哈里常常骑自行车上班。</p>
university@［ˌju:niˈvɜ:səti］@n. 大学</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：univers（看作universe，宇宙，世界）+ity（看作city，城市）→能够学习世界和宇宙万物知识的像城市一样的地方→大学</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Every year our university attracts thousands of students from all over the world. 每年我们大学都会吸引全世界成千上万的学生。</p>
comment@［ˈkɒment］@n. 评论，意见；闲话，议论 v. 评论</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> make comments on/upon sth. 评论某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our Chinese teacher made helpful comments on my workbook. 我们语文老师在我的作业本上写了很有用的评论。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> commentator（n. 评论员；讲解员）</p>

heel@［hi:l］@n. 脚后跟，踵；（鞋、袜等的）后跟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I wear high heels only on special occasions. 我只在一些特殊场合穿高跟鞋。</p>
this@［ðis］@pron. 这，这个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This blue bag is mine. 这个蓝包是我的。</p>
child@［ˈtʃaild］@n. ［pl. children］ 孩子，儿女</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Although he is 30 years old, he is still a child in his mother's eyes. 尽管他已经30岁了，但在他母亲眼里他还是个孩子。</p>
view@［vju:］@n. 看法，观点；视野，眼界；景色，风景 v. 考虑，认为；观察，看</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in one's view 按…的观点；in view of 鉴于，由于；in full view of / in the view of 在被…完全看得见的地方；a point of view 一个观点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Linda gave her views on the event that happened yesterday. 琳达就昨天发生的事情发表了意见。</p>
parent@［ˈpeərənt］@n. 父亲（或母亲），家长</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many parents are very strict with their children. 许多父母对自己的孩子都很严格。</p>
sugar@［ˈʃʊgə(r)］@n. 糖 v. 在…中加糖</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She put some sugar and milk into her coffee. 她在咖啡里面加了糖和奶。</p>
wall@［wɔ:l］@n. 墙，壁，围墙 v. 筑墙围住，用墙隔开</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are a number of beautiful pictures on the wall. 墙上有很多漂亮的图片。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext">“在墙上”英语中有两种表达：如果是像钟表、镜子一样挂在墙上，用on the wall；如果是类似窗子一样嵌在墙体里，用in the wall。</p> </div>
Monday@［ˈmʌndei; -di］@n. 星期一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually have just one class on Mondays. 我通常在星期一只有一节课。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext">一周七天的表达分别如下：</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00035.jpeg"/></div>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00036.jpeg"/></div> </div>
fact@［fækt］@n. 事实，真相</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in fact 事实上，实际上；as a matter of fact 事实上，实际上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's a fact that most deaths from lung cancer are caused by smoking. 事实上，大多数由肺癌导致的死亡都是由吸烟引起的。</p>
course@［kɔ:s］@n. 过程；经过；路线，航线；方针；课程</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“考试”→上课玩，考试难→课程</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> of course 当然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to take a course in art and design. 我想上艺术和设计课程。</p>
slide@［slaid］@v. ［slid-slid］ 滑动，下滑；（使）快速而悄声地移动 n. 滑动，下滑；滑坡；幻灯片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The naughty boy slid out while his mother was cooking. 那个淘气的小男孩趁妈妈做饭时偷偷溜了出去。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> slider（n. 滑雪者，滑冰者）；sliding（adj. 滑行的）</p>
repeat@［riˈpi:t］@n. / v. 重复；重说；重做</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little boy can repeat his mother's statement word for word. 小男孩可以一字一句地重复妈妈的话。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00037.jpeg"/></div>
tooth@［tu:θ］@n. ［pl. teeth］ 牙齿；齿状物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mike had to have his tooth out at the dentist's. 迈克不得不去牙医诊室拔牙。</p>
move@［mu:v］@v. 移动，搬动，搬（家）；动摇，使改变主意；感动，激起；进展，发展</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 动，动作，行动；移动；搬家，迁移</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> move up 上升；move on 继续前进；move about 来回走动；move out 搬出；move around 走来走去</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We moved to a new house last month. 我们上个月搬进了新家。</p>
pronoun@［ˈprəʊnaʊn］@n. 代词</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I was asked to make a sentence with the pronoun“it”. 我被要求用代词it造句。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00038.jpeg"/></div>
beside@［biˈsaid］@prep. 在…旁边；在…附近；和…相比</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—All the students in Class One went to the cinema ______ Li Ping. Why?</p> <p class="bodytext">—Because he had a stomachache. （2009年 河南）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. besides</p> <p class="bodytext">B. without</p> <p class="bodytext">C. except</p> <p class="bodytext">D. beside</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—除了李平，一班的全体学生都去看电影了，这是为什么呢？</p> <p class="bodytext4">—因为他胃疼。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查besides与except作“除了”讲时的区别。besides后的名词包含在整体之内，常译为“除了…之外，还有”，而except后的名词排除在整体之外。beside意为“在…旁边”；without意为“没有”。根据句意，应该选C。</p>
suggest@［səˈdʒest］@v. 建议，提出；使想起；暗示</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I suggested that we should solve this problem in another way. 我建议我们应该换一种方式来解决这个问题。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> suggestion（n. 提议，意见）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">suggest做“建议”讲的时候宾语从句要用虚拟语气，即suggest that sb. （should） do sth.，如: The doctor suggested that the old man （should） not smoke. 医生建议那位老人不要吸烟。有类似用法的单词还有：insist, order, propose, demand, require, request，它们表示坚持、命令、建议、要求时从句用虚拟语气。</p> </div>
its@［its］@pron. 它的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have no idea about its value. 我不知道它的价值。</p>
recent@［ˈri:snt］@adj. 新近的，近来的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The climate has changed a lot in recent years. 近年来气候变化很大。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> recently（adv. 最近）</p>
infinitive@［inˈfinətiv］@n. 原形；不定式</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> In the sentence“I want to watch TV.”“to watch”is an infinitive. 在句子“I want to watch TV.”中，“to watch”是不定式。</p>
sit@［sit］@v. ［sat-sat, sitting］ 坐，就座；坐落，被安放；使坐，使就座</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The girl always sits on that chair near her mother. 那个女孩总是坐在靠近她妈妈的椅子上。</p>
push@［pʊʃ］@v. 推，按；推动，推进；催逼，逼迫</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 推，推力；促进，推进</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：这扇门可以推（push），也可以拉（pull）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mother pushed the button on the camera to take photos for us. 妈妈按下相机按钮为我们拍照。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00039.jpeg"/></div>
again@［əˈgen］@adv. 再一次，又一次；回到原处，复原；再则，而且</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom is late for work again. 汤姆上班又迟到了。</p>
bright@［brait］@adj. 明亮的，光明的；聪明的，机灵的；欢快的；鲜艳的；清晰的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little boy is bright and lovely. 那个小男孩既聪明又可爱。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> brighten（v. 使发光）</p>
pink@［piŋk］@adj. 粉红色的，桃红色的 n. 粉红色，桃红色</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lucy dressed in a pink skirt. 露西穿了一件粉色的短裙。</p>
late@［leit］@adj. 迟的，晚的；末期的，晚期的；最近的，新近的；已故的；以前的</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 迟，晚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be late for 迟到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The train was 10 minutes late. 火车晚点了十分钟。</p>
clock@［ˈklɒk］@n. 钟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is 7 o'clock；I have to get up. 现在都7点了，我要起床了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00040.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">lock, watch</p>   <p class="bodytext">clock和watch都有“表”的意思，但是要注意区别。clock指墙上挂的钟表；watch指戴在手上的手表。</p> </div>
sixty@［ˈsiksti］@num. 六十，六十个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The school admits sixty new students every year. 这所学校每年招收60位新生。</p>
most@［məʊst］@adv. 最；极其，十分 adj. 最多的，最大的；大多数的，大部分的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Most of the students study hard. 大多数的学生学习都很刻苦。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> mostly（adv. 主要地，大部分）</p>
horse@［hɔ:s］@n. 马</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：房子（house）门前拴大马（horse）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The horses are eating grass on the grassland. 马在草地上吃草。</p>
November@［nəʊˈvembə(r)］@n. 十一月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It never snows in November here. 这里十一月从来没有下过雪。</p>
mom@［mɒm］@（=mum） n. 妈妈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The girl said her mom was good at cooking. 女孩说她母亲很擅长烹饪。</p>
standard@［ˈstændəd］@n. 标准，规则 adj. 标准的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：stand（站）+ard→站有站相→标准</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is no absolute standard for the definition of beauty. 对美的定义没有绝对的标准。</p>
wise@［waiz］@adj. 有智慧的，聪明的；英明的，明智的；博学的，贤明的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is wise to learn English from an early age. 从小学英语是明智的。</p>
spread@［spred］@v. 展开，伸开；散布，蔓延；涂，敷 n. 传播，蔓延；幅度，范围；涂抹在食物上的东西；（尤指横贯两版的）文章（或广告等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：sp+read（阅读）→通过阅读来扩展我们的视野→展开</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> spread out 展开</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Sue spreads the map out on the floor to find where her city is. 苏在地板上展开地图查看自己所在城市的位置。// The infectious disease is spread by mosquitoes. 这种传染病是由蚊子传播的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> spreading（adj. 扩展的 n. 扩展，伸展）</p>
instance@［ˈinstəns］@n. 例子，实例，事例；情况</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> for instance 例如</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher gave the students some instances of water pollution. 老师给学生们举出了一些水污染的实例。</p>
ache@［eik］@v. 痛，疼痛；渴望 n. 疼痛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“癌克”→止痛药是癌症的克星→疼痛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> ache for 渴望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are some aches in my arms. 我的胳膊疼。</p>
queen@［kwi:n］@n. 女王，王后</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't like the evil queens in the fairy tales. 我不喜欢童话故事里那些邪恶的王后。</p>
skirt@［skɜ:t］@n. 裙子；边缘，外围</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is very popular to wear mini-skirts these days. 最近超短裙很流行。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> skirted（adj. 穿裙子的）</p>
fear@［fiə(r)］@n. 害怕，恐惧；恐惧的原因；令人恐惧的事物</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 畏惧，害怕</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：f+ear（耳朵）→危言耸听→害怕，恐惧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> for fear of sth. / doing sth. 唯恐…，忧虑…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Marie has a great fear of fire because her house had caught fire when she was very young. 玛丽对火有着巨大的恐惧，因为小时候她家里着过一场大火。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00041.jpeg"/></div>
girlfriend@［ˈgɜ:lfrend］@n. 女朋友；女性朋友</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：girl（女孩）+friend（朋友）→女朋友</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My girlfriend is younger than me. 我的女朋友比我小。</p>
hunger@［ˈhʌŋgə(r)］@n. 饿，饥饿；食欲，胃口；渴望 v. 渴望，渴望得到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I felt faint with hunger. 我饿得有点头晕了。</p>
march@［ma:tʃ］@v. 行军，前进；游行示威 n. 行进，行军；游行示威；进行，进展；［M-］ 三月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The soldiers marched 20 miles to reach the capital. 士兵们行进20英里到达首都。</p>
warn@［wɔ:n］@v. 警告，告诫；注意，通知</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：发动战争（war）之前，总要先发出警告（warn）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The doctor warned the patient to stop smoking. 医生告诫病人要戒烟。</p>
hurry@［ˈhʌri］@v. 使加快，催促；急运，急派；匆忙，赶紧 n. 急忙，匆忙，仓促</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> hurry up 快点；催促；in a hurry 匆忙，赶忙；in no hurry 不用着急，慢点</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Hurry up!We'll be late for school. 快点！ 我们上课要迟到了。</p>
business@［ˈbiznəs］@n. 交易，生意；营业（额）；商业；工作，任务；事务</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> have business with 与…有关；on business 因公，出差；get down to business 言归正传；开始干正事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'll fly to Shanghai on business next Friday. 下周五我要坐飞机去上海出差。</p>
soldier@［ˈsəʊldʒə(r)］@n. 士兵，军人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy said he wanted to be a soldier. 男孩说他想成为一名士兵。</p>
clerk@［kla:k］@n. 〈美〉店员；办事员，职员</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Paul used to be a bank clerk. 保罗曾经是一名银行职员。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> clerical（adj. 办公室工作的；神职人员的）</p>
way@［wei］@n. 方法，手段；路，路线；方面；方向；习俗，作风；状况，状态</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> no way 不可能，没门；by the way 顺便说一下；on the way 在途中；in a way 在某种程度上，稍稍；all the way 一直</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People have different ways to solve this problem. 人们解决这一问题有不同的方法。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">on the way to...是“在去…的路上”，如：on my way to school 在我去学校的路上。注意on my way home（在我回家的路上）没有to，因为home在这里是副词。</p> </div>
conference@［ˈkɒnfərəns］@n. （正式）会议；讨论（会），商谈（会）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mark is in conference and he cannot come to the telephone. 马克正在开会，他无法接电话。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">conference, meeting</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“会议”的意思，但是使用场合不同。conference一般指重大的国际会议等，比较正式；而meeting是一般用语，使用范围比较广。</p> </div>
industry@［ˈindəstri］@n. 工业，产业；勤劳，勤奋</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Li Lei got a job in light industry. 李雷在轻工业领域找到了一份工作。</p>
represent@［ˌrepriˈzent］@v. 作为…的代表（或代理）；描述；表示；象征；描绘，表现；阐明，说明；扮演</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The olive branch represents peace. 橄榄枝象征和平。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> representation（n. 表现；代表）；representative （n. 代表 adj. 有代表性的）</p>
bottom@［ˈbɒtəm］@n. 底，底部；末尾，尽头；臀部 adj. 最低的，最下的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a book at the bottom of the box. 箱底有一本书。</p>
alone@［əˈləʊn］@adj. 单独的，孤独的；单单，仅；独一无二的，唯一的</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 单独地；孤独地；独自地；仅仅，只</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> let alone 更不用说</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I went to the cinema alone yesterday. 我昨天一个人去看的电影。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00042.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">alone, lonely</p>   <p class="bodytext">The old man lived alone, but he didn't feel lonely. 这个老人独居，但是他并不觉得孤独。从这句话可以看出二者的区别。alone强调客观上的“独自的（地）”，指没有同伴或助手；而lonely多指感情与感觉上的“孤独”。</p> </div>
whale@［weil］@n. 鲸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People can enjoy whale watching during the trip. 人们在旅途中可以欣赏到鲸鱼。</p>
x-ray@［eksˈrei］@adj. X射线的，X光的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> X-ray machines are used in many fields. X射线机器被应用于很多领域。</p>
cow@［kaʊ］@n. 母牛；奶牛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is very interesting to milk a cow. 给奶牛挤奶非常有意思。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00043.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">cow, ox</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“牛”的意思，但是所指不同。cow指“母牛；奶牛”，ox指“公牛”。</p> </div>
ask@［a:sk］@v. 询问，问；要求</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> ask for sth. 要求，请求；ask （sb.） about sth. （向某人）打听某事；ask sb. to do sth. 要求某人做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Tomorrow's meeting is very important. Please ask them ______ there on time. （2008年 北京）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. go</p> <p class="bodytext">B. going</p> <p class="bodytext">C. to go</p> <p class="bodytext">D. went</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>明天的会议很重要。请通知他们准时到达。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查ask sb. to do sth.这一结构，意为“要求某人做某事”，故选C。</p>
sudden@［ˈsʌdn］@adj. 突然的，意外的 n. 突然发生的事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> all of a sudden 突然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> When he saw the terrible scene, the boy suddenly began crying. 小男孩看到恐怖的一幕，突然哭了起来。</p>
mark@［ma:k］@n. 痕迹，斑点，污点；记号，标记；（考试等的）分数</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 作记号于，标明；纪念；给（试卷等）打分</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：树皮（bark）上做记号（mark）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We marked on the map which road we should take. 我们在地图上标记出该走哪条路。</p>
since@［sins］@conj. 自…以来，从…以后；因为，既然 prep. 自…以来，从…以后 adv. 后来，以后</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> since then 从那以后</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Over 400 million people have visited Disneyland parks around the world ______ American Disneyland opened in July 1955. （2008年 哈尔滨）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. after</p> <p class="bodytext">B. before</p> <p class="bodytext">C. since</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>自从1955年7月美国迪士尼乐园开园以来，全球有四亿多人去那里游玩过。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查几个连词的用法。since表示“自…以来”，从句用一般过去时，主句用现在完成时，符合题意。after是“…之后”的意思，before是“…之前”的意思，均不符合题意，因此选C。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">since, as, because</p>   <p class="bodytext">since表示“因为”时，一般指对方已知的、无需加以说明的原因或事实，语气比because要弱，如：You have no chance to travel since you have no desire to go out. 你没机会出去旅游，因为你根本没有出去的欲望。as说明的是一般的因果关系，引导的从句通常放在句首，有时放在句末，如：I got up late as I was sleepy. 我起床晚了，因为我很困。because的语气是最强的，在回答why的问句时，一般都要用because，如：Why are you late? Because I'm tired. 你为什么迟到了？因为我太累了。</p> </div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">since引导的短语或从句表示事情从过去某个时间开始一直持续到现在，如：I've never seen him since I left the city. 自从我离开那个城市，就再也没有见过他。</p> </div>
belong@［biˈlɒŋ］@v. 属于，应归入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> belong to 属于</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The notebook belongs to Jane, because her name is on it. 这个笔记本是简的，因为上面有她的名字。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">belong是不及物动词，不能直接接宾语，常与介词to连用，此外, 这个词不能用于进行时中。</p> </div>
shark@［ʃa:k］@n. 鲨鱼；勒索者，诈骗者；放高利贷的人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I saw a great white shark in the National Marine Animal Museum. 我在国家海洋动物博物馆看到了一条大白鲨。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00044.jpeg"/></div>
everyday@［ˈevridei］@adj. 每天的；日常的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Internet has become part of everyday life. 互联网已成为日常生活的一部分。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">everyday, every day</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“每天”的意思，但词性和用法不同。everyday是形容词，只能作定语修饰名词，如：everyday life日常生活；every day是短语，相当于副词，只能作状语，如：Mike baths every day. 迈克每天都洗澡。</p> </div>
impolite@［ˌimpəˈlait］@adj. 不礼貌的，粗鲁的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is impolite to ask others personal questions such as their age. 问别人一些诸如年龄之类的私人问题是不礼貌的。</p>
solution@［səˈlu:ʃn］@n. 解决，解答，解决办法；溶液</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We are all trying to find the perfect solution to all the problems. 我们都在试图为所有问题找到完美的解决办法。</p>
above@［əˈｂʌｖ］@prep. 在…上方；多于，超过 adv. 在（向）上面，在顶上；（在级别、权力、数目等方面）超过；在上文</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> above all 最重要的是</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The plane is flying above the clouds. 飞机正在云层上方穿梭。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00045.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">above, over</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“在…上方”之意。above指一般意义的上方，但不一定是正上方，它的反义词是below，如：The sun is rising above the horizon. 太阳正从地平线上升起。over指在正上方，反义词是under，如：There is a bridge over the river. 河上有座桥。</p> </div>
every@［ˈevri］@adj. 每一，每个；每…一次的；所有可能的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I enjoyed every minute of the party. 我很享受这次聚会的每一分钟。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">every, each</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“每一个”的意思，但是有区别。every指三者或三者以上中的每一个，强调整体，只能作形容词，如：I heard every word of their talking. 我听到了他们谈话的每一个字。而each指两者或两者以上中的每一个，强调个体，可以作代词和形容词，如：Each of us has a car. 我俩各有一辆车。</p> </div>
face@［feis］@n. 脸，面孔；面部表情；面，表面 v. 面向，正对；面对，面临</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> face to face 面对面</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a 5-centimeter long scar on his face. 他的脸上有一道5厘米长的疤痕。</p>
soup@［su:p］@n. 汤</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：这汤（soup）里可不能加肥皂（soap）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We had some chicken soup which was very delicious. 我们喝了一些非常美味的鸡汤。</p>
double@［ˈdʌbl］@adj. 双的，双重的；两倍的，加倍的；供两人用的，双人的；两面派的，虚伪的</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 两倍；双份；［pl.］ （网球等的）双打 v. 使加倍，是…的两倍；把…对折，折叠</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He got double salary because of his hard work. 由于工作努力，他得到了双倍薪水。</p>
east@［i:st］@n. 东，东部 adj. 东方的；来自东方的 adv. 向东方</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：东（east）西（west）南北中</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The sun rises from the east every morning. 太阳每天早晨从东方升起。</p>
proud@［praʊd］@adj. 骄傲的，傲慢的；自豪的，得意的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：骄傲的（proud）孔雀态度非常傲慢（pride）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be/feel proud of 为…感到骄傲</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> If we study hard, our parents will feel proud of us. 如果我们刻苦学习，我们的父母会为我们感到骄傲的。</p>
shy@［ʃai］@adj. 腼腆的，害羞的；胆怯的；有戒心的，畏缩的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The young man was too shy to talk to anyone at the party. 这个年轻人太害羞了，在宴会上不敢跟任何人说话。</p>
schoolwork@［ˈsku:lwɜ:k］@n. 学校作业，课堂作业；家庭作业</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Simon is new here and he is struggling to keep up with his schoolwork. 西蒙是新同学，他正在努力赶上功课。</p>
ever@［ˈevə(r)］@adv. 在任何时候，从来；曾经</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Have you ever been to Malaysia before? 你以前去过马来西亚吗？</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">ever常用在现在完成时的疑问句中，如：Have you ever been to London? 你去过伦敦吗？另外，在作“曾经”讲的时候，ever一般不用于肯定句中，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（〇） I once lived in Beijing. 我曾经在北京生活过。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（✕） I ever lived in Beijing. 我曾经在北京生活过。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">但在修饰比较级、最高级或强调“总是，经常”时，ever可以用于肯定句中，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">It is the most interesting book I have ever read. 这是我看过的最有意思的书了。</p> </div>
small@［smɔ:l］@adj. 小的；少的；不重要的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> These shoes are too small for me and I would like to change another pair. 这双鞋对于我来说太小了，我想换一双。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00046.jpeg"/></div>
west@［west］@n. 西，西方，西部 adj. 西方的，西部的，来自西方的 adv. 向西方</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> in the west 在西方</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Regions in west China began to develop in recent years. 近些年中国西部地区开始发展起来了。</p>
labor@［ˈleibə(r)］@n. 劳动；工作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Wealth comes from human labor. 财富源自人类的劳动。</p>
space@［speis］@n. 空地，场地；空间，太空；篇幅；间隔，距离；持续时间，期间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The bed takes up too much space. 这张床占了很大的地方。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> spacing（n. 间隔，间距）；spacious（adj. 广阔的，宽敞的）</p>
key@［ki:］@n. 钥匙；关键，要害；键；（乐曲的）调；答案，题解；图例</p> <p class="bodytext1">adj. 主要的，关键的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> key to …的答案</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can you find the key to the question? 你能找到问题的答案吗？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> keyboard（n. 键盘）</p>
old@［əʊld］@adj. 老的，年老的；古老的，陈旧的，过时的；…岁的，…久的；以前的，过去的；老练的，有经验的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The boy doesn't want to wear the old clothes. 男孩不想穿旧衣服。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">old的比较级是older或elder，最高级是oldest或eldest。older和oldest泛指普通的新旧关系，而elder和eldest专门用来表示兄弟姐妹之间的长幼关系，如：elder sister 姐姐；my eldest brother 我大哥。</p> </div>
game@［geim］@n. 游戏，娱乐；运动（项目），比赛（项目）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do you want to join in the game? 你想参加比赛吗？</p>
Sunday@［ˈsʌndei; -di］@n. 星期日</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We're going to visit my grandparents on Sunday. 我们周日要去看爷爷奶奶。</p>
one@［wʌn］@num. 一，一个 pron. （其中的）一人，一个；（泛指）一个人，任何人</p> <p class="bodytext1">adj. （任何）一个的，某一（个）的，同一的；一体的，完整的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> one at a time 一次一个；one by one 一个接一个；one more...再来一个…；one day 总有一天；one another 互相</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> One Sunday morning I cleaned the house. 一个周日的早晨，我打扫了房子。</p>
enjoy@［inˈdʒɔi］@v. 享受；喜爱；享有</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：en（使…进入状态）+joy（欢乐，喜悦）→进入欢乐状态→享受</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> enjoy oneself 玩得高兴；enjoy doing sth. 喜欢做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I really enjoy watching movies with my friends. 我真的很喜欢跟朋友们一起看电影。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">enjoy后常接动名词作宾语，考生一定要牢记。</p> </div>
ours@［ˈaʊəz］@pron. 我们的（所有物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This classroom isn't ours. 这间教室不是我们的。</p>
ugly@［ˈʌgli］@adj. 难看的，丑陋的；有敌意的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is an ugly scar on his face. 他的脸上有一块丑陋的伤疤。</p>
sheep@［ʃi:p］@n. ［pl. sheep］ （绵）羊；易受人摆布的人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can't distinguish goats from sheep. 我分不清山羊和绵羊。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">sheep的单复数同形，注意不要跟规则的名词混为一谈，如：Sheep were grazing in the fields. 羊群在田野上吃草。此时，句中的谓语动词用复数。这样单复数同形的常用名词还有deer（鹿）、means（方法）和 series（系列）等。</p> </div>
people@［ˈpi:pl］@n. 人，人们；人民，民众，平民；国民；民族</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People all over the world are watching the performance. 全世界的人都在观看这场演出。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">people作“人们”讲时是集合名词，谓语动词用复数形式，如：So many people are watching the Olympic Games. 如此多的人正在看奥运会。而作“民族”讲时是可数名词，如：There are 56 peoples in our country. 我们国家有56个民族。</p> </div>
upstairs@［ʌpˈsteəz］@adv. 在楼上，往楼上 adj. 楼上的 n. 楼上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：up（上面）+stairs（楼梯）→在楼上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The girl who is living upstairs is so pretty. 住在楼上的女孩十分可爱。</p>
bird@［bɜ:d］@n. 鸟；禽</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The bird is singing in the tree. 鸟儿正在树上歌唱。</p>
trouble@［ˈtrʌbl］@n. 麻烦，苦恼，困难；疾病；故障；纠纷，动乱</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 使烦恼，使苦恼，折磨；麻烦，使费神</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> get into trouble 招致不幸，陷入困境；（be） in trouble 处于困境中；have trouble with... 和…有纠纷；有…病痛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I had a lot of trouble with the new computer system. 新的电脑系统给我带来很多麻烦。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext5">get into trouble, be in trouble</p>   <p class="bodytext">get into trouble含义是“陷入困境”，强调过程，如：How did you get into the trouble? 你是怎么陷入这个麻烦的？be in trouble是“处于困境中”，强调的是状态，如：I don't want to see you in trouble. 我不想看见你处于危难中。</p> </div>
fight@［fait］@v. ［fought-fought］ 打架；打仗 n. 打；战斗；争吵</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：打架（fight）是不正确的（right）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> fight against 与…战斗，与…对抗；fight with 和…作战；fight for 为…而战</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I had a big fight with one of my classmates. 我跟一个同学大打出手。</p>
duck@［dʌk］@n. 鸭；鸭肉 vi. 鸭子似的突然扎入水中；突然低下</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：唐老鸭（duck）运气（luck）总是不好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Beijing Roast Duck is famous around the world. 北京烤鸭世界闻名。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> ducking（n. 闪避；钻入水中）</p>
fast@［fa:st］@adv. 快地；牢固地 adj.快的，迅速的；敏捷的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I couldn't believe that the boy ran faster than me. 我不敢相信，这个男孩比我跑得快。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">fast, soon</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“快”的意思。fast形容速度或动作快，如：He runs fast. 他跑得快。soon指时间短，如：I'll come back soon. 我一会儿就回来。</p> </div>
theirs@［ðeəz］@pron. 他（她、它）们的（所有物）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is my fault, not theirs. 这是我的错，不是他们的。</p>
pronounce@［prəˈnaʊns］@v. 发音；宣布；宣判</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is difficult to pronounce the word“pronunciation”. pronunciation这个词很难发音。</p>
oneself@［wʌnˈself］@pron. 自己，自身；亲自，本人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> help oneself to 自用</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> To do something by oneself is not easy. 自己去做一件事并不容易。</p>
slice@［slais］@v. 切成片，削 n. 薄片，切片；一份，部分</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Joan only has a slice of bread every morning to lose weight. 为了减肥，琼每天早上只吃一片面包。</p>
foot@［fʊt］@n. ［pl. feet］ 脚，足；英尺；最下部，底部</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually go to school on foot. 我经常步行去上学。</p>
amount@［əˈmaʊnt］@n. 总额 v. 合计</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：a+mount（看作mountain，山）→一块合计，堆积如山→合计</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> an amount of 许多</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Martin and Henry spend the same amount of time reading every day. 马丁和亨利每天花一样多的时间看书。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">短语an amount of后要接不可数名词。</p> </div>
slipper@［ˈslipə(r)］@n. 拖鞋；轻便舞鞋 v. 用拖鞋打（孩子等）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：穿着拖鞋（slipper） 容易滑倒（slip）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I bought a pair of slippers. 我买了一双拖鞋。</p>
turkey@［ˈtɜ:ki］@n. 火鸡（肉）；［T-］ 土耳其</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：土耳其（Turkey）没有火鸡（turkey）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> People in some western countries have turkey on Christmas Day. 在一些西方国家，人们在圣诞节时吃火鸡。</p>
international@［ˌintəˈnæʃnəl］@adj. 国际的，世界（性）的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is going to be an international airport in this city. 这座城市将要建造一个国际机场。</p>
open@［ˈəʊpən］@adj. 开着的；公开的；坦率的；开阔的；开始营业（或工作）的；（职位等）空缺的；可利用的 v. 开，打开，张开；开始，开设，开办</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> open up 展开；开张；in the open air 在户外</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Don't leave the door open when you leave. 你离开时，不要把门敞着。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> open-air（adj. 露天的）</p>
second@［ˈsekənd］@num. 第二 adj. 次等的，二等的 n. 秒，瞬间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I never make the same mistake a second time. 我绝不会再犯同样的错误。</p>
birthday@［ˈbɜ:θdei］@n. 生日</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I invited many friends to my birthday party. 我邀请了许多朋友参加我的生日聚会。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00047.jpeg"/></div>
million@［ˈmiljən］@num. 百万 n. ［pl.］ 许多，无数</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“米粒儿”→成千上万的米粒→百万</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Have you seen the CCTV news on TV?</p> <p class="bodytext">— Yes, ______ children had a good festival on the ______ Children's Day. （2009年 黄冈）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. millions of; sixty</p> <p class="bodytext">B. ten million; sixty</p> <p class="bodytext">C. millions of; sixtieth</p> <p class="bodytext">D. ten millions; sixtieth</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 你在电视上看中央电视台的新闻了吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 是啊，数百万的孩子在第60个儿童节那天度过了一个美好的节日。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>这道题考查的是million的用法以及序数词的用法。一定要记住，如果有具体的数字修饰million的时候，不能加-s。本题选C。</p>
everybody@［ˈevribɒdi］@pron. 每人，人人，各人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Everybody should respect other people. 每个人都应该尊重他人。</p>
station@［ˈsteiʃn］@n. （车）站，台，局；身份，地位 v. 安置；派驻，驻扎</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't know the way to the railway station. 我不知道去火车站的路。</p>
nice@［nais］@adj. 好的；令人愉快的；友好的，好心的；细致的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It was a nice day after the snowy day. 雪天过后是个大晴天。</p>
tree@［tri:］@n. 树</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I liked climbing trees when I was about 10 years old. 我10岁左右时喜欢爬树。</p>
breath@［breθ］@n. 气息，呼吸的空气，呼吸；微风，（空气的）轻微流动</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take a breath 吸气；hold/catch one's breath 屏住呼吸；out of breath 上气不接下气</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man stopped to take a breath. 老人停下来喘了口气。</p>
capital@［ˈkæpitl］@n. 资本，资金；首都，首府；大写字母 adj. 首要的，重要的；死罪的；大写的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Beijing is the capital of China. 北京是中国的首都。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> capitalist（n. 资本家；资本主义者）</p>
make@［meik］@v. ［made-made］ 做，制造；作出，制定；使，迫使；获得，挣得；成为，到达</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：生米做（make）熟饭，蛋黄做蛋糕（cake）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> make money 挣钱；make bed 整理床铺；make a living 谋生；make use of 利用；make up of 由…构成；make up one's mind 下定决心；make sure 保证，确保；make sense 有意义</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Believe in yourself and in the end you'll make progress. 相信你自己，你最终会取得进步的。</p>
twelve@［twelv］@num. 十二，十二个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually go out for lunch at twelve. 我通常在12点的时候出去吃午饭。</p>
September@［sepˈtembə(r)］@n. 九月</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> This semester will begin on September 10th. 这个学期9月10日开学。</p>
verb@［vɜ:b］@n. 动词</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The use of verbs is sometimes different between English and Chinese. 英语和汉语中动词的使用有时不一样。</p>
elephant@［ˈelifənt］@n. 象</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Elephants are sometimes regarded as a kind of useless animal. 有时大象被认为是一种没用的动物。</p>
sail@［seil］@v. 航行；驾驶（船只）；在…上航行 n. 帆；航行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：水手远航（sail），邮件（mail）报平安</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Magellan was the first person to sail around the world. 麦哲伦是第一个驾船环游世界的人。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00048.jpeg"/></div>
or@［ɔ:(r)］@conj. 或，或者，还是；即，或者说；否则，要不然</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> either...or... 或者…或者…；or so 大约，左右</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> What kind of music do you like, pop or classical? 你喜欢哪种音乐，流行乐还是古典乐？</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">在否定句中表示并列时，不能用and，而要用or，如：I don't like bread, rice or porridge. 我不喜欢面包、米饭和粥。</p> </div>
specially@［ˈspeʃəli］@adv. 特意地，专门地；格外地，特别地，特殊地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The chairs are specially made for the disabled. 这些椅子是特别为残疾人制作的。</p>
block@［blɒk］@v. 阻碍；堵塞 n. 大块；一排房屋；街区</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：b+lock（锁）→封锁→阻碍</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> a block of 一块；block sth. （up） 阻碍；堵塞</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> John's house is two blocks from here. 约翰的房子离这儿有两条街。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> blockade（n./v. 封锁）；blockage（n. 障碍物）</p>
let@［let］@v. ［let-let］ 允许，让；假设；出租；排放</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> let alone 更不用说；let out 放走；泄漏；let off 排放；let in 让…进来；使陷入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— You always spend only a little time on your study. You really ______ me down.</p> <p class="bodytext">— I'm sorry, Mum. I won't do that again. （2008年 咸宁）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. take</p> <p class="bodytext">B. put</p> <p class="bodytext">C. let</p> <p class="bodytext">D. look</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 你花在学习上的时间总是太少，真让我失望。</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 对不起，妈妈。我不会再那样了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查let sb. down（使某人失望）的意思，因此答案选择C。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">let, make等使役动词的后面常接不带to的动词不定式，如：Let's go to school. 我们去上学吧。</p> </div>
pound@［paʊnd］@n. （重量单位）磅；英镑 v. 强烈打击，（连续）猛击；心怦怦跳；费力地移动</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“砰”→心怦怦跳</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Father pounded the table angrily when he found out that his son had lied to him. 父亲得知儿子骗了自己时，生气得直敲桌子。</p>
maybe@［ˈmeibi］@adv. 大概，也许</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：may（可能）+be（是）→也许</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The coat will cost one, maybe two hundred yuan. 这件外套将卖100或是200元。</p>
lose@［lu:z］@v. ［lost-lost］ 失去，损失；迷失，使迷路；输，输掉；白费，浪费；（钟、表）走慢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom lost his job two months ago. 汤姆两个月前丢掉了工作。</p>
cup@［kʌp］@n. 杯子；（一）杯；奖杯</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is a waste to use paper cups. 使用纸杯是一种浪费。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00049.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">cup, glass</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都是“杯子”的意思。cup指碗状带柄的杯子，用来喝茶、咖啡等，还可以指比赛的奖杯；而glass指一般的玻璃杯。</p> </div>
on@［ɔ:n］@prep. 在…上；向，朝，针对；靠近…，在…旁；关于，论及；凭，靠，根据；处于…情况中，从事…中；在…的时候；是…成员 adv. （放、穿、连接）上；向前，（继续）下去 adj. 工作着的，开着的；安排好的，计划中的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on the moment 立刻；on time 按时，准时；on the contrary 正相反；on duty 值班；上班；on foot 步行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Have you seen the book that was on the desk? 你看见放在桌上的那本书了吗？</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext">on, in和at都可以表示时间或日期，但用法不同，大家要注意区分：</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00050.jpeg"/></div>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00051.jpeg"/></div> </div>
guidebook@［ˈgaidbʊk］@n. 指南，手册，便览</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I bought a guidebook to England. 我买了一本英国指南。</p>
rich@［ritʃ］@adj. 富的，有钱的；富饶的，充足的；盛产的；（食物）油腻的；（气味）浓郁的；（色彩）鲜艳的；（声音）浑厚的 n. ［pl.］ 财富；资源</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Australia is rich in coal and wool. 澳大利亚盛产煤和羊毛。// Mr. Smith is a rich man—— ￡100 is nothing to him. 史密斯先生是个有钱人，100英镑对他来说算不上什么。</p>
owner@［ˈəʊnə(r) ］@n. 物主，所有人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：own（拥有）+er（表人的后缀）→物主</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can you help me to find the owner of the dog? 你能帮我找到这条狗的主人吗？</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00052.jpeg"/></div>
woman@［ˈwʊmən］@n. ［pl. women］ 成年女子，妇女 adj. 女人的，女性的，妇女的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Women face many more social challenges than men. 女性比男性面临更多的社会挑战。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">woman的复数形式的是women，读音也发生了变化读作<span class="yinbiao1">［ˈｗiｍiｎ］</span>，要注意。</p> </div>
queue@［kju:］@n. （人或车辆的）行列 v. 排（成）队（等候）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：q走在前面，后面跟着ue+ue→真是一支长队</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> join the queue 排队；jump the queue 插队；stand/wait in a queue 排队等待</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a long queue of people waiting to buy the tickets. 人们排成一长队等着买票。</p>
line@［lain］@n. 线条，界线；条纹，皱纹；方针，路线；线路，电话线；线，绳；排，行；铁路线；行业，专长 v. 使排成一行；用线标出，划线于；排齐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：人物鲜明，线条（line）优美（fine）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be in line 排成一行，成直线</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I was asked to hang the clothes on the line. 我得知要将衣服挂在绳上。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> linear（adj. 直线的；线性的）</p>
exercise@［ˈeksəsaiz］@n. 锻炼，运动；练习，习题；（权力等的）运用，行使；操练，演习</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 锻炼，训练；运用，行使</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> do/take some exercise 锻炼</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We should take more exercise to keep fit. 我们应该多锻炼身体以保持健康。</p>
improve@［imˈpru:v］@v. 改进，改善</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can improve my oral English by talking to foreigners. 我可以通过跟外国人交谈来提高英语口语。</p>
absent@［ˈæｂｓəｎｔ］@adj. 缺席的，不在场的；不存在的；心不在焉的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：送（sent）人玫瑰，人不在场（absent）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be absent from 缺席…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The manager was absent from the meeting. 经理缺席了会议。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> absent-minded（adj. 心不在焉的）</p>
own@［əʊn］@adj. 自己的 v. 有，拥有</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on one's own 单独地，独自地；of one's own 某人自己的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> —Can you do this business on your own?</p> <p class="bodytext6">—Yes, I can.</p> <p class="bodytext6">—你能自己做这项工作吗？</p> <p class="bodytext6">—是的，我能。</p>
