spend@［spend］@v. ［spent-spent］ 花费，用（钱）；花（时间等）；度过，消磨；消耗，用尽</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> spend...on... 花（时间或金钱）在…上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You'd better not spend too much time watching TV. 你最好不要花太多时间看电视。</p>
equipment@［iˈkwipmənt］@n. 装备，配备</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our factory has to purchase a lot of new equipment this year. 今年我们厂需要购置很多新设备。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">考生要注意equipment是不可数名词，不能和冠词an连用。</p> </div>
sense@［sens］@n. 感官，官能；感觉；判断力，见识 v. 觉得，意识到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> make sense 有意义；讲得通</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Western people have a sense of humor. 西方人有幽默感。</p>
so@［səʊ］@adv. （表示程度）如此，那么；非常，很；（表示方式）这样，那样；（避免重复）如此，这样；同样，也一样 conj. 因而，所以；为了，以便；那么，这样看来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> so as to 为了；or so 大约；so far 到目前为止；so that 目的是，以便；so...that... 如此…以至于…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">Look out! The traffic is ______ fast ______ we can't cross the street now. （2007年 潜江）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. too; to</p> <p class="bodytext">B. enough; to</p> <p class="bodytext">C. so; that</p> <p class="bodytext">D. such; that</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>当心！车辆行驶得太快了，我们现在不能横穿马路。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查“so+形容词/副词+that...”这一结构，表示“如此…，以至于…”。too...to...表示“太…而不能…”，to后面跟动词原形，不能跟句子。enough修饰名词、形容词或副词，其后接动词不定式。“such用于such a/an+形容词+名词+that”结构，表示“如此…以至于…”，不符合题意，因此本题选C。</p>
lost@［lɒst］@adj. 失去的，丧失的；错过的；迷惑的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The lost schoolbag was a present from my dad. 丢失的书包是我爸爸买给我的礼物。</p>
string@［striŋ］@n. 弦，线，细绳；一串，一行</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［strung-strung］ 用线串；（用线）悬挂；缚，捆</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：管弦（string）乐里有关于春天（spring）的乐曲</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My mother bought me a string of pearls as my birthday gift. 妈妈送了我一串珍珠项链作为生日礼物。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> stringed（adj. 有弦的）</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">string, wire, cord</p>   <p class="bodytext">string是指捆绑小件物品的细绳子或带子；而wire一般指金属制成的线；cord比string粗，比rope细，一般引申为“约束”。</p> </div>
emotion@［iˈməʊʃn］@n. 感情；激情；情绪</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You should learn how to control your emotions. 你应该学会如何控制情绪。</p>
Saturday@［ˈsætədei］@n. 星期六</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I made an appointment with Mark to go fishing on Saturday. 我跟马克约好周六一起去钓鱼。</p> 
waste@［weist］@n. 浪费，糟蹋；废料，废弃物 v. 浪费，未充分利用</p> <p class="bodytext1">adj. 废弃的，无用的；荒芜的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Don't let all this food go to waste. 别浪费了这些食物。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">waste后面经常跟介词on，表示“在…上浪费”，如：Please don't waste your money on such kind of useless things. 请不要把钱浪费在这些没用的东西上。</p> </div>
program@［ˈprəʊgræm］@n. 节目单；节目，表演，演出；计划，方案；程序</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 为…安排节目；为…制订计划</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The TV program today is about music. 今天的电视节目是关于音乐的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> programmer（n. 节目编排者；计划制订者；程序编制员）；programming（n. 节目的编排；编制程序）</p>
seven@［ˈsevn］@num. 七，七个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tim is seven years older than his younger brother. 蒂姆比他弟弟大七岁。</p>
down@［daʊn］@adv. 向下，在下面；处于低等地位，处于潦倒状况 prep. 沿着…而下 adj. 沮丧的，情绪低落的；向下的，下行的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— You always spend only a little time on your study. You really ______ me down.</p> <p class="bodytext">— I'm sorry, Mum. I won't do that again. （2008年 咸宁）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. take</p> <p class="bodytext">B. put</p> <p class="bodytext">C. let</p> <p class="bodytext">D. look</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 你花在学习上的时间总是太少，真让我失望。</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 对不起，妈妈。我不会再那样了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>down经常与动词构成固定搭配。take down 意为“记下；写下”；put down 意为“放下；镇压”；let down 意为“使…失望”；look down 意为“看不起”。根据上下文的意思，本题应该选C。</p>
love@［lʌv］@v. 爱，热爱；喜欢，爱好 n. 爱，喜爱</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：生活（live）无爱（love）无乐趣</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I love sports very much. 我非常喜欢运动。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> lovely（adj. 可爱的）</p>
library@［ˈlaibrəri］@n. 图书馆，藏书室；藏书</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I saw her in the library this morning. 今天早上我在图书馆看到她了。</p>
twice@［twais］@adv. 两倍；两次</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> When I was in high school, I went home twice a month. 我上高中的时候，一个月回家两次。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">表达次数的时候，1次用once，2次用twice，而3次以上就用数字加times来表达，如：three times 3次，four times 4次。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">英文中表示倍数常用的句式是：倍数+as+adj./adv.+as，如：This ruler is twice as long as that one. 这把尺子的长度是那把的两倍。</p> </div>
yesterday@［ˈjestədei］@adv. / n. 昨天</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We went to Fahrenheit's concert yesterday. 昨天我们去了飞轮海的演唱会。</p>
guy@［gai］@n. 家伙，伙计</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He is a sly guy and we don't like him. 他是一个狡猾的家伙，我们都不喜欢他。</p>
star@［sta:(r)］@n. （恒）星；星形（物）；明星，名角</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［starred-starred, starring］ （使）主演，（使）成为明星</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The sky was filled with stars. 夜空中挂满了星星。</p>
danger@［ˈdeindʒə(r)］@n. 危险；危险事物；威胁</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：d+anger（生气）→生气的人很危险→危险</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be in danger 处于危险中</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Although the building is new, it is in danger of collapsing. 这栋大楼虽然是新建的，但有倒塌的危险。</p>
succeed@［səkˈsi:d］@v. 成功；接着发生；接在…后面；接替，继承</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> succeed in （doing） sth. 成功做成某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Very few people succeed in losing weight. 很少有人减肥成功。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> succeeding（adj. 以后的）</p>
blackboard@［ˈblækbɔ:d］@n. 黑板</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher is standing in front of the blackboard. 老师站在黑板前。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00053.jpeg"/></div>
flee@［fli:］@v. ［fled-fled］ （尤指遇到危险等）逃离，逃跑</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：为了自由（free），插翅逃走（flee）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> flee from 从…逃走</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The criminal was caught when he was trying to flee the country. 罪犯试图逃出境的时候被抓了。</p>
avoid@［əˈvɔid］@v. 避免；避开，躲开；预防</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are a lot of ways to avoid catching cold. 有很多方法可以避免得感冒。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> avoidable（adj. 可避免的）；avoidance（n. 回避，躲避）；unavoidably（adv. 不得已；无可奈何地）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">在考试中，常会考到avoid doing sth.的用法，考生一定要牢记，如：Jim tries to avoid meeting his teacher. 吉姆试图避免撞见老师。</p> </div>
subject@［ˈsʌbdʒikt］@ n. 主题，题目；学科，科目；（试验等的）对象；主语；臣民 adj. 受…支配的，取决于…的；易遭…的</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［səbˈdʒek］</span> v. 使服从；使遭受；隶属</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We have six subjects to study this semester. 这个学期我们有六门功课要学。//Smokers are more subject to heart attacks than non-smokers. 吸烟者比不吸烟者更容易患心脏病。</p>
tape@［teip］@n. 带子；磁带；录像带 v. 系，捆；把…录在磁带上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The police have seized various illegal books and tapes. 警方已经缴获各类非法图书和磁带。</p>
about@［əˈｂａʊｔ］@prep. 关于，对于；在…周围，在…各处</p> <p class="bodytext1">adv. 大约，差不多；到处，各处；在附近</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> talk about 谈论，议论；think about 考虑；hear about 听说；know about 了解，知道；look about 四下环顾</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—What's the TV news ______?</p> <p class="bodytext">—The Chinese Team won five gold medals at World Table Tennis Championships. （2009年 连云港）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. at</p> <p class="bodytext">B. across</p> <p class="bodytext">C. above</p> <p class="bodytext">D. about</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—电视新闻是关于什么的？</p> <p class="bodytext4">—中国队在世界乒乓球锦标赛上获得了五枚金牌。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查介词的用法。at后面常接表示具体地点或时间的名词，如：at home 在家；across表示“穿过”；above表示“在…上”；about在此处意为“关于”。故选D。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">注意be about to do本身就有“即将”的意思，因此不再与表示具体时间的词语连用，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（〇） I'm about to leave my room. 我马上离开房间。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（✕） I'm about to leave my room immediately. 我马上离开房间。</p> </div>
restroom@［ˈrestru:m］@n. （公共场所的）洗手间；休息室</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：rest（休息）+room（房间）→休息室；洗手间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Nowadays it is easy to find a restroom in a public place. 如今，在公共场所很容易找到洗手间。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00054.jpeg"/></div>
ninth@［nainθ］@num. 第九 n. 九分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man said he was the ninth child in his family. 这个人说他是家里的第九个孩子。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">注意ninth的拼写，中间没有字母e。</p> </div>
month@［mʌnθ］@n. 月，一个月的时间</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— How often do you write to your uncle?</p> <p class="bodytext">— ______. （2007年 济南）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. Once a month</p> <p class="bodytext">B. One month</p> <p class="bodytext">C. In a month</p> <p class="bodytext">D. For a month</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 你多久给你叔叔写一次信？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 一个月一次。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查的是对how often引导的句子的回答。how often提问做某事的频率。在四个选项中，one month表示一段时间；in a month是“在一个月内”，常用来回答how long引导的句子；for a month也表示一段时间；只有once a month表示频率，是“一个月一次”的意思，因此选A。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">月份前用介词in，具体到一个月的某一天，用on，如：on the 5th day of May 在五月的第5天。一年12个月的表达分别如下：</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00055.jpeg"/></div> </div>
remain@［riˈmein］@v. 仍然是，依旧是；留下，逗留；剩余，余留；留待</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. ［pl.］ 剩余物，残余；残骸，遗体；遗迹</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> It remains to be seen... …有待观望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man remained poor all his life. 那位老人一生贫困。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">remain, retain</p>   <p class="bodytext">remain意为“保持原来的状态”，侧重于状态，如：remain standing 一直站着；而retain有“留存”的意思，如：The couple retained the fireplace when they decorated the room. 这对夫妇装修房间时保留了壁炉。</p> </div>
wound@［wｕ:nd］@n. 创伤，伤口 v. 使受伤，伤害</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He was wounded in the second World War. 他在第二次世界大战中受伤了。</p>
advice@［ədˈvais］@n. 劝告，忠告，意见，建议</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> ask for advice 征求意见；give/offer some advice 提建议；take/follow one's advice 接受某人的意见；a piece of advice 一则建议</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">We need to come up with a/an ______ and make a decision at once. （2009年 通化）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. information</p> <p class="bodytext">B. advice</p> <p class="bodytext">C. idea</p> <p class="bodytext">D. news</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>我们需要提出建议，然后立刻作出决定。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查名词的单复数。在以上四个选项中，information, advice和news都是不可数名词，前面不能直接加a/an修饰，但可以说a piece of news/information/advice。只有idea是可数名词，前面可以直接加冠词an，故选C。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">advice, suggestion</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“建议”的意思。advice是不可数名词，suggestion是可数名词，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">Can you give me a piece of advice? 你能给我一条建议吗？</p>   <p class="bodytext">Can you give me a suggestion? 你能给我个建议吗？</p> </div>
rabbit@［ˈræbit］@n. 兔子</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My little nephew keeps a rabbit as a pet. 我的小外甥养了一只兔子当宠物。</p>
supper@［ˈsʌpə(r)］@n. 晚餐</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We'll have an early supper tonight. 今晚我们早一点吃晚餐。</p>
know@［nəʊ］@v. ［knew-known］ 知道，了解；认识，熟悉；通晓，会；认出，分辨</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I really want to know what is wrong with my brother. 我非常想知道我弟弟怎么了。</p>
arm@［a:m］@n. 臂，前肢；臂状物，扶手；［pl.］ 武器，军备 v. 以（武器）装备；提供，配备；支持</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> arm in arm 手挽手；arm sb. with sth. 以…武装某人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The little boy is sleeping in his mother's arms. 小男孩正在母亲的臂弯里睡觉。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> armed（adj. 武装的）；army（n. 军队）</p>
quick@［kwik］@adj. 快的，迅速的；灵敏的，敏捷的；性急的，不耐烦的 adv. 快，迅速地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom can always give a quick answer to the teacher's questions. 汤姆总能迅速回答出老师的问题。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">quick, fast</p>   <p class="bodytext">quick多指动作发生得突然，且持续时间短暂，侧重指急速、匆忙，如：a quick response 敏捷的反应；fast多指运动物体的快速、持续且不间断，既能作形容词也能作副词，如：There is a fast steamboat on the river. 河上有一艘快艇。</p> </div>
care@［keə(r)］@v. 关心，关怀；担心；介意 n. 照顾，护理；小心，注意；忧虑；挂念</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> take care of 照顾，照料；take care 当心</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think I've learned how to take good care of myself and my family. 我想我已经学会了怎样照顾好自己和家人。</p>
ten@［ten］@num. 十，十个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are ten people at the party. 聚会上有10个人。</p>
guest@［gest］@n. 客人；旅客；特邀嘉宾</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There were more than 100 guests attending the wedding. 有100多位客人参加了婚礼。</p>
dog@［dɒg］@n. 狗；犬科动物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like dogs better than goldfish. 比起金鱼，我更喜欢狗。</p>
outstanding@［aʊtˈstændiŋ］@adj. 杰出的；明显的；未解决的；未偿付的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：out（超出）+stand（站）+ing→站出来的，鹤立鸡群的→杰出的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The man who died yesterday was an outstanding actor. 昨天去世的那个人是一位杰出的演员。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> outstandingly（adv. 非常）</p>
silk@［silk］@n. 丝，丝绸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The girl's skin was as smooth as silk. 那个女孩的皮肤像丝绸一样光滑。</p>
band@［bænd］@n. 乐队；群，伙；带，箍；条纹；波段，频带</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 用带绑扎</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Martin wants to be a band member. 马丁想成为乐队成员。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> bandage（n. 绷带）</p>
specific@［spəˈsifik］@adj. 特定的，特有的；明确的，具体的 n. ［pl.］ 详情，细节</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The money was collected for a specific purpose. 这些钱是为了一个特殊目的募集的。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> specifically（adv. 特定地；明确地）</p>
produce@［prəˈdju:s］@n. 产品；农产品 v. 生产，制造；展现，出示；上演，制作</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We produce a lot of nice and healthy food. 我们生产许多可口又健康的食品。</p>
champion@［ˈtʃæmpiən］@n. 冠军；拥护者 v. 拥护</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：为冠军（champion）开香槟（champagne）庆祝</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lucy used to be the champion of the badminton game. 露西曾经是羽毛球比赛的冠军。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> championship（n. 锦标赛）</p>
local@［ˈləʊkl］@adj. 地方性的，本地的；局部的；狭隘的 n. 当地人，本地人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Alice works as a teacher in a local school. 艾丽斯在当地的一所学校当老师。</p>
her@［hə(r)］@pron. 她 adj. 她的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Her bag is the red one. 她的包是红色的那个。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">her的名词性物主代词是hers，注意二者的区别：前者需要修饰名词，后者不可以修饰名词，要单独使用。</p> </div>
probably@［ˈprɒbəbli］@adv. 大概，或许，很可能</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> We would probably be bored to death. 我们很可能会无聊至极。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">probably在句中的位置很灵活，但不能跟在否定词的后面，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（〇） The man has probably not known the truth. 那个人可能还不知道真相。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">（✕） The man has not probably known the truth. 那个人可能还不知道真相。</p> </div>
distance@［ˈdistəns］@n. 距离，间距；遥远，远方；冷淡，疏远；（时间的）久远</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 来自distant（adj. 遥远的）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a long distance from his school to his home. 从学校到他家距离很远。</p>
river@［ˈrivə(r)］@n. 河流，江，川</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The Changjiang River is one of the longest rivers in the world. 长江是世界上最长的河流之一。</p>
servant@［ˈsɜ:vənt］@n. 仆人；公务员</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My father is a government servant. 我父亲是一名公务员。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00056.jpeg"/></div>
group@［gru:p］@n. 组，群；团体，集团 v. 把…分组</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'm glad to join in the music group. 我很高兴加入这个音乐团体。</p>
up@［ʌp］@adv. 向上，向较高处；往北；成直立姿势，起来；彻底地，完全地 n. 上升；繁荣</p> <p class="bodytext1">prep. 沿…往上；在…上面 adj. 结束了的，完了的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> up to 多达；be up to sb. 是某人的义务或职责；ups and downs 沉浮；兴衰</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> They walked slowly up the hill. 他们缓慢地向山上爬。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">up经常跟动词形成搭配，含有“完全地，彻底地”之意，如：use up 用光了，drink up 喝光了。</p> </div>
member@［ˈmembə(r)］@n. 成员，会员</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I became a member of the sports club. 我成了这个体育俱乐部的会员。</p>
especially@［iˈspeʃəli］@adv. 特别，尤其，格外</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 来自especial（adj.特别的）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I love the scenery of the countryside, especially in spring. 我喜欢乡下的风景，尤其是春天的景色。</p>
immediately@［iˈmi:diətli］@adv. 立即，马上；直接地，紧接着地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I went to work immediately after breakfast. 吃完早餐我立刻去上班了。</p>
material@［məˈtiəriəl］@n. 材料，原料；素材；布料 adj. 物质的，实际的；客观存在的；重要的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：所有的材料（material）都属于物质（matter）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The material of these clothes is so soft. 这些衣服的面料非常柔软。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang">   <p class="bodytext3">material当“材料，原料”讲的时候，可以作可数名词，如：These materials are soft. 这些面料很软。而当“素材”讲的时候是不可数名词，如：The writer found some material for his novel. 作家为他的小说找到了一些素材。</p> </div>
phrase@［freiz］@n. 短语，词组，用语 v. 用语言表达，叙述</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The teacher taught the students some phrases. 老师教给学生一些短语。</p>
speech@［spi:tʃ］@n. 讲话，演说；言语，言论；说话方式</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The President gave a speech at the university. 总统在这所大学做了一次演讲。</p>
five@［faiv］@num. 五</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are five oranges on the table. 桌子上有五个橙子。</p>
cross@［krɒs］@v. 穿过，越过；（使）交叉，（使）相交；（使）杂交 n. 十字架；十字形记号</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's very dangerous to cross the street when traffic lights are red. 当交通信号灯是红色时横穿马路很危险。</p>
latest@［ˈleitist］@adj. 最近的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I read newspapers to get the latest news every day. 我每天看报纸了解最新消息。</p> <div class="xian">   <p class="bodytext2">the last, the latest</p>   <p class="bodytext">the last指一系列事物中的最后一个或者正在谈论的事物之前的一个，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">The last train leaves at 23:00. 最后一班火车23点出发。</p>   <p class="bodytext">I prefer this job to the last one I had. 比起上份工作我更喜欢这一份。</p>   <p class="bodytext">the latest意思是“最近的”，如：The famous writer's latest novel is a great succuss. 这位著名作家最新的小说十分成功。</p> </div>
thank@［θæŋk］@v. 感谢 int. ［pl.］ 谢谢 n. ［pl.］ 感谢，谢意</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Thank you so much for helping me. 多谢您帮助我。</p>
memory@［ˈmeməri］@n. 记忆（力）；回忆；纪念；存储（器）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：有些人经常带着备忘录（memo），因为他们记忆力（memory）不好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My grandmother has a bad memory. 我的祖母记性不好。</p>
dish@［diʃ］@n. 碟，盘；菜肴，一盘菜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> She put the dishes on the table. 她把碟子放到了餐桌上。</p>
include@［inˈklu:d］@v. 包括，包含，计入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The high price includes tax and service charge. 昂贵的价格里面包含税费和服务费。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">include, contain</p><p class="bodytext">二者都有“包含”之意。include只包含部分，而contain包含某事物的整体或部分。如：</p><p class="bodytext">The bag included a book. 那个包里还有一本书。</p><p class="bodytext">The bag contained a book. 那个包里装的是一本书。</p> </div> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00025.jpeg"/></div>
race@［reis］@n. （速度的）比赛，赛跑；竞争；人种，种族</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. 参加（与…的）比赛，（与…）赛速度；（使）高速运转，全速进行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：种族（race）不同，脸（face）部线条也不太一样</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom took part in the relay race at the sports meet. 汤姆参加了运动会上的接力赛跑项目。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> racial（adj. 种族的）</p>
tonight@［təˈnait］@adv. / n. 今晚</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like to invite Lucy to come for dinner tonight. 今晚我想邀请露西过来吃晚饭。</p>
map@［mæp］@n. 地图，图 v. 在地图上标示出；绘制…的地图</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There is a map of the world on the wall. 墙上有一张世界地图。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00026.jpeg"/></div> <div class="hui"> </div>
refuse@［riˈfju:s］@v. 拒绝，不接受，谢绝</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Why do you refuse to go to the party? 你为什么拒绝参加这个聚会？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> refusal（n. 拒绝，回绝）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00027.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">refuse, deny</p><p class="bodytext">refuse表示拒绝时强调主观意愿，如：He refused my invitation. 他拒绝了我的邀请。deny主要是因为客观条件的限制而拒绝，也有“否认”的意思，如：No one can deny the fact that our society has changed a lot. 无人能否认我们的社会发生了很大变化。</p> </div>
step@［step］@n. 步，脚步；步骤，措施；台阶，梯级</p> <p class="bodytext1">v. ［stepped-stepped, stepping］ 跨步，行走；踩，走，踏上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> step by step 逐步地</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He took a step towards the door when he heard the talking outside. 听到外面有人说话，他便向门的方向走了一步。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">step, pace</p><p class="bodytext">step一般指脚步，也指“步骤”或“措施”等抽象概念，如：You should practise your English step by step. 你应该一步步练习你的英语。而pace指走路的速度，如：I can't walk at that pace, or I will be late. 我不能以那样的速度走，不然我会迟到的。</p> </div>
difference@［ˈdifrəns］@n. 差别，差异；差，差额；（意见的）分歧</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can't find the difference between the two pictures. 我找不出这两幅图有什么不同。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> different（adj. 不同的）；differently（adv. 不同地）</p>
seventeenth@［ˌsevnˈti:nθ］@num. 第十七（个） n. 十七分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The story happened in the seventeenth century. 这个故事发生在17世纪。</p>
strategy@［ˈstrætədʒi］@n. 谋略，战略，策略</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I believe I can work out a strategy to deal with this problem. 我相信我可以想出解决这个问题的策略。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> strategic（adj. 战略的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00028.jpeg"/></div> <div class="hui"> </div>
uncle@［ˈʌŋkl］@n. 伯父，叔父，舅父，姑父，姨父</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My uncle is a high school teacher. 我叔叔是一名中学教师。</p>
complain@［kəmˈplein］@v. 抱怨，诉苦；投诉，控告</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> complain to sb. about sth. 向某人抱怨某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Neighbors complained to the police about the cats' meow in the midnight. 邻居们向警方抱怨午夜的猫叫声。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> complaint（n. 埋怨，不满）；complainingly（adv. 不满地）</p>
green@［gri:n］@adj. 绿色的；生的，未成熟的；缺乏经验的，幼稚的；主张保护环境和生态的</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 绿色；<span class="yinbiao1">［pl.］</span> 绿色蔬菜</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Ivy never wears the color green. 艾维从不穿绿色的衣服。// I was pretty green when I graduated from college. 我大学毕业时缺乏经验。</p>
bike@［baik］@n. 自行车</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> by bike 骑自行车</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Why are you walking to school?</p> <p class="bodytext">— Because my ______ is broken. （2008年 上海）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. radio</p> <p class="bodytext">B. watch</p> <p class="bodytext">C. bike</p> <p class="bodytext">D. bag</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 你为什么步行去上学？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 因为我的自行车坏了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题是语境题，考查几个名词的区别。radio意为“收音机”；watch意为“手表”；bike 意为“自行车”；bag意为“书包”。因此答案是C。</p>
effort@［ˈefət］@n. 努力，尝试；努力的成果，成就</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> make an effort to do sth. 努力做某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have to make great effort to study English. 我必须努力学习英语。</p>
grammar@［ˈgræmə(r)］@n. 语法（书）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I need to follow the basic rules of grammar. 我需要遵循语法的基本规则。</p>
pancake@［ˈpænkeik］@n. 薄煎饼，烙饼</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：pan（平底锅）+cake（饼）→用平底锅摊煎饼→薄煎饼</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can you teach me how to make pancakes? 你能教我怎么做煎饼吗？</p> <div class="hui"> </div>
essay@［ˈesei］@n. 短文，文章；随笔，散文</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：光说（say）不写非文章（essay）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The book contains a number of interesting essays. 这本书里有很多有趣的文章。</p>
abroad@［əˈｂｒɔ:ｄ］@adj. 在国外；广泛四散 adv. 到（在）国外；广为流传</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：ab（离去）+road（路）→离开故乡，起程上路→到国外</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> be/go abroad 在/去国外</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> John is abroad on business now. 约翰正在国外出差。</p>
cough@［kɒf］@n. / v. 咳，咳嗽</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I've got a headache and a cough. 我头痛，而且还咳嗽。</p>
like@［laik］@v. 喜欢；想要；希望，愿意 n. ［pl.］ 喜爱的东西，相似的人（或事物）</p> <p class="bodytext1">prep. 像，如 adj. 相像的，相同的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I would like something to drink. 我想喝点东西。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">like, alike</p><p class="bodytext">两个词都有“相同的”之意，但是用法不同。like只能作定语，而alike只能作表语，如：The two brothers are very much alike. 这两兄弟长得非常像。</p> </div>
join@［dʒɔin］@v. 参加，加入；连接，接合</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> join in 参加，加入</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I joined a sports club when I was in college. 大学的时候，我加入了一个体育俱乐部。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">join后可以直接接人或组织，表示加入其中成为成员；而与介词in搭配时，in后接表活动的名词，表示参加，如：</p><p class="bodytext3">We hope you can join us. 我们希望你能加入到我们当中来。</p><p class="bodytext3">Jim decided to join in the game. 吉姆决定参加比赛。</p> </div>
without@［wiˈðaʊt］@prep. 无，没有</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many people in Africa live without enough food. 非洲有许多人没有充足的食物来维持生活。</p>
nervous@［ˈnɜ:vəs］@adj. 神经紧张的，情绪不安的；神经系统的；神经性的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I feel so nervous when I stand on the stage. 我站在舞台上时感觉很紧张。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00029.jpeg"/></div> <div class="hui"> </div>
soon@［su:n］@adv. 不久，即刻；早，快</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：别急，儿子（son）马上（soon）就出生了！</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> as soon as possible 尽快；sooner or later 迟早</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— ______ will the supper be ready? I'm very hungry.</p> <p class="bodytext">—In a minute. （2009年 重庆）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. How soon</p> <p class="bodytext">B. How long</p> <p class="bodytext">C. How much</p> <p class="bodytext">D. How often</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>—晚餐还要多长时间才好？我很饿。</p> <p class="bodytext4">—马上。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查几个词组的区别。how soon表示“再过多久”，主要用于对表示将来的一段时间（如in an hour, in two weeks等）进行提问；how long是对“时间或长度”提问；how much 是对“价格或数量”提问；how often是对“频率”提问。本题应选A。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">当soon前有too, quite, very等词修饰的时候，一般都放在句末，如：We'll reach the place quite soon. 我们很快就要到那个地方了。</p> </div>
only@［ˈəʊnli］@adv. 只，仅仅，才；不料，反而，结果却 adj. 唯一的，仅有的；最好的，独一无二的 conj. 可是，只不过</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> not only...but （also）... 不但…而且…；if only 但愿，要是…就好了（须用虚拟语气）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Jane is the only child of her family. 简是家里唯一的孩子。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">not only...but also...是平行结构，即前后的结构要一致，如：I not only clean the house but also water the flowers. 我不仅打扫房子，还浇花。</p> </div>
poster@［ˈpəʊstə(r)］@n. 招贴（画），海报，广告</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> When he got off the train, Mark saw a poster on the wall of the station. 马克走下火车时，看见车站的墙上贴着一幅海报。</p>
restaurant@［ˈrestrɒnt］@n. 餐馆，饭店</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I usually have my breakfast in the small restaurant downstairs. 我经常在楼下的小餐馆吃早餐。</p> <div class="hui"> </div>
destroy@［diˈstrɔi］@v. 破坏，毁灭</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Heat can gradually destroy Vitamin C. 高温会逐渐破坏维生素C。</p>
finish@［ˈfiniʃ］@v. 完成，结束 n. 结束，末尾，最后阶段（或部分）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> finish doing sth. 完成某事</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> When will you finish your homework? 你什么时候能完成家庭作业？</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">考试中曾考过finish后面接动名词的情况，考生要牢记。</p> </div>
deep@［di:p］@adj. 深的，厚的；深切的，强烈的；（声音）深沉的；（颜色）浓的；深刻的，深奥的 adv. 深深地；在深处</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：夜深（deep）人静睡眠（sleep）好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The water is only a few inches deep. 这水只有几英寸深。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">deep, deeply</p><p class="bodytext">二者都可以作副词，但是有区别。deep作副词表示“深地”，如：dig deep 挖得深；而deeply则带有感情色彩或表示精神方面的内容和抽象内容，如：deeply moved 深深地感动。</p> </div>
elder@［ˈeldə(r)］@adj. 年龄较大的，年长的 n. ［pl.］ 长者，前辈</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My elder sister works in the university. 我姐姐在大学里工作。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">elder, elderly</p><p class="bodytext">二者都与“老”有关，注意区别。elder既可以作形容词“年长的”讲，又可以作名词“长者”讲，常用复数；elderly不是elder的副词形式，而是old的礼貌说法，与定冠词the连用可以表示“老年人”。</p> </div>
photo@［ˈfəʊtəʊ］@n. 照片</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I'll take photos for you. 我会帮你拍些照片。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">photo的复数形式是photos，该词不符合以元音字母o结尾变复数时加-es的规律，类似的单词还有：radio→radios；piano→pianos。</p> </div> <div class="hui"> </div>
weekday@［ˈwi:kdei］@n. 平常日，工作日</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：week（周）+day（天）→每周的天→工作日</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The shop is open from nine in the morning to five in the afternoon on weekdays. 这家店工作日早9点到晚5点营业。</p>
bush@［bʊʃ］@n. 灌木，灌木丛</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：灌木丛（bush）中行走，树枝轻轻拂（brush）过</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Some leaves from a nearby bush fell into the river. 附近灌木丛掉下来的落叶落进了小河里。</p>
wind@［wind］@ n. 风；气息，呼吸</p> <p class="bodytext1"><span class="yinbiao1">［wａiｎｄ］</span> v. ［wound-wound］ 绕，缠绕；（给…）上发条；迂回前进</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The wind is strong in the northern part of China in spring. 春天，中国北方的风很大。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> winded（adj. 通风的）；winding（adj. 弯曲的，蜿蜒的）</p>
fox@［fɒks］@n. 狐狸；狡猾的人</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：狐狸（fox）掉进了箱子（box）里</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The old man is known as a wily old fox. 那个老家伙被公认为是一只狡猾的老狐狸。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00030.jpeg"/></div>
grape@［greip］@n. 葡萄</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I like dark-skinned grapes rather than green grapes. 我喜欢紫葡萄，不喜欢绿葡萄。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00031.jpeg"/></div>
new@［nju:］@adj. 新的；新鲜的，新型的，流行的；更新的 adv. 新近</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Can you tell me something new about the country? 关于这个国家，你能告诉我一些新的东西吗？</p>
divide@［diˈvaid］@v. 分，分隔；分配，分享；除；使产生分歧 n. 分歧；分开；分界线，分水岭</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> divide...into... 把…分成…；divide by 除</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He divided the cake into eight pieces. 他把蛋糕分成了八块。</p>
company@［ˈkʌmpəni］@n. 公司，商号；陪伴，交往；同伴（们），朋友（们）；客人（们）；（一）群，（一）伙</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Bill runs a very large computer company. 比尔经营着一家很大的电脑公司。</p> <div class="hui"> </div>
listen@［ˈlisn］@v. 听；听信</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Listening to music can relieve tiredness. 听音乐可以减轻疲劳。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> listener（n. 听众，收听者）</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">listen是不及物动词，后面不能直接跟宾语，要和介词to连用，如：I am listening to the radio. 我正在听广播。</p> </div>
want@［wɒnt］@v. 想要；希望；需要</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I wanted to be a basketball player when I was young. 小时候，我很想成为篮球运动员。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">当want作“需要”讲的时候，后面可以跟动名词，表达的意思含有被动的成分，如：This old building wants repairing. 这栋老建筑需要修缮一下。</p> </div>
iron@［ˈaiən］@n. 铁；烙铁，熨斗 v. 熨，烫</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom has to iron his shirt every day. 汤姆每天都要熨他的衬衫。</p>
can@［kæn］@v. aux. ［could］ 能，可以；可能，会 n. 罐，罐头 v. ［canned-canned,canning］ 把…装罐保存</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I can do the house keeping myself. 我可以自己做家务。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">can, may</p><p class="bodytext">二者都有“可能”的意思，注意它们的区别。</p><p class="bodytext">（1）表示“可能”时，can和may的可能性大小不同，can的可能性更大。</p><p class="bodytext">（2）can还可以表示有能力做某事，但may不能。如：Can you swim? 你会游泳吗？</p><p class="bodytext">（3）这两个词都可以表示请求允许做某事，can较为口语化，更为常用；may多用于正式文体。</p> </div>
kilometer@［kiˈlɒmitə(r)］@n. 千米</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The tunnel is five kilometers long. 这条隧道长五千米。</p>
extra@［ˈekstrə］@adj. 额外的；特别的 adv. 特别地 n. 额外的事物，另外收费的事物</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The passenger was so nice that he paid the extra cost without complaint. 那位乘客非常好，他付了额外的费用，没有一句怨言。</p> <div class="hui"> </div>
cigarette@［ˈsigəret］@n. 香烟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：cigar（雪茄）+ette（小的）→小雪茄→香烟</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Alcohol and cigarettes should not be allowed to be sold to students. 不允许向学生出售烟酒。</p>
fruit@［fru:t］@n. 水果，果实；成果，结果</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“富肉的”→富含果肉的→水果</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It's good for our health to eat more fruit and vegetables. 多吃水果和蔬菜对我们的健康有益。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">fruit在作水果这一总称时是不可数名词，在做具体某一类水果时是可数名词。如：</p><p class="bodytext3">Eating fruit is good for our health. 吃水果有益健康。</p><p class="bodytext3">The shop sells all kinds of tropical fruits. 商店里卖各种热带水果。</p> </div>
environment@［inˈvairənmənt］@n. 周围状况，环境</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Working environment is very important to me when I'm looking for a new job.在找新工作的时候，工作环境对于我来说非常重要。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> environmental（adj. 环境的）</p>
thirtieth@［ˈθɜ:tiiθ］@num. 第三十（个） n. 三十分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I was asked to hand in my article no later than July the thirtieth. 老师要求我在7月30日之前交论文。</p>
is@［iz］@v. 存在，是（be 动词的第三人称单数形式）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Money is important but it's not the most important thing. 钱很重要，但它不是最重要的东西。</p>
lesson@［ˈlesn］@n. 课；教学单元；一堂课，一节课；教训，经验</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our first lesson on Tuesday is French. 我们周二的第一节课是法语课。</p>
attention@［əˈtenʃn］@n. 注意力，专心；关注；关心；立正姿势</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：at+tent（伸）+ion→伸长脖子听→专心</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> have one's attention 引起某人注意；pay attention to 注意</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The government should pay attention to the needs of the poor. 政府应该关注穷人的需求。</p> <div class="hui"> </div>
I@［ai］@pron. 我</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am a middle school student. 我是一名中学生。</p>
anymore@［ˈeniˌmɒ:(r)］@adv. 再，更，还；目前，现在，今后</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I didn't live in London anymore. 我不在伦敦住了。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"><p class="bodytext3">anymore在考试中常用在not...anymore这一结构中，表示“不再”，相当于not...any longer。如：Lucy didn't live here anymore.= Lucy didn't live here any longer. 露西不在这里住了。</p> </div> <div class="two"><p class="bodytext3">Better to light one candle than to curse the darkness.</p><p class="bodytext-right">—Strong</p><p class="bodytext3">与其诅咒黑暗，不如燃起蜡烛。</p><p class="bodytext-right">——斯特朗</p> </div>
fourteenth@［ˌfɔ:ˈti:nθ］@num. 第十四 n. 十四分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> It is my daughter's fourteenth birthday today. 今天是我女儿的14岁生日。</p>
season@［ˈsi:zn］@n. 季节</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are four seasons in a year and I like spring the most. 一年有四个季节，而我最喜欢春天。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> seasonal（adj. 季节的，季节性的）</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00009.jpeg"/></div>
dentist@［ˈdentist］@n. 牙科医生</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My tooth ached so I had to see the dentist. 我牙疼，得去看牙医。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> dentistry（n. 牙科）</p>
worth@［wɜ:θ］@adj. 相当于…价值的，值得…的 n. 价值，财产</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think the book is worth reading. 我觉得这本书值得一读。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">worth, worthy</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都表示“值得”，但用法有所差别。worth的常见用法是“be worth+名词”或者be worth doing sth.，如：The car is worth 50,000 dollars. 这辆车价值5万美元。This idea is worth considering. 这个主意值得考虑。worthy的常见用法是be worthy of sth.或者be worthy to be done，如：The news is worthy of attention. 这条新闻值得关注。The question is not worthy to be discussed again and again. 这个问题不值得一再讨论。</p></div>
blood@［blʌd］@n. 血，血液；血统，家族</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：心底流（bleed）血（blood）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom was afraid of seeing blood. 汤姆害怕见到血。</p>
scared@［skeəd］@adj. 惊恐的，恐惧的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The thieves got scared and ran away. 盗贼们受到惊吓，逃跑了。</p>
area@［ˈeəriə］@n. 面积；地区，地方；领域，范围</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Many poor people live in rural areas. 许多穷人生活在乡村。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">area, district</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“地区”的意思，但有区别。area侧重表示某一区域的面积或范围，而district侧重表示行政区划，如：Washington District of Columbia 华盛顿特区。</p></div>
lend@［lend］@v. ［lent-lent］ 把…借给，出借；贷</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom lent me some money to buy a new house. 汤姆借给我一些钱来买新房。</p>
tourist@［ˈtʊərist］@n. 旅游者，观光者</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The tourist complained that the room was too dirty to live in. 游客抱怨房间太脏了，没法住。</p>
uncomfortable@［ʌnˈkʌmftəbl］@adj. 不舒服的；不舒适的；感到（或引起）不安的，不自在的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 派生词：un（不）+comfort（舒服）+able（可…的）→不舒服的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I couldn't sleep well last night because the bed was so uncomfortable. 我昨天晚上没有睡好，因为床很不舒服。</p>
scientist@［ˈsaiəntist］@n. 科学家</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Einstein, a famous scientist, was born in March, 1879. 著名科学家爱因斯坦出生于1879年3月。</p>
mile@［mail］@n. 英里</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My home is three miles away from the school. 我家距学校3英里远。</p>
example@［igˈza:mpl］@n. 例子，实例；榜样，楷模</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> for example 例如；give an example 举例；take...for example 以…为例</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Li Ming has set a good example for all of us. 李明为我们树立了好榜样。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00011.jpeg"/></div>
aim@［eim］@n. 目的，目标；瞄准 v. 瞄准，对准；目的是，旨在；针对；力争做到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：我的目标（aim）是（am）做我自己</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> aim at 瞄准；针对</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My aim is to find a good job. 我的目标是找到一份好工作。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">aim, goal</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“目标”之意。aim是从本义“靶子”延伸出来的意思，侧重具体而明确的目标，可接不定式或与at连用。goal指经过考虑和选择，需经坚持不懈的努力奋斗才能达到的最终目标。</p></div>
see@［si:］@v. ［saw-seen］ 看，观看；参见，会晤；领会，理解；想象；把…看作；发现，学懂；体验，经历；搞清楚，查询</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> see to 处理，照料；see sb. off 给某人送行</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I haven't seen Mary for a long time. 我好久没有见过玛丽了。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">see, look, watch</p>   <p class="bodytext">三者都有“看”的意思，注意它们的区别：</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00012.jpeg"/></div></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"> <p class="bodytext3">see sb. do sth.是“看见某人做了某事”（已经做完了），如：I saw him steal things. 我看见他偷了东西。而see sb. doing sth.是“看见某人正在做某事”，如：I saw him stealing things. 我看见他正在偷东西。</p></div>
chew@［tʃu:］@v. 咀嚼；（因为紧张等）咬住，不停地啃</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 发音记忆：“刍”→一些动物咀嚼后反刍→咀嚼</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> chewing gum（n. 口香糖）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Lily's tooth ached so much that she felt it difficult to chew food. 莉莉牙疼，她觉得咀嚼食物都很困难。</p>
reply@［riˈplai］@n. / v. 回答，答复，以…作答</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> reply to 回答，对…作出反应</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I sent an e-mail to Sandy but there was no reply. 我给桑迪发了一封邮件，但是没有收到回复。</p>
achieve@［əˈtʃi:v］@v. 实现，完成；获得，达到</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：相信（believe）自己能取得（achieve）成功</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">—My dream is to be a well-known star.</p> <p class="bodytext">—I believe you will realize your dream if you keep on working hard.</p> <p class="bodytext">（2009年 黄冈）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. imagine</p> <p class="bodytext">B. complete</p> <p class="bodytext">C. come true</p> <p class="bodytext">D. achieve</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span><span class="calibre6">—我的梦想是成为明星。</span></p> <p class="bodytext4">—我相信如果你一直勤奋努力，你会实现你的梦想。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span><span class="calibre6">本题考查词义与画线部分含义相近的词。其中最具迷惑性的是come true，意思是“实现”，但是该短语后面不能接名词，只能说My dream will come true. 我的梦想将会实现。imagine意为“想象”；complete意为“完成”；只有achieve可以表示梦想的实现，故选D。</span></p>
die@［dai］@v. ［dying］ 死，死亡；消失；停止运行；渴望；消逝，熄灭</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> die out 灭绝，熄灭；die for 渴望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My grandfather died when I was only eight years old. 我八岁的时候我爷爷就去世了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00014.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"> <p class="bodytext3">die经常和of或from连用，表示“死于”，考生要注意区别。die of后接的名词是死亡的内因，如：die of cancer死于癌症，而die from后接的名词是外因，如：die from fire死于火灾。</p></div>
fresh@［freʃ］@adj. 新的，新到的；新鲜的，未经腌熏的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：新来的（fresh）人自由（free）散漫</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> You can enjoy fresh air when you go fishing in the countryside. 去乡间垂钓的时候你可以呼吸一下新鲜空气。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> freshen（v. 使新鲜，使清新）</p>
top@［tɒp］@n. 顶，顶端；上部，上端；首位，最高位</p> <p class="bodytext1">adj. 最高的；最优良的 v. ［topped-topped, topping］ 居于…之上，位于…之首；高过，超过</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> on top of 在…之上</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> All of us climbed to the very top of the mountain. 我们所有人都爬上了山顶。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00015.jpeg"/></div>
nothing@［ˈnʌθiŋ］@pron. 没有东西，没有事情，一点儿也没有；无关紧要的人（或事）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：no（不，无）+thing（东西）→没有东西</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I have nothing to do at the moment. 我此刻无事可做。</p>
boss@［bɒs］@n. 老板，上司，头儿</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our boss is a young man. 我们老板是一个年轻人。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> bossy（adj. 专横的，爱发号施令的）</p>
depend@［diˈpend］@v. 依靠，依赖；信赖，相信；取决于，视…而定</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> depend on 依靠，指望</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mark is the kind of person that we can depend on. 马克是个可以信赖的人。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> dependable（adj. 可信赖的）；dependence（n. 依赖）；dependent（adj. 依赖的；取决于…的）</p>
silent@［ˈsailənt］@adj. 寂静的；沉默的；无声的，不发出声音的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：英文圣诞歌曲Silent Night 《平安夜》</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Both of their parents nodded in silent agreement. 双方父母都点头表示默认。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> silence（n. 寂静；沉默）</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">silent, quiet</p>   <p class="bodytext">silent不仅有“寂静的”之意，还有“沉默的”之意；而quiet强调的是“安静的，轻声的”，如：Please be quiet!请安静一点儿！</p></div>
honor@［ˈɒnə(r)］@n. 尊敬，敬意；荣誉，光荣 v. 尊敬</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I consider it a great honor to be invited to the party. 能够受邀参加此次聚会，我感到十分荣幸。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"> <p class="bodytext3">注意该词中的h不发音，在听的过程中要留心。</p></div>
rude@［ru:d］@adj. 粗鲁的，无礼的；粗糙的，粗陋的；猛烈的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Our physics teacher is so rude. We don't like him. 我们的物理老师太粗暴了，我们都不喜欢他。</p>
thief@［θi:f］@n. 贼，小偷</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The thief slid into the room and stole a lot of money. 小偷溜进房间偷了许多钱。</p>
junk@［dʒʌŋk］@n. 废旧物品，破烂 v. 丢弃，废弃</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I don't like junk food. 我不喜欢垃圾食品。</p>
weight@［weit］@n. 重量，体重；砝码，秤砣；重压，负担；重要性，重大</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> lose weight 减肥；put on weight 长胖</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Considering his health condition, he should lose weight. 考虑到健康情况，他应该减肥。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00016.jpeg"/></div>
think@［θiŋk］@v. ［thought-thought］ 认为，以为；想，思索；想要，打算 n. 想，思考</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：仔细想想（think），这事还是要感谢（thank）你</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> think of 看待；想到，想起；think about 考虑，思考；think over 仔细考虑，琢磨；think out 认真考虑；仔细盘算</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I think my mother will come to see me. 我想妈妈会来看我。</p>
activity@［ækˈtivəti］@n. 活动，行动；活跃，活力</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 词根记忆：act（活动）+ivity（名词后缀）→活动</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom had a rest after an activity. 汤姆活动后休息了一会儿。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> activist（n. 积极分子；活动家）</p>
captain@［ˈkæptin］@n. 船长，机长；上尉；队长，领队</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The captain gave the order to turn left. 船长下令向左转。</p>
brave@［breiv］@adj. 勇敢的，无畏的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：勇敢的（brave）人不畏生死，不惧坟墓（grave）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The young soldier was very brave. 那个年轻的士兵非常勇敢。</p>
still@［stil］@adv. 依然，还，仍旧；然而，尽管如此；甚至更，还要；静止地</p> <p class="bodytext1">adj. 静止的，寂静的，平静的 n. 寂静 v. （使）平静，（使）静止</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：好莱坞科幻电影《地球停转之日》（The Day the Earth Stood Still）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Do you still live in the town? 你还在这个镇上住吗？</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">still, yet</p>   <p class="bodytext">still指过去已经开始的动作，说话时仍在继续，可用于肯定、否定或疑问句中；yet通常用在疑问句和否定句中，用于预料即将发生但尚未发生的事情。</p></div>
hang@［hæŋ］@v. ［hung-hung］ 悬挂，吊；徘徊；［hanged-hanged］ 吊死，绞死</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> hang out/around 闲荡；hang on（打电话时）不挂断；hang up 挂断（电话）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— Sorry, I have to ______ now. It's time for class.</p> <p class="bodytext">— OK, I'll call back later. （2009年 天津）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. hang up</p> <p class="bodytext">B. break up</p> <p class="bodytext">C. give up</p> <p class="bodytext">D. hold up</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span><span class="calibre6">— 不好意思，我要挂断电话了，我该上课了。</span></p> <p class="bodytext4">— 好的，晚些时候我再打给你。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查词组的辨析。hang up意为“挂断（电话）”；break up意为“打断”；give up意为“放弃”；hold up意为“保持通话”。因此，根据句意，本题应该选A。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00017.jpeg"/></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"> <p class="bodytext3">考生要注意hang的过去式和过去分词，在表示“悬挂，吊；徘徊”时，其过去式和过去分词是hung；在表示“吊死，绞死”时，其过去式和过去分词是hanged。</p></div>
happen@［ˈhæpən］@v. 发生；碰巧，恰好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> An accident happened on the street last night. 昨晚街上发生了一起事故。</p>
sixteen@［ˌsiksˈti:n］@num. 十六，十六个</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> His father moved to Paris when he was sixteen. 他父亲在他16岁那年搬到了巴黎。</p>
thirteenth@［ˌθɜ:ˈti:nθ］@num. 第十三（个） n. 十三分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> I am the thirteenth student to receive the health checkup in my class. 我是我们班里第13个接受健康体检的学生。</p>
heaven@［ˈhevən］@n. 天堂，［pl.］ 天国；天，天空；上帝，神</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Snow fell from the heavens all day long. 雪已经下了一整天了。</p>
empty@［ˈempti］@adj. 空的；空闲的；空虚的 v. （使）空，倒出</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The bottle is empty. 瓶子空了。</p> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00018.jpeg"/></div> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">empty, blank</p>   <p class="bodytext">二者都有“空的”之意。 empty指房间等空间是空的，而blank常指空白的，还可以指大脑的空白或表情茫然，此外，blank还可以作名词，意为“空格”，如：fill in the blank 填空。</p></div>
neither@［ˈnaiðə(r)］@pron. 两者都不 adv. 也不</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：n（看作no，不）+either（任一个）→两者都不</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> neither...nor... 既不…也不…</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">______ Lucy ______ Lily may go dancing with you, because they are not allowed to go out on school nights. （2008年 恩施）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. Either; or</p> <p class="bodytext">B. Neither; nor</p> <p class="bodytext">C. Both; and</p> <p class="bodytext">D. Not only; but also</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>露西和莉莉都不能和你跳舞，因为她们被禁止在晚自习期间离校。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>either...or... 意为“要么…要么…”，neither...nor...意为“既不…也不…”，both...and...意为“…和…都”，not only..., but also...意为“不但…而且…”。根据后半句的句意可知，前半句要表达的是否定含义，故选B。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">neither, either</p>   <p class="bodytext">neither表示两者中的任何一个都不，常和nor连用，也可单独使用，如：Tony's house is neither big nor small. 托尼的房子不大也不小。Neither of the twins is here. 双胞胎一个也不在这儿。either是指两者之一，常和or连用，也可单独使用，如：I think Susan is either American or British. 我想苏珊不是美国人就是英国人。Please wear either coat. 请随便穿件外套。当either作连词时，表示否定含义的“也”，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext">— I don't smoke.</p>   <p class="bodytext">— Me either.</p>   <p class="bodytext">— 我不抽烟。</p>   <p class="bodytext">— 我也不抽。</p></div>
sky@［skai］@n. 天（空）</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The sky grew dark, and a heavy rain began to fall. 天色转暗，一场大雨倾盆而下。</p>
toward(s)@［təˈwɔ:d(z)］@prep. 向，朝，面对；接近</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> He was standing with his back towards me. 他背对我站着。</p>
third@［θɜ:d］@num. 第三（个） n. 三分之一</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">— I hear your pen friend is visiting Lianyungang again. Is it the ______ time for him?</p> <p class="bodytext">— Yes, and he will come for a third time next spring. （2009年 连云港）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. first</p> <p class="bodytext">B. second</p> <p class="bodytext">C. third</p> <p class="bodytext">D. fourth</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>— 我听说你的笔友又要来连云港旅游了，这是他第二次来吗？</p> <p class="bodytext4">— 是的，明年春天他再来就是第三次了。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题是一道语境题，根据答语可知应该选B。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"> <p class="bodytext3">third和thirdly在汉语中都有“第三”的意思，但third前面经常跟定冠词the，是序数词；而thirdly是“第三”，经常在一些文章中，与firstly，secondly并列，分别表示“第一”、“第二”和“第三”。</p>   <p class="bodytext3">英语中表达分数一般用“基数词+序数词”的方法，基数词表示分子，序数词表示分母。当分子为1的时候序数词用单数，分子大于1的情况下序数词要用复数，如：</p>   <p class="bodytext3"><img alt="" class="zaozi3" src="xdfcz-00019.jpeg"/> one-fourth / a quarter</p>   <p class="bodytext3"><img alt="" class="zaozi3" src="xdfcz-00020.jpeg"/> two-thirds</p>   <p class="bodytext3"><img alt="" class="zaozi3" src="xdfcz-00021.jpeg"/> a half / one half</p>   <p class="bodytext3"><img alt="" class="zaozi3" src="xdfcz-00022.jpeg"/> three and two-fifths</p></div>
newspaper@［ˈnju:zpeipə(r)］@n. 报纸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 合成词：news（新闻）+paper（纸）→印有新闻的纸→报纸</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Did you read today's evening newspaper? 你读了今天的晚报没？</p>
volleyball@［ˈvɒlibɔ:l］@n. 排球</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My brother was a volleyball player when he was in college. 我哥哥上大学的时候是排球选手。</p>
pupil@［ˈpju:pl］@n. （小）学生；瞳孔</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> There are 40 pupils in our class. 我们班里有40名学生。</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">pupil, student</p>   <p class="bodytext">pupil一般指小学生，而student泛指学生，包括大学生和专科学校的学生。</p></div> <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00023.jpeg"/></div>
fantastic@［fænˈtæstik］@adj. 极好的，极出色的；了不起的；异想天开的，不实际的；奇异的，古怪的</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> My family watched a fantastic play yesterday evening. 昨晚我们一家人看了一场非常精彩的演出。</p>
dare@［deə(r)］@v. 敢，敢做 v. aux. 敢，竟敢</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> No one dares to answer the question without the permission of the head. 没有领导的允许，没人敢回答这个问题。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"> <p class="bodytext3">dare除了可以作实义动词之外，还可以作情态动词。dare作实义动词时有人称和数以及时态的变化，其后的动词不定式可带to也可不带to。dare作情态动词时，后跟动词原形，主要用于疑问句、否定句和条件句中。</p></div>
treat@［tri:t］@v. 对待，处理；治疗，医治；款待，招待 n. 款待，招待</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：tr+eat（吃）→吃药→治疗</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> No matter how old you are, your parents still treat you like a child. 不管你多大了，父母都会拿你当孩子看。</p>
us@［ʌs］@pron. 我们</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Please contact us if you have any problems. 如果您有任何问题请联系我们。</p>
should@［ʃəd］@v. aux. （shall的过去式）将要；（表示义务、责任）应当，应该；（表示假设）万一，竟然；（表示意愿）就，该；（表示推测）可能</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">真题点评</span></p> <p class="bodytext">This printer is of good quality. If it ______ break down within the first year, we would repair it at our expense. （2009年 天津）</p> <p class="bodytext">A. would</p> <p class="bodytext">B. should</p> <p class="bodytext">C. could</p> <p class="bodytext">D. might</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">译文：</span>这台打印机质量很好。如果它在第一年内出现任何问题，将由我们承担维修费用。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="blue-title">解析：</span>本题考查虚拟语气的用法，表示对将来的情况进行推测，用“If+主语+should / did / were to do”这一结构，因此本题选B。</p> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"> <p class="bodytext3">should+have done表示应该做而没有做，有责备的语气，如：I should have studied harder last term. 上学期我本该更努力学习的。</p></div>
engineer@［ˌendʒiˈniə(r)］@n. 工程师，机械师</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：engine（发动机）+er→修理发动机的人→工程师</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Tom's father is a software engineer. 汤姆的父亲是一位软件工程师。</p>
connect@［kəˈnekt］@v. 连接，衔接；联合，关联；接通电话</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> connect A to/with B 把A和B联系/连接起来</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> The two subjects are closely connected with each other. 这两门学科联系得非常紧密。</p>
hobby@［ˈhɒbi］@n. 业余爱好，嗜好</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Playing badminton is one of my hobbies. 打羽毛球是我的爱好之一。</p>
wear@［weə(r)］@v. 穿着，戴着，留（须、发）；面露，面带，呈现；磨损，用旧</p> <p class="bodytext1">n. 穿，戴；服装，穿戴物；磨损，损坏</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">记</span> 联想记忆：穿得（wear）这么漂亮，准备去哪儿（where）啊？</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">搭</span> wear down 磨损，损耗；wear out （常用于被动语态） 穿破；累坏</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">例</span> Mary is wearing a pair of black shoes. 玛丽穿着一双黑色的鞋子。</p> <p class="bodytext"><span class="juli">派</span> wearable（adj. 可穿戴的；耐磨的）</p> <div class="xian"><p class="bodytext2">wear, dress, put on</p>   <div><img alt="" src="xdfcz-00024.jpeg"/></div>   <p class="bodytext">此外，wear还可以表示戴表、戴眼镜、洒香水，dress和put on则没有这种用法，如：What perfume do you wear? 你喷的什么香水啊？</p></div> <p class="tips-title">▸ Tips</p> <div class="kuang"> <p class="bodytext3">wear与疑问代词where的读音是一样的，注意在听力材料中区分这两个词。</p></div>
